brāhmaṇāḥ pūjitā bhaktyā nānāratnavibhūṣitāḥ ।
praśaśaṃsuśca nṛpatiṃ surāḥ pūrṇamanorathāḥ ।।

athānyat kathayiṣyāmi tīrthāt tīrthamanuttamam ।
revāmatsyāsamāyoge surāsuranamaskṛtam ।।

nābhāgasya ca saṃvādam āpastambasya cānagha ।
manvantare cākṣuṣe vai saṃprāpte dvāpare yuge ।।

nāmnā matsyeśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ jalamadhye vyavasthitam ।
pūjyate nāgakanyābhir na taṃ paśyanti mānuṣāḥ ।।

mahātejo maṇimayaṃ candrabimbasamaprabham ।
smaraṇād yasya devasya brahmahatyā praṇaśyati ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
sādhubhiḥ saha saṃvāsāt ke guṇāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।
kāḥ kathāḥ kāni puṇyāni saṅgame sāptakalpage ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
atraivodāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam ।
nābhāgasya ca saṃvādam āpastamba taponidheḥ ।।

maharṣiścātmavān pūrvam āpastambo dvijottamaḥ ।
upavāsakṛtārambho babhūva bhagavāṃs tathā ।।

nityam krodhaṃ ca kāmañca lobhaṃ mohaṃ visṛjya ca ।
revāmatsyāsamāyoge viveśa salilāśaye ।।

sa matsyaiḥ salilāvarte saritaścānugais tadā ।
tatrānyotpatitair jālaiḥ samānīto mahāyaśāḥ ।।

tasmād uttārayām āsuḥ salilād brahmanandanam ।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā tapasā dīptaṃ kaivartā bhayavihvalāḥ ।।

śirobhiḥ praṇipatyoccair idaṃ vacanamabruvan ।
ajñānāt kriyamāṇānāmasmākaṃ kṣantum arhasi ।।

kiṃ vā kiṃ ca priyaṃ te adya tadājñāpaya suvrata ।
sa munistan mahad dṛṣṭvā matsyānāṃ kadanaṃ kṛtam ।।

kṛpayā parayāviṣṭo dāśān provāca duḥkhitaḥ ।
duḥkhitānīha bhūtāni yo na bhūtaiḥ pṛthag vidhaiḥ ।।

kevalātma sukhecchāto aven nṛśaṃsataro asti kaḥ ।
aho asvastheṣvakāruṇyaṃ svaārthe caiva balirvṛthā ।।

jñāninām api ced yas tu kevalātmahite rataḥ ।
jñānino hi yathā svārtham āśritya dhyānam āśritāḥ ।।

duḥkhārtānīha bhūtāni prayānti śaraṇaṃ tataḥ ।
yo abhivāñchati bhoktuṃ vai sukhānyekān tato janaḥ ।।

pāpāt parataraṃ taṃ hi pravadanti mumukṣavaḥ ।
ko nu me syād upāyo hi yenāhaṃ duḥkhitātmanām ।।

antaḥpraviśya bhūtānāṃ bhaveyaṃ sarvaduḥkhabhuk ।
yanmamāsti śubhaṃ kiṃcit tad dīnān upagacchatu ।।

yat kṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ taiśca tadaśeṣamupaitu mām ।
dṛṣṭvā tān kṛpaṇān vyaṅgān anaṅgān rogiṇas tathā ।।

dayā na jāyate yasya sa rakṣa iti me matiḥ ।
prāṇasaṃśayamāpannān prāṇino bhayavihvalān ।।

yo na rakṣati śasto api sa tatpāpaṃ samaśnute ।
āhūtānāṃ nayārtānāṃ sukhaṃ yad upajāyate ।।

tasya svargāpavargau ca kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।
tasmāccaitān ahaṃ dīnāṃ chaktuṃ mīnān suduḥkhitān ।।

yādṛṅmātraṃ na paśyāmi kiṃ punas tridaśālayam ।
niśamyaitan muner vākyaṃ dāśāste jātasaṃbhramāḥ ।।

yathārthaṃ tu tathā sarvaṃ nābhāgāya nyavedayan ।
nābhāgo api tataḥ śrutvā taṃ draṣṭuṃ brahmanandanam ।।

tvaritaḥ prayayau tatra sāmātyaḥ sapurohitaḥ ।
sa samyak pūjayitvā tu devakalpaṃ nṛpas tataḥ ।।

provāca bhagavan vidvan kiṃ karomi tavājñayā ।

āpastamba uvāca śrameṇa mahatāviṣṭāḥ kaivartā duḥkhajīvinaḥ ।।

mama mūlyaṃ prayaccheti yad yogyaṃ manyase nṛpa ।

nābhāga uvāca sahasrāṇi śataṃ mūlyaṃ niṣādebhyo dadāmy aham ।।

niṣkrayārthaṃ hi bhagavan nītaṃ te brahmanandana ।

āpastamba uvāca nāhaṃ śatasahasreṇa niyamyaḥ pārthiva tvayā ।।

sadṛśaṃ dīyatāṃ mūlyam amātyaiḥ saha cintaya ।

nābhāga uvāca koṭiṃ pradīyatāṃ mūlyaṃ niṣādebhyo dvijottama ।।

yady etad api yogyaṃ no tato bhūyaḥ pradīyatām ।

āpastamba uvāca rājannārhā vayaṃ koṭimadhikaṃ cāpi pārthiva ।।

sadṛśaṃ dīyatāṃ mūlyaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ saha saṃvada ।

rājovāca arddhaṃ rājyaṃ samastaṃ vā niṣādebhyaḥ pradīyate ।।

etan mūlyam ahaṃ manye kiṃ vālaṃ manyase dvija ।

āpastamba uvāca arddhaṃ rājyaṃ samastaṃ vā nāham arhāmi vai nṛpa ।।

sadṛśaṃ dīyatāṃ mahyaṃ ṛṣibhiḥ saha cintaya ।
maharṣes tadvacaḥ śrutvā nābhāgas tu vivādayan ।।

cintayāmāsa dharmātmā sāmātyaḥ sapurohitaḥ ।
tataḥ kaścid ṛṣis tatra lomaśastu mahātapāḥ ।।

nābhāgam abravīt mābhaiḥ toṣayiṣyāmi taṃ munim ।

rājovāca brūhi mūlyaṃ mahābhāga me jñātikulabāndhavān ।।

nirdagdhavān ṛṣiḥ kruddhas trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।
kiṃ punar mānavaṃ dīnam atyalpaṃ viṣayātmakam ।।

lomaśa uvāca
tvaṃ samartho mahārāja jagatpūjyā dvijottamāḥ ।
gāvaśca divyāstasmād vai mūlyam asmai pradīyatām ।।

tataḥ śrutvā tu vacanaṃ sa sāmātyapurohitaḥ ।
harṣeṇa mahatāviṣṭaḥ provācedaṃ vaco munim ।।

uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha bhagavan kṛtameva na saṃśayaḥ ।
etad yogyataṃ mūlyaṃ bhavato munisattama ।।

āpastamba uvāca
uttiṣṭhāmy eva saṃprītyā samyak krīto asmi pārthiva ।
gobhyo mūlyaṃ na paśyāmi pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam ।।

gāvaḥ pradakṣiṇī kāryyā vandanīyā hi nityaśaḥ ।
maṅgalāyatana divyās sṛṣṭās tvetāḥ svayambhuvā ।।

apyāgārāṇi viprāṇāṃ devatāyatanāni ca ।
yadgomayena śuddhyanti kiṃ brūmo hyadhikaṃ tataḥ ।।

gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi sarpis tathaiva ca ।
gavāṃ pañca pavitrāṇi punanti sakalaṃ jagat ।।

gāvo me cāgrato nityaṃ gāvaḥ pṛṣṭhata eva ca ।
gāvo me hṛdaye caiva gavāṃ madhye vasāmyaham ।।

eva yaḥ paṭhate nityaṃ trisandhyaṃ niyataḥ śuciḥ ।
mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ svargalokaṃ sa gacchati ।।

agre grāsaparo bhāvaḥ kartavyo bhaktito anvaham ।
akṛtvā svayamāhāraṃ kurvannāpnoti durgatim ।।

tenāgnayo hutās samyak pitaraś cāpi tārpitāḥ ।
devāśca pūjitās tena yo dadāti gavāhnikam ।।

mantraḥ
saurabheyī jagatpūjyā nitya viṣṇupade sthitā ।
sarvadevamayī grāsaṃ mayā dattaṃ pratīkṣatām ।।

rakṣaṇād brahmaputrāṇāṃ gavāṃ kaṇḍūyanāt tathā ।
kṣīṇārtarakṣaṇāc caiva tataḥ svarge mahīyate ।।

ādirhi gāvo yajñasya madhyaṃ cāntyaṃ prakīrtitāḥ ।
kṣaranti tās tu sakalaṃ kṣīrājyamamṛtaṃ tathā ।।

tasmād gāvaḥ pradātavyāḥ pūjanīyā hi nityaśaḥ ।
svargasya saṅgamāyaitās sopānaṃ hi vinirmitāḥ ।।

etacchrutvā niṣādāste gavāṃ māhātmyam uttamam ।
praṇipatya mahābhāgam āpastambam athābruvan ।।

niṣādā ūcuḥ
sambhāṣā darśanasparśavarṇanaṃ kīrtanaṃ tathā ।
pāvanāni samastāni sādhūnām iti naḥ śrutam ।।

sambhāṣā darśanaṃ caivam ihāsmābhiḥ kṛtaṃ dvija ।
kuruṣvānugrahaṃ tasmāt tvāṃ vayaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।।

āpastamba uvāca
etāṃ gāṃ pratigṛhṇantu tatas te muktakilbiṣāḥ ।
niṣādāśca gatāḥ svargaṃ saha matsyair jalodbhavaiḥ ।।

prāṇināṃ prītimutpādya ninditenā api karmaṇā ।
narakaṃ yadi paśyāmi vatsyāmi svargam eva vā ।।

yanmayā sukṛtaṃ kiṃcin manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ ।
kṛta tenāpi duḥkhārtāḥ sarve yāntu śubhāṃ gatim ।।

tatas tasya prasādena maharṣer bhāvitātmanaḥ ।
niṣādās tena vākyena saha matsyā divaṃ gatāḥ ।।

tān dṛṣṭvā atha gatān svargaṃ samatsyān matsyajīvinaḥ ।
sāmātyabhṛtyo nṛpatir vismayād idam abravīt ।।

sevyāḥ śreyo arthibhiḥ santaḥ tīrthaṃ puṇyaṃ jalottamam ।
kṣaṇopāsanamapyatra na teṣāṃ niṣkalaṃ bhavet ।।

sadbhissaha samāsīta sadbhiḥ kurvīta satkathām ।
āpastambo munis tatra lomaśaśca mahātapā ।।

padais tu vividhair iṣṭair bodhayāmāsa tu nṛpam ।
tataḥ saṃdhārayāmāsa dharmabuddhiṃ sudurlabhām ।।

tatheti kṛtvā coktvā ca nṛpaṃ taṃ praśaśaṃsatuḥ ।
aho dhanyo asi rājendra yat te dharmaparāmatiḥ ।।

dharmaḥ sudurlabhaḥ puṃsāṃ viśeṣeṇa mahīkṣitām ।
yadi rājyamadāviṣṭaḥ svadharmaṃ na parityajet ।।

tato jagati kas tasmāt punar abhyadhiko bhavet ।
dhruvaṃ dharmaśca rājyaṃ vai mohaścaiva sadā dhruvaḥ ।।

mahādhruvaśca narako rājyaṃ nindanti te budhāḥ ।
rājyaṃ hi manyate mūḍho naro viṣayalolupaḥ ।।

manīṣiṇas tu paśyanti sadaiva narakopamam ।
tasmācchokaśca mohaśca na kartavyo madas tvayā ।।

yadīcchasi mahārāja śāśvatīṃ gatimātmanaḥ ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca ityuktvā mahātmānau jagmatuḥ svaṃ svamāśramam ।।

nābhāgo api varaṃ labdhvā prahṛṣṭastvaviśat puram ।
etat te kathitaṃ rājan ye gaṇāḥ satsamāgame ।।

māhātmyaṃ vai gavāṃ tadvat kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchasi ।
revāmatsyāsamāyoge gavāṃ māhātmyamuttamam ।।

tatra snātvā mahārāja matsyeśvaramathā arcaya ।
āpastambo mahābhāgo niṣādā matsyajīvinaḥ ।।

matsyaiḥ saha gatāḥ svargaṃ tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।
divyakāntidharāḥ sarve loke krīḍanti vaiṣṇave ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe matsyeśvaratīrthavarṇanonāma trayodaśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athānyat kathayiṣyāmi tīrthaṃ pāpavimokṣaṇam ।
matsyāyāḥ śubhatāpyāśca saṅgame surasevitam ।।

devo matsyeśvaro nāma nāgakanyābhirarcitaḥ ।
tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtā na punarbhavāḥ ।।

pañcavaktrāstrinetrāśca matsyatīrthaprabhāvataḥ ।
kalahaṃsa iti khyāto devarṣir dhyānatatparaḥ ।।

tasyāśramaṃ paraṃ ramyaṃ brahmarṣi viniṣevitam ।
śākamūlaphalāhāro japadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ।।

so atiṣṭhad ayutaṃ sārddham ekapādena bhārata ।
śivadhyānaparo bhūtvā sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।।

tatas tu dhyānayogena tasya devaḥ śatakratuḥ ।
cakampe tapasā cāsau devarājo bhaviṣyati ।।

hariṣyati na sandeho purīṃ caivāmarāvatīm ।
brāhmaṇaśca sureśānaḥ kubjo vāmanarūpadhṛk ।।

jagāma vṛddharūpeṇa kalahaṃsāśramam prati ।
uvāca vacanaṃ śakro brāhmaṇaṃ tapasi sthitam ।।

kimarthaṃ tapase śīghraṃ kāmam etad bravīhi me ।
ārādhayasi kaṃ devaṃ satyam etat tapodhana ।।

saṃhṛtya tapasā yogaṃ prahasannabravīd vacaḥ ।
jānāmi tvāṃ mahābhāga śakras tvaṃ tridaśeśvaraḥ ।।

na kāmaye aham indratvaṃ rājyaṃ kuru yathepsitam ।
ārādhayāmyahaṃ devaṃ nānyaṃ devaṃ kathañcana ।।

etacchrutvā vacas tasya maharṣer abravīd vṛṣaḥ ।
varaṃ vṛṇu mahābhāga yathā drakṣyasi śaṅkaram ।।

kalahaṃsa uvāca
vinā ahaṃ tryambakaṃ yāce nānyād devādaho varam ।
vijayī bhava śakra tvaṃ nānyaṃ vṛṇe varaṃ tvaham ।।

evamukto yayau śakraḥ sarvakāmasamanvitaḥ ।
jñātvā tasya parāṃ bhaktiṃ devadevo maheśvaraḥ ।।

adarśayad athātmānaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ trilocanam ।
dṛṣṭvā rūpaṃ maheśasya sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇipatya ca ।।

kalahaṃso muniśreṣṭhaḥ stotuṃ samupacakrame ।
namo astu te mahādeva nīlakaṇṭhatrilocana ।।

namaḥ śivāya śāntāya śūlahasta namo astu te ।
namaḥ śivāya śambhavāyā anāthāya namo namaḥ ।।

tryambakāya mahādevetyādi nāmādibhiḥstuta oṃ namo devāya śambhavāya bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ ।
somarudradhvāntasūryāya namo rudrāgnaye namaḥ ।।

namaḥ śambho pañcavaktra mahāśiva namo astu te ।
svayambhūvana pātāla nīlakaṇṭha namo astu te ।।

brahmaśarvasureśānahariharāya namo namaḥ ।
jñānaśaktikriyāśakticarācara namo astu te ।।

hāṭakāya namas tubhyam umānātha namo astu te ।
brahmaviṣṇumaheśāya sarvajñāya namo namaḥ ।।

sadyojātas tathā ghoras tat puruṣāya namo namaḥ ।
tvayā vyāptam idaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।।

ādimadhyāntarūpāya kalikāla namo astu te ।
umākāntārdhadehāya śrīkaṇṭhoragabhūṣaṇa ।।

anantagaṇarūpāya nāgayajñopavītine ।
śabdaḥ sparśaś ca gandhaśca raso rūpaṃ ca pañcamam ।।

buddhir manastv ahaṅkāro hy aṣṭamūrte namo astu te ।
sūryo aryamā bhagas tvaṣṭā pūṣārkaḥ savitā raviḥ ।।

gabhastimāṃś ca tvaṃ kālo mṛtyur dhātā prakāśakaḥ ।
pṛthivyāpas tathā tejo vāyurākāśam eva ca ।।

somo bṛhaspatiḥ śukro budho aṅgāraka eva ca ।
indro vivasvān dīptāṃśuḥ śuciḥ śaurirjaneśvaraḥ ।।

kalāste viṣṇubrahmādyā vedo vaiśravaṇo yamaḥ ।
kalākāṣṭhāmuhūrtāś ca pakṣamāsartavas tathā ।।

saṃvatsaras tvam evāsi kālacakro vibhāvasuḥ ।
puruṣaḥ śāśvato yogo vyaktāvyaktaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।

lokādhyakṣaḥ surādhyakṣo viśvakarmā tamonudaḥ ।
varuṇaḥ śītabhāraś ca jīmūto jīvano arihā ।।

bhūto yajño bhūtapatir lokapālair niṣevitaḥ ।
manaḥ suparṇo bhūtādiḥ sadāśiva namo astu te ।।

jihvācāpalyabhāvena khedito asi mayā prabho ।
brahmaviṣṇvādibhir devair yasyānto naiva labhyate ।।

bhavasāgaramagnānāṃ kaḥ stotuṃ śaktimān bhavet ।
ajñānāñjñānato vā api śūlapāṇe kṣamasva tat ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śrutvā stotram idaṃ devaḥ kalahaṃsasya bhārata ।
varaṃ vṛṇu mahāprājñaprītaḥ stotreṇa te anagha ।।

kalahaṃsa uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo asi me deva varaṃ dātum ihecchasi ।
kalahaṃseśvaraṃ nāma tīrthaliṅgaṃ sureśvara ।।

akṣayā devadevā atra homadānabalikriyāḥ ।
atrākṣayaṃ kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ tvat prasādāt maheśvara ।।

śivājñā vartate te atra naraḥ svargamavāpnuyāt ।
utkrāntiṃ kurute yas tu avaśaḥ svavaśo api vā ।।

stavenānena ya stautiyastvā stoṣyati śaṅkara ।
brahmahā vā surāpo vā steyī ca gurutalpagaḥ ।।

tīrthasyāsya prabhāveṇa sarve yāntu śivālayam ।
idaṃ varamahaṃ manye sarvakāmasamṛddhaye ।।

īśvara uvāca
yaṃ yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ trailokye sacarācare ।
matprasādān na sandeha sarvam etad bhaviṣyati ।।

evamuktvā yayau devaḥ kailāsanilayaṃ nṛpa ।
kalahaṃso atha munibhir brahmiṣṭhaiḥ sajitendriyaḥ ।।

varṣāyutāni sāgrāṇi bhuṅkte bhogāñchivālaye ।
divyayānasamārūḍhaḥ stūyamāno apsarogaṇaiḥ ।।

veṇuvīṇāninādena sarvālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ ।
daśa varṣasahasrāṇi tathaiva śivasannidhau ।।

dakṣiṇottaradigbhāgapañcakrośapramāṇataḥ ।
snānāt tatra divaṃ yāti mriyate vibudho bhavet ।।

etat te kathitaṃ rājan kalahaṃsasya kīrtanam ।
svārociṣe antare prāpte ādikalpe kṛte yuge ।।

kalahaṃsasya cākhyānān na sīdanti kalau janāḥ ।
putradārāvṛtānāgha māyāmohasamanvitāḥ ।
ākhyānasahitaṃ devaṃ karmaṇā manasā girā ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe śivamahimavarṇano nāma caturdaśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
bhūyaś cecchāmyahaṃ śrotuṃ narmadākīrtanaṃ śubham ।
ākhyānasahitaṃ deva viditaṃ vada sāmpratam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājendra tīrthaṃ vai śivena kathitaṃ purā ।
kāmadaṃ mokṣadaṃ caiva yajñadānaprabhāvataḥ ।।

revāyā uttare kūle kapilāsaṃgamāt param ।
vaidūryāt paścime bhāge vikhyātaṃ narmadāpuram ।।

ardhakoṭis tu tīrthānāṃ mahādevena bhārata ।
śatamaṣṭottara tatra liṅgānāṃ parikīrtitam ।।

yatra vai vasurudraiśca brahmād yaiś ca surāsuraiḥ ।
siddhagandharvayakṣaiś ca vidyādharamahoragaiḥ ।।

vedadhvani ninādena vyāptamasti carācaram ।
yatrāgnir huta homena tridivaṃ paryapūrayat ।।

devarṣayo mahārāja tathā brahmarṣayaḥ pare ।
āsan rājarṣayas tatra tāpasā vyavasāyinaḥ ।।

brāhmaṇāś ca vasanti sma manasā brahmacintanāḥ ।
āśramaṃ jamadagneś ca ṛṣikoṭisamāvṛtam ।।

kaśyapo gālavo gargo bādarāyaṇaśākaṭau ।
atriś caiva vaśiṣṭhaśca pulastya pulahaḥ kratuḥ ।।

bhṛguś caiva marīciś ca bhāradvājo mahātapāḥ ।
śākalya ṛṣyaśṛṅgaś ca manur viṣṇur yamo aṅgirāḥ ।।

vāśiṣṭhadakṣau saṃvartaḥ śātātapaparāśarau ।
āpastambaḥ śuko vyāsāḥ kātyāyanabṛhaspatī ।।

hārītaḥ śaṅkhalikhitau yājñavalkyo atha gautamaḥ ।
agastyaḥ pāvakākhyaś ca durvāsā ugratāpasaḥ ।।

śatānandas tathā jahnur vaiśampāyanajaiminī ।
lomaśaś ca vihaṅgaś ca śaunako harir eva ca ।।

ete cānye api munayo bahavaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ ।
jvalantas tapasā tatra sūryatejaḥ samaprabhāḥ ।।

caturvidyāvedavidaḥ śrutismṛtiviśāradāḥ ।
saṃvatsarakṛtāhārā apāhārakarās tathā ।।

māsopavāsinaś cānye tathā pakṣopavāsinaḥ ।
śākāhārānirāhārāḥ tathā anye mārutāśanāḥ ।।

kandamūlaphalāhārā mahātmānas tathā pare ।
itihāsapurāṇādi nānāśāstravicintakāḥ ।।

mokṣopāyadhṛtātmāno maunikāś ca na maunikāḥ ।
ekapādārddhapādāś ca bhūmau kāraṇabhojinaḥ ।।

ākhyānaṃ kathayiṣyāmi narmadāpuravāsinām ।
jamadagnis tu nivasan muniḥ śivaparāyaṇaḥ ।।

narmadāsaṅgame snātvā tatrābhyarcyamaheśvaram ।
vividhair gandhapuṣpaiśca tathā agurumanoharaiḥ ।।

dakṣiṇāmūrtim āśritya japannāsīt tathā muneḥ ।
māsaṃ ca japatas tasya devadevo maheśvaraḥ ।।

siddheśvaraṃ nāma liṅgaṃ siddhā yatra surāsurāḥ ।
uvāca vacanaṃ devo brāhmaṇaṃ prati bhārata ।।

tuṣṭo ahaṃ tava bhaktyā tu rudrajāpyena toṣitaḥ ।

jamadagniruvāca yadi tuṣṭo mahādeva varaṃ dātuṃ mamecchasi ।।

homārthaṃ caiva dhenuṃ me dadasva parameśvara ।
dharmakarmaśubhārtheṣu śivapūjāsu tarpaṇe ।।

pitṛkārye devakārye gāvaḥ puṇyatamāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
etasmāt kāraṇād īśa homadhenuṃ prayaccha me ।।

dattā caiva mahābhāga sarvakāmasamṛddhaye ।
evam uktvā dadau rājaṃs tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।

yān yān prārthayate kāmāṃs tāṃs tān prāpnoty asau tataḥ ।
ṛṣīṇāṃ ca sahasrāṇi kāmair bhojayate dvijaḥ ।।

hiraṇmayaiḥ svarṇapātrair nānābhakṣyair yathecchayā ।
kīrtir brahmarṣibhir mānyaiḥ sarvaiḥ suragaṇais tathā ।।

jamadagner munīndrasya āśrame copavṛṃhitā ।
etāvati gate kāle kārtavīryo nṛpottamaḥ ।।

māhiṣmatīṃ parityajya svargasopānam uttamam ।
ekasmin divase rājā mṛgayāṃ ca samāśritaḥ ।।

vindhyaṃ girimanuprāpto revātīraṃ samāśritaḥ ।
hatvā paśusahasrāṇi jamadagnyāśramaṃ gataḥ ।।

dehyetāṃ māṃ nijāyogyāṃ gāṃ jagāda muniṃ prati ।
kārtavīryavacaḥ śrutvā jamadagnir bhayākulaḥ ।
cintayāmāsa suciraṃ kimetad iti vismitaḥ ।।

dharmo hy adharmarūpeṇa karmabhiḥ puṇyasaṃcitaiḥ ।
adharmo dharmaphalado gahanā karmaṇo gatiḥ ।।

iti cintayatas tasye na kiṃcid bruvato muneḥ ।
apahṛtya balād dhenuṃ ghātayitvā ca taṃ munim ।।

sthānān niragamat tasmāt kārtavīryo nṛpādhamaḥ ।
kaśādibhis tāḍitā tu homadhenur muhurmuhuḥ ।।

śāpaṃ dattvā tatas tasya punar dhenur divaṅgatā ।
kariṣyate kulāntaṃ ca raiṇukeyo nṛpādhama ।।

hāhākāro mahānāsīlokānāṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira ।
durācāras tataḥ ko ayaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca kopakṛt ।।

atha śrutvā mahādevo bhārgavaḥ pitṛsūtakam ।
sahasaivāgataḥ kopāt samidho agniriva jvalan ।।

nihataṃ pitaraṃ dṛṣṭvā kopād dviguṇavikramaḥ ।
jagāma sahasotthāya purīṃ māhiṣmatīṃ prati ।।

kārtavīryārjunaṃ dṛṣṭvā kruddhaḥ provāca bhārgavaḥ ।
tiṣṭha tiṣṭha kva gantāsi nihatya pitaraṃ mama ।।

ityuktvā adāya paraśuṃ ciccheda ca bhujāvanam ।
śirasaiva samaṃ kopāt kṣatriyāntakaro muniḥ ।।

hate tasmin mahāvīrye kārtavīrye durātmani ।
devadundubhayoneduḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca ।।

tat kopād akarot sarvāṃ niḥkṣatrāṃ pṛthivīṃ tadā ।
pratijñāṃ saphalīkṛtya sa jagāma tam āśramam ।।

mātaraṃ ca namaskṛtya tataś cānyān munīśvarān ।
devaṃ paraśurāmeśaṃ saṃsthāpya vidhipūrvakam ।।

viśokairaṇḍikā caiva tṛtīyā pāvanī tathā ।
pituścakāra tatraiva sahasaivottarāṃ kriyām ।।

devadroṇīti vikhyātā tatrāste kapilā śilā ।
tatra piṇḍapradānena divaṃ gacchanti pūrvajāḥ ।।

etat te kathitaṃ rājan narmadāpuram uttamam ।
śravaṇāt kīrtanāt tasya divi devatvam āpyate ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe kārtavīryākhyāne pañcadaśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athānyaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi saṅgamaṃ lokaviśrutam ।
bṛhatyā narmadāyās tu surāsuraniṣevitam ।।

nānādrumalatākīrṇaṃ vindhyaparvatasevitam ।
campakair bakulair yuktamaśokaiḥ stabakair api ।।

punnāgaiḥ kiṅkirātaiś ca sugandhair nāgakeśaraiḥ ।
mallikotpalajātībhiḥ pāṭalaiḥ pārijātakaiḥ ।।

āmrajambūkapitthaiś ca śrīphalaiḥ panasais tathā ।
kharjūrair badarībhiś ca dāḍimair bījapūrakaiḥ ।।

aruṣkaraiḥ kṣīravṛkṣair nāraṅgair upaśobhitaiḥ ।
bharaṇāyātmavargasya saṃvidhāya vanecaraḥ ।।

mukhagaṇḍūṣasalilaṃ śivāya sa samāharat ।
ajñānabhaktigarbhas tu snāpayitvā phalaṃ dadau ।।

vāsare vāsare caiva niṣādo dharmatatparaḥ ।
saumyāyane ca cakṣur vai dattvā saumyaṃ tathātmanaḥ ।।

evaṃ sampūjayāmāsa tryambakaṃ vidhipūrvakam ।
etat te kathitaṃ rājan kalpagā netrasaṅgamam ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
bhagavan chrotum icchāmi mahākautūhalaṃ hi me ।
saṃjāto muniśārdūla sa kathaṃ netrasaṅgamaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ekasmin vāsare prāpte vyatīpāte ca saṃkrame ।
sa puṣpabhāramādāya praviveśa śivālaye ।।

tṛtīyam īkṣaṇaṃ tatra devasya ca na paśyati ।
tadā tu cintayāmāsa vismayāviṣṭa cetanaḥ ।।

kenāpahṛtam etasya netraṃ devasya pāpmanā ।
ity uktvā ca svakaṃ netraṃ tīkṣṇabāṇena bhārata ।।

lalāṭe devadevasya utkṛtya saṃnyaveśayat ।
na kampo na ca kārpaṇyaṃ nā anyathā tasya mānasam ।।

tatas tuṣṭaḥ sureśāno niṣādaṃ prati bhārata ।
prahasan na bravīd devo varaṃ vṛṇu yathepsitam ।।

śivaprasādasampannā buddhir anyā pracakrame ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca śrutvā tu vacanaṃ śambhoḥ sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇipatya saḥ ।।

yadi tuṣṭo asi deveśa varaṃ dātuṃ mamecchasi ।
niṣādāsta ime sarve mṛgapakṣigaṇaiḥ saha ।।

saputradārapaśavo ye cānye pāpayonayaḥ ।
tvat prasādān maheśāna śivalokaṃ prayāntu te ।।

etad varam ahaṃ manye bhūtānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।
etacchrutvā vacas tasya niṣādādhipateḥ śivaḥ ।।

uvāca sarvakāmāptiṃ matprasādāt tvamāpsyasi ।
evam uktvā śivo rājaṃs tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।

divyayānasamārūḍho niṣādo anucaraiḥ saha ।
dhṛtasvarṇātapatraṃ tu vījyamāno apsarogaṇaiḥ ।।

divyābharaṇaśobhāḍhyaḥ sarvālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ ।
divyavastraparīdhāno divyagandhānulepanaḥ ।।

surāsuraiḥ stūyamāno veṇuvīṇāpuras saraḥ ।
prāyācchivapuraṃ kṣipraṃ tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।।

etat te kathitaṃ rājan chivanetrahradāśritam ।
anekaśatasaṃkhyātāḥ pāpayoniratā narāḥ ।।

narmadāśivasaṃyoge saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ gatāḥ ।
avaśa svavaśo vā api yas tu prāṇān parityajet ।।

vased varṣasahasrāṇi umāmāheśvare pure ।
śravaṇāt kīrtanāc cāpi mucyate bhavabandhanāt ।।

dhanyās te puruṣā rājan ye mriyante śivāyane ।
na teṣāṃ garbhabhūtiś ca janma caiva yudhiṣṭhira ।।

putradāraparigrastā mohajālasamāvṛtāḥ ।
kalpagāṃ tu na paśyanti pāpopahatacetasaḥ ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye hradākhyānaṃ nāma ṣoḍaśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athānyat paramaṃ tīrthaṃ kathyamānaṃ nibodha me ।
sahasrayajñaṃ vikhyātaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam ।।

tatra snātvā ca japtvā ca pūjayitvā maheśvaram ।
na tasya punarāvṛttir ghore saṃsārasāgare ।।

kathayāmi tavākhyānam itihāsaṃ purātanam ।
tārābalirnāma nāgaḥ kambalāśvatarau tathā ।।

śvetoragās tathā cānye bhujaṅgāś ca tathā apare ।
nāgeśvaraṃ te arcayanti nānāpuṣpavilepanaiḥ ।।

nāgapūgāḥ samāsādya pūjayanti maheśvaram ।
gargo aghamarṣaṇaś caiva cyavanaḥ śaunako aṅgirāḥ ।।

ete cānye api bahavo brahmavidyāṅgapāragāḥ ।
nāgānāṃ cāśramaṃ hartuṃ tatra sarve hy upasthitāḥ ।।

tatastaiḥ kupitair nāgair daṣṭāś caiva dvijottamāḥ ।
viṣāghrātān munīn dṛṣṭvā kupitaś cāghamarṣaṇaḥ ।।

vāhanaṃ vāsudevasya pakṣirājaṃ samāhvayat ।
tatkṣaṇād āgataḥ pakṣī garuḍaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ ।।

kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā brāhmaṇaṃ cedamabravīt ।
bhujaṅgān bhakṣayiṣyāmi brāhmaṇā nirviṣās tataḥ ।।

brahmaśāpabhayārtena garuḍena viṣolbaṇāḥ ।
bhakṣitāḥ pannagāḥ sarve mocitā munayo viṣāt ।।

pakṣīndre ca gate sthāne bhakṣayitvā bhujaṅgamān ।
avaśiṣṭās tu ye nāgā viviśuste rasātalam ।।

āplave ca susaṃprāpte pravāho nārmadaḥ kṣaṇāt ।
asthīni srāvayāmāsa tato nāgā divaṃ yayuḥ ।।

sarpayoniṃ parityajya loke krīḍanti śāmbhave ।
nāgeśvarasya revāyāḥ samparkāt pāpamokṣaṇam ।।

tatra nāgahradaś cāste triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ ।
tatra snāto divaṃ yāti yo nāgeśvaramarcayet ।।

ayaṃ te kathito rājannitihāsaḥ purātanaḥ ।
śravaṇāt kīrtanād vā api mucyate bhavabandhanāt ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe nāgeśvarākhyānaṃ nāma saptadaśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athānyat kathayiṣyāmi tīrthaṃ ca janakottamam ।
revāyā uttare kūle sarvasiddhipradāyakam ।।

aśvamedhaṃ tu tatraiva śatamedhaṃ tathāparam ।
sahasramedhaṃ vijñeyaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam ।।

lakṣamedhaṃ tathā cānyaṃ śivena parikīrtitam ।
janako nāma rājarṣir yatreṣṭvā tridivaṃ yayau ।।

svārociṣe antare prāpte tretāyāṃ ca narādhipa ।
purodhasaṃ yājñavalkyaṃ brahmarṣiṃ brahmavittamam ।।

kaśyapasyāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ brahmarṣigaṇasevitam ।
siddhagandharvagītāḍhyaṃ vedadhvaninināditam ।।

yuktaṃ kāmaphalair vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpitaiḥ phalitaiḥ śubham ।
dhanadasya purī yadvad alakā devanirmitā ।।

tadvac ca śobhitaṃ nānāmuni vṛnda niṣevitam ।
kāmadhenūs tathā divyāḥ śatasaṃkhyāḥ payasvinīḥ ।।

yājñikānṛtvijaś caiva kratuṃ kartuṃ yathāvidhi ।
yajñopaskarasaṃbhāraṃ sarvamādāya gacchati ।।

ādideśa tato martyān bhṛtyāṃś caiva sahasraśaḥ ।
bhakṣabhojyādi saṃbhārasaṃkhyāṃ kartuṃ na śakyate ।।

evaṃ pravartitas tatra lakṣamedhaḥ kratūttamaḥ ।
jagṛhur yajñabhāgaṃ ca śakrādyāḥ surasattamāḥ ।।

nivartitas tato yajño harir brahmā śatakratuḥ ।
nānavidhais tathā ratnair vāsoyugmaiś ca tārpitāḥ ।।

svaṃ svaṃ yānaṃ samārūḍhā jagmurdevāstriviṣṭapam ।
narmadāvabhṛthaṃ snātvā putradāropaśobhitaḥ ।।

haraṃ hariṃ cā'rcayitvā varadānaprabhāvataḥ ।
divyaṃ yānaṃ samārūḍho yathā śakro amaraiḥ saha ।।

dhṛtasvarṇātapatras tu bījyamāno apsarogaṇaiḥ ।
gīyamāno apsarobhiś ca nānālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ ।।

dṛṣṭo janakarājā ataḥ dharmarājaḥ samutthitaḥ ।
yānasyā agre pādacārī arghapādyādisaṃyutaḥ ।।

kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā vacanaṃ cedamabravīt ।
tapasā dhyānayogena dānadevārcanair api ।।

śivarevāprasādena jitā lokāstvayākhilāḥ ।
uvāca janako rājā dharmarājaṃ yaśasvinam ।।

tathaiva tava mūrtiś ca yathā bhānuḥ prabhākaraḥ ।
brahmāviṣṇus tathā śambhuḥ sākṣī sakalakarmaṇām ।।

evaṃ janakasaṃvāde dharmādharmavicāraṇāt ।
etasminn antare prāptaḥ kiṅkiṇījālamaṇḍitam ।।

veṇuvīṇāninādāḍhyam apsarogaṇasevitam ।
vimānaṃ divyam ārūḍho devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ ।।

nāradaḥ parvataś caiva tathānye munisattamāḥ ।
dharmarājapuraṃ prāptāḥ śrutvā janakamāgatam ।।

adhyāsus tam akrudhyantam āsanāni mahānti ca ।
prasamīkṣya yathārhantu pūjitāś ca pṛthak pṛthak ।।

teṣāṃ madhye mahārāja nārado dharmam abravīt ।
ke deśāḥ parvatāḥ puṇyāḥ kā nadyaś cāśramāś ca ke ।।

kāni tīrthāni loke asmin yatra dattaṃ hutaṃ tapaḥ ।
na kṣīyate manuṣyāṇāṃ tanme kathaya tattvataḥ ।।

jānāmi tvāṃ mahārāja sūryaputro bravīhi me ।
svarūpamadya sarveṣāṃ yathā vadanupūrvaśaḥ ।।

dharma uvāca
śrūyatāṃ muniśārdūlaśivaloke yathā śrutam ।
kalmāṣapādo vikhyāto mathurāyāṃ narādhipaḥ ।।

nābhāgo nāma rājarṣir ayodhyādhipatis tathā ।
yānaṃ copari rājarṣer nābhāgasya mahātmanaḥ ।।

adhaḥ kalmāṣapādasya dṛśyate sarvadaivataiḥ ।
śivaloke vivādo abhūt tayos tatra mahātmanoḥ ।।

kalmāṣapāda uvāca
puṣkare daśayajñāś ca mayā ceṣṭā vidhānataḥ ।
gaṅgāyāṃ naimiṣāraṇye prabhāse śaśibhūṣaṇe ।।

gaṅgāyamunayor yoge vārāṇasyāṃ tathaiva ca ।
iṣṭaṃ yajñaśataṃ sāgraṃ mayā tatra maheśvara ।।

adhobhāge vimāno me nābhāgasya mamopari ।
kalpagāṃ varjayitvā tu tīrthe tīrthe makhottamāḥ ।।

kṛtā mayā mahādeva vimānaṃ me tathā apyadhaḥ ।

īśvara uvāca śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga kathyamānaṃ nibodha me ।।

lakṣamedhaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ revāyā uttare taṭe ।
lakṣamedheśvaraṃ nāmnā liṅgaṃ tatra paraṃ smṛtam ।।

cakāra tatra nābhāgo yajñamekaṃ yathoditam ।
tattīrthayajñamāhātmyād yānamasyopari sthitam ।।

asaṃkhyeṣv api tīrtheṣu tvayeṣṭaṃ rājasattama ।
vihāya kalpagāṃ tena tava yānamadhaḥ sthitam ।।

dharma uvāca
na śaṅkarāt paro devo na revāyāḥ parā nadī ।
na satyāt paro dharmo kāruṇyaṃ sarvajantuṣu ।।

mayā śrutaṃ sūryeloke sūryeṇāpi maheśvarāt ।
etat te sarvamākhyātaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ purātanam ।।

vāsīyo narmadātīre śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ।
na tasya vai yamaḥ śāstā yamalokaṃ na paśyati ।।

brahmā viṣṇuḥ śivaḥ śāstā satyameva yathoditam ।
dharmarājñā samagraṃ tu nāradādyāmaharṣayaḥ ।।

dharmākhyānam idaṃ śrutvā mudāparamayāyutāḥ ।
svaṃ svaṃ yānaṃ samāruhya śakrādyās tridivaṃ yayuḥ ।।

dharmākhyānam idaṃ puṇyam itihāsaṃ purātanam ।
kathitaṃ tava yatnena videhādyā narādhipāḥ ।।
dānayajñaprabhāveṇa tridivaṃ varamāyayuḥ ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe janakayajño nāmāṣṭādaśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
saptasārasvataṃ tīrtha śaṃsa me atra mahāmune ।
utpattiṃ cāsya tīrthasya kathayasva yathārthataḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
saptasārasvato nāma gandharvaḥ śivagāyanaḥ ।
vīṇāveṇuprekṣaṇīya yantragītaviśāradaḥ ।।

maṇibhadrā subhadrā ca hemagarbhā tathā parā ।
ābhirvarāpsarobhiś ca cikrīḍe prativāsaram ।।

madirā naṣṭacaitanyaḥ kāmārtaḥ kāmamohitaḥ ।
vihāya śāṅkarīṃ pūjāṃ bhakṣyabhojyarato abhavat ।।

kiyatyapi gate kāle yayau draṣṭum umāpatim ।
gītanṛtyaiś ca tuṣṭāva kailāse taṃ nagottame ।।

gandharvaṃ taṃ samālokya cirakāle samāgatam ।
śaśāpa nandī kopena śivabhaktiparāṅmukham ।।

cāṇḍālayoniṃ gaccha tvaṃ pāpasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।
kṣutkṣāmastvaṃ nirāhāro martyaloke cariṣyasi ।।

prasādya nandinaṃ so atha gandharvo vākyam abravīt ।
śāpasyāntaṃ mahābhāga dātuṃ me tvamihārhasi ।।

nandyuvāca
narmadāyāṃ vyatīpāte snātvā abhyarcya maheśvaram ।
antaṃ śāpasya saṃprāpya punastvaṃ cāgamiṣyasi ।।

evaṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā cāṇḍālīṃ yonim āśritaḥ ।
jātismaratvaṃ saṃprāpya saśailavanakānanām ।।

babhrāma dharaṇīṃ sarvāṃ tīrthayātrāprasaṅgataḥ ।
atha cakrāṅgayogena narmadā tīramāgataḥ ।।

śaṅkarasthaṇḍile yāgaṃ tatra gatvā cakāra saḥ ।
puṣpopahārair vividhair vīṇāvādyair manoharaiḥ ।।

gandharvabhaktiṃ vijñāya pratyakṣo abhūt maheśvaraḥ ।
sthaṇḍilādutthitaṃ liṅgaṃ mahāpāvanamambhasi ।।

uvāca taṃ mahādevo gītavāditratoṣitaḥ ।
varaṃ vṛṇu mahābhāga yatte manasi vartate ।।

kalpagātoyasaṃsparśāt prāpnoṣi paramāṃ gatim ।

gandharva uvāca yadi tuṣṭo maheśāna varaṃ dātumihecchasi ।।

saptasārasvataṃ tīrthaṃ liṅgaṃ sārasvataṃ tathā ।
khyātiṃ yātu mahādeva tvatprasādāt mahītale ।।

tiryag yonigatāḥ pāpāś cāṇḍālāś ca narādhamāḥ ।
sarve te tridivaṃ yāntu tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।।

evam astviti taṃ coktvā maheśo antaradhīyata ।
divyayāna samārūḍhaḥ sarvālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ ।।

śivalokam avāpyaivaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ tathaiva saḥ ।
saptasārasvate snātvā arcayitvā vṛṣadhvajam ।।

kulaikaviṃśam uddhṛtya svargaloke mahīyate ।
tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtā na punarbhavāḥ ।।

śivājñā vartate rājaṃs tatra yastridivaṃ jayet ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca kaḥ sraṣṭā cāsya jagato hartā dhartā ca bho mune ।।

yathārtham etad ācakṣva vistareṇa tapodhana ।
tvatto ahaṃ śrotumicchāmi sarvam etan mudāyutaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
yathā śrutaṃ mayā pūrvaṃ purāṇaṃ skandakīrtitam ।
tathā te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu rājan yathārthataḥ ।।

skandena tu purā pṛṣṭo haraḥ kalpāntakārakaḥ ।
carācaram idaṃ sarvaṃ kathaṃ gacchati saṃlayam ।।

kutra gacchantyamī devāḥ kathaṃ caiṣāṃ sthitir bhavet ।
kvaca gacchati vai brahmā kutra gacchati keśavaḥ ।।

vedās tu kutra gacchanti saṣaḍaṅgapadakramāḥ ।
agnayaḥ parvatāḥ sarve samudradvīpasaṃyutāḥ ।।

siddhāḥ sarve sanakṣatrāḥ sūryādyāś ca tathā grahāḥ ।
pātālabhuvanādīni devalokāś ca śāśvatāḥ ।।

kalpānte ca suraśreṣṭha kva līyante ca devatāḥ ।

hara uvāca kathayāmi paraṃ guhyaṃ sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakam ।।

pralaye sarvabhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।
śivaliṅge vilīyante naṣṭe jagati śāśvate ।।

śūnyaṃ caitaj jagat sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।
ātiṣṭhati yadā vahṇir visphuran sarvatomukhaḥ ।।

tato bṛhaspatir gāyan vedatrayasamanvitam ।
tadaivātibalo devaḥ kūrmarūpo mahādyutiḥ ।।

narakāṃścādahat sarvās tataḥ prajvalito mahān ।
sarvaṃ dagdhaṃ tu pātālaṃ nāgānāṃ bhuvanāni ca ।।

kālarūpeṇa dagdhāni bhuvanāni caturdaśa ।
jvālāmālākulībhūte vāṅmaye sacarācare ।।

naṣṭe triviṣṭape sarve saśailavanakānane ।
māyāmaye tu sarve asmiṃs traiguṇye pralayaṃ gate ।।

vinaśyati tato brahmā sahitaḥ sarvadaivataiḥ ।
nāśayitvā ca bhūtāni brahmāṇḍaiḥ saha daivataiḥ ।।

sthitā tu narmadā caikā sutīrthā surapūjitā ।
narmadāyā avatāro ayaṃ martyaloke vyavasthitaḥ ।।

gatamindrasahasraṃ tu yāvad vai daśapañca ca ।
atītaṃ brahmaṇaḥ ṣaṭkaṃ saptamo ayaṃ prajāpatiḥ ।।

tad evam agnimadhyasthaṃ tena sarvam acetanam ।
avyakte sarvabhūtānām īśe jāgarti jāgrati ।।

yadā svapiti śāntātmā tadā sarvaṃ nimīlitam ।
sa viṣṇuḥ sṛṣṭikartā ca hartā ca jagataḥ prabhuḥ ।।

ekībhūteṣu bhūteṣu vyapāsyan sarvatejasām ।
punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ prakurute devadevaḥ sadāśivaḥ ।।

brahmā bhūtvā asṛjallokaṃ viṣṇur bhūtvā hyapālayat ।
rudraḥ kālāgnirūpeṇa haratyante sa eva hi ।।

tanmayā kathitaṃ sarvaṃ kim anyat paripṛcchasi ।
iḍā nāma kalā hyeṣā śambhor vai saptakalpagā ।।

akṣayā tena loke । aṣṭau yugasahasrāṇi ahorātraṃ prajāpateḥ ।।

anenaiva tu mānena śataṃ brahmā sa jīvati ।
pitāmahaśatenaiva viṣṇor mānaṃ vidhīyate ।।

nimeṣārddhaṃ ca śambhos tu sahasrāṇi caturdaśa ।
etāvati vinaśyanti hy asaṃkhyātāḥ pitāmahāḥ ।।

tatra dvādaśasāhasraṃ daivataṃ yugam ucyate ।
tad ekasaptatiyugaṃ manvantaram ihocyate ।।

etac caturdaśaguṇaṃ kalpam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ।
harārkacandramanavaḥ śakrasyāyuḥ prakīrtitam ।।

lokapālādayo devāḥ sādhyāś caiva marudgaṇāḥ ।
aṣṭāviṃśatiparyanta yugānāṃ santi te api ca ।।

etat te kalpagā kālamānaṃ nigaditaṃ mayā ।
ye mṛtāḥ kalpagātīre dānayajñatapaḥ sthitāḥ ।।

durgamaṃ yamalokaṃ ca na paśyanti kadācana ।
tapasā dhyānayogena brahmārcanaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

narmadātīramāsādya ye atra prāsādakārakāḥ ।
dāruṇaṃ narakaṃ ghoraṃ nāśrayante yamālayam ।।

narmadāṃ tu niṣevante vārddhakye tu subuddhayaḥ ।
etad eva paraṃ dhyānaṃ śeṣam anyan nirarthakam ।।

narmadādakṣiṇe tīre aśokavanikāsu ca ।
aśokajananaṃ nāma tīrtha tatra vyavasthitam ।।

aśokeśvaraliṅgaṃ tu sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।
tatra golakṣadānena yatphalaṃ tatra gacchataḥ ।।

saptasārasvataṃ liṅgaṃ tathā liṅgaṃ surārcitam ।
sāptarṣaṃ nāma liṅgaṃ ca liṅgaṃ yogeśvaraṃ tathā ।।

candrakāntaṃ tathā liṅgaṃ varuṇeśvaram eva ca ।
abhyarcya parayā bhaktyā yamalokaṃ na paśyati ।।

tilodakapradānena piṇḍapātena bhārata ।
pitṝn samuddharatyāśughorāt pūrvaṃ paraṃ śatam ।।

tatra dattaṃ hutaṃ yac ca tasya saṃkhyā na vidyate ।
purā devagaṇāḥ sarve tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।।

saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ prāpya divi devatvam āyayuḥ ।
saṃsārasāgare rājan sañcaranti na dāruṇe ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
liṅgāni kīrtitānīha tathā tīrthāni yāni ca ।
nānākhyānasametāni prasādāt kathayasva me ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga itihāsaṃ purātanam ।
nāgeśvaraṃ siddhaliṅgaṃ sthitaṃ nāgahrade śubhe ।।

siddhidaṃ sarvalokānāṃ nāgakanyābhirarcitam ।
brahmatejovapuḥ śrīmān nāmnā caivāghamarṣaṇaḥ ।।

dvādaśādityasaṃkāśo dīpyamāna ivānalaḥ ।
āpastambo atha maitreyaḥ saṃvartaścātrir eva ca ।।

ete cānye api bahava ṛṣayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ ।
ayutāni munīndrāṇām aṣṭau tatrāśrame nṛpa ।।

kandamūlaphalāhārāḥ śākāhārās tathā apare ।
jalāhārās tathaivā anye kecid gomayabhakṣiṇaḥ ।।

cāndrāyaṇaparāścā anye śrutismṛtiviśāradāḥ ।
mokṣopāyaṃ vicinvanti brahmiṣṭhā brahmavittamā ।।

aghamarṣā aśramapadaṃ brahmalokasamaṃnṛpa ।
dharmas tu vaiśyarūpeṇa jijñāsārthaṃ samāgamat ।
saptasārasvate tīrthe so arcitvā vṛṣabhadhvajam ।।

gandhapuṣpais tathā dīpair upahārair manoramaiḥ ।
varteran ṛṣayas tatra śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tathā ।।

bhikṣā ca bhikṣave dattā kaupīnaṃ mṛgacarma ca ।
sāṣṭāṅgaṃ ca namaskṛtya tān devarṣigaṇān munīn ।।

māsopavāsanirato nāśikāraṇyam āgamat ।
putradārasnuṣās tasya nityaṃ tad gātagamānasāḥ ।।

māse māse tvatikrānte ravisaṃkramaṇe nṛpa ।
ṛtavaḥ ṣaḍatikrāntā nirāhāraṃ tapasyata ।।

na bhogo na ca kārpaṇyaṃ na māno na ca matsaraḥ ।
na kāmakrodhalobhāś ca nirjitās tena bhārata ।।

vedārthe brāhmaṇārthe ca mama vittasya cārjanam ।
viṣṇudharmaparo nityaṃ viṣṇvārāthana tat paraḥ ।।

uttare cāyane māse saptasārasvate tathā ।
snātvā devaṃ samabhyarcya liṅgarūpaṃ janārdanam ।।

yathā vibhavayogena bhikṣāṃ dattvā yathā purā ।

hara uvāca varaṃ brūhi mahābhāga siddhastvaṃ dharmato yataḥ ।।

mahārāja mahābhāga yat te manasi vartate ।
idaṃ vimānam āruhya divyabhogasukhaṃ kuru ।।

putradārasnuṣopeto viṣṇulokamito vraja ।

śārṅga uvāca yadi tuṣṭo asi me deva varaṃ dātuṃ yathepsitam ।।

varaṃ daśasahasrāṇi lokaṃ yāntu dvijottamāḥ ।
idaṃ varamahaṃ manye harer nānyaṃ kadācana ।।

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
vaiśyaḥ pāpo durācāro mahatāṃ lāghavaṃ yataḥ ।
sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇo gurur ucyate ।।

trīn varṇān yājayitvā ca tvaṃ yadā divamānayeḥ ।
na dṛṣṭaṃ na śrutaṃ cāsīd evaṃ śrutipurāṇayoḥ ।।

brāhmaṇasyāpamānena dharmo vai jāyate kvacit ।
tapasā dhyānadharmābhyāṃ na yāsyasi divamune ।।

api varṣasahasreṇa durgamaste surālayaḥ ।
vraja tvaṃ vaiśyadharmeṇa svagṛhaṃ prati sāmpratam ।।

sa evam ukto vipraistān sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇipatya ca ।
uvāca vacanaṃ vaiśyo vimuktaṃ munipuṅgavam ।।

ajñānāñjñānato vā api kopaṃ kartuṃ na yujyate ।
ajñātaṃ tvāṃ na gṛhṇīyāc chraddhāhīnaṃ ca devatā ।।

sakrodhena tapas taptaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati niṣphalam ।
daivatair api durjñeyā gahanā karmaṇo gatiḥ ।।

satyena dhriyate dharmas tataḥ svargaḥ prajāyate ।
svakarmanirataṃ caivam uddharantaṃ tathā dvijam ।।

vaiśyaṃ brāhmaṇam ityāhur brāhmaṇaṃ vaiśyameva ca ।
niṣṭhuraṃ nirghṛṇaṃ krūraṃ kṛtaghnaṃ dīrghakopinam ।।

dvijaṃ vācālarūpaṃ tu dūrataḥ parivarjayet ।

brāhmaṇā ūcuḥ ko bhavān vaiśyarūpeṇa brahmā śakro janārdanaḥ ।।

sāṅgopāṅgās tathā vedās tvayi dharmaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।

śārṅga uvāca dharmo ahaṃ vaiśyarūpeṇa jijñāsā artham ihāgataḥ ।।

idaṃ vimānamāruhya gamyatāṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।
ete vimānam āruhya samprāptās tridaśālayam ।।

saptasārasvataṃ natvā tīrthaṃ devaṃ haraṃ harim ।
vaiśyaḥ putrādibhir yukto prāpa lokaṃ tu vaiṣṇavam ।।
etat te kathitaṃ rājan narmadātīrthamuttamam ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe sṛṣṭisaṃhārasārasvatatīrthakathanaṃ nāmaikonaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śāṇḍilyākalpagāyogaḥ sarvapāpaharaḥ paraḥ ।
śāṇḍilyeśvaraliṅgaṃ ca sarvapāpaharaṃ param ।।

snātamātro naras tasminn arcayitvā maheśvaram ।
karmabhūmiṃ na labhate harasya vacanaṃ yathā ।।

tilodakapradānena haviṣā piṇḍapātanāt ।
tṛpyanti pitaras tasya yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ।।

rāhusomasamāyoge kurukṣetre mahāphalam ।
tatraiva janma rājarṣeḥ kārtavīryanṛpasya ca ।।

snātvābhyarcya mahādevaṃ gandhapuṣpādyupaskaraiḥ ।
sūryācandramasau yāvadumāmāheśvare pure ।।

bhuṅkte sa vividhān bhogāṃs tāvad vai śivasannidhau ।
tatra śāṇḍilyakauṇḍinyau māṇḍavyo munimattamaḥ ।।

kauśikaś ca mahātejāḥ kaśyapo bhṛgur eva ca ।
ete cānye api bahavo japadhyānaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

munīnāṃ ṣaṣṭisāhasraṃ tapasyugre vyavasthitam ।
tasyāśramapadaṃ ramyaṃ śāṇḍilyākalpagāyuji ।।

śāṇḍilyapuram ityeva brahmarṣi viniṣevitam ।
dvādaśādityatīrthaṃ ca narmadādakṣiṇe taṭe ।।

devadāru tathā tīrtham anyad devavanaṃ tathā ।
daśalakṣāṇi tīrthāni tatra tiṣṭhanti saṃgame ।।

dvādaśārkam idaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam ।
anyāni yāni liṅgāni kathitāni tavā anagha ।।

mūṣakaśca tathā tīrthe mārjāreṇaiva bhakṣitaḥ ।
niśāyāṃ mūṣakaḥ kaścidaṭamāna itas tataḥ ।।

mārjareṇa tataḥ so api bhakṣitaś ca dhṛtaḥ purā ।
tato meghāgame kāle pravāhas tatra nirgataḥ ।।

asthipravahaṇaṃ tasya nimagnaṃ tatra saṅgame ।
tīrthasyāsya prabhāveṇa yakṣarājo abhavat nṛpa ।।

bṛhadvṛndaḥ samākhyāto yakṣāyutasamāvṛtaḥ ।
haṃsayuktavimānena yakṣaloke mahīyate ।।

athānyat kathayiṣyāmi śāṇḍilyānarmadāśritam ।
nāmnā cāpsarasaṃ liṅgaṃ muktāścāpsaraso yataḥ ।।

jñānarūpamayaṃ devaṃ siddhaliṅgaṃ prakīrtitam ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca kasmādapsarasaḥ śaptāḥ kathaṃ yātāś ca saṅgamam ।।

kathaṃ ca mokṣaṇaṃ śāpād viditaṃ kuru sāmpratam ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca śṛṇu rājan yathā nyāyaṃ kathayāmi tavā anagha ।।

madhūtsavaṃ śivasyāgre vihāyendrotsavaṃ gatāḥ ।
urvaśī ca tathā rambhā ahalyā ca tilottamā ।।

ghṛtācī menakā caiva citrarekhā ca śālinī ।
etāś cāpsaraso bahvyaḥ sarvā vai deva nirmitāḥ ।।

vasante tā viśanti sma śakralokaṃ suraiḥ saha ।
madirānandapānena mohitāḥ kāmapīḍitāḥ ।।

samatīte vasante tu umāmāheśvaraṃ puram ।
kailāsanilayaṃ devaṃ samārādhayituṃ gatāḥ ।।

śāpasya bhayabhītās tā devedevasya suvratāḥ ।
sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇipatyātha mantragītena tuṣṭuvuḥ ।।

tāś caivāpsaraso gaurī jñātvā tatra parāṅmukhī ।
gauryāḥ paramacittajñāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।।

anaṅgakusumā cānyā rūpayauvanaśālinī ।
dhanapālī tathā cānyā vyomarekhā tathāparā ।।

cāmaragrāhiṇī cānyā gāndharvī ca tathā aparā ।
hemadaṇḍā pratīhārā ūcurapsarasaḥ prati ।।

umāmāheśvaraṃ nāma bhavatyo na samāgatāḥ ।
aparādho ayam evādya bhavatīnāṃ suduḥsahaḥ ।।

anenaivāparādhena ajā martye bhaviṣyatha ।
divyaṃ varṣaśataṃ sāgram evaṃ bhavata duḥkhitāḥ ।।

apsarasa ūcuḥ
śāpāntaṃ no varārohe dātumarhasi pārvati ।
iti tāsāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā devī vacanam abravīt ।।

śāṇḍilyākalpagāyoge narmadādakṣiṇe taṭe ।
tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti śāṇḍilyeśvarapūjanāt ।।

gaurītīrthaṃ tu tatraiva jñātuṃ yogyaṃ hi kalpagām ।
uttīrṇā tena mārgeṇa lagnā skandasya pṛṣṭhataḥ ।।

tatra snātvā śivaṃ natvā kailāsaṃ cā gamiṣyatha ।
śāpabhraṣṭās tu tās sarvāḥ kṣmāṃ gatvā atiduḥkhitāḥ ।।

śāpāvasāne samprāpte kalpagātīramāśritāḥ ।
tatra snātvā tu śāṇḍilyaṃ pūjayitvā vidhānata ।।

ajārūpadharās sarvās tasminnapsarasaḥ kṣaṇāt ।
divyayānasamārūḍhās sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ ।।

gaurītīrthaṃ tathaivāpur yathāpūrvaṃ tathaiva tu ।
ajātīrtham iti khyātaṃ devaścājeśvaras tathā ।।

sarvapāpaharaṃ caiva liṅgamāpsarasaṃ tathā ।
tatra snātvā vyatīpāte nārī vā yadi vā naraḥ ।।

avaśaḥ svavaśo vā api prāṇatyāgaṃ karoti yaḥ ।
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi rājā vidyādhare pure ।।

kanakeśvaramanyat tu kanakāmokṣadaṃ śubham ।
jvareśvaraṃ tatra liṅgaṃ jvaro yatra na vidyate ।।

jvaritā ṛṣayo yatra babhūvur jvaravarjitāḥ ।
pañcabrahmeśvaraṃ nāma liṅgaṃ pāpavimocanam ।।

asuro malaketuś ca śakrasyaiva bhayena tu ।
pañcabrahmātmakair mantraiḥ sthaṇḍilasthaṃ tu śaṅkaram ।।

nānāvidhaiḥ puṣpadhūpaiḥ sampūjya svapuraṃ yayau ।
aparāhṇe atha saṃsmāra sa pāpo liṅgamaiśakam ।।

namaskṛtvā atha nirmālyaṃ yāvad uddhartum icchati ।
tāvat tat sthāṇubhūtaṃ vai liṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahāsuraḥ ।।

viṣasādamahābāhuḥ kim etad iti vismitaḥ ।
ākāśavācācoktaṃ vai viṣādaṃ tyajaputraka ।।

pañcabrahmeśvaraṃ nāma liṅgam etat mahāsura ।
ākāśavacanaṃ śrutvā namaskṛtya divaṃ yayau ।।

pañcabrahmeśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ liṅgaṃ puṣpeśvaraṃ tathā ।
tṛtīyaṃ tu tathā viddhi liṅgaṃ vai sthaṇḍileśvaram ।।

nitye naimittike kārye grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ ।
śraddhayā saṅgame snātvā liṅgatritayapūjanāt ।।

gacchanti pitaraḥ svargaṃ havirdānādibhir yathā ।
manvantaraśataṃ yāvan modate brahmaṇaḥ pure ।।

narmadāyāpyabhāge tu gopyaliṅgaṃ vyavasthitam ।
brahmahatyādikaṃ pāpaṃ saptarātreṇa naśyati ।।

tvaṣṭā pūṣeti vikhyātau balinau brahmarākṣasau ।
vajreṇa svena śakreṇa hatau tau sindhucāriṇau ।।

buddhvā brahmādibhirdevair brahmahā tveṣa vāsavaḥ ।
indrāṇyā caiva saṃtyaktaḥ sarvaiḥ suragaṇais tathā ।।

brahmahatyā samāyuktaḥ samprāpto vai himālayam ।
candrahīnā yathā rātrir anādityaṃ yathā nabhaḥ ।।

iyamābhāti vai tadvac chakrahīnā amarāvatī ।
tato devagaṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ preṣito havyavāhanaḥ ।।

śakrasyānveṣaṇārthāya kṛśāno gamyatāṃ tvayā ।
jale dṛṣṭvā nivartyā atha devatās saṃnyavedayat ।।

tatas saṃpreṣito devaiḥ sarvavyāpī prabhañjanaḥ ।
sa taṃ praveśayāmāsa provāca tridaśeśvaram ।।

devānāṃ śāsanād eva samāgacchaṃ ca tvatkṛte ।
tamānīya puraṃ divyaṃ brahmaviṣṇupurasmarāḥ ।।

tato devagaṇāḥ sarve śakreṇa sahitā gatāḥ ।
īśāno bhagavān yatra kailāse parvatottame ।।

namaskṛtya mahādevaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam ।
praviṣṭāṃs tu yathānyāyaṃ papraccha bhagavān haraḥ ।।

kimāgamanakāryaṃ vaḥ kuto vo bhayamāgatam ।

devā ūcuḥ eṣa tvāṃ prati saṃpraṣṭuṃ devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ ।।

mokṣaṇaṃ brahmahatyāyāḥ syād yathā vai tathā kuru ।

īśvara uvāca vārāṇasyāṃ kratuṃ ceṣṭvā hayamedhaṃ yathā vidhi ।।

tīrthayātrākrameṇaiva brahmahatyā praṇaśyati ।
namaskṛtya tato devaṃ surāḥ kāśīpuraṃ yayuḥ ।।

yajñopaskaramādāya tatra ceṣṭo makhottamaḥ ।
pauṣkaraṃ naimiṣāraṇyaṃ kurukṣetraṃ tathā punaḥ ।।

kedāraṃ bhairavaṃ tīrthaṃ gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgamam ।
oghatīrthaṃ prayāgaṃ ca prabhāsaṃ śaśibhūṣaṇam ।।

babhramuḥ sarvatīrthāni pṛthivyāṃ yāni kāni ca ।
kṛṣṇamasya śarīrārddhamarddhaṃ gauraṃ nirīkṣya ca ।।

vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmuḥ sarve devagaṇās tathā ।
vārāṇasīṃ purīṃ gatvā surā vijñāpayanti tam ।।

antarikṣe purī khyātā vārāṇasyasamā tathā ।
pañcakrośāntare tasyā brahmahatyā na sarpati ।।

purāṇe śrūyate deva devarāja śatakrato ।
yāvat tiṣṭhati gaṅgāyāṃ vārāṇasyāṃ samāgame ।।

na tāvad brahmahatyā tu nirgame punarāviśet ।

kāśyuvāca nāhaṃ samarthā haraṇe muktvā kācit tu kalpagām ।।

brahmahatyā yathā naśyed upadeśaṃ dadāmi te ।
śāṇḍilyā narmadāyoge yāmye bhāge tu nārmade ।।

tatra snātvā mahārāja trīṇi liṅgāni cārcayet ।
pañcabrahmeśvaraṃ devaṃ puṣpeśvaram athāparam ।।

tṛtīyaṃ tu tathā śakraliṅgaṃ caiva sthaṇḍileśvaram ।
śivena kīrtitaṃ pūrvaṃ pārvatyāḥ ṣaṇmukhasya ca ।।

kāśīpuryā vacaḥ śrutvā devadevaḥ śatakratuḥ ।
taṃ deśaṃ samanuprāpya sarvaṃ snānādikaṃ vyadhāt ।।

tat kṣaṇād divyadehaś ca sūryasaṃkramaṇaṃ yayau ।
śarīrāt tasya nirgatya brahmahatyā ha vāsavam ।।

asya tīrthasya māhātmyād ekahatyā tavaiva kā ।
brahmahatyāsahasraṃ hi tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā ।।

tīrthe asmin na viśeddhatyā yojanāni caturdaśa ।
etasminn antare śakraṃ pratyakṣaṃ prāha kalpagā ।।

śivam astu mahārāja svagṛhaṃ yāhi sāmpratam ।
iti tasyā vacaḥ śrutvā namaskṛtya tu narmadām ।।

divyaṃ yānaṃ samārūḍho mudā paramayā yutaḥ ।
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ siddhagandharvasevitam ।।

tatrārūḍhaḥ surapatir yathāpūrvaṃ tathaiva ca ।
dhṛtadivyātapatras tu vījyamāno apsarogaṇaiḥ ।।

stūyamānaḥ suragaṇaiḥ praviveśāmarāvatīm ।
śivena kathitaṃ hy etat pārvatyāḥ ṣaṇmukhasya ca ।।
mayā tu kathitaṃ rājaṃs tava brahmarṣipūrvakam ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe brahmahatyāchedano nāma viṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
bhūyaścecchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ narmadātīrthakīrtanam ।
tṛptiṃ naivādhigacchāmi śṛṇvannapi mahāmune ।।

idānīṃ śrotum icchāmi revākubjāsamāgamam ।
ākhyānasahitaṃ brahman kathayasva prasādataḥ ।।

kubjikā karmaṇā kena triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā ।
etannastvaṃ paraṃ brahman saṃśayaṃ chettumarhasi ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājan kathāṃ divyāṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm ।
kathitāmīśvareṇaiva pārvatyāḥ ṣaṇmukhasya me ।।

ṛṣīṇāṃ brahmamukhyānāṃ gaṇānāṃ cānucāriṇām ।
nānāṛkṣāṇi sūryasya jagadudyotakāriṇaḥ ।।

śaśisūryopagamane tārā bhānti nabhastale ।
nānyā payasvinī śaktā saṃsārārṇavatāraṇe ।।

pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ muktvā caiva tu kalpagām ।
tatra snātā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtā na punarbhavāḥ ।।

cāndrāyaṇasahasraṃ ca brahmakūrcāyutaṃ tathā ।
narmadātoyapānena tulyaṃ bhavati vā na vā ।।

tilodakapradānena pitṝṇāṃ prītirakṣayā ।
gāyanti pitaro gāthā tathaiva ca pitāmahāḥ ।।

mātāmahādyāḥ satataṃ sarva eva parasparam ।
api syāt svakule asmākaṃ putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ ।।

havis tilayutaṃ dadyād yo revāsalilārcitam ।
varṣalakṣaṃ tathā tena tṛptā yāmaḥ parāṃ gatim ।।

yajñakriyā kṛtā tena samagrā bhūridakṣiṇā ।
etat te kathitaṃ rājaṃ śivenokta yathā purā ।।

svārociṣe antare prāpte ādikalpe kṛte yuge ।
mā gayāṃ gaccha kaunteya mā gaṅgāṃ mā sarasvatīm ।।

tatra gaccha nṛpaśreṣṭha yatra kubjā sanarmadā ।
vārāṇasīṃ prayāgaṃ ca gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgamam ।।

kedāraṃ kanakhalaṃ ca prabhāsaṃ śaśibhūṣaṇam ।
hariścandrapuraṃ cāndraṃ śrīśailaṃ tripurāntakam ।।

māhendra malayaṃ caiva gokarṇaṃ ca mahābalam ।
kālañjaraṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ tryambakaṃ dhūtakilbiṣam ।।

rudrakoṭiṃ himasthānaṃ bhairavaṃ ca mahāpatham ।
tīrthāny etāni cānyāni kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।।

nānātīrthasahasrāṇi purāṇe kīrtitāni ca ।
brahmaviṣṇuśivoktaṃ hi tatpramāṇaṃ hi siddhaye ।।

some prasiddhā amāvāsyā revākubjāsamāgame ।
eraṇḍyāṃ caṇḍavegāyāṃ revayā saha saṃgame ।।

rājan darśe yadā somaḥ saṃviśed ravimaṇḍale ।
vyatīpāte ca saṃkrāntau vaidhṛtau viṣuve tathā ।।

dakṣottarāyaṇe caiva ṣaḍaśītimukhe tathā ।
darśe syād viṃśatiguṇaṃ vyatīpāte samāṃ śataḥ ।।

saṃkrame vaidhṛtau rājaṃ chatārdhaṃ parikīrtitam ।
amāsomasamāyoge rāhusomasamāgame ।।

kurukṣetrāc chataguṇaṃ puṇyam āha śivaḥ svayam ।
bilvāmrakaṃ siddhaliṅgaṃ brahmahatyāvyapohanam ।।

darśanāt sparśanāt tasya śivaloke mahīyate ।
kubjeśvaraṃ tathaivānyat na tat paśyanti mānavāḥ ।।

narmadākubjikāmadhye nāgakanyābhir arcyate ।
svārociṣe antare prāpte ādikalpe kṛte yuge ।।

kālāgnirudrasaṃkāśaṃ bhittvā pātālasaṅgamam ।
sūryakoṭisamaprakhyaṃ pradīptajvalanaprabham ।।

utthitaṃ kalpagāmadhye devā avāhanakāmyayā ।
oṃkārasya yavaikena hīnaṃ liṅgaṃ nṛpottama ।।

pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni loke asmin sacarācare ।
hīnān yasmād yavārddhena satyam etac chivoditam ।।

tatra yas tyajati prāṇānamāsomasamāgame ।
divyayānasamārūḍhaḥ stūyamāno apsarogaṇaiḥ ।।

dhṛtadivyātapatras tu sarvālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ ।
triṃśacchatasahasrāṇi vasec chivapure śubhe ।।

tyajeddhi tatra yaḥ prāṇān na vaśaḥ svavaśo api vā ।
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi rājā vidyādhare pure ।।

rantidevaś cakravartī śakratulyo mahīpatiḥ ।
ayodhyādhipatiḥ śrīmān sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।।

kaṇvāśramapade ramye surāsuraniṣevite ।
ākhyānasahitaṃ rājaṃ chṛṇu veda yathākramam ।।

tīrthasaṃkhyāpramāṇaṃ ca itihāsaṃ purātanam ।
haranti ke ca kārttikyāṃ kailāse parvatottame ।।

brahmādayo gatās tatra viṣṇuśakrapurogamāḥ ।
umayā sahito rudro gaṇakoṭisamanvitaḥ ।।

nandiskandamahākālasurāsuraniṣevitaḥ ।
saritaḥ sāgarāḥ śailās tīrthānāṃ koṭayas tathā ।।

teṣāṃ madhye samutthāya skando vacanam abravīt ।
kasyaitāni vimānāni dīvyante divi śaṅkara ।।

sāptabhaumā gṛhā ramyā hemaprākāratoraṇāḥ ।
gītanṛtyaninādena kāminīnāṃ manoharāḥ ।।

īśvara uvāca
śṛṇu skanda mahābhāga kathyamānaṃ yathoditam ।
tīrthadānaprabhāveṇa tīrthajyeṣṭhakrameṇa tu ।।

ye mṛtā narmadātīre parvate amarakaṇṭake ।
māheśvarāditīrtheṣu bhṛgukacchāvasānataḥ ।।

imāni yāni tīrthāni liṅgamūrtidharāṇi ca ।
saritaścāpi gaṅgādyās tāsu dānaprabhāvataḥ ।।

etat te kathitaṃ skanda harmyās santi samuddhṛtāḥ ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca evaṃ purā mahārāja kailāse parvatottame ।।

brahmā papraccha tīrthānāṃ śaṅkaraṃ vidhipūrvakam ।
devakhātāni sarvāṇi saritaḥ sāgarās tathā ।।

nadyaḥ sarvāś ca bhūpṛṣṭhe gaṅgādyā girisambhavāḥ ।
uttamāḥ katicid deva kathayasva prasādataḥ ।।

hara uvāca
kathayāmi paraṃ tīrthaṃ pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam ।
kautukena tvayā pṛṣṭā nadīnāmuttamā nadī ।।

sarvāsāṃ saritāṃ madhya uttamā saptakalpagā ।
sarveṣāṃ jananī ceha nadī trailokyasundarī ।।

brahmovāca
surasindhuṃ parityajya narmadā varṇyate katham ।
viruddhaṃ sarvalokānāṃ devānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

brahmaṇas tu vacaḥ śrutvā agastyo vākyam abravīt ।
madhye pade niyuktaś ca vaktum eva na yujyate ।।

dharmāḥ sarve vedamūlā brāhmaṇā vedasambhavāḥ ।
vedahīnā na sidhyanti yajñadānavidhikriyāḥ ।।

svayambhūr bhagavāṃ chambhuḥ śambhuś ca bhagavān hariḥ ।
vedāś ca bhagavāṃ chambhuḥ kalpagā śambhusambhavā ।।

avyaktāvyaktarūpeṇa jagataḥ kāraṇecchayā ।
saṃhārasṛṣṭirūpeṇa pralayotpattikāriṇī ।।

bhagīrathaneminītā hariṇā atrāvatāritā ।
gaṅgā sā jahnunā pītā muninā culukena ca ।।

kruddhaḥ pītvā munistāṃ tu sthito dhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ।
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu sā tu tasyodare sthitā ।।

vismayo devatānāṃ hi samāpede kutūhalam ।
brahmādyā devatāḥ sarvā gatvā tasyāśramaṃ prati ।।

śāpaśaṅkākulātmāno muniṃ vijñāpayanti te ।
mahānadīṃ mune muñca pavitrāṃ pāpanāśinīm ।।

martye vahatu sā nityaṃ lokasantāpahāriṇī ।
devatā ṛṣiproktena muktā tena mahānadī ।।

muktā tu jahnunā tatra tena sā jāhnavī smṛtā ।
sā tu kiṃ varṇyate brahman pītāyā jahnunā purā ।।

mayā culukamātreṇa śoṣitāḥ saptasāgarāḥ ।
hariś ca bhagavān śambhuś śambhuś ca bhagavān iti ।।

vindhyaḥ saptaśailarājo narmadāyāḥ prabhāvataḥ ।
tenoddhatā devamārgā vartamānāni vāritāḥ ।।

yajñaparvataparyaṅkāvubhau vindhyastau purā ।
mayā nivāritau buddhyā devamārga pravṛttaye ।।

evaṃ vigarhito brahmā saṃvādena parasparam ।
tatas tuṣṭāḥ surāḥ sarve hy agastyaṃ prati bhārata ।।

devadundubhayo neduḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca ।
iti te kathito rājann itihāsaḥ purātanaḥ ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe kubjāmāhātmya ekaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kathaṃ nivartito yajño rantidevasya dhīmataḥ ।
kaṇvāśramapade ramye revākubjāsamāgame ।।

nikhilaṃ śrotumicchāmi kathayasva śivoditam ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca śṛṇvantu munayaḥ sarve śrotukāmās samāgamam ।।

mayā khyātam idaṃ puṇyam itihāsaṃ purātanam ।
śaṇḍāmarko atha rājarṣir mānaso brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।।

sūryatejaḥ samaprakhyas tejasā prajvalann iva ।
brahmiṣṭhaḥ satyavādī ca vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।।

brahmacārī jitakrodhaḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।
ṣaḍaśītisahasrāṇi munīnāṃ dīptatejasām ।।

tapastatraiva tapyante mokṣopāyavicintakāḥ ।
kandamūlaphalāhārā jalāhārās tathā pare ।।

māsopavāsinaś cānye tathā pakṣopavāsinaḥ ।
caranti ke sāntapanaṃ prājāpatyaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

cāndrāyaṇaparāś cānye brahmakūrcās tathāpare ।
śaṇḍāmarkāśritāḥ sarve sarveṣāṃ gurur eva ca ।।

vedadhvanitanirghoṣair divaṃ bhūmiṃ vyanādayan ।
nirdhūmo jvalanas tatra hūyamāno hutāśanaḥ ।।

kāmakrodhavinirmuktair brahmacārijitendriyaiḥ ।
śaṇḍāmarkāśramaṃ divyaṃ yuktaṃ brahmasamadvijaiḥ ।।

tathākāmaphalair vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpitais tvatiśobhitam ।
sarvāśramaguruś cāsīd rantidevo mahīpatiḥ ।।

śāsitā dharaṇī tena saśailavanakānanā ।
na narāḥ śokamātsaryarogadāridryaduḥkhitāḥ ।।

cirāyuṣaḥ prajāḥ sarvā dhanadhānyasamākulāḥ ।
svayaṃ kāmadughā gāvaḥ pṛthivī sasyaśālinī ।।

kauśeyaṃ paṭṭasūtraṃ ca sarveṣāṃ vimalaṃ citam ।
parjanyaḥ kāmavarṣī ca kāle kāle ṛtāvṛtau ।।

nānā purāṇi ramyāṇi hemaratnānvitāni ca ।
nānā cāmaramālā ca hemaratnāvagaṇṭhitā ।।

kiṅkiṇījālasaṃchannā maṇimālāvilambitā ।
budbudair ardhacandraiś ca pārijātakadambakaiḥ ।।

gopuraiś ca mahādivyair nānānakanināditā ।
nāṭyaharmyaiś ca saṅgītair vicitrakusumāvṛtaiḥ ।।

bhūmir hemamayī caiva cārcitā yatra saṃcitaiḥ ।
prāsādaś ca mahāratnair devadevasya śūlinaḥ ।।

merumandarakailāse yādṛśaś ca virājate ।
nānāratnaśilābhiś ca anekaśikharotkaraiḥ ।।

candraśālāgavākṣaiś ca ratnamālāvibhūṣitaiḥ ।
śatārdhasāptabhaumaiś ca tathaivāyutabhūmikaiḥ ।।

candrānanapatākābhir yajñaiś cāpi virājitā ।
evaṃ vidhā nṛpaśreṣṭha sarvaśobhā samanvitā ।।

rantidevasya rājarṣer ayodhyānagarī śubhā ।
itthaṃ śaśāsa dharaṇīṃ yathā śakrastriviṣṭapam ।।

nṛpo yāgasahasraiś ca bhūmipṛṣṭhaṃ dadāha saḥ ।
purodhasaṃ vaśiṣṭhaṃ ca papraccha munisattamam ।।

kasmiṃs tīrthe tu nirvighnā yajñasiddhir mahāmune ।
iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā rājarṣer munisattamaḥ ।।

uvāca rantidevaṃ ca vaśiṣṭho brahmavittamaḥ ।
durvāsāḥ kaśyapo gargo nāradaḥ parvataḥ kratuḥ ।।

agniś ca śaunakaś caiva bṛhaspatir athāṅgirāḥ ।
bhṛgur atris tathā vatsyaḥ pulastyaḥ pulahastathā ।।

kāśyapo gālavaś caiva ṛṣyaśṛṅgo vibhāṇḍakaḥ ।
ahaṃ ca munayaś caite munayo brahmavarcasaḥ ।।

sarveṣāṃ matamevaṃ vai mama caiva narādhipa ।
anyatīrthāt paraṃ tīrthaṃ purāṇe parikīrtitam ।।

koṭikoṭiguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ kalpagā yatra vartate ।
evam eveti taṃ brūyāt satyam etat tvayoditam ।।

tataścājñāpayām āsa bhṛtyāmātyapurodhasaḥ ।
yajñopaskarasambhāraḥ śīghram eva vidhīyatām ।।

ādideśa tato dūtān nānādeśeṣu satvarān ।
ghoṣaṇā kriyatāṃ rāṣṭre samāgacchantu bhūmipāḥ ।।

āgatās te tataḥ sarve rantidevasya śāsanāt ।
yathā vibhavaśobhāḍhyāḥ śakratulyā mahībhṛtaḥ ।।

gāvaś ca daśalakṣāṇi savatsāś ca payasvinīḥ ।
hemabhārairbhūṣitāś ca kāmadhenupayasvinīḥ ।।

lakṣamekaṃ hayānāṃ tu ayutaṃ dantināṃ tathā ।
maṇimāṇikyaratnānāṃ tatra saṃkhyā na vidyate ।।

anekāni sahasrāṇi karabhānāṃ ca bhārata ।
divyayānaṃ samāruhya sāntaḥpuraparicchadaḥ ।।

nānātūryair gītavādyair mekalātīram āgataḥ ।
tatra maṇḍapakuṇḍāni yajñayūpā hiraṇmayāḥ ।।

nānābhakṣāṇi bhojyāni pakvāni vividhāni ca ।
nānābharaṇaratnaiś ca brāhmaṇāḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ ।।

yajñadīkṣāṃ ca jagrāha patnyā saha narādhipaḥ ।
tataḥ pravartito yajño revātīre suśobhane ।।

tatra jvalati nirdhūmaḥ pratyakṣo havyavāhanaḥ ।
brahmaśakrādayo devā lokapālā marudgaṇāḥ ।।

viśvedevāś ca sādhyāś ca vasavaścandrabhāskarau ।
saritaḥ sāgarāḥ śailāḥ sarvatīrthāni cāpagā ।।

mātaraḥ siddhagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ ।
umayā sahito rudro viṣṇuś caiva sureśvaraḥ ।।

sarveṣā yajñabhāgāṃś ca pṛthak pṛthag akalpayat ।
etasminn antare rājan vedadhvani niveditam ।।

vismitā hyabhavan sarve śrutvā smṛtibhayānakam ।
dānavā balavanto adya te krauñcapuravāsinaḥ ।।

mahābāhuḥ subāhuś ca daityakoṭisamāvṛtāḥ ।
āgatā narmadā tīre sabhṛtyabalavāhanāḥ ।।

dakṣiṇāṃ diśamāśritya yajñavighnaṃ vicakrire ।
brahmādyā munayaḥ sarve bhayatrastāś ca kampire ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ brahmā devatulyaṃ purodhasam ।
mayā vidhir vismṛtaś ca mantrādīnāṃ mahābhayāt ।।

uvāca rantidevaṃ ca yajñadhvaṃsaṃ nivāraya ।
brahmiṣṭhas tad vacaḥ śrutvā rantidevo mahīpatiḥ ।।

yadi me vidyate satyaṃ śivabhaktiparā matiḥ ।
daityarākṣasaduṣṭāś ca ye cānye vighnakārakāḥ ।।

sarve te vilayaṃ yānti tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā ।
paśyantu mama sāmarthyaṃ devā vigatakalmaṣāḥ ।।

evamuktvā tato rājan kuśāgreṇa tu nārmadaḥ ।
pravāho duṣṭarakṣārthaṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ prakalpitaḥ ।।

viṣṇuś caiva smṛtas tatra śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।
uttare devayānasya pravāhaḥ parikalpitaḥ ।।

evaṃ kṛtvā tu ghoreṇa devamantreṇa suvrataḥ ।
juhāvāhavanīye tu kuṇḍe bilvāmravetasam ।।

tasmāt samutthitaṃ liṅgaṃ jvalat kālānalaprabham ।
nānto nādir na madhyaṃ ca tasya liṅgasya bhārata ।।

tataḥ surāsurāḥ sarve cakruḥ stotram idaṃ puraḥ ।
oṃ namo bhuvaneśāya ādideva namo astu te ।।

carācarakhyāpakāya sṛṣṭisaṃhārakāriṇe ।
stotraṃ śrutvā mahādevaḥ śāntarūpo jagat patiḥ ।।

babhūva paramaprītaś carācaragurus tadā ।
tad dṛṣṭvā tādṛśaṃ karma rantidevasya dhīmataḥ ।।

āgatya dānavādhīśo rantidevamapūjayat ।
ādeśo dīyatāṃ mahyaṃ kiṃ karomīti cābravīt ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ rājā prahasann iva bhārata ।
ātithyakāle samprāpte yajñabhāgaṃ vadāmi te ।।

devānāṃ yajñabhāṃgaṃ ca dānavānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।
parikalpya yathānyāyaṃ mudā paramayā yutaḥ ।।

svaṃ svaṃ yānaṃ samāruhya dānavās te ca sarvaśaḥ ।
liṅgaṃ bilvāmrakaṃ nāma juṣṭaṃ daivair jagat pateḥ ।।

namaskṛtya mahādevaṃ rantidevaṃ pratuṣṭuvuḥ ।
tataḥ pramuditā devā rantidevam apūjayan ।।

umayā saha deveśaṃ gaṇakoṭisamanvitam ।
brahmā viṣṇuś ca devāś ca varaṃ dattvā divaṃ yayuḥ ।।

gateṣu teṣu deveṣu rantidevaḥ puraṃ yayau ।
kadācid vṛtrahā tatra brahmahatyāsamāvṛtaḥ ।।

revākubjāsamāyoge sarvaṃ snānādikaṃ vyadhāt ।
tatkṣaṇād divyadehas tu sūryasaṃkāśatejasaḥ ।।

śarīrāt tasya nirgatya brahmahatyāha vāsavam ।
asya tīrthasya māhātmyād ekahatyā tavaiva kā ।।

brahmahatyāsahasraṃ hi tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā ।
tīrthe asmin vinaśed yāvad yojanāni caturdaśa ।।

etasminn antare śakraṃ pratyakṣaṃ prāha kalpagā ।
śāntis te astu mahābhāga yatheṣṭaṃ gaccha sāmpratam ।।

iti tasyā vacaḥ śrutvā tāṃ namaskṛtya kalpagām ।
divyayānaṃ samāruhya mudā paramayā yutaḥ ।।

apsarogaṇasaṃyuktaṃ divyagandharvanāditam ।
tatrārūḍhaḥ surapatir yathā pūrvaṃ tathaiva saḥ ।।

dhṛtadivyātapatras tu vījyamāno apsarogaṇaiḥ ।
stūyamānaḥ suragaṇaiḥ praviveśāmarāvatīm ।।

śivena kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ pārvatyāḥ ṣaṇmukhasya ca ।
mayā ca kathitaṃ rājaṃs tava brahmarṣipūrvakam ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe bilvāmrakotpattivarṇano nāma dvāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
harikeśa iti khyātaḥ śālagrāme dvijottamaḥ ।
śiloñchavṛttirdharmātmā satyavrataparāyaṇaḥ ।।

brāhmaṇī suvratā tasya dharmapatnī yaśasvinī ।
pativratā mahābhāgā patiśuśrūṣaṇe ratā ।।

kāle ṛtumatī sā tu ṛtugāmī ca sa dvijaḥ ।
tasya putraśataṃ jajñe kapilāpuram āśritam ।।

śiloñchavṛttiyogena prasthamekamupārjayat ।
kṣutkṣāmāḥ te ca śiśavo rudanti karuṇaṃ tataḥ ।।

śiśūn bubhukṣitān dṛṣṭvā mātā śokārtivihvalā ।
garhayantī suduḥkhārtā brāhmaṇī patim abravīt ।।

vṛddhau ca mātāpitarau sādhvī bhāryā sutaḥ śiśuḥ ।
bharaṇīyāḥ prayatnena eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।

bharaṇaṃ poṣyavargasya putrāṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ brāhmaṇyāḥ śokavihvalaḥ ।।

harikeśo abravīd vākyaṃ brāhmaṇīṃ prati bhārata ।
na mayā saṃcitaṃ dhānyaṃ na vittaṃ gṛhamedhinā ।।

grāme grāme bhikṣayitvā savibhāgaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।
dadāmi paramaṃ dhānyaṃ nānyāṃ vṛttiṃ tu kāraye ।।

brāhmaṇy uvāca
bālahatyāsamaṃ pāpaṃ bāle vṛddhe kṣudhārdite ।
tasmāt pratigrahaṃ kṛtvā bhartavyā mama putrakāḥ ।।

putreṇa lokaṃ jayati putreṇa sukhamedhate ।
putreṇa svargam āpnoti pitṝṇāṃ paramā gatiḥ ।।

ambarīṣasya nṛpater ayodhyādhipateḥ kila ।
vartamāne mahāyajñe kurukṣetre dvijottamāḥ ।।

gatāś ca brāhmaṇās tatra pratigrahajighṛkṣayā ।
gāḥ kāṃcanaṃ dhanaṃ prāpya śālagrāmanivāsinaḥ ।।

nānābharaṇaśobhāḍhyā āgatāḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ ।
yāhi yatra dvijāḥ sarve śālagrāmanivāsinaḥ ।।

sutārthaṃ harikeśo atha rakṣite kurujāṅgale ।
ambarīṣasya nṛpater vartamāne mahāmakhe ।।

gṛhītvā brāhmaṇīṃ putrān kurukṣetraṃ jagāma ha ।
praviṣṭaścādhvare tasmin yatra te santi ṛtvijaḥ ।।

brahmaghoṣasvareṇaiva sa dṛṣṭvā divi devatāḥ ।
yamo aṅgirāmunir viṣṇurvaśiṣṭho dakṣa eva ca ।।

bṛhadviṣṇuḥ prasannātmā śātātapaparāśarau ।
āpastambośanovyāsāḥ kātyāyanabṛhaspatī ।।

hārītaḥ śaṅkhalikhitau yājñavalkyo atha gautamaḥ ।
durvāsāḥ kāśyapo gargo bhāradvājo atrireva ca ।।

nāradaḥ parvataś caiva pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ ।
vibhāṇḍako bhṛguś caiva śākaṭo bādarāyaṇaḥ ।।

bālakhilyā brahmaputrā brahmatejo vapurdharāḥ ।
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi brahmadaṇḍaṃ samāruhan ।।

ambarīṣo mahārāja dṛṣṭvā brāhmaṇapuṅgavam ।
brahmarṣīṃs tān namaskṛtya arghapādyair apūjayat ।।

kimarthamāgato viprasabhāryaḥ sahaputrakaiḥ ।
anugraham imaṃ manye yanmāṃ vadasi suvrata ।।

ātithyakāle samprāpto yācayasva yathocitam ।

brāhmaṇa uvāca vittaṃ varṣaśataṃ yāvadekaikāya sutāya me ।।

tvaṃ dehi jīvanāyāśa homadhenuṃ tathottamām ।
ayutaṃ tu gavāṃ bhūpa hemabhārapariṣkṛtam ।।

koṭimekāṃ hiraṇyasya vastrabhūṣaṇamuttamam ।
iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā dvijasya pṛthivīpatiḥ ।।

śraddhayā parayā yuktaḥ sarvaṃ dattvā yathoditam ।
śālagrāmapadaṃ yānaiḥ śīghraṃ prāveśayat tataḥ ।।

kratum iṣṭvā sa rājarṣir mumude devavac ciram ।
nānāvidhān sa bhuktvā atha bhogān patnīsutaiḥ saha ।।

kālāntare tataḥ prāpte ṛṣir mṛtyuvaśaṃ gataḥ ।
marudeśe nirudake brahmarakṣastvamāgataḥ ।।

rājapratigrahād duṣṭāt punarjanma na vidyate ।
brāhmaṇyaṃ yaḥ parityajya dravyalobhena mohitaḥ ।।

viṣayāmiṣalubdhas tu kuryād rāja pratigraham ।
narake raurave ghore tasyeha patanaṃ dhruvam ।।

vṛkṣādāvāgninā dagdhāḥ prarohanti vanāgame ।
rājapratigrahād dagdhā na prarohanti karhicit ।।

śocanti pūrva janmāni anyajanmakṛtāni ca ।
bhāryāputrakṛtenaiva gato ahaṃ narakārṇavam ।।

evam uktvā kurukṣetraṃ putradārādibhiḥ saha ।
tatra dvādaśavarṣāṇi uṣitvā sububhukṣitaḥ ।।

ucchiṣṭaṃ kaśmalaṃ bhuṅkte rākṣasīṃ yonimāśritaḥ ।
vārāṇasīṃ prayāgaṃ tu puṣkaraṃ naimiṣaṃ tathā ।।

gaṅgāsāgarasam bhedaṃ kṣetraṃ kanakhalaṃ tathā ।
kedāraṃ ca mahāpuṇyaṃ prabhāsaṃ śaśibhūṣaṇam ।।

aṭitvā sarvatīrthāni pāpayonirato nṛpa ।
cintayāmāsa dehaṃ me na nivṛttaṃ kathaṃcana ।।

tasmāt pāpaviśaddhyarthaṃ praviśāmi hutāśanam ।
bhāryā tasya saputrā vai bhartāraṃ suvratā abravīt ।।

kiṃcid vijñāpayāmi tvāṃ yadi māṃ manyase vibho ।
kṣaṇamātreṇa duḥkhena sādhayāmi sukhaṃ bahu ।।

brāhmaṇasya hi dharmo ayaṃ sarvas tad vahṇisādhanena ।
tatsamāhṛtya dārūṇi pradīpya ca hutāśanam ।।

ahaṃ viśāmyavidhavā bhartāraṃ prathamaṃ drutam ।
na paśyāmi patantaṃ vai jvalane dāruṇe bhṛśam ।।

uktā sā akāśavāṇyā ca mā te mṛtyubhayaṃ śubhe ।
śrūyatāṃ mama vākyaṃ hi yathā dharmo na hīyate ।।

kubjārevāsamāyoge brahmarakṣovimokṣaṇam ।
tatra snātvā divaṃ yāti bilvāmrakam arcanāt ।।

labhate brahmalokaṃ ca rakṣoyoneś ca mokṣaṇam ।

brahmarākṣasa uvāca kā asi tvaṃ ca varārohe kasya cāsi yaśasvini ।।

anugrahārthaṃ bhūtānāṃ pūrvajanma kṛtaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।

ākāśavāṇy uvāca dhanyā ahaṃ sarvabhūtānāmavyaktāvyaktarūpiṇī ।।

evamustvā tu sā devī tatraivāntaradhīyata ।
putradārānvito natvā harikeśaḥ sureśvaram ।।

samprāpta sumudāyuktaḥ kubjārevāsamāgamam ।
tatra snātvā yathānyāyam arcayitvā maheśvaram ।।

hutāśanaṃ praviviśuḥ smṛtvā devaṃ hāriṃ haram ।
svīyaṃ gṛhamivākleśāḥ kāmakrodhavivarjitāḥ ।।

tatkṣaṇād divyadehās tu brahmatejovapurdharāḥ ।
divyayānaṃ samāruhya brahmalokam avāpnuyuḥ ।।

putradārasamāyukto harikeśo nṛpottama ।
tasya tīrthasya māhātmyād divi dīvyati devavat ।।

śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tatra liṅgānāṃ puṇyasaṅgame ।
mārkaṇḍeśvaram ityekaṃ madhureśvaram eva ca ।।

śūlapāṇiṃ tathaivānyam agastyeśvaram eva ca ।
etāny anyāni caiveha siddhaliṅgāni santi vai ।।

etat sarvaṃ yathā nyāyaṃ kathitaṃ tava suvrata ।
kubjārevāsamāyogaṃ surāsuraniṣevitam ।।

prātaryaḥ kīrtayed bhaktyā narmadāṃ saptakalpagām ।
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sa śaivaṃ labhate puram ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe kubjāmāhātmye trayoviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
samutpattiṃ ca kubjāyā yasyāṃ vimalamānasāḥ ।
sarvapāpavinirmuktā gandharvo ragarākṣasāḥ ।।

etad vai śrotum icchāmi vistareṇa mahāmune ।
kathyatāṃ muniśārdūla samākhyānaṃ purātanam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājan kathāṃ divyāṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm ।
citrāṅgadaḥ śakrasuto gandharvaḥ kāmamohitaḥ ।।

samālambya kumārīṇāṃ daśalakṣāṇi bhārata ।
reme yathecchayā so api paścān muktaś ca kilviṣāt ।।

ākhyānaṃ kathayiṣyāmi yathāvṛtta purātanam ।
suvarṇo nāma gandharvas tasya bhāryā yaśasvinī ।।

hemagarbheti vikhyātā śakrasyaiva yathā śacī ।
sutā tasyāḥ sukāmeti viditānaṅgamohinī ।।

rūpayauvanasampannā ūḍhā vai dhanadena sā ।
gauryārādhanayogena tasyāḥ putro apy ajāyata ।।

ketumāla iti khyāto rājā vaidyādhare pure ।
śaśirekhā priyā tasya bhārvyā vai rūpaśālinī ।।

dve kanye janayāmāsa ratiḥ prītirmanorame ।
dadau sa kāmadevāya pāṇigrahaṇapūrvakam ।।

kanyānāṃ daśalakṣāṇi bhūṣaṇair bhūṣitāni ca ।
tās tu yānasamārūḍhāḥ kāmarūpā manoramāḥ ।।

vicitravastrābharaṇā gauryārādhana tat parā ।
tāvanna bhujyate tābhis tāmbūlaṃ bhojanādikam ।।

yāvanna kāryam asmābhir iti saṅkalpamādadhuḥ ।
nityaṃ tairyatrikaṃ tās tu cakruḥ sarvā samāhitā ।।

vasante samanuprāpte draṣṭuṃ prekṣaṇakaṃ purā ।
puṣpakeṇa vimānena jagmus tā indramandiram ।।

krīḍayitvā yathā nyāyaṃ madirāmadavihvalāḥ ।
adṛṣṭvaiva bhavānīṃ tāś cakre tāmbūlabhakṣaṇam ।।

citrāṅgadasya cāpāraṃ rūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā varāṅganāḥ ।
mohitā nā abhijānanti madironmattamānasāḥ ।।

taiś cāpi kāmitāḥ sarvā gandharvyo muditānanāḥ ।
nānāvidhais tathā kāryaiś cikrīḍurmanmathād divi ।।

atīte vatsare tās tu gandharvapuramāgatāḥ ।
gaurīṃ draṣṭuṃ samājagmur umā māheśvaraṃ puram ।।

namaskṛtya tato devīm idaṃ vacanam abruvan ।
rakṣasvāsmākamīśāni cyutānāṃ niyamāt svakāt ।।

tataś cukopa devī tān pāpakarmaratān prati ।
vratādikaṃ hatā ye ye paradārāvidūṣakāḥ ।।

apatrapā durācārāḥ sarvalokabahiṣkṛtāḥ ।
tad adharmasya pāpasyāniṣkṛtir dharaṇītale ।।

kumārīṃ kāmayed yas tu kāmalobhena mohitaḥ ।
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ ।।

etasminn antare rājaṃs tataścaitrāṅgadaḥ stuvan ।
praṇamya śirasā devīm idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।

śāpasya sa bhayād bhūri vilalāpa narādhipa ।
akāryaṃ kṛtam asmābhir gandharvatanayānvitaiḥ ।।

prāyaścittaṃ kim asyādya pāpasya gada niṣkṛtim ।
uvāca vacanaṃ devī gandharvaṃ kāmamohitam ।।

dharmakriyāviluptasya svargalokacyutasya ca ।
kumārīdūṣaṇe pāpaṃ mahatāṃ lomaharṣaṇam ।।

kumārīdūṣaṇe pāpe niṣkṛtir na vidhīyate ।
mama gandharvakanyāś ca madhupānair viḍambitāḥ ।।

yūyaṃ tv anena pāpena gandharvāḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
kubjāvāmanahīnāṅgā bhaviṣyatha sahasraśaḥ ।।

divyavarṣasahasraṃ tu martyaloke cariṣyatha ।
kanyāvikṛtadoṣeṇa kubjāmarkaṭakānanāḥ ।।

svakarmakṛtadoṣeṇa pāpaṃ bhuñjantu bhūtale ।
eva śaptās tu te devyā sarve martya samāgaman ।।

śocantaḥ svāni karmāṇi pūrvajanmakṛtāni ca ।
babhramuḥ sarvatīrthāni loke caiva carācare ।।

viṣaṇṇavadanās sarve pāpenā anena kārṣitāḥ ।
śāpasyā antaṃ na vindanti sarvatīrthān bhramantyapi ।।

ekaviṃśatilakṣāṇi gandharvāṇi tathā anagha ।
na devā na ca tīrthāni pāpasyā asya viśuddhaye ।।

nānyad vā yujyate karma muktvā caiva hutāśanam ।
karmaṇāṃ doṣadāhena muñcāmaḥ pāpakarmaṇaḥ ।।

datto asmākaṃ mahāśāpo pāpamārganivartakaḥ ।
etasminn antare prāptaḥ sakuberaḥ purādhipaḥ ।।

samprāpto naimiṣāraṇye yatra citrāṅgadādayaḥ ।
tān dṛṣṭvā so abravīd devaḥ kṣaṇamātraṃ pratīkṣata ।।

umāmāheśvare yāvad vacmi gatvā yathoditam ।
evam uktvā yayau devaḥ kailāsaṃ parvatottamam ।।

sāṣṭāṅgaṃ ca namaskṛtya umayā sahitaṃ haram ।
jaya devi sureśāni saṃsārārṇavatāriṇi ।।

tvayā sṛṣṭam idaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।
vyāpinī śaktirūpeṇa sarveṣāṃ prāṇinām api ।।

ityevam ādibhir vākyair devīṃ tuṣṭāva vāsavaḥ ।
stotraiḥ stutā mahādevī śakraṃ vacanam abravīt ।।

ārtiḥ kā te samutpannā yathārthaṃ kathayasva me ।
uvāca vacanaṃ śakraḥ pārvatīṃ prati bhārata ।।

varadā yadi me devi varaṃ dātuṃ tvam icchasi ।
citrāṅgadādipāpasya mokṣaṇaṃ kriyatāṃ śubhe ।।

devyuvāca
śivājñā vartate loke pāpasyāsya viśuddhaye ।
tasmāt pāpaviśuddhyarthaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam ।।

devadevaṃ mahādevaṃ yācasva parameśvaram ।
evaṃ devyā vacaḥ śrutvā śakraḥ provāca śaṅkaram ।।

niṣkṛtis tv asya pāpasya kriyatāṃ vacanāt mama ।

śaṅkara uvāca yajñapākāśramaṃ gatvā mekalātīram āśritam ।।

yajñaparvatamāsādya vindhyasyaiva sutottamam ।
tatra yajñeśvaraṃ devaṃ liṅgaṃ paramasiddhidam ।।

bilvāmrakaṃ tathā cānyat kalpagā tīram āśritam ।
puṇyasthāne tu tatrāsya śāpasyānto bhaviṣyati ।।

ekaviṃśatilakṣāṇi tatra muktāni saṅgame ।
gandharvāṇāṃ mahārāja kubjabhāvam upeyuṣām ।।

mahānadī nṛpaśreṣṭha kubjā tena prakīrtitā ।
divyayānasamārūḍhāḥ stūyamānā marudgaṇaiḥ ।।

mudā paramayā yuktā gāndharvaṃ lokam āpnuyuḥ ।
bilvāmrakaṃ pūjayitvā gandharvā gatakilbiṣāḥ ।।

yathā pūrvaṃ tathedānī tīrthasyā asya prabhāvataḥ ।
harṣeṇa mahatā yuktaḥ śakro api tridivālayam ।।

jagāma tridaśaiḥ sārdhaṃ paripūrṇamanorathaḥ ।
ṣaḍasya cottare bhāge ṣaḍasya dakṣiṇe tathā ।।

evaṃ te kathito rājan revākubjāsamāgamaḥ ।
aneke yasya māhātmyāt saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ gatāḥ ।।
śravaṇāt kīrtanād vā api mucyate bhavabandhanāt ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe kubjāmāhātmye citrāṅgadaśāpamocano nāma caturviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athānyat kathayiṣyāmi tīrthānāṃ tīrthamuttamam ।
sarvapāpaharaṃ divyaṃ svargasopānasannibham ।।

sapādakoṭitīrthāni pure māheśvare nṛpa ।
raudraṃ vāruṇam āsādya krośamātrapramāṇataḥ ।।

atrāntare mahārāja śivakṣetramudāhṛtam ।
prāṇatyāgaṃ ca yaḥ kuryāc chivaloke ca modate ।।

tiryagyonigatāḥ pāpāḥ kīṭapakṣimṛgādayaḥ ।
te api yānti śivasthānaṃ yatra devo maheśvaraḥ ।।

tilodakapradānena mātṛkāḥ pitṛkās tathā ।
pitaras tasya tṛpyanti yāvad ābhūtasamplavam ।।

tatreṣṭā brahmaṇā pūrvamasaṃkhyeyāṃ makhottamāḥ ।
śakraśca devarājratvaṃ tatreṣṭvā samavāptavān ।।

kārtavīryeṇa tatraiva kṛtaṃ yajñaśataṃ purā ।
ayodhyāyāṃ purā rājan yajñadānaparāyaṇaḥ ।।

ādityasya sutaścāsīt sūryavaṃśe mahīpatiḥ ।
jitvā asurāṃs tathā daityān rakṣogaṇasamanvitān ।।

manurnāmnā cakravartī śakrādīśād guṇottamaḥ ।
purottame na sarpanti mṛtyurogajarās tathā ।।

śatārddhasāptabhaumaiś ca gṛhair hemamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।
vāpīkūpataḍāgānāṃ dīrghikānāṃ śatair yutā ।।

suśobhitā prekṣaṇīyair nānārūpair vilāsibhiḥ ।
veṇuvīṇādhvaniyutā nānāvādyaiḥ sahasraśaḥ ।।

alakeva kuberasya śakrasyevāmarāvatī ।
purī virājate tadvad ayodhyā devanirmitā ।।

lakṣāṇi dve ca sārdhāṇi prajā jīvanti tatra ca ।
tatraiva vaṃśe rājarṣīr abhūt paramadhārmikaḥ ।।

nānāmakhasahasrair yo dadāha pṛthivīm imām ।
na tad deśo na tat tīrthaṃ na tad rāṣṭaṃ na cāśramaḥ ।।

neṣṭaṃ yatra mahāyajñaiḥ sālaṅkāyanabhūbhṛtā ।
sasyamālādhṛtā pṛthvī dhanadhānyasamanvitā ।।

svayaṃ kāmadughā gāvaḥ paṭṭavastramahīruhāḥ ।
yajñaiḥ sarvair vivāhaiś ca vedair māṅgalyamaṅgalaiḥ ।।

evaṃ tu satataṃ dhātrī kālena mahatā tataḥ ।
anāvṛṣṭirabhūd rāṣṭre purā dvādaśavārṣikī ।।

mṛtā jānapadāḥ sarve dvipadāś ca catuṣpadāḥ ।
tṛṇagulmalatāvalyo bhūtagrāmaṃ caturvidham ।।

hāhākāromahānāsīd devāsuranṛṇāṃ tathā ।
sālaṅkāyanarājarṣiḥ cintayāmāsa bhārata ।।

janmaprabhṛti me pāpaṃ kiṃcid eva na vidyate ।
pūjayāmi hariṃ devaṃ saṃsārārṇavatāraṇam ।।

brāhmaṇāṃś ca munīṃś caiva tarpayāmāsa cecchayā ।
bṛhaspatisamaṃ buddhyā vaśiṣṭhaṃ brahmavādinam ।।

papraccha nṛpatir bhaktyā sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇipatya ca ।
anāvṛṣṭir abhūd vipra kathaṃ dvādaśavārṣikī ।।

nā aparādho mayā kaścit kṛto brāhmaṇadevayoḥ ।
saṃśayo me mahāstatra vedānugrahatatpara ।।

vaśiṣṭha uvāca
śṛṇu rājan mahābāho anāvṛṣṭeś ca kāraṇam ।
purā sāṃvatsare yajñe vṛddhāś ca munayo avadan ।।

teṣāṃ ca vacanaṃ śrutvā kartavyaṃ janasaṃsadi ।
tāvad eva muniścātriḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ ।।

bhṛguragnir marīciś ca kaśyapo atha vibhāṇḍakaḥ ।
jamadagniś ca māṇḍavyo yamo viṣṇus tathāṅgirāḥ ।।

bṛhaspatis tathā dakṣaḥ śātātapaparāśarau ।
uśanā gautamaś caiva vyāsaḥ kātyāyanas tathā ।।

viśvāmitro atha śāṇḍilyaḥ kakṣaḥ kātyāyanis tathā ।
hārītaḥ śaṅkhalikhitau yājñavalkyo atha gālavaḥ ।।

ātreyaḥ śaunako gargo jahnur uddālakas tathā ।
kauśiko bhārgavo agastyo durvāsāścyavanas tathā ।।
ete cānye api bahavo ṛṣayaḥ sūryavarcasaḥ ।।
dharmāṇāmupadeṣṭāro vedaśāstrānuyāyinaḥ ।
anāvṛṣṭiṃ tu vai jñātvā pratyayodhyāṃ pratasthire ।।

āgatān sa munīn dṛṣṭvā rājā paramadhārmikaḥ ।
udatiṣṭhan mahābhāga divi śakra iva aparaḥ ।।

tān abhyarcya yathā nyāyam arghapādyādibhiḥ svayam ।
upaviṣṭān yathā nyāyam āsane śubhadarśane ।।

sa kāraṇam anāvṛṣṭeḥ tān papraccha mahātmanaḥ ।
abruvan munayo vākyaṃ sālaṅkāyanabhūpatim ।।

bhaviṣyabhūtatattvajñaṃ saptakalpāntavāsinam ।
mārkaṇḍeyaṃ mahātmānaṃ sarveṣāṃ gurum arcaya ।।

tasyāśramapadaṃ gatvā brāhmaṇaiḥ saha cintaya ।
yaṃ yaṃ dharmaṃ sa vadati taṃ taṃ kartum ihārhasi ।।

evamukto dvijaiḥ sarvaiḥ sālaṅkāyanabhūpatiḥ ।
uvāca vacanaṃ sarvān munīndrāṃ chaṃsitavratān ।।

anugraham imaṃ manye prasādaṃ munisattamāḥ ।
ādideśa tato rājā bhrātarau dvārapālakau ।।

sudhanvavīradhanvānau pratīhārau mahābalau ।
rathe hayāni yujyantāṃ brāhmaṇārohaṇaṃ prati ।।

brahmaśarmā devaśarmā mantriṇau tattvadarśinau ।
papraccha gamanārthāya kartavyaṃ ca yathā adiśat ।।

mantriṇāvūcatuḥ
samayajño mahābāho tvam eva vihitaṃ kuru ।
rājā tadvacanaṃ śrutvā dharmaśāstraviśāradaḥ ।।

uvāca ślakṣṇāyā vācā harṣagadgadamānasaḥ ।
gantavyaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ yatra kalpāntago muniḥ ।।

evamuktvā yayau rājā brāhmaṇaiḥ saha bhārata ।
divyayānasamārūḍhaḥ samprāptaḥ kalpagātaṭam ।।

dharmāraṇyaṃ samāsādya mārkaṇḍaṃ munibhiḥ saha ।
sa samīpe samāsīnaṃ praṇamya praṇatikṣamam ।।

āpṛṣṭaḥ kuśalaṃ tena tadā vai brahmavādinā ।
uvāca vacanaṃ rājā mārkaṇḍaṃ jñānacakṣuṣam ।।

adya me kuśalaṃ brahmaṃs tvatpādāmbujadarśanāt ।
kiṃtu māṃ bādhate nityaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ caiva tattvavit ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
apamārgeṇa prajānāṃ deva brāhmaṇahiṃsayā ।
varṇāśramavilopena adharmo dharmabādhakaḥ ।।

śambhur na pūjyate yatra rudrabhāgo na dīyate ।
deśe tasmin anāvṛṣṭir durbhikṣaṃ maraṇaṃ dhruvam ।।

vinaśyanti prajā rāṣṭre alpāyur nṛpatir bhavet ।
abrahmaṇyā brāhmaṇāś ca śūdrā vai brahmavādinaḥ ।।

śivajapaṃ yajñasūtraṃ śūdro dhārayate yadā ।
aliṅgino liṅginaś ca avratā vratadhāriṇaḥ ।।

svapāpaṃ kṛtavantaś ca tān svarāṣṭre pravāsinaḥ ।
savyāṅge brahmasūtraṃ ca vahṇisūtraṃ ca kārayet ।।

gardabhārohaṇaṃ tasya kārayel lokagārhitam ।
etat te kathitaṃ rājann anāvṛṣṭeś ca kāraṇam ।।

anāvṛṣṭyā sasyahānis tatkṣayān mriyate prajā ।
prajākṣayād vedahānis taddhānau yajñasaṃkṣayaḥ ।।

tatkṣayād dharmahāniś ca taddhānau varṇasaṅkaraḥ ।
tatsaṅkarāt karmalopaḥ patanaṃ narake dhruvam ।।

gaṅgāsāgarasambhede cāṇḍālāḥ saptasāmpratam ।
kaṇadhūmaṃ pibantyāśu ūrdhvapādā hyadhaḥ śirāḥ ।।

cakampire surāḥ sarve siddhagandharvakinnarāḥ ।
devarājaḥ suraiḥ sārdhamāsanāc calito nṛpa ।।

tapasas tu prabhāvo ayam api dṛṣṭo narādhipa ।
naimiṣe ca mahāraṇye surāsuranamaskṛte ।।

śatamaṣṭottaraṃ sarve tāpasāḥ śūdrajanmanaḥ ।
brahmakarma samāsādya sthitā dharmaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

adharmacāriṇāṃ puṃsāṃ rājā pāpena lipyate ।
ayajñayājakasthāne anāvṛṣṭir bhavet sadā ।।

apūjanāt tathā nityaṃ devedevasya śūlinaḥ ।
na svargo nāpavargaś ca na bhogāś cāpi puṣkalāḥ ।।

brahmaviṣṇusurendrād yā arcayanti maheśvaram ।
kiṃ punar mānuṣāḥ pāpā rājānaḥ pāpajīvinaḥ ।।

nārcayanti maheśaṃ ye te narāḥ pāpabhāginaḥ ।
na ca svargasya mokṣasya phalaṃ bhogam avāpnuyuḥ ।।

tasmān nṛpa tvaṃ śreyāṃsi brāhmaṇaiḥ saha cintaya ।
narmadātīramāsādya rudrayajñaṃ samārabha ।।

teṣāṃ śirāṃsi home asmin pātaya tvaṃ yathāvidhi ।
samarcaya sureśānaṃ tataḥ śāntir bhaviṣyati ।।

kāmavarṣī ca parjanyaḥ punaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ pravartate ।
mucyatāṃ pāpadoṣeṇa rājyaṃ svargamavāpsyasi ।।

tavaitat kathitaṃ rājan yathādṛṣṭaṃ mayā anagha ।
tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā rājā paramadhārmikaḥ ।।

namaskṛtya muniśreṣṭham ṛṣibhiḥ saha bhārata ।
anugraham imaṃ manye tvatprasādād yathoditam ।।

ādideśa pratīhārān yajñasambhārasiddhaye ।
gatvā ayodhyāṃ purīṃ ramyāmādeśaṃ makhasambhavam ।।

yajñopaskaramādāya sarvair āgamya tām iti ।
rājñīnāṃ ca kumārāṇāṃ sahasraṃ sāṣṭakaṃ tathā ।।

sarvāṃś caiva mahīpālān nānādeśasamudbhavān ।
saptarātrābhyantarato yathā yajñaḥ pravartate ।।

namaskṛtya gatau tau tu pratīhārau puraṃ prati ।
kathayāmāsatustatra yathoddiṣṭaṃ nṛpeṇa tu ।।

aṣṭottarasahasraṃ tu rājñīnāṃ divyavāsasām ।
kumārā ye ca rājāno ye cānye gṛhakarmiṇaḥ ।।

asūtākṣatayonīnāṃ lakṣam ekaṃ tu yoṣitām ।
rambhorvaśīsamānānāṃ rūpeṇāpratimatviṣām ।।

mahoraskandhagātrāṇāṃ vāhānāmayutāni ṣaṭ ।
suvarṇāratnapūrṇānāṃ mudrāṇāmayutaṃ tathā ।।

savasānāṃ ca dhenūnāṃ triṃśal lakṣāṇi yantritaḥ ।
pāṇḍurāṇāṃ hayānāṃ tu ayutāni daśaiva tu ।।

ghaṇṭābharaṇaśobhānāṃ dantināmayutaṃ tathā ।
yajñopaskaramādāya sarvasambhārasambhṛtam ।।

prasthitau narmadāṃ rājñe sanniveśayatāṃ puraḥ ।
praṇamya cābravīd rājā saptakalpāntavāsinam ।।

ādeśo dīyatāṃ mahyaṃ makhaṃ yatra pravartate ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca vaidūryasya ca vāruṇyāṃ yajñayūpāṃś ca maṇḍapān ।।

anyāṃś ca yajñasambhārān sarvāṃs tatraiva kāraya ।
vaśiṣṭhaṃ vāmadevaṃ ca bhṛgumaṅgirasaṃ tathā ।।

pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ caiva bhāradvājaṃ ca kaśyapam ।
yājñavalkyaṃ muniṃ caiva muniṃ durvāsasaṃ tathā ।।

vibhāṇḍakaṃ parvataṃ ca viśvāmitraṃ ca nāradam ।
śaunakaṃ caiva gargaṃ ca saṃvartaṃ ca parāśaram ।।

āpastambośano vyāsān sakātyāyanagautamam ।
hārītaṃ śaṅkhalikhitau ṛṣyaśṛṅgaṃ ca somapam ।।

aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi vālakhilyān munīṃs tathā ।
sarvadevanamaskāryo yajñaparvatasaṃjñitaḥ ।।

hiraṇmayā mahāstambhā yādṛśair upaśobhitāḥ ।
bahudhā yatra śobhante tathokte yajñamaṇḍape ।।

kuṇḍasthalīḥ sruvās sarvāḥ kṛtvā hemamayā nṛpaḥ ।
nānāvidhair bhakṣyabhojyai rasaiś ca vividhais tathā ।।

saritaḥ sāgarāṃ śailāṃs tīrtharājaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।
lokapālān mahābāhurasurān daityadānavān ।।

candrādityau grahaiḥ sārdhaṃ nakṣatradhruvamaṇḍalam ।
brahmādyāṃś ca surāṃs tatra maruto devatās tathā ।।

viṣṇuṃ caiva sureśānaṃ yajñe tatpuruṣaṃ svayam ।
āvāhayan mahādevaṃ gaṇakoṭisamanvitam ।।

āvāhitas tataś cāgnir brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ ।
nirdhūmaḥ prajvalaṃś caiva sūryakoṭisamaprabhaḥ ।।

vedadhvanitanirghoṣair divaṃ bhūmiṃ ca nādayan ।
kaṇadhūmakṛtāhārāṃś cāṇḍālān saptavānaya ।।

tān ānaya tathā śūdrān naimiṣāraṇyavāsinaḥ ।

vaśiṣṭha uvāca anugraham imaṃ manye yanmāṃ vadasi pārthiva ।।

kuśāgreṇa tato rājā teṣāṃ mūrdhno nyapātayat ।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā mānuṣaṃ homaṃ sāmiṣaṃ pretarūpiṇam ।।

praṇaṣṭatoyā revā tu vihāya tridivaṃ gatā ।
homāvasāne samprāpte snānārthaṃ narmadāṃ yayuḥ ।।

śuṣkatoyāṃ tato apaśyan narmadāṃ śaṃsitavratāḥ ।
vismayaṃ paramaṃ prāptaḥ prāha durvāsasaṃ nṛpaḥ ।।

cukopa rājā vipreṣu pāpakarmā durāsadaḥ ।
parjanyārthaṃ vṛṣṭikāmaiḥ kṛto yajño nirarthakaḥ ।।

payaḥ purātanaṃ naṣṭaṃ na jātaṃ varṣaṇaṃ kvacit ।
rājñas tu vacanaṃ śrutvā durvāsāścā abravīt nṛpam ।।

munīṃś ca sarvāṃs tatrasthān dharmatattvaviśāradān ।
udakaṃ sarvalokānām īpsitaṃ ca na saṃśayaḥ ।।

brāhmaṇānāṃ tapo homo vedamantrā vaśe sthitāḥ ।
dakṣiṇā yajñarakṣā ca yajamānavaśe nṛpa ।।

yajñopaskaraṇaṃ kiṃcid yaccānyad vedasammitam ।
tatsarvaṃ yajamānena vedamūlaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।।

vitoyā narmadā jātā parjanyo naiva varṣati ।
tatsarvaṃ kṛtam evaṃ tu śrutir eṣā sanātanī ।।

yā yayau tāṃ pratīkṣasva narmadāmāpagottamām ।
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā kṣamasvety abravīt nṛpaḥ ।।

vaśiṣṭho vāmadevaśca vadatyevaṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।
kāśīpuryāṃ prayāge vā gaṅgāyamunasaṅgame ।।

tatraiva vartate yajñaḥ satyameva tapodhanāḥ ।
kecid āhuḥ kurukṣetraṃ sthāne yatra sarasvatī ।।

samuddiṣṭāni tīrthāni munibhis tu pṛthakpṛthak ।
abravīt sahasā rājan durvāsā raudratāpasaḥ ।।

nārado api muniśreṣṭhaḥ tāpaso gatakilbiṣaḥ ।
sarasvatyāṃ mahārāja tatra toyaṃ na vidyate ।।

teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sālaṅkāyanabhūpatiḥ ।
abravīc ca tato vākyaṃ sarvān ṛṣigaṇān prati ।।

kṣaṇamekaṃ pratīkṣadhvaṃ yāvad vahati kalpagā ।
ityuktvā sa nṛpaśreṣṭhaḥ tatastuṣṭāva kalpagām ।।

namaste astu sureśāni namaste śaṅkarātmaje ।
iḍā ca piṅgalā caiva umā gaṅgā sarasvatī ।।

gāyatrī vedamātā ca sāvitrī ca sarasvatī ।
brāhmī ca vaiṣṇavī gaurī lokamātā yaśasvinī ।।

samuddiṣṭāni tīrthāni pṛthivyāṃ yāni kāni ca ।
tvayā avṛtāni sarvāṇi jagac ca sacarācaram ।।

na tat paśyāmi tvadvārā avṛtaṃ yanna pradṛśyate ।
tvattoyasnānamātreṇa tṛptā yānti parāṃ gatim ।।

śrutvā stotram idaṃ devī rājñaś cāmitatejasaḥ ।
makarāsanamārūḍhā pratyakṣā saptakalpagā ।।

prāha brūhi varaṃ rājan yat te manasi vartate ।

rājovāca pūrvān sapta parān sapta pravāhān akṣayān kuru ।।

varam etam ahaṃ manye saptakalpāntavāsini ।

narmadovāca datto varo mayā hyeṣa satyaṃ tava narādhipa ।।

evamuktvā saric chreṣṭhā jalaughena pariplutā ।
pravāhair vistṛtais tatra vahantī sā vyavasthitā ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā tādṛśaṃ karma sālaṅkāyanabhūpateḥ ।
tuṣṭuvur munayaḥ sarve satyadharmaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

snānāvagāhanaṃ pānaṃ cakrus te pitṛtarpaṇam ।
tato nirvatito yajño vipraiḥ sarvasvadakṣiṇaiḥ ।।

yo yatkāmayate kāmaṃ tattasmai pratipāditam ।
vastrālaṅkāradānaiś ca divyayānaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ ।।

ṛtvijaḥ pūjitāḥ sarve sālaṅkāyanabhūbhṛtā ।
yugapat pūjitāḥ sarve brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।।

tataḥ śivālayaṃ gatvā liṅgaṃ tridaśapūjitam ।
nāmnā māheśvarākhyātaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam ।।

umayā sahitaṃ śambhuṃ bhuktimuktipradāyakam ।
oṃ maheśvarāya devāya śambhavāya namo namaḥ ।।

ityādinā tu mantreṇa samabhyarcya vidhānataḥ ।
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā sthitas tatraiva pārthivaḥ ।।

tato vinirgatā devī padamūlena śūlinaḥ ।
pravāho narmadā bhede nārmadaḥ surapūjitaḥ ।।

īśvarādyās tathā devāḥ sarve tuṣṭās tu bhārata ।
varaṃ yācasva bhūpāla yatheṣṭaṃ manasepsitam ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ devān rājā paramadhārmikaḥ ।
yadi me varadā yūyaṃ kāmadāś ca prasādataḥ ।।

idaṃ sthānaṃ tu na tyājyam īśvarād yaiḥ surair api ।
yāntu rāṣṭre prajāvṛddhim anāvṛṣṭyā prapīḍitāḥ ।।

idaṃ varam ahaṃ manye pāpā yāntu triviṣṭapam ।
agniś cāhavanīyo atra svayaṃ tiṣṭhati sarvadā ।।

devā ūcuḥ
yat tvayā bhāṣitaṃ rājaṃs tat sarvaṃ tu bhaved iti ।
evam uktvā yayuḥ sarve hy antardhānaṃ ca khecarāḥ ।।

punaḥ pravardhitaṃ rāṣṭraṃ kāmavarṣī ca vāsavaḥ ।
yajñaṃ nivartayitvā tu divyāmātyaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।।

mahīpālasahasrais tu sāntaḥpuraparicchadaḥ ।
viveśa nagarīṃ ramyām ayodhyāṃ devanirmitām ।।

etat te kathitaṃ rājann umāmāheśvaraṃ prati ।
tiryag yonigatāḥ pāpā mṛgapakṣisarīsṛpāḥ ।।
avaśaḥ svavaśo vā api śivalokamavāpnuyāt ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe pañcaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athānyat kathayiṣyāmi maṇḍapeśvaram uttamam ।
snātamātro naras tatra na viśed yonisaṅkaṭam ।।

daśalakṣāṇi tīrthāni tasmiṃs tiṣṭhanti bhārata ।
maṇḍapeśvaratīrthasya kūrmavṛddhivadarcanam ।।

surāsuragaṇair iṣṭaṃ tasmiṃs tīrthe narādhipa ।
anekabhāvikaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati ।।

tilodakapradānena piṇḍapātena bhārata ।
tṛpyanti pitaraḥ sarve yāvat tiṣṭhati kalpagā ।।

tatra yas tyajati prāṇān avaśasvavaśo api vā ।
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi rājā vaidyādhare pure ।।

mānasau brahmaṇaḥ putrau bādarāyaṇa śākaṭau ।
agastyasyāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ maharṣigaṇasevitam ।।

kandamūlaphalaiḥ śākaiḥ śivabhaktiparāyaṇaiḥ ।
ekadā avasare prāpte ajāpālo nṛpātmajaḥ ।।

ayodhyādhipatiḥ śrīmān cakratulyaparākramaḥ ।
aṣṭottaraṃ śataṃ vyāghrānajāḥ kṛtvā rarakṣa ca ।।

sapādalakṣaṃ jīvanti prajāstasmin mahīpatau ।
dhanāḍhyā dhanadasyeva praśaśāsa purīṃ tathā ।।

sa kadācit mahābhāgaḥ sasainyo mṛgayāṃ gataḥ ।
mahīpālasahasreṇa mudā paramayā yutaḥ ।।

so apaśyat parvatasyāgre merutulye mahīpatiḥ ।
puṣpārāmasahasrāṇi harmyāṇi vividhāni ca ।।

tatraiva śatasāhasraṃ yatīnām ūrdhvaretasām ।
bhaktyā abhyarcya vidhānena deveśaṃ ca munīṃs tathā ।।

praṇamyovāca madhuraṃ bādarāyaṇaśākaṭau ।
pitṝṇāṃ tāraṇārthāya śrāddhakālatvasiddhaye ।।

mahānayaṃ bhavadbhiś ca prasāda kriyatāṃ mayi ।
abhyarcya tān munīn sarvān praṇipatya sthitas tataḥ ।।

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā ajāpālasya bhūbhṛtaḥ ।
ṛṣīṇāṃ tāpasau vṛddhau bādarāyaṇaśākaṭau ।।

ūcatustau tu vacanam ajāpālaṃ narādhipam ।
na rājagrāhakāḥ sarve munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ ।।

rājapratigraho ghoro raudraḥ pāpo bhayāvahaḥ ।
narake yātanāṃ ghorāṃ kaḥ soḍhuṃ śaktimān bhavet ।।

svasti te astu nṛpaśreṣṭha panthānaḥ santu te śivāḥ ।
evam uktvā tu cakrus te munayo vākyasaṃyamam ।।

brahmaśāpabhayādbhīto nṛpastūṣṇīṃ babhūva ha ।
gajānāṃ daśasāhasraṃ ghaṇṭābharaṇabhūṣitam ।।

prādād viprāya saṃkalpya maṭhaṃ hemamayaṃ śubham ।
kālañjaragiriṃ rājā triścakāra pradakṣiṇām ।।

namaskṛtvā maheśānaṃ bhaktiyuktaḥ suhṛdvṛtaḥ ।
jagāma svapuraṃ rājā yathā śakro amarāvatīm ।।

gate tasmin mahīpāle ṛṣayaḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।
