annadaḥ prāṇadaḥ proktas tasmād annaprado bhavet ।।

tasmād annapradānena dattāny anyāni sarvaśaḥ ।
trailokye yāni dānāni bhogastrīvāhanāni ca ।।

annapānādi yatkiṃcid aiśvaryaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira ।
annadānasya tatsarvam ihāmutra phalaṃ smṛtam ।।

yasmād annena puṣṭāṅgaḥ kurute dharmasaṃcayam ।
pavitramamṛtaṃ divyaṃ śuddhaṃ sattvaṃ rasāyanam ।।

annapānāśvagovatsaśayyāchatrāṇy upānahau ।
pretalokapraśastāni dānānyaṣṭau yudhiṣṭhira ।।

evaṃ dānaviśeṣeṇa dharmarājapure narāḥ ।
sukhenaiva tu gacchanti tasmād dharmaṃ samācaret ।।

annadānaṃ mahārāja jalaṃ caiva tu puṣkalam ।
pitṛbhyaḥ prayato dadyāt tīrthe caivāmareśvare ।।

tīrthāni puṇyakṣetrāṇi yāni vai kīrtitāni ca ।
kāmamokṣapradānīha sarvasiddhikarāṇi ca ।।

sarveṣām eva teṣāṃ tu mātā vai parikīrtitā ।
narmadā saritā śreṣṭhā saptakalpavahā śubhā ।।

tapaso yajñadānānāṃ saṃkhyā tīrtheṣu vidyate ।
narmadāyāṃ na saṃkhyāsti teṣām ity āha śaṅkaraḥ ।।

yathā śivas tathā revā pūjanīyā prayatnataḥ ।
eṣu ye tu kukarmāṇaḥ pāpā dānavivārjitāḥ ।।

pathā ghoreṇa te yānti dakṣiṇena yamālayam ।
ṣaḍaśītisahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ samantataḥ ।।

puraṃ jñeyaṃ mahāraudraṃ nānārūpair adhiṣṭhitam ।
samīpastham ivābhāti narāṇāṃ krūrakarmaṇām ।।

pāpinām api dūrasthaṃ pathā raudreṇa yānti te ।
tīvrakaṇṭakayuktena śarkarābhūṣitena ca ।।

kṣuradhārāvṛtais tīkṣṇaiḥ pāṣāṇair nirmitena ca ।
kecit tv anena mahatā dārudāraiś ca ghātakaiḥ ।।

lohasūcībhir ugrābhir grastena ca kvacit kvacit ।
latāpratānaviṣamaiḥ parvatair vṛkṣasaṃkulaiḥ ।।

sutaptāṅgārayuktena yānti mārgeṇa duḥkhitāḥ ।
kvacid viṣam agartābhis taptaloṣṭeṣṭakair api ।।

sutaptabālukābhiś ca tathā tīkṣṇaiś ca śaṅkubhiḥ ।
anekabhagnaśākhābhir āvṛtena kvacit kvacit ।।

kaṣṭena tamasā kecid gacchanti hi yamālayam ।
mārgasthāṅgārakais taptair grastā dāvāgnibhis tathā ।।

kvacit taptaśilābhiś ca paṅkena kaṭimānataḥ ।
kvacid duṣṭāmbunā vyāptaṃ duṣkarīṣāgninā kvacit ।।

kvacid gṛdhrair bakair vyāghrair duṣṭaiḥ kīṭaiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ ।
kvacin mahākulīrādyaiḥ kvacit tvajagaraiḥ punaḥ ।।

makṣikābhiś ca raudrābhiḥ kvacit sarpair viṣolvaṇaiḥ ।
mattamātaṅgayūthaiś ca samantāc ca pramāthibhiḥ ।।

panthānamullikhadbhiś ca tīkṣṇaśṛṅgair mahābalaiḥ ।
siṃhair viṣāṇamahiṣair raudrair mattaiś ca śvāpadaiḥ ।।

ḍākinībhiś ca raudrābhir vikarālaiś ca rākṣasaiḥ ।
vyādhibhiś ca mahāghoraiḥ pāvakaiś ca durāsadaiḥ ।।

mahānalavimiśreṇa mahācaṇḍena vāyunā ।
mahāpāṣāṇavarṣeṇa bhidyamānā nirāśrayāḥ ।।

kvacit kvacit prataptena dīpyamānā vrajanti hi ।
mahatā va bāṇavarṣeṇa bhidyamānāḥ samantataḥ ।।

patadbhirvajrasaṅghātair ulkāpātaiś ca dāruṇaiḥ ।
pradīptāṅgāravarṣeṇa hanyamānā vrajanti hi ।।

mahāghoraravair ghorair vitrasyanto muhur muhuḥ ।
niśitāyudhavarṣeṇa pūryamāṇāś ca sarvaśaḥ ।।

mahākṣarāmbudhārābhiḥ sicyamānā muhurmuhuḥ ।
mahāśītena raudreṇa kṣuradhārādibhis tathā ।।

anyair bahuvidhākāraiḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।
itthaṃ ca taptaraudreṇa mārgeṇa viṣameṇa ca ।।

aviśrāntena mahatā hy avidūreṇa bhārata ।
avidūreṇa kaṣṭena sarvaduḥkhāśrayeṇa ca ।।

nīyante dehinaḥ sarve mūḍhāḥ pāpaparāyaṇāḥ ।
yamadūtair mahāghorair yamājñākāribhir balāt ।।

ekākinaḥ parādhīnā mitrabandhuvivarjitāḥ ।
śocantaḥ svāni karmāṇi dahyante ca muhurmuhuḥ ।।

pretabhūtavimiśrāś ca śuṣkakaṇṭhoṣṭhatālukāḥ ।
kṛśāṅgā bhītabhītāś ca dahyamānā hutāgninā ।।

baddhāḥ śṛṅkhalayā kecit majjantaḥ pāpino bhṛśam ।
kṛṣyante dahyamānās tu yamadūtair balotkaṭaiḥ ।।

urasyadhomukhasthāne tathaiva khalu duḥkhitāḥ ।
keśapāśe vibaddhāś ca kṛṣyante pāpinas tathā ।।

lalāṭe cāśugair biddhvā kṛṣyante dehinaḥ kvacit ।
uttānā duṣṭapanthānaṃ nīyante pāpakarmaṇā ।।

pārśvabāhuvibaddhāś ca jaṭhare paripīḍitāḥ ।
grīvāpāśavikṛṣyāś ca ke api yānti suduḥkhitāḥ ।।

jihvāśaṅkupradānena samānīyakṛkāṭikāḥ ।
arddhacandreṇa gṛhyante kṣipyamāṇā itas tataḥ ।।

śiśne ca vṛṣaṇe caiva rajjvā baddhās tathā paro ।
vicchinnahastapādāś ca chinnakarṇoṣṭhanāsikāḥ ।।

vicchinnaśiśnavṛṣaṇāś chinnaśīrṣāṅgasaṃcayāḥ ।
aṅkuśair bhidyamānās tu khādyamānāḥ sarīsṛpaiḥ ।।

itaś cetaś ca dhāvanti krandamānā nirāśrayāḥ ।
mudgārair lohadaṇḍaiś ca hanyamānā muhur muhuḥ ।।

kaśābhir vividhābhiś ca ghorābhiś ca samantataḥ ।
bhindipālaiś ca tudyante vamantaḥ śoṇitaṃ muhuḥ ।।

pātyamānāś ca salile chāyāṃ vai prārthayanti ca ।
dānahīnāḥ prayānty evaṃ prāyaścittakṛto narāḥ ।।

gṛhītvā caiva pātheyaṃ sukhaṃ yāti yamālayam ।
evaṃ pathā nikṛṣṭena prāptā yamapuraṃ narāḥ ।।

prājñāpitais tathā dūtaiḥ praveśyante yamāgrataḥ ।
tatra ye śubhakarmāṇas tān vai saṃsmārayed yamaḥ ।।

svāgatāsanadānena pādyārgheṇa priyeṇa ca ।
dhanyā yūyaṃ mahātmānātmano hitakāriṇaḥ ।।

yais tu divyasukhārthaṃ hi bhavadbhiḥ sukṛtaṃ kṛtam ।
narmadātaṭamāśritya parvate amarakaṇṭake ।।

dānaṃ dattaṃ tapastaptaṃ hutaṃ ceṣṭaṃ vidhānataḥ ।
vārāṇasyāṃ kurukṣetre prayāge puṣkare tathā ।।

gayāyāṃ naimiṣāraṇye gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgame ।
kedāre bharaive cāpi prabhāse śaśibhūṣaṇe ।।

mahākālavane ramye śrīśaile tripurāntake ।
traiyambake dhautapāpe nīlakaṇṭhe tathaiva ca ।।

gaṅgādvāre himadvāre tathā kālañjare girau ।
eteṣvanyeṣu tīrtheṣu kṣetreṣu ca yathākramam ।।

labdhaṃ janmaphalaṃ caiva bhavadbhir nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
idaṃ vimānam āruhya divyastrībhogabhūṣitam ।।

saṃgacchadhvaṃ śivaṃ svargaṃ sarvakāmasamanvitam ।
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān anantān puṇyasaṃkhyayā ।।

yatkiṃcid anyad aśubhaṃ svalpaṃ tadapi bhokṣyatha ।
ākhyātaṃ tu mayā tāvat kalpagātīravāsinaḥ ।।

ārohanti vimānāni sarveṣāmupari sthitāḥ ।
sarvatīrtheṣu saṃkhyāsti hyuktaṃ brahmādibhiḥ purā ।।

tatra yad dīyate dānaṃ tena svarge mahīyate ।
mriyate tatra yaḥ kaścid vratenānaśanena ca ।।

divyayānaṃ samāśritya sa prayāti śivālayam ।
etat te kathitaṃ rājan kalpagāpuṇyamuttamam ।।

paśyanti puṇyakarmāṇo yamaṃ mitram ivātmanaḥ ।
ye punaḥ krūrakarmāṇaste paśyanti bhayānakam ।।

daṃṣṭrā karālavadanaṃ bhrukuṭīkuṭilekṣaṇam ।
ūrddhvakeśaṃ mahāśmaśruṃ sphuradoṣṭhādharottaram ।।

aṣṭādaśabhujaṃ krūraṃ nīlāñjanacayopamam ।
sarvāyudhohyatakaraṃ garjantaṃ daṇḍapāṇinam ।।

mahāmahiṣamārūḍhaṃ taptāgnisamalocanam ।
raktamālyāmbaradharaṃ mahāmerum ivotthitam ।।

pralayāmbudanirghoṣaṃ pibantam iva vāridhīn ।
grasantam iva trailokyamudgiratam ivānalam ।।

mṛtyus tasya samīpasthaḥ kālānalasamaprabhaḥ ।
kālaś cāñjanasaṃkāśaḥ kṛtāntaś ca bhayānakaḥ ।।

vividhā vyādhayastīkṣṇā nānārūpā bhayānakāḥ ।
śaktiśūlāṅkuśadharāḥ pāśacakrāsipāṇayaḥ ।।

vajradaṃṣṭrādharā raudrāḥ krūrāś cāñjanasannibhāḥ ।
sarvāyudhodyatakarā yamadūtāś ca ghātakāḥ ।।

evaṃ vidhaṃ yamaṃ tatra paśyanti pāpacāriṇaḥ ।
nirbhayo yāti cātyarthaṃ yamo vā pāpakāriṇam ।।

citraguptaś ca bhagavān dharmaṃ teṣāṃ prabodhayan ।
bho bho duṣkṛtakarmāṇaḥ paradravyāpahārakāḥ ।।

gārjitā rūpavīryeṇa paradāropamardakāḥ ।
yas tu yat kurute karma tena tad bhujyate punaḥ ।।

tat kim ātmopaghātārthaṃ bhavadbhir duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ।
kim arthaṃ paritapyadhvaṃ pīḍyamānāḥ svakarmabhiḥ ।।

bhujyante svāni karmāṇi nāsti doṣo atra kasyacit ।
ete ca pṛthivīpālāḥ saṃprāptāś ca mahīpate ।।

svakīyaiḥ karmabhir ghorair duṣprajñābalagarvitāḥ ।
bho bho nṛpā durācārāḥ prajāvidhvaṃsakāriṇaḥ ।।

svalpakālasya rājyasya kiṃ vai tad duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ।
bhavadbhī rājyalobhena mohenānyāyavṛttibhiḥ ।।

yadgṛhītaṃ phalaṃ tasya yūyaṃ bhuṅgdhvaṃ yathātatham ।
kutra rājyaṃ kalatraṃ vā yadartham aśubhaṃ kṛtam ।।

tatsarvasvaṃ parityajya yūyam ekākinas tathā ।
tvad bāndhavā na paśyanti yena vidhvaṃsitāḥ prajāḥ ।।

yamadūtaiḥ pātyamānā adhunā kīdṛśaṃ bhavet ।
evaṃ bahuvidhair vākyair upalabdhā yamena te ।।

śocanti svāni karmāṇi tūṣṇīṃ bhūtāś ca pārthiva ।
iti vākyaiḥ samādiśya nṛpāṃs tān dharmarāṭ tataḥ ।।

teṣāṃ pāpaviśuddhyarthaṃ yamo dūtān athābravīt ।
bho bhoś caṇḍa mahācaṇḍa gṛhītvā nṛpatīnimān ।।

viśodhayadhvaṃ pāpebhyaḥ krameṇa narakāgninā ।
tataḥ śīghraṃ samāsthāya nṛpān saṃgṛhya pādayoḥ ।।

bhrāmayitvā tu vegena cikṣipuryamakiṅkarāḥ ।
sarve vegena mahatā supratapte mahītale ।।

āsphālayanti mahati cāśmasāramaye drume ।
tatas te sarva evāśu prahārair jarjarīkṛtāḥ ।।

visaṃjñāś ca tadā santi niśceṣṭāś ca yudhiṣṭhira ।
tatas te vāyunā spṛṣṭāḥ śanais tu jīvitāḥ punaḥ ।।

tānānīya viśuddhyarthaṃ kṣipanti narakārṇave ।
aṣṭāviṃśatir evādyās tīvrānarakakoṭayaḥ ।।

saptamasya talasyānte ghore tamasi saṃsthitāḥ ।
atighorā ca raudrā ca tathā ghoratamā sthitā ।।

atyantaduḥkhajananī ghorarūpā ca pañcamī ।
ṣaṣṭhī taraṇatārākhyā saptamī ca bhayānakā ।।

aṣṭamī kālarātriś ca navamī ca ghaṭotkaṭā ।
daśamī caiva caṇḍā ca mahācaṇḍā tato apyadhaḥ ।।

caṇḍakolāhalā caiva pracaṇḍā ca parāgnikā ।
jaghanyā hyavarā lomā bhīṣaṇī caiva nāyikā ।।

karālā vikarālā ca vajraviṃśatirāśritā ।
astā ca pañcakoṇā ca sudīrghā parivartulā ।।

saptabhaumāṣṭabhaumā ca dīrghamāyetihāparā ।
iti tā nāmataḥ proktā ghorā narakakoṭayaḥ ।।

aṣṭāviṃśatiretās tu bhūtānāṃ mānataḥ smṛtāḥ ।
tāsāṃ krameṇa vijñeyāḥ pañcapañcaiva nāyakā ।।

pratyekaṃ sarvakoṭīnāṃ nāmatas tu viśāmpate ।
rauravaḥ prathamas teṣāṃ rudanti yatra dehinaḥ ।।

mahārauravapīḍābhir mahānto api rudanti hi ।
tamaḥ śītaṃ tathā coṣṇaṃ pañcaite nāyakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

aghoraḥ prathamas tīkṣṇaḥ padmaḥ saṃjīvanaḥ śaṭhaḥ ।
mahāmāyo vilomaś ca kaṇṭakaḥ kaṭakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

tīvro vāmaḥ karālaś ca kiṅkarālaḥ prakampanaḥ ।
mahācakraḥ supadmaś ca kālasūtraḥ pragarjanaḥ ।।

sūcīmukhaḥ sunemiś ca khādakaḥ suprapīḍitaḥ ।
kumbhīpākaḥ supākaś ca krakacaś ca sudāruṇaḥ ।।

aṅgārarātriḥ pacanaḥ asṛkpūyabhavas tathā ।
sutīkṣṇāḥ śaṇḍaśakunī mahāsaṃvartakaḥ kratuḥ ।।

taptajantuḥ paṅkaleṣaḥ pūtimān ca hradastrapuḥ ।
ucchvāsaś ca nirucchvāsaḥ sudīrghaḥ krūraśālmalī ।।

uṣṭritastu mahānādaḥ pravāhaḥ supravāhanaḥ ।
vṛṣāśrayo vṛṣāśvaś ca siṃhavyāghragajānanāḥ ।।

śvaśūkarājamahiṣameṣamūṣakharānanāḥ ।
grāhakumbhīranakrāsyā mahāghorā bhayānakāḥ ।।

sarvabhakṣāḥ svabhakṣāś ca sarvakarmā aśvavāyasāḥ ।
gṛdhrolūka ulūkaś ca śārdūlakapikacchurāḥ ।।

gaṇḍakaḥ pūtivaktraś ca raktāsyaḥ pūtimūtrikaḥ ।
kaṇadhūmras tuṣārāgniḥ kṛmimān nirayas tathā ।।

ātodyaś ca pratodyaś ca rudhirodyaś ca bhojanam ।
kālātmago anubhakṣaś ca sarvabhakṣaḥ sudāruṇaḥ ।।

karkaṭas tu viśālaś ca vikaṭaḥ kaṭapūtanaḥ ।
ambarīṣaḥ kaṭāhaś ca kaṣṭā vaitaraṇī nadī ।।

sutapto lohaśaṅkuś ca ekapādo aśrupūraṇaḥ ।
asipatravanaṃ ghoram asthiliṅgaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।।

tilātasīkṣuyantrāṇi kūṭapāpapramardanāḥ ।
mahācullī vicullī ca taptalohamayī śilā ।।

parvataḥ kṣuradhārākhyo mayo yamalaparvataḥ ।
sūcīviṣṭhāndhakūpāś ca patanaḥ pātanas tathā ।।

muśalī vṛṣalī caivāśivā saṅkaṭalā tathā ।
tālapatrāsigahanaṃ mahāmohaka eva ca ।।

saṃmohano asthibhaṅgaś ca taptācalamayo aguṇaḥ ।
bahuduḥkho mahāduḥkhaḥ kaśmalo yamalas tathā ।।

hālāhalo virūpaś ca śvarūpaścyutamānasaḥ ।
ekapādastripādaś ca tīvraś ca viditas tataḥ ।।
aṣṭāviṃśatir ity ete kramaśaḥ pañcakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe narakavarṇanaṃ nāma dvipañcāśattamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
koṭī nāmanurūpāś ca pañcapañcaiva nāyakāḥ ।
rauravādyaṃ marīcyantaṃ narakānāṃ śataṃ smṛtam ।।

catvāriṃśat samadhikaṃ mahānarakamaṇḍalam ।
ekakramāt prabhujyante naraiḥ karmānurūpataḥ ।।

kāmanābhir virūpābhir akarmapracayād drutam ।
sugūḍhayā tato dhvānte taptaśṛṅkhalayā narāḥ ।।

mahāvṛkṣasya śākhāyāṃ lambyante yamakiṅkaraiḥ ।
tatas tān sarvataś caiva dolayanti hi kiṅkarāḥ ।।

dolitāś cātivegena niḥsaṃjñāṃ yānti pāpinaḥ ।
antarikṣe sthitānāṃ ca lohabhāraśataṃ tadā ।।

pādayor badhyate teṣāṃ yamadūtair balotkaṭaiḥ ।
tena bhāreṇa mahatā bhṛśaṃ santāpitā narāḥ ।।

dhyāyanti svāni karmāṇi tūṣṇīṃ tiṣṭhanti niścalāḥ ।
tataḥ kramād agnivarṇair lohadaṇḍaiḥ sakaṇṭakaiḥ ।।

nihanyante prayatnena yamadūtaiś ca mastake ।
viṣṭhāpūrṇe tataḥ kūpe kṛmīṇāṃ nilaye tataḥ ।।

samantāt kiṅkarair ghoraiḥ pacyante pāpakāriṇaḥ ।
tataḥ kṣāreṇa nīreṇa vahṇāvapi viśeṣataḥ ।।

vārtākavat prapacyante tapte lohakaṭāhake ।
amedhyakūpe prakṣipya jalajantu samākule ।।

medosṛkpūyapūrṇāyāṃ vāpyāṃ kṣiptās tu te tataḥ ।
bhakṣante kṛmibhis tīkṣṇair lohatuṇḍaiś ca vāyasaiḥ ।।

pacyante māṃsavac cāpi pradīptāṅgārarāśiṣu ।
protāḥ śūleṣu tīkṣṇeṣu narāḥ pāpasamanvitāḥ ।।

pacyante pāpinas te vai yamadūtair anekadhā ।
tailapūrṇakaṭāheṣu sutapteṣu tataḥ punaḥ ।।

teṣāṃ cotpāṭyate jihvā asatyā priyavādinām ।
sudṛḍhena sutaptena prapīḍyorasi pādataḥ ।।

mithyāgamaprayuktasya dvijasyāpi tathaivaca ।
yajñārthakośavistīrṇaṃ bhallais tīkṣṇaiḥ pratodyate ।।

nirbhatsayanti ye mūḍhā mātaraṃ pitaraṃ teṣāṃ ।
teṣāṃ vaktraṃ bālukābhir muhur āpūrya sicyate ।।

tataḥ kṣāreṇa dīptena payasā tu punaḥ punaḥ ।
drutaṃ sampūryate atyarthaṃ taptatailena tanmukham ।।

viṣṭhābhiḥ kṛmipūrṇābhiḥ śvānavac caraṇair bhaṭaiḥ ।
paripīḍya viṣāṇena praviṣṭā lohaśālmalīm ।।

hanyante pṛṣṭhadeheṣu punar bhīmair mahābalaiḥ ।
dantureṇātikuṇṭhena krakacena balīyasā ।।

śiraḥ prabhṛti pāṭyante ghoraiḥ karmabhir ātmajaiḥ ।
khādayanti svamāṃsāni pāyayanti svaśoṇitam ।।

annaṃ pānaṃ na dattaṃ yair mūḍhair nāpy anumoditam ।
ikṣuvatte prapīḍyante jarjarīkṛtya mudgaraiḥ ।।

asitālavane ghore chidyante khaṇḍakhaṇḍaśaḥ ।
sūcībhir bhinnasarvāṅgās tataḥ śūle praropitāḥ ।।

cācalyamānāḥ kṛṣyante na mriyante tathāpi ca ।
dehād utpāṭyate māṃsaṃ teṣām asthīni mudgaraiḥ ।।

bahuśaḥ kṛṣyate tūrṇaṃ yamadūtair balotkaṭaiḥ ।
te anucchvāsenānuchvāsās tiṣṭhanti narake ciram ।।

ucchvāse ca sadocchvāsā bālukāvadanāvṛtāḥ ।
rauraveṣu tu dante vai pīḍyante vividhaiś caraiḥ ।।

mahārauravapīḍābhir mahānto api rudanti hi ।
upasthāsye gude pārśve pāde corasi mastake ।।

nihanyante bhaṭais tīkṣṇaiḥ sutaptair lohamudgaraiḥ ।
nindanti ye svarūpeṇa paradārān hasanti ca ।।

āliṅganti patīn anyān na vindanti svakān striyaḥ ।
kimu dhāvasi vegena na smarer atiśāśvatīm ।।

vañcitaś ca tvayā bhartā pāpāndhaś ca yathā sukham ।
lohakumbhe vinikṣiptāḥ citāś ca śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।।

samṛddhāgnau prapācyante praveśyante śilāsu ca ।
kṣipyante cāndhakūpeṣu daśyante ajagarair bhṛśam ।।

ye nindanti mahātmānam ācāryaṃ dharmardarśinam ।
śivabhaktaṃ ca vipraṃ ca śivadharmaṃ ca śāśvatam ।।

teṣām urasi kaṇṭhe ca jihvāyāṃ dehasandhiṣu ।
kīlakairoṣṭhapuṭake kīlyante yamakiṅkaraiḥ ।।

evam ādimahāghorā yātanāḥ pāpakarmiṇām ।
ekaika narake jñeyāḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।।

yātanā gahanā rājan sarveṣāṃ pāpakarmiṇām ।
ityeva yātanānantāḥ sarveṣu narakeṣu ca ।।

kastā varṣaśatenāpi vaktuṃ śaknoti mānavaḥ ।
ity evaṃ vividhair ghoraiḥ pātyamānāḥ svakarmabhiḥ ।।

kramāt sarveṣu pacyante narakeṣu na saṃśayaḥ ।
mahāpātakinaś cāpi sarveṣu narakeṣu ca ।।

ācandratārakaṃ yāvat pīḍyante vividhaiś caraiḥ ।
tathā pātakinaḥ sarve nirayeṣv eṣu sarvadā ।।

caturdikṣu supacyante narakeṣu na saṃśayaḥ ।
upapātakinaś cāpi tadarddhaṃ yānti mānavāḥ ।।

mṛtyur na jñāyate tāta kadā kasya bhaviṣyati ।
prāpte cākasmike mṛtyau varṣaṃ vindati ko naraḥ ।।

parityajya yataḥ sarvam ekākī yāsyasi dhruvam ।
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena satyadharmaparo bhava ।।
etat te sarvamākhyātaṃ narakāṇā tu lakṣaṇam ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe narakāyātanānuvarṇano nāma tripañcāśattamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca tīryate kena dharmeṇa saṃsārābdhiḥ sudustaraḥ ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca tena nirbhartsitaiḥ pāpaiḥ kathyamānāṃ kathāṃ śṛṇu ।।

rakto mūḍhaś ca loko ayam akārye saṃpravartate ।
na cātmānaṃ vijānāti na paraṃ na ca daivatam ।।

na śṛṇoti paraṃ śreyaḥ sati cakṣuṣi nekṣate ।
same pathi śanair gacchan plavate sma pade pade ।।

evam ukto dharmarājaḥ saṃkṣepāt pāpadehinām ।
vistareṇa yadā cakhyau teṣāṃ tac chṛṇu sāmpratam ।।

yama uvāca
mayā mukto na jānāti bodhyamāno budhair api ।
saṃsāre kliśyate nānā rāgalobhavaśāt naraḥ ।।

garbhapātena bhāvena śāstram uktaṃ na budhyate ।
narair na śrūyate karma svargamokṣaprasādhakam ।।

santapyati śivadhyāne sarvakāmārthasādhane ।
narakād ātmanaḥ śreyo yadatra mahadadbhutam ।।

pretabhūtā narāḥ sarve yamalokaṃ samāgatāḥ ।
ākhyānaṃ kathayiṣyāmi yathoddiṣṭaṃ purātanam ।।

sūryeṇa kathitaṃ tv āsīn narmadākhyānam uttamam ।
devatānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca mama pitrānukampayā ।।

sapādalakṣam adhikaṃ brahmaṇā kathitaṃ raveḥ ।
tatra śrutaṃ mayā kṛtsnaṃ brahmaṇā tu śivāc chrutam ।।

śivena kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ pārvatyāḥ ṣaṇmukhasya tu ।
jambūdvīpaṃ samāsādya mānuṣīṃ yonim āśritaḥ ।।

nāśrayennarmadāṃ devīṃ saptakalpavahāṃ tu yaḥ ।
snānāvagāhanāt pānāt tathā dānakriyādibhiḥ ।।

loke asmin gatidā kānyā pāpopahatacetasām ।
ye dhyāyanti mahādevīṃ narmadāṃ pāpahāriṇīm ।।

aghāni teṣāṃ naśyanti tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā ।
narmadāṃ saṃsmared yas tu kīrtayed yas tu vā girā ।।

paralokaṃ samāyāto yamadūtair na bādhyate ।
narmadāṃ kīrtayed yas tu pāpakarmā narādhamaḥ ।।

narakān samayoddiṣṭān na ca krāmati karhicit ।
gaṅgādyāḥ saritastatra tīrthakoṭir anekadhā ।।

revātejaḥ pratāpena śuddhiṃ gacchanti tatkṣaṇāt ।
narakasthaḥ smared yas tu mekalāṃ tu haraṃ harim ।।

mucyate yamadūtaiḥ sa tatkṣaṇān nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
yadi tiṣṭhati vaidūryaparvate amarakaṇṭake ।।

oṃkāraḥ parameśāno bhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ ।
kimarthaṃ tv iha śocanti pāpopahatacetasaḥ ।।

siddheśvaraṃ siddhaliṅgaṃ lokānugrahakārakam ।
yajñeśvaraṃ ca madhye tu tatraiva śaśibhūṣaṇam ।।

narmadā dakṣiṇe bhāge liṅgaṃ caiva maheśvaram ।
caturthaṃ kapileśaṃ ca śivakṣetraṃ vidurbudhāḥ ।।

ye arcayanti sadā bhaktyā puṣpadhūpārtitarpaṇaiḥ ।
śivalokaṃ tu te yānti narakān nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ yathā pṛṣṭaṃ tvayānagha । pāpiṣṭhān nṝnadharmasthān kathayāmāsa bhārata ।। [steht so dort] 
godānaṃ hemadānaṃ ca tiladānaṃ tathaiva ca ।
annadānaṃ payodānaṃ sarvopaskaram eva ca ।।

prāsādārāmadānaṃ ca ye kurvanti narottamāḥ ।
yamalokaṃ na te yānti narakaṃ ghorarūpiṇam ।।

mucyante sarvapāpebhyaḥ śivasya vacanaṃ yathā ।
sanmānaṃ cāpamānena viyogeneṣṭasaṅgamam ।।

yauvanaṃ jarayā grastaṃ kaṣṭāt saukhyamupadrutam ।
valibhiḥ palitaiś cāpi jarjarīkṛtavigrahaḥ ।।

kiṃ karoti naraḥ prājño jarayā jarjarīkṛtaḥ ।
strīpuṃsor yauvanaṃ rūpaṃ yadanyo anyaṃ priyaṃkaram ।।

tad eva jarayā grastam ubhayor api na priyam ।
apūrvavat tathātmānaṃ śaithilyena samanvitam ।।

yaḥ paśyan na virajyeta ko anyas tasmād acetanaḥ ।
jarābhibhūtaḥ puruṣaḥ patnīputrādibāndhavaiḥ ।।

aśaktatvād durācārair bhṛtyaiś ca paribhūyate ।
dharmam arthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca mokṣaṃ na jarayā yutaḥ ।।

śaktaḥ sādhayituṃ tasmāt purā dharmaṃ samācaret ।
vātapittakaphādīnāṃ vaiṣamyaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhira ।।

vātādīnāṃ samūhaś ca dehajaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।
tasmād vyādhiparaṃ jñeyaṃ śarīram idam ātmanaḥ ।।

vātotpatty atirekeṇa bādhito vai jvareṇa ca ।
rogair nānāvidhibhavair bahuduḥkhāny anekadhā ।।

tāni ca svātmavedyāni kim anyat kathayāmy aham ।
ekottaraṃ mṛtyuśatam asmin dehe pratiṣṭhitam ।।

atraikaṃ kālarūpaṃ ca śeṣāstvāgantavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
ye tv ihāgantavaḥ proktāste praśāmyanti bhaiṣajaiḥ ।।

japahomapradānaiś ca kālamṛtyur na śāmyati ।
apamṛtyuś ca sarvasya viṣam adyādisambhavaḥ ।।

na cātipuruṣas tasmād apamṛtyor babheti vai ।
vividhā vyādhayaḥ kaṣṭāḥ savaidyāḥ prāṇinas tathā ।।

viṣāṇi tv abhicārāś ca mṛtyor dvārāṇi dehinām ।
pīḍitaṃ rogasarpādyair api dhanvantariḥ svayam ।।

svasthaṃ kartuṃ na śaknoti kālaprāptaṃ hi dehinam ।
naiṣadhaṃ na tapo dānaṃ na mitrāṇi na bāndhavāḥ ।।

paritrātuṃ no samarthāḥ kālena paripīḍitam ।
nāsti mṛtyusamaṃ duḥkhaṃ nāsti mṛtyusamo ripuḥ ।।

nāsti mṛtyusamaḥ kālaḥ sarveṣām eva dehinām ।
sadbhāryā putramitrāṇi rājyaiśvaryasukhāni ca ।।

mṛtyuśchinatti sarvāṇi vividhāny api bhārata ।
idaṃ te kathitaṃ rājañjñātisaṃsāradustaram ।।

pariṇāma iti jñātvā sarvaṅkālasya bhojanam ।
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena saṃsevyā saptakalpagā ।।

sarvaduḥkhāpahā nityaṃ sarvaśokavināśinī ।
yo yān kāmayate kāmāṃstāṃstān devī prayacchati ।।

idaṃ jñānam idaṃ dhyānaṃ pāṇḍityaṃ veda vedanam ।
nivāsaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sevyate saptakalpagā ।।

yajño dānaṃ tapaḥ satyaṃ svādhyāyaḥ pitṛtarpaṇam ।
saphalaṃ labhate teṣāṃ yo revāmbu niṣevate ।।

brahmakūrcasahasrāṇi somapānāyutaṃ tathā ।
narmadātoyapānasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।।

saṃyukto api mahāpāpair nānājanmakṛtair api ।
oṃkāradakṣiṇe ghoraṃ mucyate tatkṣaṇāj japan ।।

godānānna paraṃ dānaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam ।
narmadāpayasi snātvā yo dadyād gāṃ dvijanmane ।।
saṃkhyāṃ kartuṃ yathāvac ca na devair api śakyate ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe karmagatiyamavākyaṃ nāma catuṣpañcāśattamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
dhenuḥ katividhā proktā kasmin kāle ca dīyate ।
sarvopaskarasaṃyuktā tvatta icchāmi veditum ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājan mahābāho kathyamānaṃ nibodha me ।
kathayāmi tavākhyānam ādikalpe kṛte yuge ।।

cakravartī śaśāṅko abhūt sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।
na ca varṇayituṃ śakyaḥ satyadharmavrate sthitaḥ ।।

bubhuje sa mahīmetāmekacchatrāṃ samāhitaḥ ।
navakhaṇḍāṃ saptadvīpā yathā śakro amarāvatīm ।।

hariścandrasya tasyāpi saṃvādaś cakravartinaḥ ।
hariścandraḥ kurukṣetre gavām ayutam uttamam ।।

hemabhāramalaṅkārasarvaratnavibhūṣitam ।
brahmarṣir mudgalo nāma svayaṃ brahma pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।।

mudgalāś ca dvijāḥ sarve satyadharmaparāyaṇāḥ ।
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ sāgraṃ brāhmaṇā brahmavādinaḥ ।।

hariścandro dadau tebhyo rāhusūryasamāgame ।
dvijān sampūjya vidhicchraddhayā parayā yutaḥ ।।

arcayitvā maheśānaṃ sthānaṃ paramasiddhidam ।
cakrapāṇiṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ mudā paramayā yutaḥ ।।

sarasvatyāṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha tiladarbhānvitasya tu ।
dānasyāsya prabhāveṇa lokāstenākhilā jitāḥ ।।

antarikṣe purī prāptā sarvalokamanoharā ।
hariścandrapurī khyātā sā asmil loke carācare ।।

satyadānasarvatyāgair ityādibhir alaṃkṛtaḥ ।
hariścandrasamo rājā na bhūto na bhaviṣyati ।।

evaṃ gāthā purā gītā śakrādyaiḥ surasattamaiḥ ।
śaśāṅko apyakarot sarvaṃ narmadātīramāśritaḥ ।।

dānaṃ yajña tapaḥ satyaṃ parvate amarakaṇṭake ।
dadau cārdhaprasūtāṃ brāhmaṇāya mahātmane ।।

dānasyāsya prabhāveṇa hariścandrādhiko abhavat ।
anekabhāvikaṃ pāpaṃ dagdhvā tūlaughavacchikhī ।।

yāvad vatsasya pādau dvau mukhaṃ yonau pradṛśyate ।
tāvad gauḥ pṛthivī jñeyā saśailavanakānanā ।।

svarṇaśṛṅgī raupyakhurī savatsā kāṃsyadohanā ।
narmadāsnānayuktā tu sakuśā tilasaṃyutā ।।

oṃkārāmarayor madhye koṭitīrthe narādhipaḥ ।
etāḥ sahasrasakhyātā brāhmaṇebhyo nyavedayat ।।

etasminn antare nedurdevadundubhayo divi ।
tatkṣaṇād yānam ārūḍho jvalan maṇigaṇair iva ।।

stūyamānaḥ samīpasthair asaṃkhyātair vimānibhiḥ ।
dhṛtasvarṇātapatras tu vījyamānas tu cāmaraiḥ ।।

yojanānāṃ sahasreṇa hariścandro apy adhaḥ sthitaḥ ।
tad dṛṣṭvā tādṛśaṃ karma śaśāṅkasya viśāmpateḥ ।।

sa vinindya kurukṣetraṃ vismayāviṣṭacetanaḥ ।
mahānadyāṃ śaśāṅkena rāhusomasamāgame ।।

dattaṃ dānaṃ na sāmānyaṃ bhaved iti samāsataḥ ।
viṣaṇṇavadano bhūtvā hariścandro nṛpottamaḥ ।।

brahmalokaṃ gataḥ kṣipraṃ yatra lokeśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।
abhivādya yathā nyāyaṃ papraccha sa pitāmaham ।।

dānena nirjitā devāḥ śaśāṅkena mahātmanā ।
kiṃ ca puṇyamidaṃ brahman kurukṣetrād viśiṣyate ।।

amareśvaratīrthaṃ tu nāma revāsamudbhavam ।
kenāpi na samaṃ bhūtam uparyupari dīpyate ।।

iti śrutvā vacas tasya hariścandrasya dhīmataḥ ।
uvāca vacanaṃ brahmā hariścandraṃ nṛpottamam ।।

viṣādaṃ tyaja rājendra gahanā karmaṇāṃ gatiḥ ।
śaśāṅkasadṛśo rājā na dṛṣṭo na śruto mayā ।।

evaṃ vaktuṃ na yogyo ahaṃ na devāpi savāsavāḥ ।
anekāni sahasrāṇi purā vai cakravartinā ।।

iṣṭāni ca vidhānena parvate amarakaṇṭake ।
rāhusūryasamāyoge tīrthalakṣāṇi bhārata ।।

sarasvatīṃ kurukṣetraṃ puṣkaraṃ naimiṣaṃ tathā ।
tīrthāny etāni cānyāni snānaṃ kartuṃ samāyayuḥ ।।

mekalāyāṃ hariścandra koṭitīrthe narādhipa ।
tīrthānāṃ tyaja rājendra sāmyaṃ mekalayā saha ।।

vārāṇasyā kurukṣetraṃ tolitaṃ ca mayā purā ।
tīrthāni na samaṃ yānti tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।।

khyātamātraṃ kurukṣetraṃ lokayātrāpravartakam ।
purāṇaṃ na śrutaṃ yais tu mithyājñānasamanvitaiḥ ।।

sevyatāṃ kalpagā devī yadīcchet paramaṃ padam ।
namaskṛtya vidhātāram ayodhyādhipatis tadā ।।

mudā paramayā yuktaḥ sa yayāv amareśvaram ।
etat sarvaṃ samākhyātaṃ yathāvat tava suvrata ।।
yaḥ śṛṇoti naro rājan gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe godānamahimānuvarṇano nāma pañcapañcāśattamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
māhiṣmatyāḥ paścime vai tīrthaṃ pāpaharaṃ param ।
aśokavanikā nāma sarvaśokavināśanam ।।

snātvā tatrārcayed gaurīṃ yathā vibhavavistaraiḥ ।
mātaṅgasyāśrama tadvat siddhagandharvasevitam ।।

śuklakṛṣṇātṛtīyāyāṃ gandhadhūpavilepanaiḥ ।
upahārair anekaiś ca dīpamālāprabodhanaiḥ ।।

tatra yā pūjayen nārī gaurīṃ bhaktisamanvitā ।
rūpasaubhāgyasampannaṃ labhate satpatiṃ tu sā ।।

kārttikyāṃ tu gataprāṇā modamānā tu saṃyatā ।
asya tīrthasya māhātmyāt prāptā māheśvaraṃ puram ।।

mātaṅgo nāma devarṣiḥ purākalpe yudhiṣṭhira ।
narmadātīramāśritya tapas tepe suduṣkaram ।।

purā janmaniṣādaḥ sa jātiṃ smarati pūrvikām ।
aghamarṣaṇadeśasthaḥ sarvadharma bubodha ca ।।

maharṣīṇāṃ prasaṅgena narmadādarśanena ca ।
pāpabuddhiṃ parityajya dharmabuddhiṃ cakāra saḥ ।।

nirviṇṇo ahaṃ ca bhikṣuś cādhunā śvapacayoniṣu ।
evam uktvā tato rājann aśokavanikāṃ gataḥ ।।

jaṭāvalkaladhārī ca kandamūlaphalāśanaḥ ।
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu śivārādhanatatparaḥ ।।

śivadhyānaparaḥ so abhūd ugre tapasi saṃsthitaḥ ।
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ hi tathā tasya tapasyataḥ ।।

ekāśītisahasrāṇi jaṭāgrebhyo viniḥsmṛtāḥ ।
svayaṃ patanti vividhā narmadātoyam adhyataḥ ।।

tatkṣaṇād yakṣiṇīrūpā anantāś cāpramāṇikāḥ ।
śyāmavarṇāḥ sutejaḥ kāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।।

yakṣalokaṃ vrajanty āśu tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।
mantrayantravihīno api śivabhaktiparāyaṇaḥ ।।

ṣaḍakṣaram imaṃ mantraṃ hṛdi cakre divāniśam ।
oṃnamaḥ śivāya iti sarvamantrottamottamam ।।

tasya bhaktiṃ parāṃ jñātvā devadeva umāpatiḥ ।
pratyakṣarūpo bhagavān chūlapāṇiḥ samāgataḥ ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ devo mātaṅgaṃ prati bhārata ।
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te dhyānenānena suvrata ।।

mātaṅga uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo asi deveśa varaṃ dātum ihecchasi ।
mātaṅganāmnā vikhyātiṃ tīrtham etat prayātu vai ।।

cāṇḍālāḥ śvapacāś caiva pāpayonigatā api ।
japādi rahitāś cāpi mucyante atrāpi kilbiṣāt ।।

mātaṅganāmaliṅgaṃ tu narmadātīram āśritam ।
snātvā yo atrārcayet tasya bhaved bandhavimokṣaṇam ।।

idaṃ varam ahaṃ manye tvatprasādāt maheśvara ।
tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā praty uvāca śivāpatiḥ ।।

evam bhavatu tatsarvaṃ matprasādān na saṃśaya ।
evam uktvā yayau deva kailāsaṃ parvatottamam ।।

varaṃ samprāpya mātaṅga umāmāheśvaraṃ puram ।
kāmikaṃ yānam ārūḍhaḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣita ।।

jagāmāśu ciraṃ bhoktuṃ bhogān snānaprabhāvataḥ ।
yā caitramāse amāvāsyā kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśī ।।

tasyāṃ tatra hutaṃ dattam anantaphalam aśnute ।
tilodakapradānena pāpayonigatā api ।।

saktvāḍhyaguḍapiṇḍena pitṝn modayate tu yaḥ ।
pitarastasya tṛpyanti yāvadindrāś caturdaśa ।।

tilataṇḍulamiśraṃ yaḥ kuryāl liṅgasya pūjanam ।
so api varṣasahasrāṇi śivaloke mahīyate ।।

aśokavanikā nāma mātaṅgaṃ tīrtham ucyate ।
revāyā uttare kūle kathitaṃ tava bhārata ।।

athānyat kathayiṣyāmi yāmyabhāge vyavasthitam ।
tīrthaṃ mṛgavanaṃ nāma sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।।

tatra snātvā arcayed viṣṇuṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।
ekādaśyāṃ mahārāja nirāhāro niśāṃ nayet ।।

hariṃ mṛgavane tatra gandhapuṣpaiś ca pūjayet ।
ekasmin bhojite vipre lakṣaṃ bhavatu bhojitam ।।

tilodakapradānena pitṝṇāṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।
tatraiva sanniviṣṭaṃ tu vārāhaṃ tīrthamuttamam ।।

yatra vārāharūpeṇa dharā caiva samuddhṛtā ।
viśvarūpaṃ tathā cānyaddhariṇāmitatejasā ।।

pativratā ca nārī vai tathā māsopavāsinī ।
tatra snātvā vidhānena lokaṃ prāpnoti vaiṣṇavam ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe mātaṅgāśramavarṇano nāma ṣaṭpañcāśattamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ākhyānaṃ kathayiṣyāmi khyātaṃ mṛgavanaṃ yathā ।
vyādha kaścid durācāraḥ sarvabhūteṣu nirdayaḥ ।।

pāśahasto dhanuṣpāṇir vicaran girikandare ।
ājaghāna mṛgān sarvān kuṭumbārthe nṛpottama ।।

jyeṣṭhe māsi tu saṃprāpte nidāghe jvalanaprabhe ।
bhramati sma tṛṣārtaś ca vṛkṣamūle samāśritaḥ ।।

rātrau svapiti niśceṣṭo duḥkhārtaś ca kṣudhānvitaḥ ।
vanasaṃgharṣajo vahnir utthito girikandarāt ।।

pradagdhaṃ ca vana tena mṛgavyāghrasamāvṛtam ।
bhasmībhūtaṃ ca tatsarvaṃ reṇubhūtaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥ ।।

meghāgamoktakāle tu pravāhe nārmade śubhe ।
kanyārāśigate bhānau dvādaśyāṃ śravaṇena tu ।।

narmadātoya saṃsargād yakṣā jātās tu pannagāḥ ।
tatkṣaṇād divyadehās tu vaiṣṇavaṃ yānamāsthitāḥ ।।

sa vyādhaś cābhavad rājā tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi bhogān bhuṅkte manoharān ।।

ye api dagdhā mṛgās tatra te api gandharvatāṃ gatāḥ ।
vaiṣṇavenaiva yānena prāptās tu vaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।।

avaśaḥ svavaśo vāpi yas tu prāṇān parityajet ।
divyavarṣasahasraṃ tu viṣṇuloke sa modate ।।

tilodakapradānena pitṝṇāṃ paramā gatiḥ ।
manorathaṃ nāma tīrtham anyat paramasiddhidam ।।

triṣu lokeṣu vikhyātaṃ revātīrasamudbhavam ।
yaṃ yaṃ prārthayate kāmaṃ taṃ taṃ snātvāpi mānavaḥ ।।

sarva ca samavāpnoti tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।
aṅgarāvartasaṃbhedo gosahasraphalapradaḥ ।।

aṅgāreśvaradevaś ca tatra tiṣṭhati saṅgame ।
snānamātro naras tatra gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt ।।

aṅgāraś ca caturthyāṃ ca yadā bhavati bhārata ।
hiraṇyapuruṣaṃ kṛtvā raktavastreṇa veṣṭayet ।।

ghṛtapūrṇaṃ tāmrapātraṃ guḍenāpi prapūritam ।
tatsarvaṃ vidhivad dadyāc chrotriyāya viśeṣataḥ ।।

dānatīrthaprabhāveṇa śakrārddhāsanabhāg bhavet ।
yasmāt pāpāni duḥkhāni tīvrāṇy api bahūnyapi ।।

tasmāt pāpaṃ na kartavyam ātmapīḍākaraṃ hi tat ।
yasmin kāle ca deśe ca vayasā yādṛśena ca ।।

kṛtaṃ śubhāśūbhaṃ karma tat tathā tena bhujyate ।
tasmāt sadaiva dātavyam avicchinna tayārthine ।।

vicchidyante anyathā bhogā grīṣme kusarito yathā ।
saṃsevyate yathā devī saptakalpavahā śubhā ।।

saṃsārasya samucchittyai jñānayogaṃ bravīmi te ।
śivaprakāśakaṃ jñānaṃ yogas tatraiva cintitaḥ ।।

durvijñeya gatir yogo narmadāśivasannidhau ।
śivājñā vartate tatra snānapūjāvidhir yathā ।।

sa siddhāntā avirodhena pustakair na virodhayet ।
dharmajñānāpavargārthaṃ sahitaṃ vindate naraḥ ।।

pūrvottaravirodhena kutrārtho abhimato bhavet ।
dṛṣṭvādyamūlatas tarkaṃ śrutyā saha vivarjayet ।।

tasmād āgamayuktena sadātmārthavicāraṇam ।
kartavyaṃ nānumānena kevalena vipaścitā ।।

hīnottamādyasya phalaṃ bahudhā svaṃ ca tatsmṛtam ।
tasmāt parīkṣāṃ kurvīta puṇyaṃ sādhu mahatphalam ।।

pākhaṇḍino vikarmasthān vaiḍālavratikāṃ śaṭhān ।
varjayed dūrato dhīmān haitukyān tīrthanindakān ।।

digambarān śvetapaṭān ye cānye hetuvādinaḥ ।
etaiḥ saha na saṃvādaṃ saṃsargaṃ na kathaṃcana ।।

viparītaṃ kalau dharmaṃ nagnā muṇḍā malāśinaḥ ।
tasmāt taṃ ca parityajya tretādharmaṃ samācaret ।।

pramāṇaṃ sarvadharmeṣu brahmaviṣṇuśivoditam ।
anyathā kurute yas tu narake patati dhruvam ।।

sarveṣām eva śāstrāṇām evaṃ śāstraviniścayaḥ ।
sevyatāṃ kalpagā devī śivapūjārataiḥ sadā ।।

pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ kuryād bhikṣāṃ dadyāc ca bhikṣave ।
kāruṇyaṃ sarvabhūteṣu narmadākhyānacintanam ।।

idaṃ jñānamaśeṣaṃ ca sarvakarmaviśodhanam ।
ādimadhyāntarahitaḥ svabhāvavimalaḥ prabhuḥ ।।

sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaś ca śivo jñeyaḥ śivāgame ।
sarvārthasādhakaṃ jñānaṃ tatpraṇītam asaṃśayam ।।

yaḥ sarvajñaḥ susampūrṇaḥ svabhāvavimalaḥ śivaḥ ।
sarvadoṣavinirmuktaḥ sa brūyāt katham anyathā ।।

śivājñām antareṇāpi jagatsṛṣṭiḥ katham bhavet ।
acaitanyāt pradhānena ajñatvāt puruṣasya ca ।।

pradhānaṃ paramāṇvādi yāvat kiṃcid acetanam ।
tanna kartṛ svayaṃ draṣṭṛ buddhimatkaraṇaṃ vinā ।।

na yathā ghaṭam ānena mṛtpiṇḍaḥ svayam ṛcchati ।
tathājñābuddhibhāvena na tiṣṭhet prakṛtiḥ svayam ।।

dharmādharmopadeśo na dharmādharmavicāraṇam ।
sarvajñena vinā jātu nādisarge prasiddhyati ।।

yathānādi pravṛtto ayaṃ ghoraḥ saṃsārasāgaraḥ ।
śivo api hi tathānādiḥ saṃsārān mocakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

vyādhīnāṃ bhaiṣajaṃ yadvat pratipakṣaṃ svabhāvataḥ ।
tadvatsaṃsāraghorāṇāṃ pratipakṣaḥ śivaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

vaidyaṃ vinā nirākrandāḥ kliśyante rogiṇo yathā ।
śivena tu vinā sarvaṃ nirākrandaṃ jagat tathā ।।

tasmād anādiḥ sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ ।
asti nātaḥ paritrātā pumān saṃsārasāgare ।।

ye abhyasanti śivajñānaṃ hṛdaye śivabhāvitāḥ ।
yadi vedāḥ pramāṇaṃ tu teṣāṃ jñānaṃ prajāyate ।।

iyaṃ ca sarvabhūtānāṃ śaraṇaṃ bhuvi narmadā ।
apāṃ rūpatayā devī lokānugrahakāriṇī ।।

sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ caiva bhūtagrāmaṃ caturvidham ।
bhagavaty uddharaty eṣāṃ patantaṃ narake dhruvam ।।

evaṃjñātvā naraśreṣṭha śivam anvīkṣya kalpagām ।
uccairgṛhāṇi divyāni dhanadhānyānvitāni ca ।।

sarvopaskaradivyāni brāhmaṇebhyo nivedayet ।
anāthāyātivṛddhāya vikalāya kuṭumbine ।।

kāṣṭhamṛnmayagehaṃ ca yo dvijāya prayacchati ।
evaṃ vidhān gṛhān ramyān sarvato amarakaṇṭake ।।

kārayed yaḥ pumān divyāṃs tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ।
kiṃ tasya bahubhir dattair dānair bhavati bhārata ।।

etad eva paraṃ dānaṃ sarvakāmārthasādhakam ।
yaḥ śṛṇoti naro bhaktyā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye saptapañcāśattamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
śrutvaitat paramaṃ guhyaṃ gavāṃ devasam udbhavam ।
brahmakūrcasya māhātmyaṃ śrotum icchāmi tattvataḥ ।।

ākhyāhi bhagavan sarvaṃ golokaḥ kīdṛśaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
prāpyate karmaṇā kena ke tasminn aniśaṃ sthitāḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śrūyatām abhidhāsyāmi namaskṛtya maheśvaram ।
gomātṛlokaṃ paramaṃ sarvakām asamanvitam ।।

yathāvat sarvalokānām uparyupari saṃsthitam ।
pātālāni tataḥ sapta pātālaṃ ca tatas tathā ।।

yāvat pramāṇaṃ paritaḥ paricchinnaṃ mahītalam ।
tāvat pramāṇaṃ tasyāḥ samudrās tāni caiva tu ।।

teṣāṃ pratyekam utsedhapramāṇaṃ parikīrtitam ।
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśārdhāni tatas tataḥ ।।

sahasrayojanotsedhas tasyābhyantaratas tathā ।
vivarāṇāṃ samastānāṃ sahasrāṇi nava smṛtam ।।

teṣāṃ ruciramāhātmyaṃ nāmatas tu mahītale ।
divyadivyopasampannaḥ śrīmaccāmīkaradyutiḥ ।।

nāgarājaḥ sadaivāste tasmin kṛtaniketanaḥ ।
ananto anantadhāmā ca mukundo nṛpaśaivalaḥ ।।

tato rasātalaṃ nāma śivasantoṣabhūmikam ।
vāsuker nāgarājasya tatra cāru mahāpuram ।।

pura ca suralomnas tu dānavādhipater mahat ।
suparṇasya ca daityānām aśeṣāṇāṃ mahātmanām ।।

tataḥ sutalanāmāsti śarkarāñcitabhūmikam ।
nāgādīnāṃ svastikānāṃ tatraiva vasatiḥ sadā ।।

dānavādhipatīnāṃ ca tatraiva nilayaḥ paraḥ ।
vairocanahiraṇyākhyaprabhṛtīnāṃ mahātmanām ।।

tataścātalam ityuktaṃ pātālānāṃ tasya tu vai ।
teṣām ūrdhvavastusarveṣāṃ mṛnmayaṃ ca talaṃ kṣiteḥ ।।

asurādhipates tāvat kālanemermahāpuram ।
cārucāmīkarābhāsaṃ vainateyasya cāparam ।।

tataś ca vitalaṃ nāma pātālaṃ raktabhūtalam ।
tasmin mahāntako nāma dānavendrakṛtālayaḥ ।।

tālako agnimukhas tasmin nalahrādaś ca dānavāḥ ।
nivasanti kṛtāgārās tathā prahlādavarcasaḥ ।।

pātālaṃ vitalaṃ nāma śuklaṃ kṣititalaṃ tataḥ ।
kambalāśvatarau nāgau sahitau tatra tiṣṭhataḥ ।।

mahājambhahayagrīvaprabhṛtīnāṃ mahātmanām ।
vārāṇasyasurendrāṇāṃ nivāsas tatrakalpitaḥ ।।

kṛṣṇaṃ kṣititalaṃ tasmāt pātālatalasaṃjñakam ।
śaṅkukarṇamahānādanamucīnāṃ niketanam ।।

pātālāt saptamād ūrdhvaṃ saptadvīpā mahī sthitā ।
samudraiḥ saptabhir yuktā parvataiḥ samalaṃkṛtā ।।
jambūdvīpaś ca tan madhye plakṣadvīpas tataḥ paraḥ ।।
krauñcadvīpaś ca parataḥ śākadvīpaś ca tadbahiḥ ।
parataḥ puṣkaradvīpaḥ saptamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।

kṣārodakaś cekṣurasaḥ surodaś ca ghṛtodadhiḥ ।
dadhitoyaḥ kṣīrapūrṇaḥ svādūdaḥ saptamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

saptadvīpasamudrāṇāṃ dviguṇadviguṇāntaraḥ ।
pramāṇavistaro jñeyo niyutaḥ prathamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

himavān hemakūṭaś ca niṣadhaś ceti dakṣiṇe ।
nīlaś ca śvetaḥ śṛṅgaś ca meroruttarataḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

merur asti sthito madhye jambūdvīpasya bhārata ।
mālyavān pūrvato jñeyaḥ paścime gandhamādanaḥ ।।

ete parvatarājāno jambūdvīpe nava smṛtāḥ ।
plakṣadvīpādiṣu jñeyāḥ saptasaptaiva parvatāḥ ।।

puṣkaradvīpamadhye tu parvato valayākṛtiḥ ।
ekaḥ smṛtaḥ samantāc ca nāmato mānasaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

vindhyo nāma mahābhāgo jambūdvīpe vyavasthitaḥ ।
yatraiṣā narmadādevī plavantī lokatāriṇī ।।

vindhyasya cānujo bhrātā sahyo dakṣiṇataḥ smṛtaḥ ।
urvī kūrmatalākārā kāñcanī parimaṇḍalā ।।

aṇureva tathā sā tu nirdiṣṭātividaḥ kṣitiḥ ।
tasyāḥ pramāṇaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ daśayojanakoṭayaḥ ।।

lokāloka iti khyātas tasyāḥ prānte samantataḥ ।
sphīto hemamayaḥ śrīmān saralaḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ ।।

yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi cārdhamasya vyavasthitam ।
tāvadeva ca vistīrṇaṃ tadardhe bhānurāhitaḥ ।।

prakāśayati sa jyotiḥ parabhāge nihanyate ।
lokāloka iti proktas tato asāvacalo mahān ।।

lokālokāvasāno ayaṃ bhūrlokaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।
gandharvayakṣarakṣobhiḥ piśācaiś ca niṣevitaḥ ।।

mānuṣaiḥ paśubhiś caiva mṛgapakṣisarīsṛpaiḥ ।
sthāvarairvividhākārair bhūtair etaiś ca ṣaḍvidhaiḥ ।।

bhūrlokaś ca bhuvarloko yāvad ādityamaṇḍalam ।
vasanti satataṃ rudrās satataṃ vaktrabhāskarāḥ ।।

ādityamaṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ smṛtā svarlokasaṃsthitiḥ ।
vimānakoṭayas tasminn aṣṭāviṃśatirāśayaḥ ।।

meḍhībhūto vimānānāṃ sarveṣām upari dhruvaḥ ।
niyutā anilaskandhāḥ saptāsminn antare sthitāḥ ।।

pṛthivyāḥ prathamaḥ skandhaḥ sthitaś cāmeghamaṇḍalam ।
āhavo nāma vai vāto vyūhānāṃ vyūhakṛt tathā ।।

dvitīyaḥ pravaho nāma nibaddhaḥ sūryamaṇḍale ।
tṛtīyaḥ saṃvaho māma suskandho asau pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।।

caturthaḥ sodvahaḥ skandhaḥ sthito nakṣatramaṇḍale ।
tato dvayor vinirdiṣṭā vimānodvahanakriyā ।।

yojanānāṃ dhruvaḥ koṭir maharlokaḥ samucchritaḥ ।
skandhaḥ parivaho nāma nibaddhaḥ saptamo dhruve ।।

annādīni karoty eṣa parvaṇām upari sthitaḥ ।
vinirvṛttaṃ vikārāṇām adhivāso mahātmanām ।।

tatrādhikāridevānām aṣṭāviṃśati koṭayaḥ ।
janāt svarlokam āgatya niyogāt padmajanmanaḥ ।।

sthitā manvantaraṃ tatra svavyāpārāvasāyinaḥ ।
āruhya ca maharlokam āgacchanti tataḥ punaḥ ।।

brahmaṇo divasaikena devāḥ svarge caturdaśa ।
krameṇa kṛtvā karmāṇi maharloke vasanti te ।।

koṭidvayaṃ maharlokāj janalokaḥ samucchritaḥ ।
sādhyānām asurās tatra vasanti sukhinaḥ sadā ।।

yojanānāṃ catuḥkoṭyaḥ janād apy ucchritaṃ tapaḥ ।
prajānāṃ patayas tatra sthitās tu brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ।।

satyalokas tapolokāt koṭiṣaṭkaṃ samucchritam ।
āste parivṛtas tatra devāsuragaṇair virāṭ ।।

brahmalokād viṣṇuloko dviguṇena samucchritaḥ ।
vistareṇa tadūrdhve ca divyalokaḥ samanvitaḥ ।।

viṣṇulokāc ca parataḥ śrīmac chivapuraṃ mahat ।
dvāviṃśat koṭivistīrṇaṃ tadūrdhve samupasthitam ।।

sūryāyutapratīkāśaṃ sarvakāmasamanvitam ।
anekāraṇyavinyāsaṃ svarganadyupaśobhitam ।।

sarvaratnānvitair divyais taptajāmbūnadaprabhaiḥ ।
sahasrakhaṇḍabhaumaiś ca sarvaśobhāsamanvitaiḥ ।।

vimānaiḥ sarvato vyāptaṃ candrair ivanabhastalam ।
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ sarvavidyādharānvitam ।।

nṛtyagītaravopetair aprameyaguṇānvitaiḥ ।
manojavair asaṃkhyātaiḥ parivārasamanvitaiḥ ।।

kvacid dolāgṛhair ramyaiḥ kiṅkiṇīr avakānvitaiḥ ।
udgatair ardhacandraiś ca ghaṇṭābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ ।।

maṇimuktāvitānaiś ca maṇiratnacayaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।
sarvaratnārcitair dravyair muktādāmasuśobhanaiḥ ।।

mahāsiṃhāsanair divyaiḥ sarvaratnavibhūṣitaiḥ ।
kvacit puṇyagṛhair vyāptam asaṃkhyaguṇānvitaiḥ ।।

sadā puṣpaphalair vṛkṣaiḥ kvacid vyāptaṃ manoramaiḥ ।
puṣpodyānair mahāramyaiḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।।

saptakalpavahā puṇyā tatraivāste saridvarā ।
tatkalāyāḥ sahasrāṃśo jambūdvīpe pradṛśyate ।।

avatīrṇā mahīpṛṣṭhe lokānugrahakāmyayā ।
sarvātmanā avatāraś ca gaṅgādisaritām iha ।।

amṛtasyandinībhiś ca nadībhir upaśobhitam ।
hemaratnāñcitā vāpyaḥ sopānaiḥ sphāṭikair yutāḥ ।।

sitaraktāsitaiḥ pītaiḥ sarojairyāḥ sugandhibhiḥ ।
pañcavarṇaiś ca gurubhiḥ śobhitāḥ kāñcanākulaiḥ ।।

mahāvikāśi saṃsnigdhaiḥ śrīmadbhiḥ pañcahastakaiḥ ।
daśa dvādaśahastaiś ca tathā viṃśatihastakaiḥ ।।

nālair marakataprakhyair manoharadalānvitaiḥ ।
pūrṇanīlotpalaiś cānyair dīrghikāś ca kvacit kvacit ।।

siṃhavyāghramukhair divyair gajavājimṛgānanaiḥ ।
gomukhaiś chāgavadanaiḥ kapipakṣimukhais tathā ।।

ekavaktrair mahāvaktrair bahuvaktrair avaktrakaiḥ ।
ekapādais tripādaiś ca bahupādair apādakaiḥ ।।

vāmanair jaṭilair muṇḍair dīrghagrīvair mahodaraiḥ ।
mahākāyair mahānāsair mahākarṇair akarṇakaiḥ ।।

nānārūpākṛtidharair nānābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ ।
nānāveṣadharair divyaiḥ kāmarūpair mahābalaiḥ ।।

nānāprabhāvasaṃyuktair nānāśāstraviśāradaiḥ ।
asaṃkhyā jātayaś cānyā nivasanti tathā vidhāḥ ।।

kubjāvāmanakādīrghā varadehā varānanāḥ ।
muṇḍāś ca vikaṭā nīcā hrasvadīrghaś ca tādṛśāḥ ।।

lambodarā hrasvabhujā vinatā hrasvajānukāḥ ।
mṛgendravadanāś cānyā gajavājimukhās tathā ।।

hrasvakuñcitakeśāś ca sundarapriyadarśanāḥ ।
pañcāśatkoṭayas tatra śivasya paricārikāḥ ।।

maṇimāṇikyageheṣu ramante tā bahiḥ kvacit ।
tatra geheṣu yad dvārisahasraśatabhūmiṣu ।।

vicitrabhūmayas tatra vajravaidūryabhūṣitāḥ ।
iti sarvaguṇopetaiḥ strīsahasrair varānanaiḥ ।।

asaṃkhyātaiḥ puraṃ vyāptam īśvarasya samantataḥ ।
tan madhye sarvatobhadraṃ divyamāyatanaṃ mahat ।।

śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ sthānam ādyam umāpateḥ ।
tatrāste bhagavān somaḥ pūjyamāno gaṇeśvaraiḥ ।।

siddhaiḥ svasthānasaṃprāptair brahmaviṣṇvādibhis tathā ।
dharmas tatra sthitaḥ śrīmānīśvarāyatane anagha ।।

yatra vīravṛṣaḥ tatra nityaṃ gomātaraḥ sthitāḥ ।
tatra sā narmadādevī pūjyamānā surāsuraiḥ ।।

tenodakena tṛpyanti govatsāḥ sarvadevatāḥ ।
brahmāviṣṇuḥ sureśāna umayā sahito anagha ।।

surāś ca ṛṣayo bhūtāḥ pitaro mātaras tathā ।
sa lokaḥ śivaloko atra narmadāloka eva ca ।।

ye guṇā rudralokasya golokasya tathaiva ca ।
nandā bhadrā subhadrā ca suśīlā surabhis tathā ।।

iti gomātaraḥ pañca śivalokavinirgatāḥ ।
ṣaṣṭhī tu narmadādevī lokānugrahakāmyayā ।।

etāḥ sarvā jagatsarvaṃ sarvalokasya mātaraḥ ।
tarpayanti mahārāja nityam atrātmikair guṇaiḥ ।।

kāraṇāc ca śivasthānād īśvarecchāvaśā anugā ।
oṃkārāt sarvalokānām imaṃ lokaṃ samāśritāḥ ।।

tṛṇāni khādanti caranty araṇye pibanti toyāni sunirmalāni ।
dugdhaṃ prayacchanti punanti dehaṃ gāvo yato jīvati jīvalokaḥ ।।

kutas teṣāṃ hi pāpāni yeṣāṃ gṛhamalaṃkṛtam ।
satataṃ bālavatsābhir gobhiḥ strībhiriva svayam ।।

ye smaranti sadoṃkāraṃ narmadāṃ ca śivātmanā ।
na teṣāṃ punarāvṛttirghore saṃsārasāgare ।।

ye kurvanti parāṃ bhaktiṃ tṛṇatoyapradānataḥ ।
prasādāt tu gavāṃ tāsāṃ śivalokaṃ vrajanti te ।।

etāḥ sadānukūlena mātaraḥ sarvakāmadāḥ ।
ye rakṣanti śubhā gāś ca śivalokaṃ vrajanti te ।।

ye arcayanti śivaṃ bhaktyā sadvidhānaiḥ samāhitāḥ ।
te vindanti mahābhogān puraṃ yānti śivasya vai ।।

ye śivāśrayatīrthāni śraddhayā yānti mānavāḥ ।
kalpagāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa śailaṃ cāmarakaṇṭakam ।।

te krīḍanti mahābhogair brahmaviṣṇuśivālaye ।
payo amṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ madhudadhyādikaṃ tu yat ।।

na paśyati mahābhāga kalpagāyāṃ vimohitaḥ ।
etatte kathitaṃ rājan revāvataraṇaṃ śubham ।।

asyākhyānena bhagavān । prīyatāṃ me śivaḥ svayam ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe śivalokavarṇano nāmāṣṭapañcāśattamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
dānadharmavidhānaṃ ca śrotum icchāmi kalpaga ।
daridrā bhikṣavo vāpi kathaṃ yānti śivālayam ।।

vidhinā kena dānena mucyate duṣkṛtaṃ tathā ।
lokānāṃ ca hitārthāya kathayasva mahāmune ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājan yathā nyāyaṃ kathayāmi tavānagha ।
puṣkaraṃ bilvapatraṃ ca kuśāstoyaṃ ca nārmadam ।।

svayambhūr bhagavān āha sāmānyaṃ dharmakāraṇam ।
śraddhāpūtāḥ sarvadharmāḥ purāṇaṃ śrutayas tathā ।।

tasyopadeśadharmeṇa narā yānti triviṣṭapam ।
yas tūlapūrṇavistīrṇaṃ raktavastraṃ sasūtrakam ।।

vyāghracarmakṛtaṃ vāpi navavastrāvaguṇṭhitam ।
kṛṣṇājinopavītaṃ ca puṇyadhūpādhivāsitam ।।

śivadhyānābhiyuktāya śraddhayā vinivedayet ।
tat tūlavastratantūnāṃ romasaṃkhyāsti yāvatī ।।

tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi śivaloke mahīyate ।
modate sarvalokeṣu bhuktvā bhogān anekaśaḥ ।।

punaś ca kṣitimāsādya siṃhāsanapatir bhavet ।
tṛṇavalkalaparṇāni śayyā prāvaraṇādikam ।।

dattvā tadarthine bhūmau śivaloke mahīyate ।
śivamuddiśya naivedyaṃ yo dadyāc chivadarśine ।।

śākaṃ mūlaṃ phalaṃ vāpi tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ।
yāvat syāt taṇḍulādīnāṃ saṃkhyāphaladaleṣu ca ।।

tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi śivaloke mahīyate ।
bhikṣāṃ savyañjanāṃ dattvā śivabhaktāya bhaktitaḥ ।।

varṣalakṣaṃ mahābhāga śivaloke mahīyate ।
dadhibhaktaṃ susampūrṇaṃ bhikṣāpātraṃ suśobhanam ।।

dadyād yaḥ śivabhaktāya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ।
varṣakoṭisamaṃ divyaṃ mahābhogaiḥ samanvitam ।।

sthitvā śivapure divye tasyānte ca mahīpatiḥ ।
suśītalena toyena śivabhaktaṃ sitāyujā ।।

tarpayitvā śambhuloke varṣalakṣaṃ ca modate ।
kalaśaṃ śarkaropetaṃ vastrapūtāmbupūritam ।।

dadyād yaḥ śivabhaktāya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ।
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ vimānaṃ sarvakāmikam ।।

saṃprāpya śivaloke tu varṣakoṭiṃ sa modate ।
palāśaparṇaiḥ patrair vā yaḥ kuryāt puṭakāni tu ।।

pradadyācchivayogibhyas tāmrapātraprado hi saḥ ।
yas tāmrapātraṃ sukṛtaṃ pradadyāc chivayogine ।।

koṭiṣaṭ kaṃ sa kalpānāṃ śivaloke mahīyate ।
śūlaṃ vahati yaḥ pāṇau śaktiṃ pṛṣṭhe kamaṇḍalum ।।

taṃ bhojayitvā yatnena śivalokam avāpnuyāt ।
bhojayec ca yathā śaktyā yaḥ śivavratacāriṇam ।।

bhogaiḥ sa krīḍati śreṣṭhaiḥ śivaloke vyavasthitaḥ ।
yaḥ śivāśramadharmaṃ ca gṛhasthaṃ bhojayed budhaḥ ।।

vipulaiḥ sa mahābhogaiḥ śivaloke mahīyate ।
śivāśramavratasthaṃ yaḥ kandādyair bhojayet naraḥ ।।

sa divyānāpnuyād bhogān īśvarasya pure sthitaḥ ।
evaṃ pāśupataṃ bhaktaṃ bhojayitvā praṇamya ca ।।

nānāvidhair mahābhogaiḥ śivaloke mahīyate ।
mahāvratadharāyaiva bhikṣāṃ yaḥ pratipādayet ।।

sa divyaiḥ śobhanair bhogaiḥ śivaloke mahīyate ।
sayamaniyam ācāraṃ śivabhaktiparaṃ naram ।।

bhojayitvā yathāśaktyā śivaloke mahīyate ।
jñānayogabahiḥsthā ye lokasāmānyadharmiṇaḥ ।।

pūjayanti śivaṃ bhaktyā śivalokaṃ vrajanti te ।
anāśikenāpi karīṣavahṇinā payaḥ pradānena tapobhir ugraiḥ ।।

prayānti yajñaiś ca na tāṃ gatiṃ narā ।
nīco api yāṃ yāti hi rudrabhaktaḥ ।।

yathā revājalasparśāl labhante sadgatiṃ narāḥ ।
na tathā yajñadānādyair upāyair bharatarṣabha ।।

ity eṣa śivalokas tu prasaṅgāt samudāhṛtaḥ ।
golokaḥ kalpagālokaḥ śivabhaktaiḥ samanvitaḥ ।।

jñānayogena ye śāntā japanti paramaṃ śivam ।
te sarvaduḥkhanirmuktā bhavanti sukhinaḥ sadā ।।

śivalokaś ca vijñeyo maṇḍalāvaraṇātmakaḥ ।
pañcabhūtānyahaṃkāraḥ sattvaṃ prakṛtiraṣṭamī ।।

īdṛśānāṃ tu nāgānāṃ koṭyo jñeyāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।
sarvāṅgatvāt pradhānasya tiryagūrdhvamadhaḥ sthitam ।।

viṣṇulokāt paraṃ sthānaṃ kumārasya mahātmanaḥ ।
svacchamauktikasaṃkāśaṃ paramā śrīsamanvitam ।।

skandalokāt paraṃ sthānam umādevyāḥ prakīrtitam ।
taptacāmīkaraprakhyam aśeṣaguṇasaṃyutam ।।

umāsthānāt paraṃ caiva harasthānaṃ taduttamam ।
sūryakoṭipratīkāśaṃ sarvakām asamanvitam ।।

gaṇair adhyuṣitaṃ sarvair asaṃkhyair yogatatparaiḥ ।
hiraṇyagarbhakūrmādyair vasurudradivākaraiḥ ।।

stūyate bhagavān nityaṃ tasyānti pratikāṅkṣibhiḥ ।
jñānadhyānaparaiḥ śāntair bhikṣāhārair jitendriyaiḥ ।।

prāpyaṃ taiś ca paraṃ sthānaṃ sūryāyutasamaprabham ।
tatsatkarmakarair nityaṃ brāhmaṇair dagdhakalmaṣaiḥ ।।

vasanti yadṛtaṃ siddhāśayās tu kleśavarjitāḥ ।
narmadā sevyamānāś ca labhante tatpadaṃ narāḥ ।।

etat te kathitaṃ pārtha yathoddiṣṭaṃ tu śambhunā ।
yan mayā kathitaṃ dānaṃ narmadātīram āśritam ।।

gacchanti ye anyat tīrthaṃ tu sahasrāṃśo viśiṣyate ।
sarvajñāḥ sarvagāḥ śuddhāḥ paripūrṇā bhavanti te ।।

śuddhakarmakarā ye tu paramaiśvaryasaṃyutāḥ ।
sadehāś ca videhāś ca bhavanti svecchayā punaḥ ।।

iti nityaṃ viśuddhaṃ ca sthānam ādyam umāpateḥ ।
divyaṃ śrīkaṇṭhanāthasya jagadbhartuḥ samaṃsthitam ।।

sthānaṃ navakamity evaṃ nirgatā yatra kalpagā ।
paramāṣṭaguṇaiśvaryanityam akṣayam avyayam ।।

śaśvadgurupraṇītena dhyānayogena ye narāḥ ।
dhyāyanti devatāṃ nityaṃ te siddhā yānti tatpadam ।।

ye abhyasanti śivajñānaṃ narmadātīram āśritāḥ ।
kāmatṛṣṇāvinirmuktās te api yānti ca tatpuram ।।

apy ekadivasaṃ yāvac chivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ।
śivadharmaparas tasya dharmasyānto na vidyate ।।

yogadharmasu sāratvādabhedyaṃ pāpamudgaraiḥ ।
vajrataṇḍulavaj jñeyaṃ tasmāt tasya phalaṃ mahat ।।

dehāntenaiva dharmeṇa sthānamādyaṃ śivālayam ।
yatrāste vipulair bhogaiḥ krīḍan kalpāyutaṃ naraḥ ।।

tataḥ kalpāyutasyānte sthānaṃ kaumāram āpnuyāt ।
tatrārdhasammitaṃ kālaṃ sa krīḍan sasukhaṃ vaset ।।

tadante viṣṇulokaṃ ca saṃprāpya vasate punaḥ ।
brahmalokaṃ gataś cānte tatrāpi vasate naraḥ ।।

brahmalokaparibhraṣṭo vasec chivapure sukham ।
tat tasmād brahmaviṣṇvādyāṃl lokān prāpnoty anukramāt ।।

ity evaṃ sarvalokeṣu ramitvā kramaśas tataḥ ।
manuṣyalokam āsādya śivaṃ revāṃ samāśrayet ।।

mayā te kathitā anyatra yāni dānāni bhārata ।
tāni sarve praśaṃsanti parvate amarakaṇṭake ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye śivamahimānuvarṇano nāmaikonaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
vaiṣṇavaṃ dānadharmaṃ ca kathyamānaṃ nibodha me ।
viṣṇuyogaṃ samabhyasya sarvakleśāpanuttaye ।।

viṣṇuṃ sampūjya vidhinā ghṛtasnānādibhiḥ stavaiḥ ।
dvādaśyāṃ viṣṇum uddiśya dadyād ekāṃ payasvinīm ।।

narmadātīram āsādya tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ।
pūjyate dharmarājena yathā viṣṇus tathaiva saḥ ।।

śaivānāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca sahasram bhojayet tu yaḥ ।
garbhiṇī dhenusaṃmiśraṃ vṛṣabhair daśabhiryutam ।।

arcitaṃ gandhapuṣpādyair hemavastrair alaṃkṛtam ।
pradakṣiṇam upākramya mantrarājaṃ ca bhaktitaḥ ।।

oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevayeti samuccaran ।
vedavidbhiḥ samākīrṇaṃ viṣṇor ārādhanaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।

narmadātoyam āsādya dīpamālāṃ prabodhayet ।
gāvo mamāgrato nityaṃ gāvaḥ pṛṣṭhata eva ca ।।

gāvo me hṛdaye vāpi gavāṃ madhye vasāmy aham ।
imaṃ mantraṃ samutthāya japed āsāṃ puro gavām ।।

gandhato yākṣatair miśrair gṛhītvā tāmrabhājanam ।
śṛṅgapuccha jalasnātaḥ śuklavastrasamanvitaḥ ।।

narmadāsnānapānena gavāṃ pucchāmbhasā tathā ।
sarvakalmaṣanirmuktaḥ susiddhaḥ suciravrataḥ ।।

snāpayitvā gatas tatra sa vipro narmadātaṭe ।
paurṇamāsyāṃ pūrṇacandre rāhusomasamāgame ।।

taireva sārddhaṃ viprendraiḥ saṃprapūjya hariṃ smaret ।
bhṛtyaputrakalatrād yair yuktaḥ svajanabāndhavaiḥ ।।

nivedayet tu kṛṣṇāya mantreṇa śraddhayānvitaḥ ।
śrāddhe dāne ca home ca vivāhe maṅgale tathā ।।

gomātaraḥ sthitā nityaṃ viṣṇuloke śivātmikāḥ ।
śivāyaitā mayā dattā viṣṇave ca mahātmane ।।

evaṃ viprāya yo dadyād yajñārthaṃ samalaṃkṛtāḥ ।
evaṃ nivedya puruṣo gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।।

kulāni triṃśaduttārya narakād bhṛtyabāndhavān ।
sthāpayed vaiṣṇave loke śivasya ca mahātmanaḥ ।।

sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaś ca viśuddhaḥ sarvagaḥ prabhuḥ ।
saṃsārasāgarān mukto haritulyaḥ prajāyate ।।

anenaiva vidhānena gṛhasthāḥ prāpnuyur divam ।
vināpi jñānayogena gosahasrapradānataḥ ।।

brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpi śūdro athāpi ca bhaktitaḥ ।
narmadākapilāyoge yathā vibhavavistaraiḥ ।।

brāhmaṇāya daridrāya dīkṣitāyopaśobhine ।
candrasūryoparāge tu vyatīpāte ca saṃkrame ।।

ṣaḍaśīti mukhe dadyād amāsomasamāgame ।
kārttikyā vā yugādau vā puṇye vāhani bhārata ।।

yaddhi gāyanti pitaro gāthām etāṃ narādhipa ।
api syāt sa kule asmākaṃ putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ ।।

narmadākapilāyoge koṭitīrthe ca muktide ।
narakād uddhared asmān dattvā gā yas tu saṃyutāḥ ।।

daśavarṣasahasrāṇi loke krīḍati vaiṣṇave ।
tasmāt tvam api rājendra gosahasraprado bhava ।।

devavad divi modante yena te pitaraḥ sadā ।
kathayāmi tavāthāhamitihāsaṃ purātanam ।।

yuvanāśvaḥ purā rājā cakravartī mahāyaśāḥ ।
śakrāc chatagaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ prajāpālanatatparaḥ ।।

ayodhyānagarī yasya brahmalokasamaprabhā ।
tasyā kṛtayuge cādau sarvadharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।।

bṛhaspatibrahmasamaṃ vaśiṣṭhaṃ svapurohitam ।
abhivādya yathānyāyam uvāca munisattamam ।।

kasmin sthāne yajed yajñaṃ tīrthe deśe surālaye ।
vaśiṣṭhapramukhāḥ sarve munayaś cedam abruvan ।।

pṛthivyāṃ naimiṣaṃ tīrthaṃ sarvatīrthamayaṃ śubham ।
saphalo hayamedhas tu koṭikoṭigaṇottaraḥ ।।

purāṇe kīrtitaṃ rājan matsyarūpeṇa viṣṇunā ।
sūryeṇa kīrtitaṃ rājan manuputrāya cātmanaḥ ।।

sarveṣāṃ tu purāṇānāṃ purāṇaṃ matsyakīrtitam ।
vedāścaiva purā naṣṭā matsyarūpeṇa coddhṛtāḥ ।।

vedahīnāś ca vartante dvijā vai yajñakarmasu ।
evaṃ vidhaṃ tu tat tīrthaṃ yuvanāśva tavoditam ।।

evaṃ śrutvā tato vākyaṃ vaśiṣṭhasya purodhasaḥ ।
ādideśa tato amātyān dharmiṣṭhān satyavādinaḥ ।।

yajñopaskaram ādāya samāgacchata satvaram ।
ghoṣaṇā kriyatāṃ rāṣṭre daṇḍahastaiś ca kiṅkaraiḥ ।।

āhūtās tu tato devā nṛpater yajñakarmaṇi ।
brahmā viṣṇuḥ sureśaś ca skando vaiśravaṇas tathā ।।

śambhuś caiva viśeṣeṇa surāsuranamaskṛtaḥ ।
dhenūnāṃ daśalakṣāṇi hemaratnānvitāni ca ।।

lakṣamekaṃ hayānāṃ ca dantinām ayutatrayam ।
maṇimāṇikyamuktāś ca hiraṇyaṃ cāpy anantakam ।।

nānāvidhāni dravyāṇi bhakṣyabhojyamalaṃkṛtam ।
yajñadravyaṃ ca yac cānyat tat sarvasahito nṛpaḥ ।।

nānāsahasrayānais tu nānādeśagatair nṛpaiḥ ।
nānāvādyasahasrais tu nānāgītair manoharaiḥ ।।

vedaghoṣeṇa mahatā divaṃ bhūmiṃ vinādayan ।
viveśa naimiṣaṃ tīrthaṃ yatra devo maheśvaraḥ ।।

hariṃ sadyaḥ prabhuṃ dṛṣṭvā mucyate yatra kilbiṣāt ।
svargasopānam etat tu pratyakṣaṃ devalokavat ।।

tatra snātvā abhyarcya hariṃ haraṃ svargam avāpnuyāt ।
kīrtanān naimiṣasyāsya naro dahati tatkṣaṇāt ।।

anekabhāvikaṃ ghoraṃ tūlarāśim ivānalaḥ ।
dīkṣitā brāhmaṇā devāḥ kutaścit tu samāgatāḥ ।।

ārtānām ayutaṃ tebhyo dadau devāya cānagha ।
sahasram ekaṃ nṛpatirbhūṣaṇānāṃ ca bhārata ।।

oṃ namaḥ śaṅkarāyeti mādhavāyeti cottamaḥ ।
jaladarbhau samādāya pātre rājā hiraṇmaye ।।

evaṃ saṃkalpya rājendra yajñavāṭam akārayat ।
daśayojanaparyantaṃ yajñayūpāś ca hemajān ।।

tato nirvartito yajño vaśiṣṭhapramukhair dvijaiḥ ।
muditā devatāḥ sarvā divyayānasamāśritāḥ ।।

jayaśabdaṃ pracakrus tā rājā nānyo bhavatsamaḥ ।
nānyo mama samaḥ kaścid ityahaṃkāravān nṛpaḥ ।।

yāvad yānaṃ samāruhya sāntaḥpuraparicchadaḥ ।
niḥsṛto naimiṣāraṇyāt tāvat paśyati vānaram ।।

tiṣṭha tiṣṭhety uvācātha śṛṇu rājan vaco mama ।
kiṃ te yajñavidhānena devatādānakarmaṇi ।।

ahaṃkāravimūḍhātmā kartāham iti manyase ।
purāmareśvare yajñe satyadharmasya bhūpateḥ ।।

varjayitvā mukham me abhūt kaṇṭhādho hemavarṇakam ।
ye gatāḥ śiśavas teṣāṃ sarvāṅgāś ca hiraṇmayāḥ ।।

kapilā narmadāyoge yajñatoyapravāhataḥ ।
snānāvagāhanāt pānāl loḍanāt kardame tathā ।।

gandharvalokaṃ samprāpto bhūtagrāmaś caturvidhaḥ ।
tvadīye lulitaṃ yajñe naimiṣāraṇyasambhave ।।

paṅkena liptaṃ gātraṃ me kṣālitaṃ cāmbunā tathā ।
na kiṃcit phalamāsīn me tava yajño nirarthakaḥ ।।

gavāṃ tvayāyute dattaṃ dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ tathā bahu ।
bhūbhujā satyadharmeṇa kiṃtu tāvan nirarthakam ।।

dānena tapasā vāpi trayo lokāḥ samarjitāḥ ।
sarveṣām eva tīrthānāṃ mātā vai mekalā smṛtā ।।

etat te kathitaṃ rājan yathābhūd amareśvare ।
svasti vo astu gamiṣyāmi tvaṃ vāyodhyā prati vraja ।।

aham eva gamiṣyāmi narmadāṃ saptakalpagām ।
śrutvā tvadīyaṃ yajñaṃ hi naimiṣāraṇyam āgataḥ ।।

nirāśo ahaṃ gamiṣyāmi nābhūn me kāṃcanaṃ mukham ।
vānarasya vacaḥ śrutvā yuvanāśvo abravīd vacaḥ ।।

kastvaṃ vānararūpeṇa satyam etad bravīṣi me ।

vānara uvāca ahaṃ jābālinaḥ putraḥ kadambo nāma viśrutaḥ ।।

tiryagyonau praviṣṭaś ca prākṛtaiḥ karmabhiḥ svakaiḥ ।
bhrāntāni sarvatīrthāni veṣeṇānena suvrata ।।

paritrāṇaṃ paraṃ nābhūt satyadharmamakhottame ।
vapur hiraṇmayaṃ sarvaṃ mukhavarjaṃ mamābhavat ।।

vānarasya vacaṃ śrutvā sannivṛtya nṛpottamaḥ ।
ārādhya devadeveśaṃ naimiṣe yajñapūruṣam ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ praṇipatya prasādya ca ।
madīyayajñe dānena tapasā niyamena ca ।।

śamicchaṃ chrāvayāmāsa eko vānararūpadhṛk ।
hiraṇmayaṃ mukhaṃ cāsya yathā syāt tvaṃ tathā kuru ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ devo yuvanāśvaṃ mahīpatim ।
pratyakṣaṃ naimiṣaṃ tīrthaṃ sūryakoṭisamaprabham ।।

pṛthivyāṃ naimiṣaṃ tīrtham antarikṣe ca puṣkaram ।
triṣu lokeṣu vikhyāto giriś cāmarakaṇṭakaḥ ।।

na ca śrutaṃ tvayā tāta purāṇaṃ skandakīrtitam ।
mātā sā yatra saritāṃ tīrthānāṃ ca saridvarā ।।

nāmasaṃkīrtanādasyā mucyate bhavabandhanāt ।
viṣādaṃ tyaja tīrthānāṃ pradhāno amarakaṇṭakaḥ ।।

satyadharmaḥ punas tatra kariṣyati makhottamam ।
revākapilayor yoge mukhaṃ tatra hiraṇmayam ।।

bhaviṣyati na sandehas tava vānarasattama ।
naimiṣaṃ sa namaskṛtya ādidevaṃ haraṃ harim ।।

sthānaṃ svaṃ ca jagāmātha mudā paramayā yutaḥ ।
naimiṣasya vacaḥ śrutvā ayodhyādhipatis tathā ।।

viveśa nagarīṃ puṇyāṃ yathā śakro amarāvatīm ।
vānaro api gatas tatra satyadharmo yataḥ svayam ।।

praṇamya satyadharmākhyam idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।
revākapilayor yoge tvadīye ca mahāmakhe ।।

avabhṛthasnānajanite kardame luṭhanān mama ।
śarīraṃ kāñcanībhūtaṃ mukham evāvaśiṣyate ।।

yajñamiṣṭvā punas tatra mukhaṃ me kāñcanaṃ kuru ।
gandharvādhipatir bhūyo mukto vānarayonitaḥ ।।

hemībhūtavapus tatra yadā vānarasattamaḥ ।
devandundubhinādena nānālaṅkārabhūṣitaḥ ।।

haṃsayuktena yānena vījyamāno apsarogaṇaiḥ ।
jagāma śāṅkaraṃ lokaṃ tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।।

tatra ye śvāpadās sarve te api snātvā divaṅgatāḥ ।
etat te kathitaṃ pārtha yathāvṛttaṃ purātanam ।।
śravaṇāt kīrtanāc cāsya gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye ṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
śrutvā nānāvidhān dharmāstvatprasādān mahāmune ।
nāhaṃ tṛptiṃ tu gacchāmi narmadākhyānakīrtanāt ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
gāvaḥ pavitramatulaṃ gāvaḥ sarvārthasādhakāḥ ।
tasmāddhi gopradānena śivabhaktyā pramucyate ।।

yasmin deśe bhaven nityaṃ śivabhaktisamanvitaḥ ।
so api deśo bhavet pūtaḥ kiṃ punaś ca sabāndhavaḥ ।।

uktāni ṣaṭsahasrāṇi purāṇe mekalātaṭe ।
ityāha jñānayogasya dharmayogasya tattvavit ।।

dharmādharmagatīnāṃ ca svarūpam upavarṇitam ।
tīrthākhyānasamāyuktaṃ narmadākhyānam uttamam ।।

kīrtanāc chravaṇāt tasya mucyate bhavabandhanāt ।
vidyāṃ siṃhāsane divye vastrapuṣpādhivāsitām ।।

pūjayitvā haraṃ viṣṇuṃ śṛṇuyād vācayet tathā ।
śrīmatsiṃhāsanaṃ vāpi kḷptaṃ haimaṃ suśobhanam ।।

hemavastroparicchannaṃ nānāratnavibhūṣitam ।
rājataṃ tāmrakaṃ kāṃsyaṃ brahmacārivinirmitam ।।

tat tu tārasamudbhūtaṃ śṛṅgavad ratnabhūṣitam ।
divyaṃ siṃhāsanaṃ vāpi pūjāṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ ।।

gandhādhivasitakaraḥ śrīmadāsanasaṃsthitaḥ ।
śambhvāyatanatīrtheṣu narendra bhavaneṣu ca ।।

bodhayet paramaṃ dharmaṃ gṛhagrāmapureṣu ca ।
narmadākīrtanācchrotā śivaloke mahīyate ।।

idaṃ tīrtham idaṃ tīrthaṃ paryaṭan neti vai naraḥ ।
narmadaiva paraṃ tīrtham ity āha bhagavān chivaḥ ।।

asmiṃstīrthe naraśreṣṭha śrāddhaṃ kāryaṃ vidhānataḥ ।
svāgatena yamaḥ prītaś cāsanena śatakratuḥ ।।

pitaraḥ pādaśaucena atrādyena prajāpatiḥ ।
viprapādodakaklinnā yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī ।।

tāvat puṣkarapātreṣu pibanti pitaro jalam ।
vidyāvate snātakāya bhikṣave śrotriyāya ca ।।

tathā paramahaṃsāya viṣṇuvratadharāya ca ।
sarvopaskaraṇaṃ dattvā śivaloke mahīyate ।।

anāhitāgniṃ yo vipram āhitāgniṃ karoti ca ।
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ svavittenaiva kārayet ।।

ardhārdhaṃ saphalaṃ tasya yāvaj jīvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।
viṣṇuloke antakāle ca bhogān bhuṅkte ca puṣkalān ।।

svadravyeṇa ca yo yajñaṃ karoti vidhivad dvijaḥ ।
narmadātīram āsādya brahmaloke sa modate ।।

dhātrīṃ hiraṇmayīṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇāya prakalpayet ।
kalpagā tīram āśritya viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।।

tilataṇḍulakarpūrasusambhojyavimiśritaiḥ ।
kuṅkumair vastradhānyaiś ca nirmitaṃ śivasannidhau ।।

parvakāle ca yo dadyāt parvate mekalātaṭe ।
vaset viṣṇulokeṣu naraḥ svarge na saṃśayaḥ ।।

pratyakṣadhenuṃ yo dadyāt hemaratnavibhūṣitām ।
ghṛtadhenuṃ guḍadhenuṃ śarkarādhenum eva ca ।।

revākapilayor yoge dattvaitān narasattamaḥ ।
sarvapāpavinirmukto loke krīḍati vaiṣṇave ।।

yadi tatra mahārāja bhikṣānnaṃ ca niveditam ।
tasya saṃkhyā na vidyeta sa yāvat saṃgamo nṛpa ।।

etat sarvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ kathitaṃ tava suvrata ।
vaivasvate antare athānyac chṛṇu tvaṃ nṛpasattama ।।

vīraṇasya tu rājarṣer maitreyo abhūt purohitaḥ ।
tena cāyatanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kāritaṃ narmadātaṭe ।।

puryāś caivāmarāvatyā diśi yāmyāṃ vyavasthitam ।
tadāyatanamāhātmyān narmadāyāḥ prabhāvataḥ ।।

modate vaiṣṇave loke yugasyārddhaṃ dvijottamaḥ ।
śṛṇu tvaṃ yāni tīrthāni revāyāḥ paścimottare ।।

vanaṃ meghavanaṃ nāma yajñaparvatam āśritam ।
rantidevaḥ purā tatra cakravartī yudhiṣṭhira ।।

gavi nītaṃ kulaṃ yena sa devāsuramānuṣam ।
pitaro mocitā yena gobhir vinihatāḥ purā ।।

cāṇḍālaiś ca hatā ye ca prāpnuvanti parāṃ gatim ।
cāṇḍālād udakāt sarpād vidyuto brāhmaṇād api ।।

dantibhyaś ca paśubhyaś ca maraṇaṃ pāpaśālinām ।
viṣṇor balipradānena kriyāṇāṃ karaṇena ca ।।

tīrthapiṇḍapradānena te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।
dadhīcir nāma rājarṣir avantyadhipatis tathā ।।

sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ śakratulyaparākramaḥ ।
purā devāsure yuddhe daityair devā vinirjitāḥ ।।

devānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca hantāro daityakaṇṭakāḥ ।
naṣṭāḥ svapāpadoṣeṇa sabhṛtyakulabāndhavāḥ ।।

devāḥ samuditāḥ sarve lokapālāḥ savāsavāḥ ।
nirvighnaṃ pṛthivīṃ kṛtvā lokaṃ caiva carācaram ।।

vindhyaṃ giriṃ gatās te tu yasmin vahati kalpagā ।
samarthaṃ bhūpatiṃ jñātvā dadhīciṃ kurusattama ।।

dattāny astrāṇi rakṣārthaṃ tasya rājñaḥ surottamaiḥ ।
vajraṃ śaktiṃ tathā pāśaṃ daṇḍaṃ khaḍgaṃ dhvajaṃ gadām ।।

triśūlaṃ ceti devānām āyudhāni pracakṣate ।
tāni dattvā yathā nyāyaṃ nākapṛṣṭhaṃ mudā yayuḥ ।।

purāṇamatamājñāya dadhīciḥ satyavikramaḥ ।
śāpasyaiva bhayād bhīto namaskṛtya pragṛhya ca ।।

prabhāvāt toyatāṃ nītvā śarīrāntar nyaveśayat ।
tataḥ kālāntare prāpte dānavā baladarpitāḥ ।।

jambhakumbhahayagrīvapramukhāḥ punarutthitāḥ ।
dānavānāṃ balaṃ jñātvā trastā devāḥ savāsavāḥ ।।

kāryakāle samutpanne saṃsmṛtyāstrāyudhāni ca ।
nārada preṣayāmāsuḥ dadhīciṃ prati bhārata ।।

avantīṃ sa purīṃ prāpya devarṣir nāradas tathā ।
viveśa bhavanaṃ rājño maṇikāñcanavedikam ।।

utthito nṛpaśārdūlo muniṃ dṛṣṭvā sutejasam ।
pūjayitvā yathā nyāyaṃ hemakāsanasaṃsthitam ।।

taṃ tu dṛṣṭvā sukhāsīnaṃ rājā vacanam abravīt ।
kim arthaṃ mānuṣe loke devalokāt samāgataḥ ।।

nārada uvāca
yuddhaṃ mahat samutpannaṃ devānāṃ dānavaiḥ saha ।
samarpaya tvaṃ śastrāṇi kṣīyante dānavā yathā ।।

kuru kāryaṃ ca devānāṃ satyadharmavrate sthitaḥ ।

dadhīcir uvāca śṛṇu kāryaṃ ca devarṣe devānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।।

acireṇaiva kālena kṣayaṃ yāsyanti dānavāḥ ।
mayā tāny eva śastrāṇi rakṣaṇārthaṃ mahāmune ।।

āpobhūtāni pītāni śarīre santi tāni vai ।
upāyena hi gṛhṇantu dāsyāmy etāni vai punaḥ ।।

ityuktvā ca nṛpaśreṣṭha ājuhāva ca gāḥ purā ।
māṃsādibhakṣitaṃ gobhir asthivarjaṃ viśāmpate ।।

astragrāmas tataḥ prāpto lokapālair yathā tathā ।
gonardaṃ nāma nagaraṃ tat tu lokeṣu viśrutam ।।

dānavā nihatā devaiḥ punaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ pravartitā ।
acintayat tadā tatra rantidevo mahīpatiḥ ।।

govidyutpaśucāṇḍālasarpairvinihatā narāḥ ।
devalokaṃ na te yānti na teṣāmudakakriyā ।।

śocayitvā ciraṃ kālaṃ sāntaḥpuraparigrahaḥ ।
prakṣālya narmadātoye tadasthīni vyasarjayat ।।

liṅgaṃ brahmeśvaraṃ tatra yajñaparvatasannidhau ।
dharmasaṃśayam āpanno rantidevo mahīpatiḥ ।।

papraccha muniśārdūlān vaśiṣṭhapramukhān dvijān ।
triḥpradakṣiṇam āvṛtya yathā nyāyam idaṃ vacaḥ ।।

ke deśāḥ parvatāḥ puṇyā nadyaḥ kāḥ kīrtitāḥ śubhāḥ ।
narakasthān pitṝn yatra tadvadeyuḥ samuddharet ।।

akṣayaṃ ca pitṛśrāddhaṃ pitṝṇām akṣayā gatiḥ ।

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ mārkaṇḍeyāśramaṃ gaccha asmābhiḥ saha bhūpate ।।

so api sarvaṃ vijānīyāt kalpagā tīramāśritaḥ ।
tac chrutvā rantidevo api munibhiḥ paribhāṣitaḥ ।।

jagāma munibhiḥ sārddhaṃ kalpagātīravāsinam ।
sa rājā brāhmaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ praṇipatya tathā arcayat ।।

samutthāyābravīd vākyam upaviṣṭaḥ kuśāsane ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca kān na mocayate ghorān pitṝn saṃsārasāgarāt ।।

śṛṇvantu mama vākyāni munayo viditātmanaḥ ।
sarvatīrthamayī revā sarvārthātmamayī śubhā ।।

śivenaitat nigaditaṃ purāṇe skandakīrtite ।
kubjārevāsamāyoge viśeṣāt surapūjite ।।

tatra snātā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtā na punarbhavāḥ ।
tatra śrāddhena yogena pitṝṇāṃ paramā gatiḥ ।।

idaṃ te kathitaṃ rājan kubjārevāsamāgame ।
arcayitvā maheśānaṃ tatra bilvāmrakāhvayam ।।

sarvapāpavinirmukto gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt ।
sārdhakoṭis tu kanyānāṃ tatra siddhiṃ parāṃ gatāḥ ।।

śaptāstāḥ pūrvamunibhiḥ kāmadoṣeṇa bhārata ।
vidyādharāś ca yakṣāś ca gandharvāḥ kinnarās tathā ।।

śaptāstenaiva doṣeṇa kuberapuravāsinaḥ ।
sarve te siddhim āpannāḥ kubjārevāsamāgame ।।

amāsomasamāyoge kārttikyāṃ caiva parvaṇi ।
vārāṇasī prayāgaś ca puṣkaraṃ naimiṣaṃ tathā ।।

ete snātuṃ samāyānti kubjārevāsamāgame ।
śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya śivaloke mahīyate ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe rantidevopākhyānaṃ nāmaikaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

rantideva uvāca
yathā śaptās tu tāḥ kanyās tāsāṃ nāmāni kalpaga ।
śrotum icchāmi tattvena keṣu sthāneṣu pūjitā ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
vārāṇasyāṃ viśālākṣī naimiṣe liṅgadhāriṇī ।
prayāge lalitādevī kāmukā gandhamādane ।।

mānase kumudā nāma viśvayonis tathāmbare ।
gomante gomatī nāma mandare kāmacāriṇī ।।

madotkaṭā caitrarathe tapantī hastināpure ।
kānyakubje tathā gaurī prabhā kamalaparvate ।।

ekāgre kīrtimatyākhyā viśvā viśveśvare tathā ।
puṣkare puruhūteti kedāre mārgadāyinī ।।

nandā himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe gokarṇe bhadrakārṇikā ।
sthāneśvare bhavānīti bilvake bilvapatrikā ।।

śrīśaile mādhavī nāma bhadrā bhadreśvare tathā ।
jayā vārāhaśaile tu kamalā kamalālaye ।।

rudrakoṭyāṃ tu rudrāṇī koṭiḥ kālañjare tathā ।
mahāliṅge tu kapilā mākoṭe mukuṭeśvarī ।।

śālagrāme mahādevī śivaliṅge jalapriyā ।
māyāpuryāṃ kumārī tu santāne lalitā tathā ।।

utpalākhye sahasrākṣī hiraṇyākṣe mahotpalā ।
tīrthāyāṃ maṅgalā nāma vimalā puruṣottame ।।

vipāśāyāmamoghākṣī pāṭalā puṇḍravardhane ।
nārāyaṇī supārśve ca trikūṭe bhadrasundarī ।।

vipule vipulā nāma kalyāṇī pralayācale ।
koṭīvikoṭi tīrthe tu yamunāyāṃ mṛgāvatī ।।

karavīre mahālakṣmīr umādevī vināyake ।
ārogyā vaidyanāthe tu mahākāle maheśvarī ।।

abhayā kṛṣṇatīrthe tu amṛtā vindhyakandare ।
māṇḍavye māṇḍukā nāma svāhā māheśvare pure ।।

chāgalambā pracaṇḍe ca caṇḍikā amarakaṇṭake ।
someśvare varāhī tu prabhāse puṣkarāvatī ।।

devamātā sarasvatyāṃ pārā pārāvate tathā ।
mahālaye mahābhāgā payoṣṇyāṃ piṅgaleśvarī ।।

saṃhitā kṛtaśauce tu kārttikeye tu śāṅkarī ।
utpalā varṣake lolā subhadrā śoṇasaṅgame ।।

mālāsiddhatale lakṣmīranantā bhāratāśrame ।
jālandhare siddhamukhī tārā kiṣkindhaparvate ।।

devadāruvane puṣṭir medhā kaśmīramaṇḍale ।
bhīmādevī himādrau tu tuṣṭir vastreśvare tathā ।।

kapālamocane siddhir mātā kāyāvarohaṇe ।
śaṅkhoddhāre dhṛtir nāma dhvaniḥ piṇḍārake tathā ।।

kalā tu candrabhāgāyām akṣode śivadhāriṇī ।
vaijayanty amṛtā nāma badaryām oṣadhī tathā ।।

oṣadhī cottarakurau kuśadvīpe kuśodakā ।
manmathā himakūṭe tu pramate satyavādinī ।।

aśvatthe vandinī nāma nidhirvaiśravaṇe tathā ।
gāyatrī vedavadane pārvatī śivasannidhau ।।

devaloke tathendrāṇī brahmaṇāsye sarasvatī ।
sūryabimbe prabhā nāma mātṛkā vaiṣṇavī tathā ।।

arundhatī satīnāṃ ca apsarassu tilottamā ।
citirbrahmakalā nāma śaktiḥ sarvaśarīriṇām ।।

etad uddeśataḥ proktaṃ nāmāṣṭaśatam uttamam ।
aṣṭottaraṃ tu tīrthānāṃ śatam ekaṃ hy udāhṛtam ।।

yaḥ paṭhet prātarutthāya sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।
eṣu tīrtheṣu ye snātvā etāḥ paśyānti mānavāḥ ।।

sarvapāpavinirmuktās te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।
yaḥ karoti tanutyāgam umāsthāneṣu mānavaḥ ।।

sa bhittvā brahmasadanaṃ padamāpnoti śāṅkaram ।
nāmāṣṭakaśataṃ yas tu śrāvayec chivasannidhau ।।

tṛtīyāyāṃ tathāṣṭamyāṃ bahuputro bhaven naraḥ ।
godāne śrāddhakāle ca vivāhe maṅgale tathā ।।

devārcanavidhau vāpi paṭhan brahmatvam āpnuyāt ।
śrutvaitat stotramatulaṃ namaskṛtya ca parvatam ।।

rājā svapitṛmokṣāya yajñārthaṃ prāha kalpagam ।
kasmiṃs tīrthe bhaved yajñaḥ pitṝṇāṃ mokṣadāyakaḥ ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe mātṛstutirnāma dviṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
revātaṭe mahāpuṇye pitṝṇāṃ mokṣaṇaṃ prati ।
kuru yajñaṃ mahābhāga mucyante pitaro yathā ।।

iti śrutvā mahārāja namaskṛtya ca kalpagām ।
vaśiṣṭhapramukhaiḥ sārddhaṃ jagāma svapuraṃ nṛpaḥ ।।

sa vatsānāṃ ca lakṣaikamaprasūtāyutaṃ tathā ।
viṃśatiḥ śyāmakarṇānāṃ hayānāṃ ca daśāyutam ।।

maṇimāṇikyamuktādi bhūṣitoccaiḥ śravastviṣām ।
ayutaṃ ca karīndrāṇāṃ ghaṇṭābharaṇaśobhinām ।।

maṇimāṇikyaratnānāṃ saṃkhyāṃ kartuṃ na śakyate ।
nānādeśanṛpaiḥ sārddhaṃ brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ ।।

veṇuvīṇāninādena brahmaghoṣaraveṇa ca ।
āpūrayan diśaḥ sarvā divaṃ bhūmiṃ ca saṃspṛśan ।।

harṣeṇa mahatā yukto yajñasambhārasaṃvṛtaḥ ।
rantidevo mahīpālaḥ kalpagātīram āśritaḥ ।।

anekabhakṣabhojyānāṃ tatra saṃkhyā na vidyate ।
aṣṭayojanaparyantaṃ yajñayūpāś ca maṇḍapāḥ ।।

hemaratnamayāḥ stambhā maṇimauktikabhūṣitāḥ ।
hiraṇmayāni kuṇḍāni vedikāś ca sahasraśaḥ ।।

sruvaś ca yajñapātrāṇi sarvaṃ svarṇam ayaṃ tathā ।
samāhūtās tato devā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।।

candrādityau grahaiḥ sārddhaṃ nakṣatradhruvamaṇḍalam ।
siddhā vidyādharā yakṣāḥ surāsuramahoragāḥ ।।

devarājaś ca devāś ca bṛhaspatipurogamāḥ ।
tato yajñaḥ samārabdho brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ ।।

homena tarpitā devāḥ sarvalokanivāsinaḥ ।
nirdhūmaś ca jvalad vahṇiḥ saptajihvāsamanvitaḥ ।।

pratyakṣo havyavāhaś ca svayaṃ yajñe narādhipa ।
tato nivartito yajño brāhmaṇair āptadakṣiṇaiḥ ।।

ghoṣaṇā bhrāmitā rāṣṭre pratīhāraiḥ sahasraśaḥ ।
yo yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ so atra taṃ tvetyasaṃśayaḥ ।।

āhūtāḥ pūrvajās tatra mātṛkāḥ paitṛkās tathā ।
apamṛtyuvaśaṃ prāptās tiryagyonigatāś ca ye ।।

te sarve śubhayonitvam āpannā yajñayogataḥ ।
arcitā narmadādevīṃ pratyakṣā rūpadhāriṇī ।।

arcito bhagavāṃs tatra pārvatyā sahito haraḥ ।
śrīpatiś ca śriyā sārddhaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।।

śakrādayas tathā devāḥ sapatnīkā alaṃkṛtāḥ ।
gāścāśvāṃś ca karīndrāṃś ca brāhmaṇebhyo nyavedayat ।।

yac cānyad vidyate kiṃcid dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ payo dadhi ।
agniśaucāni vastrāṇi sarvaṃ tebhyo nyavedayat ।।

yugapat pūjitā devā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।
arcitā narmadādevī śailamūle vyavasthitā ।।

pravāho nirgato yatra kubjārevāsamāgame ।
pitaras tarpitā devāḥ prāptāś ca paramāṃ gatim ।।

divyayānasamārūḍho dadhīciś ca nṛpottamaḥ ।
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ pūrvaṃ paścimaṃ tad anantaram ।।

devayānapathe santaḥ śataśo atha nṛpottama ।
ūcuś ca devās te sarve brahmādyā rantidevakam ।।

vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te prītāḥ satyenānena bhūmipa ।
prāpto asi paramaṃ lokaṃ pitṛbhir mātṛbhiḥ saha ।।

rantidevo abravīd vākyaṃ yūyaṃ me varadā yadi ।
kalaśaḥ sthāpito yatra brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ ।।

caturvedadharairbhaktaiḥ pañcabrahmatanuḥ svayam ।
śivaliṅgaṃ bhavet tatra jvālāmālāsamaprabham ।।

yajñaparvatam āsādya pravāho yajñanirgataḥ ।
snāne vinirgatā kubjā caruke carukā tathā ।।

carmilā cāṅghrimūle tu śilpe śilpā vinirgatā ।
dhanado devatāś cānyāḥ sampūjya praṇipatya ca ।।

kalpagāṃ ca namaskṛtya kāmikaṃ yānam āśritāḥ ।
stotraṃ cakre mahābhāga liṅgarūpasya śūlinaḥ ।।

lokanātho jagatsraṣṭā praṇipatya yathāvidhi ।

brahmo vāca nāsti rudrasamo devo nāsti rudrasamo guruḥ ।।

nityadāmalakāyāya svaprabhāmalamūrtaye ।
śivabhasmāṅgarāgāya deveśāya namo astu te ।।

nīlakaṇṭhāya devāya sarvāyāmitamūrtaye ।
bahurūpāya kāntāya śāśvatāya namo astu te ।।

parāya parameśāya sarvajñāya namo astu te ।
sarvapraṇatadehāya svayam apraṇatāya ca ।।

pūjyānām api pūjyāya namastryakṣāya śūline ।
brahmendraviṣṇuvedyāya utpattisthitihetave ।।

devastuta namaste astu bhuktimuktipradāya ca ।
vāmāya vāmarūpāya vāmomāropabhāsine ।।

vāmakāntārdhavehāya īśānāya namo astu te ।
śrutvā stotram idaṃ devo brahmaṇaḥ so amitadyutiḥ ।।

vṛṇīṣva vāñchitaṃ yajñe varam ity āha śaṅkaraḥ ।
dadāmi te na sandeho yas tvayā vara īpsitaḥ ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ brahmā śaṅkaraṃ sarvagaṃ prabhum ।
pañcavaktraṃ pañcaliṅgaṃ brahmapūjyaṃ prakīrtitam ।।

bilvā niveditā yasminn āmrāś ca viniveditāḥ ।
bilvāmrakannāma liṅgaṃ saṃsārārṇavatāraṇam ।।

prasiddhiṃ paramāṃ yātu bhagavaṃs tvatprasādataḥ ।
vāmanā mekalā yatra yatredaṃ liṅgam uttamam ।।

tatra snātvā naravyāghra śivalokam avāpyate ।
idaṃ varam ahaṃ manye lokānugrahakārakam ।।

śaṅkaras tu tathety evaṃ prāha brahmāṇam avyayam ।
evam uktvā maheśāno gaṇakoṭisamāvṛtaḥ ।।

stūyamānaḥ suraiḥ sarvaiḥ jagāma bhavanaṃ svakam ।
brahmādyā devatāś caiva gatāḥ svaṃ svaṃ niveśanam ।।

rantidevaḥ pratuṣṭāva liṅgarūpadharaṃ śivam ।
niśamya rantidevasya stotraṃ prāha maheśvaraḥ ।।

varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te stotreṇānena suvrataṃ ।
rantidevo abravīd vākyaṃ yadi me varadaḥ śivaḥ ।।

idaṃ tīrthaṃ na moktavyaṃ mahādeva sadā tvayā ।
aghaughasamaplutā ye tu tiryagyonigatā narāḥ ।।

asya tīrthasya māhātmyāt te yāntu paramāṃ gatim ।
atra yad dīyate dānaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati cākṣayam ।।

idaṃ varam ahaṃ manye yadi tuṣṭo asi śaṅkara ।

śaṅkara uvāca amāsomasamāyoge kārttikyāṃ caiva parvaṇi ।।

atra yad dīyate dānaṃ tad anantaṃ samaśnute ।
etat te kathitaṃ rājaṃs tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam ।।

viśvedevāḥ parāṃ siddhim asmiṃs tīrthe samāgatāḥ ।
agastyaśaunakaś caiva parāśaro aghamarṣaṇaḥ ।।

saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ prāptā nānā munigaṇās tathā ।
atrāyutaṃ munīnāṃ ca tapasā divamāruhat ।।

saṃkrame ca vyatīpāte grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ ।
amāsomasamāyoge ṣaḍaśītimukhe tathā ।।

puṇyaṃ daśaguṇaṃ vṛddhiṃ satyam etac chivoditam ।
sapādakoṭis tīrthānāṃ kubjārevāsamāgame ।।

dakṣiṇottarabhāge tu krośamātraṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।
avaśaḥ svavaśo vā api prāṇān yas tu parityajet ।।

rājā varṣasahasrāṇi vidyādharapure bhavet ।
kṛmikīṭapataṅgādyās tīrthe asmin prāṇamokṣaṇe ।।

divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu rājā vidyādhare pure ।
bilvāmrakaṃ siddhaliṅgaṃ kāmabhogaphalapradam ।।

kubjeśvaraṃ mahac cānyad brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati ।
atrāntare mahārāja śivakṣetraṃ vidurbudhāḥ ।।

revākubjāsamāyoge yavānāṃ saptatistathā ।
amāsomasamāyoge snānāc chāntiḥ prakīrtitā ।।

vārāṇasī kurukṣetraṃ prayāgo naimiṣaṃ tathā ।
puṣkaraṃ ca gayā caiva kedāraṃ tīrtham uttamam ।।

phalam eteṣu sāmānyam amāsomasamāgame ।
akṣayaṃ ca phalaṃ proktaṃ kubjārevāsamāgame ।।

tilodakapradānena mātṛkaṃ paitṛkaṃ sutaḥ ।
narakād uddharet sarvān pūrvān api parān api ।।

so api rājā gṛhaṃ prāptaḥ sarvān uddhṛtya pūrvajān ।
ayaṃ te kathito rājan kubjārevāsamāgamaḥ ।।

rantidevo hariścandraḥ puruhūtaḥ purūravāḥ ।
atreṣṭvā vividhair yajñair divyanti divi devavat ।।

śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya tīrthasya narasattama ।
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā śivaloke mahīyate ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe kubjāmāhātmye triṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athānyat kathayiṣyāmi tīrthaṃ tīrthavaraṃ śubham ।
yāmyapradeśe revāyā āśramaḥ surapūjitaḥ ।।

suvarṇadvīpapavikhyāto devadroṇīsamāvṛtaḥ ।
hārīto gautamo viṣṇuḥ sāvarṇiḥ kauśikas tathā ।।

ete cānye ca bahavo munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ ।
māsopavāsinaḥ kecid anye pakṣopavāsinaḥ ।।

cāndrāyaṇaparāś cānye tathānye kṛcchracāriṇaḥ ।
phalamūlāśinaḥ kecit tathānye vāyubhakṣakāḥ ।।

kaṇadhūmaṃ pibanty anye jalāhārās tathā pare ।
ekapādāḥ sthitāḥ kecid anye cārdhapadāḥ sthitāḥ ।।

dantolūkhalinaḥ kecidanye sūryāvalokinaḥ ।
brāhmaṇāś ca brahmavidaḥ śrutismṛtiviśāradāḥ ।।

itihāsapurāṇāni mokṣopāyavicintakāḥ ।
agnihotraparā nityaṃ japayajñakriyāparāḥ ।।

vedadhvanitanirghoṣais tārayanti jagattrayam ।
na tasmin saṃcaret pāpaṃ tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā ।।

mekalādakṣiṇe tīre brahmaloka iva sthitaḥ ।
āmrajambūkadambaiś ca kapitthair bilvadāḍimaiḥ ।।

kadalībījapūrādyair jambīraiḥ panasais tathā ।
nyagrodhabadarair mukhyair bahuvṛkṣavibhūṣitam ।।

punnāgair nāgabakulair aśokais tilakais tathā ।
mandāraiś campakaiś cāmrātakair nīlotpalotpalaiḥ ।।

patrapuṣpaphalopetair vṛkṣaiḥ sarvair alaṃkṛtam ।
nānāpakṣigaṇopetaṃ siddhagandharvasevitam ।।

vyāharatyaṇḍajāḥ sarve mānuṣāṇāṃ girā nṛpa ।
etad guṇasamāyuktaṃ suvarṇadvīpam uttamam ।।

svāyambhuve antare rājann ādikalpe kṛte yuge ।
arcanād devadevasya suvarṇadvīpavāsinaḥ ।।

apahāya tamaḥ kṛtsnaṃ loke krīḍanti śāṅkare ।
pitṝṇām annadānena tilatoyapradānataḥ ।।

malāpakarṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā vasanti brahmaṇaḥ pure ।
puṇyāyāṃ bhūpakārtikyāṃ sarvatīrthaphalapradaḥ ।।

naitat paśyanti manujāḥ kalau māyāvimohitāḥ ।
kalpagā yāmyabhāge tu tīrthakoṭiranekadhā ।।

prasiddhaṃ siddhamunibhir jñāyate kevalaṃ hi tat ।
nāstikair bhinnamaryādaiḥ purāṇasmṛtinindakaiḥ ।।

tailābhyaktair na vedoktakarai revātaṭe tathā ।
kalimāyāvimūḍhaiś ca sthānaṃ tanna pradṛśyate ।।

hiraṇyagarbhāsthāne tu yasmin vahati kalpagā ।
yajñagarbheśvaraṃ nāma śivaliṅgaṃ prakīrtitam ।।

pūjyate siddhagandharvaiḥ surāsuramahoragaiḥ ।
yatra vaivasvato rājā sūryaputro mahāyaśāḥ ।।

tasya tīrthasya māhātmyāc candrabimbānano abhavat ।
caitrasyaiva tu māsasya śuklapakṣe narādhipa ।।

caturdaśyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ yatra sannihito haraḥ ।
tilodakapradānena piṇḍadānena bhārata ।।

pitṝn samuddharet tatra narakād bhūridakṣiṇaḥ ।
nivased vaiṣṇave loke yāvac candrārkadarśanam ।।

tatra yaddīyate dānaṃ kurukṣetrasamaṃ hi tat ।
prāṇatyāge kṛte tatra na paśyanti yamālayam ।।

revāyā uttare kūle paryaṅko nāma parvataḥ ।
sa ca vindhyasutaḥ śrīmān sarvadevamayaḥ śubhaḥ ।।

tatra pāpaharo viṣṇuḥ svayaṃ tiṣṭhati keśavaḥ ।
narapāpaharo yas tu narmadātaṭam āśritaḥ ।।

tatra snātvā mahārāja gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।
tarpitāḥ pitaras tasya tṛptā yānti hareḥ puram ।।

ekādaśīṃ dvādaśīṃ vā tatra yaḥ kurute naraḥ ।
na tasya punarāvṛttir martyaloke durāsade ।।

krośamātrapramāṇaṃ ca harikṣetraṃ prakīrtitam ।
apamṛtyumṛtā ye ca te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe viṣṇukīrtanaṃ nāma catuḥṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadāyāmyabhāge tu tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam ।
māṇḍavyasyāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ siddhagandharvasevitam ।।

vibhāṇḍakaś ca gārgyaś ca ṛṣyaśṛṅgādayas tathā ।
tasmin sahasrasaṃkhyātā munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ ।।

aśokavanikāṃ rājan chṛṇu sāmpratamuttamam ।
tatra sannihito deva umayā sahito haraḥ ।।

āviṣṭaś cāśrame tatra viśoko vimalaḥ śivaḥ ।
viśokayā saricchreṣṭhā narmadā yatra saṅgatā ।।

tatra snātā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtā na punarbhavāḥ ।
aśokeśvaraliṅgam ca pratyakṣaṃ siddhiśaṅkaram ।।

śāpabhraṣṭā dvijās tatra nāradena vimocitāḥ ।
tasya tīrthasya māhātmyāt modante divi devatāḥ ।।

nānāvṛkṣaphalaiḥ puṣpaiḥ sarvakāmasamanvitaiḥ ।
nānā pakṣigaṇairjuṣṭaṃ nānāvṛkṣaniṣevitam ।।

siddhavidyādharair yakṣair gandharvaiḥ kinnarais tathā ।
veṇuvīṇāninādena śaṅkhavāditraniḥsvanaiḥ ।।

śobhate sarvadā rājan narmadā vindhyasaṅgamaḥ ।
aśokā devatā yatra brahmaśakrapurogamāḥ ।।

viśvedevāśramaṃ taddhi sarvadevanamaskṛtam ।
viśvāyāś ca tathā putrā viśvedevāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।

aśokavanikāyāṃ ca janayāmāsa kaśyapaḥ ।
vaivasvate antare prāpte tretāyāṃ narasattama ।।

pañcāyutāni tāni tīrthāni nivasanti śubhāni ca ।
tatra siddhā ca sāvitrī devamātāditis tathā ।।

devayānī tathendrāṇī rohiṇī saṃbharāyaṇī ।
dākṣāyaṇī lokavandyā lopāmudrā mahāyaśā ।।

ratnāvalī sūryabhāryā dhruvā tārā gaṇeśvarī ।
aśokās tena vihitās tatrasthāḥ śatasaṃkhyakāḥ ।।

asya tīrthasya māhātmyān mucyate kilbiṣān naraḥ ।
śuklapakṣe caturdaśyām āśvine māsi bhārata ।।

aputriṇī tathā bandhyā durbhagā bhartṛvarjitā ।
pañcaratnaphalaiḥ snātā divyakumbhaiḥ samarcayet ।।

sahasrajanma sā bhūyaḥ putriṇī subhagā bhavet ।
aśokavanikā kṣetre tatra gauryā varaḥ kṛtaḥ ।।

yasmin vahati sā devī narmadā saptakalpagā ।
tatreṣṭaṃ dharmarājena varuṇena mahātmanā ।।

nairṛtyena tathānyaiś ca lokapālair yathā vidhi ।
pratyakṣo havyavāhaś ca lokapālānupāgataḥ ।।

atrir marīciḥ kaśyapaś cakrus tatra makhottamam ।
anyakṣetrāc chataguṇā tatra dānādikā kriyā ।।

vārāṇasī kurukṣetraṃ gayā vai naimiṣaṃ tathā ।
māyāpurī puṣkaraṃ ca prayāgaḥ śaśibhūṣaṇam ।।

kāśyapī sarvatīrthāni yatra tiṣṭhati kalpagā ।
aśokavanikāyās tu nānyat tīrthaṃ samaṃ viduḥ ।।

iṣṭaṃ yatra purā rājan hayamedhaṃ makhottamam ।
brahmaṇā mocitāḥ pūrvaṃ viprāḥ kauleyayonitaḥ ।।

asya tīrthasya māhātmyāt pāṭalīputravāsinaḥ ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca hayamedhamakheneṣṭaṃ kathaṃ tāta svayambhuvā ।।

kathaṃ ca mocitā viprāḥ pūrvaṃ kauleyayonitaḥ ।
ko vā rājā purā brahman devarājasamo abhavat ।।

etat sarvaṃ yathā nyāyaṃ śaṃsa me munisattama ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga samākhyānaṃ purātanam ।।

aśokavanikā tīrthaṃ kalpagā taṭamāśritam ।
na jānanti mahāmūḍhā manujāḥ pāpamohitāḥ ।।

guptād guptataraṃ tīrthaṃ sarvatīrthottamottamam ।
viśokeśvaraliṅgaṃ tu tasmin paramasiddhidam ।।

pūjyate siddhagandharvair na tat paśyanti mānuṣāḥ ।
darśanāt sparśanāt tasya brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati ।।

svāyambhuve antare prāpte ādikalpe kṛte yuge ।
raviś candro mahārāja cakravartī mahāyaśāḥ ।।

somavaṃśe janiṃ prāptaḥ kāñcīpurapatis tathā ।
śaśāsa pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ yathā śakras triviṣṭapam ।।

gatas tu pṛthivīpālo nānāvṛkṣasamākulam ।
nānāpakṣigaṇairjuṣṭaṃ nānāmuniniṣevatam ।।

yatrāgastyeśvaraṃ nāma śambhorāyatanaṃ śubham ।
sevyate munibhiḥ sarvair agastyād yais tapodhanaiḥ ।।

rāhusūryasamāyoge raviścandro nṛpottamaḥ ।
saptakalpavahā yatra śailaścāmarakaṇṭakaḥ ।।

hastyaśvarathapādātaiḥ sakośabalavāhanaiḥ ।
tapasyantaṃ mahātmānaṃ munisaṅghaiḥ samāvṛtam ।।

maitrāvaruṇikaṃ nāma jvalantamiti pāvakam ।
teṣāṃ madhye samutthāya śāṇḍilyaś ca mahātapāḥ ।।

urasā pṛthivīṃ gatvā so agastiṃ paripṛcchati ।
raviścandro mahātejāḥ samāyātas tavāśramam ।।

purohito aham asyāsmi jānīhi tvaṃ taponidhe ।
tvat pādārcanam ākāṅkṣī manyase ced anugrahaḥ ।।

agastya uvāca
āgacchatu nṛpaśreṣṭhaḥ śīghraṃ siṃhāsane sthitaḥ ।
āgatas tad anujñātaḥ pādau jagrāha tasya ca ।।

arghapādyaiś ca sampūjya papraccha kuśalaṃ muniḥ ।
kuśalaṃ te mahābhāga sāntaḥ puraparicchadaḥ ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ rājā munīndraṃ prati bhārata ।
adya me saphalaṃ janma rājyaṃ jīvanam eva ca ।।

muktaś ca kilbiṣād asmāt tvātpādāmbujadarśanāt ।
sarvatra kalpagā puṇyā sarvatīrthamayī śubhā ।।

kasmin sthāne yaje yajñaṃ śaṃsa me munisattama ।
yathā saṃsiddhyate yajñaḥ surāṇāṃ tṛptir akṣayā ।।

etat sarvaṃ yathā nyāyaṃ trikālajña nivedaya ।

agastya uvāca śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga kathyamānaṃ nibodha ca ।।

śivena kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ pārvatyāḥ ṣaṇmukhasya ca ।
brahmaviṣṇvādidevānāmanyeṣāṃ ca divaukasām ।।

mayā tatra śrutaṃ rājan mārkaṇḍena cirāyuṣā ।
tatte ahaṃ kathayiṣyāmi mekalātīrthasambhavam ।।

śṛṇudhvaṃ munayaḥ sarve yat praṣṭavyāvatāraṇam ।
kasya śaktir mahārāja varjayitvā maheśvaram ।।

pramāṇaṃ sarvatīrthānāṃ saṃkhyāṃ vā kartum āditaḥ ।
uddeśamātravaktā ahaṃ mārkaṇḍasya mahāmuneḥ ।।
etat te kathitaṃ rājan yathāvṛttaṃ purātanam ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe narmadāmāhātmye pañcaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
evaṃ śrutaṃ purā rājñā raviścandreṇa dhīmatā ।
uvāca vacanaṃ śrīmānagastyo munisattama ।।

sarasvatī na gaṅgā ca yamunā vā na sāgarāḥ ।
na caivānyāni tīrthāni prayāgapramukhāny api ।।

ekaiva narmadā puṇyā saptakalpavahā śubhā ।
lakṣayojanaparyantaṃ jambūdvīpaṃ prakīrtitam ।।

narmadātoyapānena lokāloke carācare ।
tapohīnā narāś caiva te api yānti śivālayam ।।

yo ayaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ sa taṃ prāpnoti puṣkalam ।
sādhu sādhu mahābhāga pṛṣṭo ahaṃ yat tvayānagha ।।

narmadā kathitā divyā hṛdyā kasya na rocate ।
santi tīrthāni yāvanti dakṣiṇottarakūlayoḥ ।।

tvatprītidāni tāvanti kathayāmi nṛpottama ।
anyāni granthalakṣeṇa na ca kīrtayituṃ kṣamaḥ ।।

trayo vedāstrayo lokās tisraḥ sandhyāstrayo agnayaḥ ।
siddhagandharvayakṣāś ca sakinnaramahoragāḥ ।।

vidyādharaś cāpsarasaḥ kalpagātaṭamāśritāḥ ।
oṃkārādīni liṅgāni vaidūryādinagāḥ purā ।।

dvāpare ca kaliṃ prāpya pāvanatvam avāpnuyuḥ ।
brahmaviṣṇvādidevānāṃ maryādā kathyate adhunā ।।

prabhābhirdyotamānāyā revāyā dakṣiṇottare ।
yajñabhūmiriyaṃ khyātā surāsuranamaskṛtā ।।

aśokavanikā tatra tasyā devo maheśvaraḥ ।
tatra siddhyati nirvighno yajña ity āha śaṅkaraḥ ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ rājā agastyaṃ munisattamam ।
svasti vo astu gamiṣyāmi tvayā saha mahāmune ।।

aśokavanikāṃ prāptaḥ sa rājā munibhirvṛtaḥ ।
revāyā dakṣiṇe kūle puṇyatīrthesu śobhane ।।

daśayojanaparyantaṃ yajñayūpāś ca maṇḍapam ।
maṇimāṇikyaratnaughaiḥ sarvadvāreṣu śobhitāḥ ।।
