patākādhvajaśobhāḍyā nānāvastrāvaguṇṭhitāḥ ।
viśvāmitro bharadvājaḥ kaśyapo bhārgavas tathā ।।

brahmadṛśyo lomaśaś ca tathānye munisattamāḥ ।
vālakhilyā mahābhāgā mānasā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ।।

ete cānye ca bahavo munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ ।
tataḥ pravartito yajño brāhmaṇair āptadakṣiṇaiḥ ।।

tṛptāś ca devatāḥ sarvāḥ pratijagmus triviṣṭapam ।
jagmuḥ sarve ca muditā munayaḥ svāśramaṃ prati ।।

tato nivartito yajño durvāsāḥ kupito gataḥ ।
nātra vaivasvato nāhaṃ nāradaḥ parvatas tathā ।।

kathaṃ nivartito yajñaḥ pāparkarminarādhamaiḥ ।
āgatas tu yamas tatra nāradaḥ parvatas tathā ।।

lekhakaścitraguptaś ca kālo mṛtyus tathaiva ca ।
ete ca kupitāḥ sarve yajñabhāgaṃ vinā nṛpa ।।

tān sarvān kupitān dṛṣṭvā raviścandro abravīd vacaḥ ।
aśokeśvaradevasya narmadāyāḥ prasādataḥ ।।

ko me samartho vighnāya surāsuragaṇeṣv api ।
tathaiva ko anyo jantūnāṃ yajñavighnasya hetave ।।

yajñakāle ca saṃprāpto ya kaścid api mānavaḥ ।
pūjanīyas tathārcyaś ca yathā devaścaturbhujaḥ ।।

yathāyātā mahābhāgā brahmaputrā mahaujasaḥ ।
dadāmi vo na sandeho manasā yadabhīpsitam ।।

durvāsā uvāca
paripūjyaś ca naḥ putro nāradaḥ parvatas tathā ।
ekākī prārthaye nāhaṃ militvā prārthayāmahe ।।

raviścandra uvāca
yo yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ taṃ tasmai pradadāmy aham ।
iti sarve api tenaiva prastutā munipuṅgavāḥ ।।

suprītā vihitā rājann arghapādyapradānataḥ ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca munayaḥ kena kāryeṇa pāṭalīputravāsinaḥ ।।

devyā śaptāḥ śvayoniṃ ca gatā muktāś ca te katham ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca purā tapodhanāḥ sarve jaṭāvalkaladhāriṇaḥ ।।

naipāle vai paśupatiṃ devadevaṃ maheśvaram ।
pūjayanti śivaṃ bhaktyā gauryā virahitaṃ haram ।।

ardhanārīśvaraṃ devaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam ।
saṃśaptās tena kāryeṇa pārvatyā liṅgabhedinaḥ ।।

varṣaṃ sahasraṃ hi mitaṃ śvayoniṃ ca gamiṣyatha ।
nirmālyabhakṣakāḥ pāpāścaṇḍadravyasya bhakṣakāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ kṛte mahārāja durvāsā nṛpam abravīt ।
śvayoniṃ samanuprāptās tatra kāle munīśvarāḥ ।।

mocaya tvaṃ tato rājann asmat priyacikīrṣayā ।
pārvatyā te abhiśaptāś ca narake majjanti dāruṇe ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ rājā muniṃ durvāsasaṃ tataḥ ।
mocayāmi na sandehas tasmāt pāpād dvijottamān ।।

preṣitāḥ kiṅkarās tena sīdanto yatra te vane ।
praṇipatya ca te sarve tānūcuś ca vanecarān ।।

smārayanti pūrvajātim ādiṣṭāḥ prabhuṇā yathā ।
tatas tad vacanāt prāptās te aśokavanikāṃ drutam ।।

raviścandraścakravartī tān vilokya tapodhanān ।
mudā paramayā yuktaḥ prāha tān prahasann iva ।।

aśokeśvaradevasya mekalāyāḥ prabhāvataḥ ।
mama dānaprabhāveṇa maharṣīṇāṃ prasādataḥ ।।

tyaktvā śvayoniṃ munayaḥ śivalokaṃ prayāntu vai ।
etat pāpaṃ mahāghoraṃ mayi sarvaṃ niṣīdatu ।।

tatkṣaṇān muktaśāpāste kāmikaṃ yānam āsthitāḥ ।
ūcur maharṣayo vākyaṃ raviścandraṃ śatakratum ।।

tvaṃ mātā tvaṃ pitāsmākaṃ gururmokṣapradāyakaḥ ।
evam uktvā yayus te tu umāmāheśvaraṃ param ।।

sādhu sādhu mahābhāga tvaṃ tu yajñataponidhiḥ ।
nā anyastvayā samaḥ kaścit somavaṃśe mahīpatiḥ ।।

tvayā hi nirjitaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।
evam uktvā suraśreṣṭhāḥ sādhuvādais tam ārcayan ।।

devadundubhayo neduḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca ।

durvāsā uvāca kṣatriyeṣu tvayā tulyo na dṛṣṭo na śruto mayā ।।

prāṇatyāgo hi sukaro dharmatyāgo hi duṣkaraḥ ।
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te yatte manasi vartate ।।

prahasann abravīd vākyaṃ rājā durvāsasaṃ munim ।
mama dānaprabhāveṇa narā duṣkṛtabuddhayaḥ ।।

prāpnuvan tu paraṃ lokaṃ vara eṣa mama priyaḥ ।
evamastviti tasyāgre abhidhāya munipuṅgavaḥ ।।

sa mudā parayā yuktas tatraivāntaradhīyata ।
tad dṛṣṭvā tādṛśaṃ karma rājñaś cāmitatejasaḥ ।।

śaṅkayā parayā yukto dharmarājo abravīd idam ।
varaṃ dadāmi bhadraṃ te yajñabhāgabahiṣkṛtaḥ ।।

śvayonitvaṃ gatā viprā mocitāḥ karmabandhanāt ।
īdṛśaṃ tava sāmarthyaṃ jānāmi ca nṛpottama ।।

pṛthivyāṃ duṣkaraṃ karma yajñaś caiva viśeṣataḥ ।
yo dadāti mahābhāga svakīyaṃ puṇyamuttamam ।।

yamaloko jitas tena devaloko jitas tathā ।
varayogyo asi rājendra satyam etat mayoditam ।।

raviścandra uvāca
yadi tuṣṭaḥ sūryaputra varaṃ dātuṃ mamecchasi ।
mama yajñaśatenaiva dānena tapasā tathā ।।

pāpayonigatā ye tu ye ca duṣkṛtakāriṇaḥ ।
prayāntu tvatprasādena dharmarāja śivālayam ।।

imaṃ varam ahaṃ manye prasādaḥ kriyatāṃ mayi ।

yama uvāca evaṃ bhavatu rājendra satyadharmaparāyaṇa ।।

prāpnuhi tvaṃ paraṃ lokaṃ satyenānena suvrata ।
yatas te mocitāḥ sarvāḥ kaśmalāt pāpayonayaḥ ।।

kṣatriyāḥ śataśo rājann anye caiva sahasraśaḥ ।
pāpāt samuddhṛtā ye ca teṣāṃ saṃkhyā na vidyate ।।

evamuktvā nṛpaśreṣṭhaṃ dharmarājo mahābhujaḥ ।
kāmikaṃ yānamāruhya surāsuranamaskṛtam ।।

yayau svabhavanaṃ rājan nāradaḥ parvatas tathā ।
tasyām aśītilakṣāṇi tīrthānāṃ narasattama ।।

aśokavanikāyāṃ tu kīrtitāni tavānagha ।
śravaṇāt kīrtanāt teṣāṃ gosahasraphalaṃ bhavet ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe aśokavanikāvarṇano nāma ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athātaḥ kathayiṣyāmi tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam ।
revāyā uttare kūle puraṃ vāgīśvarābhidham ।।

vāgurnāma nadī tatra revayā saha saṃgatā ।
tatra snātā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtā na punarbhavāḥ ।।

vāgīśā tatra cāmuṇḍā dānavakṣayakāriṇī ।
maṇibhadro vīrabhadras tathā anye śataśo nṛpāḥ ।।

babhūvur muktaśāpās te tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।
tilapiṇḍapradānena pitṝṇāṃ paramā gatiḥ ।।

brahmadattaścakravartī sūryavaṃśe mahīpatiḥ ।
ayodhyādhipatiḥ śrīmān cakratulyaparākramaḥ ।।

dhanadhānyasamāyukto bhayadāridryavarjitaḥ ।
prajās tasmin mahīpāle sarvā api mudānvitāḥ ।।

iṣṭaḥ kratuvarastena narmadāvāgusaṅgame ।
brahmādyā devatāḥ sarvāḥ śakraviṣṇupurogamāḥ ।।

pratyakṣaś ca maheśāno gaṇeśvarasamanvitaḥ ।
lokapālāś ca marutaścandrādityau dhruvas tathā ।।

ṛkṣāṇi yogasiddhāś ca somamukhyāś ca sarvaśaḥ ।
vaśiṣṭho munibhiḥ sārddhaṃ videhādhipatis tathā ।।

evamādyāḥ samāhūtā mitrāvaruṇa eva ca ।
sarve hiraṇmayās tatra yajñayūpāś ca maṇḍapāḥ ।।

daśayojanaparyantaṃ yajñabhūmir mahībhṛtaḥ ।
svārociṣe antare rājann ādikalpe kṛte yuge ।।

gavāṃ śatasahasrāṇi hemabhārānvitāni ca ।
hayānāṃ śyāmakarṇānām ayutaṃ sāgram eva ca ।।

dantinām ayutaṃ caiva ghaṇṭābharaṇabhūṣitam ।
maṇimāṇikyam uktāś ca bhakṣyabhojyāny anekadhā ।।

evaṃ rājā brahmadattaḥ sarvabhūpālasattamaḥ ।
yajñaṃ pravartayāmāsa sarvasambhārasaṃbhṛtaḥ ।।

vedanirghoṣaśabdena gītavādyaraveṇa ca ।
nānāyānasamārūḍhaiḥ stūyamāno marudgaṇaiḥ ।।

brahmadattasya yajñena vāgīśasya prasādataḥ ।
narmadāyāḥ prasādena pretās tṛptiṃ parāṃ gatāḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kathaṃ tu brahmadattasya kalpagātīrayājanam ।
kathaṃ pretā vinirmuktāḥ pretās te kena karmaṇā ।।

etat sarvaṃ yathā nyāyaṃ kathayasva tapodhana ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca śṛṇu rājan yathā nyāyam itihāsaṃ purātanam ।।

kārttikyām utsavaṃ prāpya puṣkare jyeṣṭhapuṣkare ।
ayogandhaḥ svayaṃbhūś ca puṇḍarīkākṣa eva ca ।।

pitāmahaḥ svayaṃ tatra surāsuraguruḥ pitā ।
kāvyaś ca hotṛsadanau vedagarbhaḥ kṛtadhvanaḥ ।।

svastikaś caiva sāvitro vāmadevo aghamarṣaṇaḥ ।
ete cānye ca munayo brahmatejo aśasaṃbhavāḥ ।।

tathā te hi yathāśaktā ṛtukālābhigāminaḥ ।
gārhasthye ca sthitā bhāryā bhartṛśuśrūṣaṇe ratāḥ ।।

cīravalkaladhāriṇyaḥ śākasyāmākabhakṣikāḥ ।
viṣaṇṇās tena dharmeṇa satyastā apyagarhayan ।।

dvijasya ṣaṭ ca karmāṇi yajanaṃ yājanaṃ tathā ।
adhyāpanaṃ cādhyayanaṃ dānaṃ caiva pratigrahaḥ ।।

bhūṣaṇaṃ paridhānaṃ ca yoṣitāṃ bhartṛsevanam ।
evaṃ ca garhitā rājan yoṣidbhiḥ patayas tathā ।।

bhītās te vismitāḥ sarve viṣaṇṇavadanās tathā ।
hariścandraḥ purā rājā na bhūto na bhaviṣyati ।।

dānena nirjitaṃ yena trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।
rāhusūryasamāyoge kurukṣetraṃ jagāma ha ।।

tyaktvā te puṣkaraṃ tīrthaṃ dhanalobhena mohitāḥ ।
sahasrasaṃkhyāmunayaḥ sabhāryāḥ sasutāś ca te ।।

yatra rājā hariścandraḥ pratigrahavilipsayā ।
munīnāha hariścandro mudā paramayā yutaḥ ।।

dhanyā me saphalā yātrā kurukṣetre ravigrahe ।
kṣudhārtā duḥkhitāś caiva bālā vṛddhāḥ kṛśāturāḥ ।।

valkalājinavastrāś ca yauvane pretarūpiṇaḥ ।
yanno yūyam abhiprāptāḥ patnīputraiś ca saṃyutāḥ ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ rājā sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇipatya ca ।
ādeśo dīyatāṃ mahyaṃ kiṃ karomi bhavatkṛte ।।

evamuktvā dadau śrīmānekaikasya pṛthak pṛthak ।
lakṣaṃ lakṣaṃ hiraṇyasya tathā gāvaḥ sahasraśaḥ ।।

sahasraṃ turagāṇāṃ ca dantināṃ śatam eva ca ।
sāptabhaumān gṛhān ramyān hemaprākāratoraṇān ।।

nānāvidhavilāsāṃś ca yathā dhanapatiḥ svayam ।
kalpāntare mṛtā jātāḥ pretarūpā bhayaṅkarāḥ ।।

lamboṣṭhā lambavṛṣaṇā vikṛtānanasaṃyutāḥ ।
pratigrahaprabhāveṇa dvijasya patanaṃ dhruvam ।।

jātismarāḥ svaṃ śocanti ekākīnās tu te bahiḥ ।
na bhāryā na ca me putrā na bhṛtyā na ca bāndhavāḥ ।।

na te pratigrahair dagdhā yathā pūrvaṃ tathaiva ca ।
vayam ekākino dagdhā vṛkṣā iva havirbhujā ।।

rājapratigrahair dagdhā na prarohanti mānavāḥ ।
vaiśvānareṇa dagdhānāṃ punarjanma prajāyate ।।

na mātā na pitā putro draviṇaṃ na ca bāndhavāḥ ।
yamadūtair gṛhītānāṃ dharma ekaḥ sahānugaḥ ।।

śocitvā suciraṃ kālaṃ bhāryāputravivarjitāḥ ।
bhramitvā ca mahīṃ sarvāṃ puṣkaraṃ tīrthamāgatāḥ ।।

pretarūpān munīn dṛṣṭvā viṣādaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ ।
tān uvāca muniśreṣṭhaḥ kathaṃ pretatvam āgatāḥ ।।

pretā ūcuḥ
hariścandraḥ satyadharma sūryavaṃśe mahīpatiḥ ।
ayodhyādhipatiḥ śrīmān devatulyaparākramaḥ ।।

tasya pratigraho asmābhirāptaḥ sūryagrahe sthite ।
tena pretatvam āpannāḥ sarve brahmarṣayo mune ।।

etat te kathitaṃ brahman mokṣo asmākaṃ vidhīyatām ।
bhaviṣyabhūtatattvajño brahmaputras taponidhiḥ ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ śrīmān nāradas tāṃs tapodhanān ।
kasminnavasare puṇye kārttikyāṃ divyaparvaṇi ।।

śivena kīrtitaṃ pūrvaṃ pārvatyāḥ ṣaṇmukhasya ca ।
śrutaṃ mayāpi tatraiva purāṇaṃ skandakīrtitam ।।

kānyā pāpakṣayaṃ kartuṃ śaktā revāṃ vinā nṛpa ।
gaṅgādyāḥ sarito viprāḥ puṇyatīrthās tathāpi ca ।।

vāgīśaṃ ca puraṃ tatra narmadātaṭamāśritam ।
adhvare brahmadattasya mokṣaṇaṃ tu bhaviṣyati ।।

uddeśaṃ tu tato dattvā nāradastridivaṃ gataḥ ।
te api pretā mahābhāga dhyātvā śivam umāpatim ।।

abhijagmus tam uddeśaṃ vāgīśapuram uttamam ।
tatra snātvābhyarcya śivaṃ hariṃ bhāskaram eva ca ।।

adhvare brahmadattasya muktāḥ sarve api kilbiṣāt ।
brahmayānaṃ samāruhya brahmalokaṃ samāgatāḥ ।।

pratapanti yathādityā brahmatejovapurdharāḥ ।
tasyopari nareśasya puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta vai ।।

etat te kathitaṃ rājan yathāvṛttaṃ purātanam ।
śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe vāgīśvarākhyāna nāma saptaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
pratigrahagrahagrastā lobhamohavimohitāḥ ।
majjanti narake ghore yatra gatvā na nirgatāḥ ।।

saphalā vedayajñāś ca tīrthayātrā ca bhārata ।
tathā kliśyanti cātmānaṃ pratigrahaparā narāḥ ।।

dātā ca yācakaś caiva karābhyām eva sūcitau ।
atho gacched grahītā tu dātā gacchati corddhvataḥ ।।

sahasrāvartakaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam ।
tatra snātasya vidhivad vṛṣotsargaphalaṃ bhavet ।।

āsaptamaṃ kulaṃ caiva punīte nā atra saṃśayaḥ ।
revāyā uttare kūle sahasrāyudhasaṃkhyayā ।।

tataś cānte mahābhāga kārāyā vanam uttamam ।
agniṣṭomaphalaṃ yatra snātvā svargaṃ ca gacchati ।।

revāyā uttare bhāge tīrtha paramaśobhanam ।
saugandhikaṃ vanaṃ nāma brahmacāriśucivratāḥ ।।

siṣicuḥ pitaras tat tu brahmādyāḥ sutapodhanāḥ ।
siddhacāraṇagandharvāḥ sakinnaramahoragāḥ ।।

praviśya tad vanaṃ martyaḥ sarvapāpāt pramucyate ।
tataḥ sarasvatī cāsti nadīnām uttamā nadī ।।

lakṣyā devasutā rājan mahāpuṇyā prakīrtitā ।
tatra snānaṃ prakurvīta mānavo nṛpate jale ।।

tarpayitvā pitṝn devān aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।
īśānādhyuṣitaṃ nāma tatra tīrthaṃ sudurlabham ।।

tatra snātvā vyatīpāte saṃkrāntau grahaṇe naraḥ ।
sahasrakapilādāne vājimedhe ca yatphalam ।।

sugandhāṃ chātakumbhāś ca pañcayajñāṃś ca bhārata ।
abhigamya naraśreṣṭha svargaloke mahīyate ।।

triśūlākhyaṃ tu tatraiva tīrtham āsādya bhārata ।
tatrābhiṣekaṃ yaḥ kuryād arcayet pitṛdaivatam ।।

gaṇeśatvaṃ sa labhate tyaktvā dehaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।
tato gacchen mahārāja brahmasthānam anuttamam ।।

revāyā uttare kūle kāmabhogaphalapradam ।
brahmodam iti vikhyātaṃ prakāśyaṃ bhuvi bhārata ।।

tatra saptarṣayaḥ prāptāḥ snānārthaṃ bharatarṣabha ।
kapiñjalo muniśreṣṭho havyavāhaś ca bhārata ।।

bhagavān devayānaś ca viśvāvasumahāmuniḥ ।
asya tīrthasya māhātmyād brahmalokam avāpnuyuḥ ।।

pitaraḥ śrāddhadānena prayātā brahmaṇaḥ puram ।
udumbarasya kṛtvā tu vidhivad darśanaṃ tataḥ ।।

antarddhānam avāpnoti tapasā dagdhakilbiṣaḥ ।
tato gacchen mahārāja śaṅkaraṃ lokaśaṅkaram ।।

kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyām abhigamya vṛṣadhvajam ।
labhate sarvakāmāṃś ca svargalokaṃ hi gacchati ।।

narmadāyāmyabhāge tu gopyād gopyatara mahat ।
siddhaliṅgaṃ maṇimayaṃ na tatpaśyanti mānavāḥ ।।

nāgendrasurasiddhaiś ca nāgakanyābhir arcyate ।
sapādakoṭistīrthānāṃ śaṅkare kurunandana ।।

vasūnāmāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ munīnāṃ brahmacāriṇām ।
śivabhaktiparāṇāṃca kandamūlaphalāśinām ।।

pitṝṇām akṣayā tṛptis tilatoyapradānataḥ ।
mudā paramayā yukto dātā yāti śivālayam ।।

dhruvo dharaś ca somaś ca sāvitraś cānalo anilaḥ ।
pratyūṣaś ca prabhāsaś ca vasavo aṣṭau prakīrtitā ।।

śaṅkarasya prasādena divi devatvam āgatāḥ ।
kalpagāsaumyabhāge tu somatīrtham anuttamam ।।

tatra snātvā naro rājan svargaloke mahīyate ।
saptasārasvataṃ tīrthaṃ tato gacchen nṛpottama ।।

brahmaṇā ca kṛtaṃ stotraṃ puṇyakīrte niśāmaya ।

brahmovācā vākpatir vacasāṃ nityaṃ vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

haṃsaḥ sureśo vaktā vā vasūnāmantarā vasan ।
hotā diviṣadīśāno vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

svāhākāraḥ svadhākāro vaṣaṭkāro haviṣyabhuk ।
ṛṅmūrtiryajuṣāṃ mūrtirvāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

kṣetrajñaḥ paramaḥ sūkṣmo jagatāṃ tārako hariḥ ।
īśvaro hṛdayāvāso vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

śravaṇyaḥ śravaṇopāyaḥ puṇyaślokaḥ śuciśravāḥ ।
varado vāsudevo agnir vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

puruṣaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ purāṇo bhuvaneśvaraḥ ।
ādityāntargato vahṇir vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

kaṃsakāliyahantā ca subalo balamardanaḥ ।
śiśupālanihantā agnir vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

kālaneminihantā agniryaḥ kāle niyatāntakaḥ ।
śatāsuraśarīraghno vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

kaṅkāsuranihantā ca madhukaiṭabhanāśanaḥ ।
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇir vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

śuklaḥ salilaśāyī ca viṣṇuḥ pāpakṣayāhvayaḥ ।
indro vacanasatpālo vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

hṛṣīkeśaś cendrapālopendro garuḍāsanaḥ ।
sahasranāmā dharmajño vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

śaṅkhī ca nandakī cakrī śārṅgadhanvā gadādharaḥ ।
dhīro vapuṣmān medhāvī vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

bṛhatsaṃkarṣaṇaḥ śambhuḥ svayambhūr bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।
nipuṇo lakṣaṇaḥ śuddho vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

traikālikastrikālajñastrayī kartā trilocanaḥ ।
trisāmā devakīsūnur vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

avyaktātmā mahātmā ca antarātmā janārdanaḥ ।
prāṇaścendriyabhūtātmā vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

paramātmā paraṃ brahma parameśaḥ parā gatiḥ ।
parameṣṭhī paraṃ jyotir vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

viśvātmā viśvakartā ca viśvasya patirātmavān ।
dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ kartā ca vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

sahasraśīrṣā bhagavān sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt ।
sahasrakoṭidhārī vā vāsudevo astu me gatiḥ ।।

iti vāgīśvaro vāgmī pūjitaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।
bhaktasya bhagavān viṣṇuḥ prīyatāṃ me janārdanaḥ ।।

janmaprabhṛti yat kiṃcin mayā sukṛtamarjitam ।
tatsamagraṃ phalaṃ cāstu śāśvataṃ puruṣottama ।।

idam abhyasyato nityaṃ pūjitaḥ syāt sakeśavaḥ ।
vināśayati pāpāni prakāśayati tat phalam ।।

eṣa niṣkaṇṭakaḥ panthā yatra sampūjyate hariḥ ।
kupathaṃ taṃ vijānīyād yatra nārādhyate hariḥ ।।

vāsudevaparā vedā sudevaparākriyā ।
vāsudevātmakā viprā vāsudevaparāśrayaḥ ।।

sarve devā vāsudevaṃ yajante sarve devā vāsudevāt prasūtāḥ ।
sarveṣāṃ vā vāsudevo api devo nānyat kiṃcid avāsudevātiriktam ।।

nānyaḥ puṇyataro devo nāsti viṣṇuparaṃ tapaḥ ।
nāsti viṣṇuparaṃ jñānaṃ sarvaṃ viṣṇumayaṃ jagat ।।

ye paṭhanti narā bhaktyā viṣṇunāmāṅkitastavam ।
te yānti vaiṣṇavaṃ lokaṃ paraṃ brahma sanātanam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śrutvā stotram idaṃ devo brahmaṇaḥ samahātmanaḥ ।
śriyā prabodhitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śayāno yoganidrayā ।।

dṛṣṭvā abravīt surān sarvān nānārūpān bhayānakān ।
kimasti vaḥ samutpannaṃ māṃ didṛkṣur ihāgatāḥ ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ brahmā keśavaṃ prati bhārata ।
tvāṃ vinātra jagannātha kas trātā devakaṇṭakaiḥ ।।

dānavair veṣṭitā dhātrī svargaścaiva vināśitaḥ ।
dharmakāmādikā yajñā vedā viplāvitās tathā ।।

danubhārabharākrāntā rasātatatalaṃ gatā ।
jaṭāsuraś ca jābālirdaityo mayasutas tathā ।।

daśakoṭyas tu daityānāṃ samagrabalaśālinām ।
śivaprasādayuktānāṃ svargaviplavakāriṇām ।।

tasmāt pravartitaṃ cakramuddhara svavasundharām ।
śrutvā vākyam idaṃ devo bhayārtaṃ prāṇapīḍitam ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ devo bhayaṃ tyajata daityajam ।
acireṇaiva kālena haniṣyāmi mahāsurān ।।

vārāharūpamāsthāya preṣitaṃ kalpagājale ।
daṃṣṭrāgreṇa dhṛtā dhātrī dānavānāṃ kṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।।

punaḥ pravartitā sṛṣṭir yathāpūrvaṃ tathaiva ca ।
brahmādyā muditā devāḥ pratijagmus triviṣṭapam ।।

etat te kathitaṃ rājan vārāhaṃ kalpagātaṭe ।
śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya hayamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe vārāhamahimānuvarṇano nāmāṣṭaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato devapathaṃ tīrthaṃ sarvadevamayaṃ śubham ।
tatra snātaś ca vidhivat sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet ।।

māse māse kuśāgreṇa somayāgaṃ karoti yaḥ ।
sa revājalapūtasya kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm ।।

liṅgaṃ devapathaṃ nāma surāsuranamaskṛtam ।
śraddhayā tad darśanena pitṝṇāṃ paramā gatiḥ ।।

caitre māse caturdaśyā pakṣayor ubhayor api ।
snānārthaṃ sarvatīrthāni jagmuḥ kartuṃ ca satkriyām ।।

yaddevaloke devānām īpsitaṃ ca nṛpadhvaja ।
sahasrāṇi munīndrāṇāṃ tasmiṃś śivamupāsate ।।

cāndrāyaṇaparāḥ kecid brahmakūrcaparās tathā ।
kandamūlaphalāhārā jalāhārā jalapriyāḥ ।।

agnihotraparā nityaṃ tathā hutahutāśanāḥ ।
upāsate devapathaṃ saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ gatāḥ ।।

athānyat saṃpravakṣyāmi tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam ।
sahasrayajñaṃ paramaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam ।।

ekādaśyāṃ mārgaśīrṣe pūjayitvā janārdanam ।
sahasrayajñasyeṣṭasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।।

na paśyed yamalokaṃ ca tiryagyoniṃ na gacchati ।
tīrthasyāsya prabhāveṇa naro vigatakalmaṣaḥ ।।

etat te kathitaṃ rājan puṇyākhyānam anuttamam ।
śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।।

śuklatīrthaṃ tato gacchet sarvatīrthamayaṃ śubham ।
yatra snāto api labhate daśadhenuphalaṃ naraḥ ।।

śuklīkṛtās tena devā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।
sapādakoṭistīrthānāṃ śuklatīrthe vyavasthitā ।।

aṣṭahastapramāṇaṃ ca śuklatīrthaṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।
tatra kālāgnirudraś ca śrīkaṇṭhaś ca tathā paraḥ ।।

tais tais tapobhirugraiś ca tatra siddhiṃ parā gatāḥ ।
śuklatīrthaprabhāveṇa modante divi devatāḥ ।।

śakro api ca purādhyakṣaṃ devadevam umāpatim ।
revātoyena saṃsnāpya bilvapatraiḥ samārcayat ।।

paurṇamāsyām amāvasyāṃ somaḥ sūryaḥ prabhāvatīm ।
tatra snāto grahaiḥ sārddhaṃ nakṣatradhruvamaṇḍalaiḥ ।।

tena devāś ca dīvyante śuklatīrthaprabhāvataḥ ।
kaśyapasyāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ surasiddhaniṣevitam ।।

munīnām ayutaṃ tatra svayaṃ tiṣṭhati bhārata ।
kandamūlaphalāhārā jalāhārās tathā pare ।।

śākāhārā nirāhārā brahmakūrcās tathā pare ।
cāndrāyaṇaparāḥ kecidanye māsopavāsinaḥ ।।

ṛṣikoṭyas trayastriṃśac chukleśvaramupāsate ।
rāhugraste tathā candre paurṇamāsyāṃ tithau tathā ।।

āyānti sarvatīrthāni snātum etac chivoditam ।
sthāneśvare yatphalaṃ syād rāhusūryasamāgame ।।

tatphalaṃ prāpnuyāt sarvaṃ śuklatīrthe na saṃśayaḥ ।
hemadhenudharādīni rūpyadā gajadās tathā ।।

etad dattvā mahārāja puṇyasaṃkhyā na vidyate ।
dhanadena kubereṇa devagandharvadānavaiḥ ।।

rāhusūryasamāyoge śuklatīrthe maheśvaraḥ ।
candanāgurukarpūrapuṣpamālābhir arcitaḥ ।।

vitānadhvajamukhyaiś ca dīpamālāprabodhanaiḥ ।
asya tīrthaprabhāveṇa yakṣarājo dhaneśvaraḥ ।।

bhogā nānāvidhās tena samprāptā divi devatāḥ ।
sarvatīrtham ayaṃ tīrthaṃ sarvadevam ayaṃ ca yat ।।

api varṣasahasreṇa śuklatīrthasya varṇanam ।
na śakyate suraiḥ kartuṃ purāṇe skandakīrtite ।।

pāpayonigato yaś ca tiryagyonigataś ca yaḥ ।
brahmahā ca surāpaś ca śivanirmālyabhakṣakaḥ ।।

mucyate tena pāpena tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।
tatra snānaṃ naraḥ kṛtvā pūjayitvā vṛṣadhvajam ।।

surāsuragaṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ pūjyate narasattama ।
etat te kathitaṃ rājan mahāpātakanāśanam ।।

pitāmahena yatreṣṭo yajñe yajñeśvaraḥ purā ।
stotraṃ kṛtvā yathā nyāyaṃ devadevasya śūlinaḥ ।।

pūjayitvā tu śukleśaṃ brahmā stotram udāharat ।
namaḥ śivāya śāntāya jñānavijñānarūpiṇe ।।

sūkṣmāya sūkṣmarūpāya sarvasūkṣmāya hetave ।
sūkṣmāṇām api sūkṣmāya namaḥ sūkṣmatamāya ca ।।

divyāya divyarūpāya divyadehāya setave ।
divyānām api divyāya namo divyatamāya ca ।।

vyomaprabhāya bhāvāya aghorāya namo namaḥ ।
vyomapramāṇadhāmāya vāmeśāya namo namaḥ ।।

parāya parameśāya pāramārthikahetave ।
parāya paramuktāya namaḥ paratarāya ca ।।

ekajihvadvijahvāya bahujihvāya te namaḥ ।
tathaivāsaṃkhyajihvāya triṇetrāya namo namaḥ ।।

pūjyāya pūjyapūjyāya sarvapūjyaikahetave ।
nityāyānityarūpāya nityanityaikahetave ।।

nityānām api nityāya namo nityatamāya ca ।
śaktāya śaktirūpāya sarvaśaktyekahetave ।।

śaktānām api śaktāya namaḥ śaktatamāya ca ।
śuddhāya sarvaśuddhāya sarvaśuddhyekahetave ।।

kālāya kālarūpāya sarvakālaikahetave ।
kālānām api kālāya namaḥ kālatamāya te ।।

sarvamantraśarīrāya sarvamantraikahetave ।
mantrāṇām api mantrāya namo mantratamāya ca ।।

aprameyamaheśāya īśānāya namo namaḥ ।
yogāya yogarūpāya yogapuruṣa te namaḥ ।।

ekakaṇṭhadvikaṇṭhāya bahukaṇṭhāya te namaḥ ।
asaṃkhyakaṇṭhayuktāya nīlakaṇṭhāya te namaḥ ।।

anantāya maheśāya hartre kartre namo astu te ।
namaste astu mahādeva namaste astu sadāśiva ।।

namaste astu mahāśuddha namas tubhyaṃ namo namaḥ ।
namo bhasmāṅgarāgāya namaḥ khaṭvāṅgadhāriṇe ।।

sarvātmane namas tubhyaṃ viśveśāya namo namaḥ ।
sarvajñāya namas tubhyaṃ sanāthāya namo namaḥ ।।

avyaktāya namas tubhyaṃ śāśvatāya namo namaḥ ।
kailāsavāsine tubhyaṃ namaḥ pātālavāsine ।।

tvayā vyāptam idaṃ sarvaṃ lokālokaṃ carācaram ।
api varṣasahasreṇa kaḥ stotuṃ śaktimān bhavet ।।

iti stavena divyena yaḥ stauti parameśvaram ।
vidhūya sarvapāpāni rudraloke mahīyate ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe śambhustutirnāmaikonasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kimarthaṃ saṃstuto devo brahmaṇā tena tatra vai ।
śuklatīrtham idaṃ kasmādāste yatra maheśvaraḥ ।।

etat sarvaṃ samākhyāhi pṛcchato me mahāmune ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca śṛṇu rājan kathāṃ divyāṃ svargārhaṇyām anuttamām ।।

yāṃ śrutvā sarvapāpebhyas tīrthasnānena mucyate ।
yayātir nāma dharmātmā satyadharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।।

cakravartī nṛpaśreṣṭhaḥ sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।
iyāja sa mahāyajñaiḥ śatakratur ivāparaḥ ।।

nadī madhumatī puṇyā revayā yatra saṅgatā ।
yatra yajñaḥ samārabdha ṛtvigbhir brāhmaṇaiḥ saha ।।

madhyeśvaraṃ yatra liṅgaṃ svayaṃdevo maheśvaraḥ ।
tatra snātā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtā na punarbhavāḥ ।।

cakreṇa viṣṇunā tatra ghātitau madhukaiṭabhau ।
arcanāt tasya devasya gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।।

tilatoyapradānena piṇḍadānena bhārata ।
pitaras tasya tṛpyanti yāvad indrāścaturdaśa ।।

tatra yajñaḥ samārabdho hariśaṅkaravarjitaḥ ।
jaṭāsuras tatra daityaś chidraṃ dṛṣṭvā samāgataḥ ।।

tatovidhvaṃsito yajño dānavair baladarpitaiḥ ।
yajñayūpā yajñapātraṃ daśa dikṣu nipātitāḥ ।।

bhukto hutapuroḍāśaḥ somapānaṃ ca taiḥ kṛtam ।
praṇaṣṭā devatāḥ sarvā dānavānāṃ bhayena ca ।।

aṣṭottaraśataṃ devā mṛgarūpeṇa nirgatāḥ ।
dhanado yakṣarūpeṇa praṇaṣṭaḥ svapurīṃ gataḥ ।।

mahiṣārūḍho dharmarājo gajārūḍhaś śatakratuḥ ।
meṣārūḍho havyavāho nirgatā vratamāsthitāḥ ।।

varuṇaś ca samāyātaḥ praṇaṣṭaḥ svapurīṃ gataḥ ।
makarāsanamārūḍho vāyuś ca mṛgam āśritaḥ ।।

īśāna īśarūpeṇa vṛṣārūḍhaḥ palāyitaḥ ।
astrāṇi lokapālānāṃ hṛtāni danusambhavaiḥ ।।

ekākī yānam āruhya kathaṃ yāmi striyā saha ।
cintayitvā nṛpaśreṣṭhaś cāstraṃ jagrāha bhārata ।।

tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti coktvā vai daityasiṃha durāsadam ।
na kṣatrakulasaṃjātā jātu dṛṣṭvā palāyitāḥ ।।

daśa dvādaśavarṣāṇi vimukhās tava pūrvajāḥ ।
na cātrāhvānito rudro rudra bhāgo na kalpitaḥ ।।

yajñe asmin yajñapuruṣo nāhūto bhagavān hariḥ ।
tena doṣeṇa me yajño dānavaiś ca vināśitaḥ ।।

evam uktvā nṛpaśreṣṭho rudraṃ dhyātvā maheśvaram ।
raudrarūpaṃ samāsthāya jyāghoṣaṃ ghoṣarūpiṇam ।।

jagrāha kopān nistriṃśaṃ nijaghāna ca dānavān ।
āhūtāś ca punardevāḥ sarve brahmapurogamāḥ ।।

ūcus te vacanaṃ devā rājānaṃ prati bhārata ।
tvayā samo atra rājarṣe na bhūto na bhaviṣyati ।।

devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā yayātir vākyam abravīt ।
punaḥ pravartito yajño haraviṣṇuprasādataḥ ।।

yuktaṃ palāyanaṃ cātra kṣatriyasya na vidyate ।
stutas tu tena kāryeṇa śūlapāṇiḥ pinākadhṛk ।।

pātālād utthitaṃ tatra liṅgaṃ kālānalaprabham ।
śuklīkṛtaṃ jagat sarvaṃ prabhayā tasya bhārata ।।

varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te tam uvāca vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।

yayātir uvāca yadi tuṣṭo asi me deva varaṃ dātuṃ mamecchasi ।।

idaṃ sthānaṃ na moktavyam umayā saha śaṅkara ।
yajñadānādikaṃ sarvam akṣayaṃ cātra sarvadā ।।

tapohīnā narā ye ca dānahīnāḥ sakilbiṣāḥ ।
te sarve tvatpuraṃ yāntu śuklatīrthaprabhāvataḥ ।।

tam uvāca mahādevaḥ satyam etat tavoditam ।
yaṃ yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ taṃ taṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।।

asya tīrthasya mahātmyāl liṅgasyāsya samarcanāt ।
narakaṃ naiva paśyanti janmajanmani bhārata ।।

etat te kathitaṃ rājan yathā skandaśivoditam ।
tatra ye nihatā daityāḥ prāptās te api śivālayam ।।

svaṃ svaṃ yānaṃ samārūḍhā yayur devās triviṣṭapam ।
mudā paramayā yuktaḥ stūyamāno nṛpottamaḥ ।।

yayātir nāma rājarṣī rājyaṃ kṛtvā divaṃ gataḥ ।
śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya śivaloke mahīyate ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
dīptakeśvaradeveśaṃ siddhaliṅgaṃ prakīrtitam ।
nātaḥ parataraṃ kiṃcit triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam ।।

darśanād dīptadevasya sparśanād arcanāt tathā ।
anekabhāvikaṃ ghoraṃ kṣaṇamātreṇa naśyati ।।

arcayed dinam ekaṃ tu yo muhūrtaṃ tu mānavaḥ ।
na tasya punarāvṛttir ghore saṃsārasāgare ।।

mokṣadā nāma cāmuṇḍā viddhi gaurīṃ sarasvatīm ।
stutaḥ sahasranāmnā vai viṣṇunā brahmaṇā svayam ।।

stutāni tāni liṅgāni revāyā uttare taṭe ।
oṃkāraścādhidevaś ca bilvāmrakamaheśvaraḥ ।।

śukleśvaro bhṛguś ceti dvīpeśvaratrilocanau ।
vaivasvate antare prāpte ādikalpekṛteyuge ।।

śrīpatiḥ paramādyaś ca dvitīyaś ca pitāmahaḥ ।
tṛtīyo devarājaś ca caturthaḥ sūrya eva ca ।।

pañcamaḥ kathitaḥ somaḥ ṣaṣṭho rāhuḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।
saptamaś ca śaniś caiva tvaṣṭamaḥ ketukaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

vaiśvānaraś ca navamo daśamaś ca digīśvaraḥ ।
ekādaśo vaikramaś ca dvādaśo vāruṇas tathā ।।

trayodaśaś ca vāyur vai dhanadaś ca caturdaśaḥ ।
nānā padaprakāreṇa stuto deva umāpatiḥ ।।

viṣṇunā devanāthena brahmaṇā ca surāsuraiḥ ।
sthiraḥ sthāṇuḥ prabhābhānuḥ pravaro varado varaḥ ।।

hariśca hariṇākhyaś ca sarvabhūtaharaḥ prabhuḥ ।
pravṛttiś ca nivṛttiś ca niyamaḥ śāśvato dhruvaḥ ।।

śmaśānavāsī bhagavān khecaro gocaras tathā ।
abhivandyo mahākarmā tapasvī bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।।

unmattaveṣapracchannaḥ sarvalokaprajāpatiḥ ।
mahārūpo mahākāyaḥ sarvalokaprajāpatiḥ ।।

parātmā sarvabhūtānāṃ virūpo vāmano manuḥ ।
lokapālo pihitātmā prasanno bhavanāśanaḥ ।।

pravṛttaś ca mahāṅgaś ca nicayo niyatāśrayaḥ ।
sarvakāmaḥ svayambhūś ca ādinādikaro nidhiḥ ।।

sahasrākṣo virūpākṣaḥ somo nakṣatrasādhakaḥ ।
candraḥ sūryaḥ śaniḥ keturgraho grahapatirvaraḥ ।।

tapodraṣṭā balaḥ sthātur mṛgabāṇārpaṇo anaghaḥ ।
mahātapā dīrghatapā ādirdīnānukampanaḥ ।।

savatsarakaro mantraḥ pramāṇaṃ paramaṃ tapaḥ ।
yogī yogamahāvīryo mahāretā haro haraḥ ।।

mahācetāś ca sarvajñaḥ sabījo apaharo haraḥ ।
kamaṇḍaludharo dhanvī prāṇahastaḥ pratāpavān ।।

aṃśo anīśas tathā śūlī khaṭvāṅgī paṭṭiśī tathā ।
śuciś ca śucirūpaśca tejastejaskaro nidhiḥ ।।

uṣṇīṣī ca suvaktrāśca udakyo vitanas tathā ।
hariś ca harinetraś ca sutīrthaḥ kṛṣṇa eva ca ।।

śṛgālarūpī sarvārthaḥ śuṇḍīśuddhaḥ kamaṇḍaluḥ ।
ajaś ca gandhamālī ca mṛgarūpī kapālabhṛt ।।

ūrdhvaretā ūrdhvasākṣī ūrdhvabāhurnabhaḥ sthalaḥ ।
trijaṭī ca nivāsaś ca rudraḥ senāpatirvibhuḥ ।।

ahaś caro rātricaraḥ suvāsaśca diśāmpatiḥ ।
rājahā daityahā caiva dhātārūpaguṇātmakaḥ ।।

siṃhaśārdūlarūpaś ca ārdracarmadharo haraḥ ।
kālayogī mahānādaḥ sarvavāsaścatuṣpathaḥ ।।

durvārapretacārī ca bhūtacārī maheśvaraḥ ।
bahubhūto bahudhanaḥ sarvārtho rucirā gatiḥ ।।

nṛtyapriyo nṛtyakartā nartakaś ca balāhakaḥ ।
ghoro mahātapā vāso nityo giridharo nabhaḥ ।।

sahasrabhūto vijñeyo vyavasāyaś ca niścayaḥ ।
amarṣo marṣaṇo dakṣo dakṣakratuvināśanaḥ ।।

dakṣayajñāpahārī ca sumaho madhyamas tathā ।
tejo apahārī balihā muditaś cārcito bhavaḥ ।।

gambhīraghoṣo gambhīro gabhīro havyavāhanaḥ ।
nyagrodharūpo nyagrodhaṛkṣavarṇaḥ prabhur vibhuḥ ।।

tīkṣṇabāṇaś ca haryakṣo maheśaḥ karmakālavit ।
dīkṣaḥ prasādito yajñaḥ samudro vaḍavānalaḥ ।।

hutāśaś ca hṛtāśāsyaḥ prasannātmā hṛtāśanaḥ ।
mahātejāḥ sutejāś ca vijayo jaya eva ca ।।

jyotiṣāmayanaṃ siddhiḥ sandhirvigraha eva ca ।
śikhī daṇḍī jaṭī jvālī mūrtodo durbalo bahiḥ ।।

vaiṇavī pāpavetālaḥ kālāgniḥ kāladaṇḍakaḥ ।
nakṣatravigraho vṛddhirajo gandhavaho agrajaḥ ।।

prajāpatir harir bāhurvibhāgaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ ।
vimocanaḥ suragaṇo hiraṇyakavaco bhavaḥ ।।

arajo dhūlidhārī ca mahācārī śrutaśravāḥ ।
anādiḥ sarvabhūtādiḥ sarvasyādyaḥ pitā guruḥ ।।

vyālarūpo mahāvāsī hīnamālī taraṅgavit ।
tripadas tryambako avyaktaḥ sarvabandhavimocakaḥ ।।

sāṃkhyaprasādo durvāsāḥ sarvasādhuniṣevitaḥ ।
praskandano vibhāgaś ca tulyo yajñavibhāgavit ।।

sarvavāsī sarvacārī durvāsā bhairavo yamaḥ ।
himo himakaro yajñaḥ sarvadhātā budhottamaḥ ।।

lohitākṣo mahākṣaś ca vijayākhyo viśāradaḥ ।
saṃgraho vigrahaḥ karma sarpa rājavibhūṣaṇaḥ ।।

mukhyo vimuktadehaś ca dehacārī ca kardamaḥ ।
sarvācāraḥ prasādaś ca khecaro balarūpadhṛk ।।

ākāśavṛttirūpaś ca nipāta uragaḥ khalaḥ ।
raudrarūpaḥ surādityo vasuraśmiḥ suvarcasaḥ ।।

vasuvego mahāvego manovego niśācaraḥ ।
sarvāvāsaḥ śriyāvāsa āpadīśakalo haraḥ ।।

munir ātmagatir lokaḥ sahasravadano vibhuḥ ।
yakṣī ca yakṣarājaś ca śyeno dīptir viśāmpatiḥ ।।

unmado madanākāro apy arthānarthakaro mahān ।
siddhayogo apahārī ca siddhaḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ ।।

bhikṣuś ca bhikṣurūpaś ca vibhuḥ ṣaṇṇāṃ mṛdutvacaḥ ।
mahāseno viśākhaś ca yaṣṭibhāgo gavāmpatiḥ ।।

vajrahastaś ca viṣṭambhir viṣṭhaḥ stambhana eva ca ।
ṛkṣo ripukaraḥ kālo madhurmadhukalocanaḥ ।।

vācaspatyo vājaseno naiṣṭhaścāśramasūcakaḥ ।
brahmacārī lokacārī sarvacārī suratnavit ।।

īśāna īśvaraḥ kālo niśācārī tvam ekadhṛk ।
amitaścāprameyaś ca nadīnadakaro avyayaḥ ।।

nandīśvaraḥ sunandī ca nandano nandavarddhanaḥ ।
nāgahāro vihārī ca kālo brahmavidāṃ varaḥ ।।

caturmukho mahāliṅgaścaturliṅgas tathaiva ca ।
liṅgādhyakṣaḥ suradhyakṣo kālādhyakṣo yugāvahaḥ ।।

umāpatirumākānto jāhnavī dhṛtimān varaḥ ।
sarvārthaḥ sarvabhūtārtho nityaḥ sarvavrataḥ śuciḥ ।।

yo na brahmādibhir devo jāyate na maharṣibhiḥ ।
stotavyaḥ sa kathaṃ nātha paramātmā parātparaḥ ।।

jihvācāpalyam asmākaṃ kṣamasva parameśvara ।
śivaṃ kuruṣva devānāṃ svargyāṇāṃ puṣṭivardhanam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śrutvā stotramidaṃ devaḥ śrīmān dvīpeśvaraḥ śivaḥ ।
prasannabravīd devān prārthayadhvaṃ varaṃ surāḥ ।।

devā ūcuḥ
yadi tuṣṭo maheśāno devānāṃ varadaḥ prabhuḥ ।
tad vināśāya daityānāṃ trātā bhava maheśvara ।।

pāpakarmādhamaś caiva pañcaliṅgāni yo arcayet ।
so api tāṃ gatim āpnoti durlabhā yā mahāmakhaiḥ ।।

śakreṇābhivṛtas tatra devadeva umāpatiḥ ।
purā nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa surāsuranamaskṛtaḥ ।।

śivaprasādasampanno devarājas tato abhavat ।
dhanadena stutas tatra devo lakṣeśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।।

mokṣadā nāma gaurīṃ ca tāṃ devīṃ viddhi bhārata ।
mokṣeśvaraṃ siddhaliṅgaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam ।।

siddhair vidyādharair yakṣair gandharvaiḥ kinnarair naraiḥ ।
devatvaṃ samanuprāptaṃ pañcaliṅgasamarcanāt ।।

kubero mārutaś caiva varuṇo nirṛtis tathā ।
vaivasvato yamaś caiva tataś ca narakeśvaraḥ ।।

tasya liṅgasya māhātmyāt sūryaputro mahāyaśāḥ ।
anyair abhiṣṭutas tatra pūrvaṃ dvīpeśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।।

bhaktyā nāmasahasreṇa stutaḥ pūjyatamaḥ śivaḥ ।
somenāto abhavat tatra śambhoḥ śirasi bhūṣaṇam ।।

rohiṇyā abhyarcitā gaurī subhagā tena sābhavat ।
ṛkṣair yogatarais tadvat stuto devaḥ pinākadhṛk ।।

tatas tair bhāskareṇaiva tabhaḥ sthalamalaṃ kṛtam ।
vyādhayaḥ kālamṛtyuś ca citraguptaś ca lekhakaḥ ।।

tathā śakraḥ suragaṇair etaiḥ parivṛtaḥ prabhuḥ ।
pāpiṣṭhānāṃ mahāraudro dharmiṣṭhānāṃ prasādavān ।।

koṭyo aṣṭau cordhvakeśā raudrāś ca vikṛtānanāḥ ।
pativratāsahasraiś ca tathā māsopavāsibhiḥ ।।

kilkilāravaśabdaiś ca dharmarājapurottamam ।
vyāptaṃ tu paritaḥ śrīmadasaṃkhyātair manoramaiḥ ।।

śrutvā teṣāṃ ravaṃ sārddhaṃ dharmarājaḥ sabhāsadaiḥ ।
śvetavastraparīdhānaḥ śvetamālyānulepanaḥ ।।

pādacārī gataḥ kṣipraṃ yatra te yānasaṃsthitāḥ ।
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā papraccha śubhakarmaṇaḥ ।।

yathā śaktena yogena dharmaṃ dharmottaraṃ mahat ।
kasmād deśāt samāyātāḥ kathaṃ puṇyamupārjitam ।।

vimānārūḍhā ūcuḥ
kurukṣetre tapas taptaṃ gaṅgāyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
sarveṣām eva lokānāṃ dvāraṃ taddhi pratiṣṭhitam ।।

dharmādharmaṃ tava balaṃ kāraṇaṃ ceti tattvataḥ ।
vārāṇasī prayāgaś ca gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgamaḥ ।।

pitṛtīrthaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ puṣkaraṃ naimiṣaṃ tathā ।
kedāraṃ bhairavaṃ caiva tathā rudramahālayam ।।

sarasvatīrudrakoṭiḥ prabhāsaṃ śaśibhūṣaṇam ।
nānātīrthasahasreṣu dānayajñatapaḥ kṛtam ।।

etat te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ sūryaputramahāyaśaḥ ।
anye dṛṣṭvā yathā nyāyaṃ dharmarājaṃ tatas tathā ।।

ūcuḥ sarve vacaḥ ślakṣṇaṃ dharmarājaṃ yathoditam ।
na tvaṃ prabhuḥ sukṛtināṃ brahmā viṣṇuḥ śivaḥ prabhuḥ ।।

pāpakarmaratā ye tu teṣāṃ śāstā yamaḥ svayam ।

yama uvāca gatvā kailāsamāyāmi yāvat tāvat pratīkṣatām ।।

evam uktvā yayau rājan kailāsaṃ sa nagottamam ।
yasmin śivādyās te sarve pārvatī ṣaṇmukhas tathā ।।

stuvanti devatāḥ sarvādevadevam umāpatim ।
nṛtyanti cāgrataḥ kecid utpatya nipatanti ca ।।

taṃ dṛṣṭvā tādṛśaṃ śambhuṃ stuvantaṃ dīptatejasam ।
stuvannāmasahasreṇa devadevaṃ pinākinam ।।

sāṣṭāṅgaṃ ca namaskṛtya dharmarājo abravīd idam ।
ye asmatpurīṃ samāyātās teṣāṃ kā gatir ucyate ।।

prahasann abravīd devo dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।
atra prayāntu te sarve ye revātīravāsinaḥ ।।

anyatīrthanivāsā ye bhogān bhuñjantu te divi ।
śivavākyaṃ tataḥ śrutvā brahmāviṣṇur yathātatham ।।

tuṣṭā devasya vākyena sarvadevagaṇeśvaruḥ ।
āgataḥ kṣaṇamātreṇa dharmarājaḥ purottamam ।।

śivoktāḥ preṣitāḥ sarve śivalokaṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।
yathā yathā samādiṣṭās tato anye api śūbhānvitāḥ ।।

purākalpe mayā dṛṣṭaṃ kārttikyāṃ devatāgame ।
tato gacchen mahārāja vaiṣṇavaṃ tīrthamuttamam ।।

kokilā nāma vikhyātaṃ sarvapāpavimokṣaṇam ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ kṣetramity āha devadevo janārdanaḥ ।।

sapādakoṭistīrthānāṃ tatrāste caiva bhārata ।
upoṣyaikādaśīṃ puṇyāṃ dīpamālāṃ prabodhayet ।।

na tasya punarāvṛttir martyaloke durāsade ।
sarvakāmasamṛddhena vimānāgreṇa bhārata ।।

asaṃkhyakālikā tṛptiḥ pitṝṇāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
vipre ca toṣite tatra dānasaṅkhyā na vidyate ।।

atrāntare tyajet prāṇānavaśaḥ svavaśo api vā ।
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi rājā vaidyādhare pure ।।

dhruvo dhruvatvaṃ svarge tu tārātejaḥ samujjvalan ।
martyayoniṣu sambhūtā bhūtagrāmā tathāpare ।।

arcanrāḍ devadevasya divi devatvam āpnuvan ।
devapuṇyakṣaye martyā bhaktyā puṇyaiś ca devatāḥ ।।

svargamartyaprabhedo ayaṃ dharmādharmaprabhedataḥ ।
kenāpi tatprakāreṇa pūjanīyo maheśvaraḥ ।।

yad vā tad vā śive deyaṃ bhaktiyuktena cetasā ।
arundhatyā sā bharaṇyā sāvitryā ca tathā tathā ।।

ahalyayā menakayā marutvatyā ca rambhayā ।
apsarogaṇasaṅghaiś ca surasiddhagaṇais tathā ।।

narmadātaṭam āśritya pūjito yena śaṅkaraḥ ।
tena vai vipulā bhogāḥ prāptā mokṣaś ca bhārata ।।

na pūjayed dharaṃ yas tu śivamāyāvimohitaḥ ।
na tasya svargamokṣau ca kailāsaṃ prati kā kathā ।।

na ca svargasya rājyasya bhājanaṃ ca narādhipa ।
sarvatīrthamayī revā sarvadevamayo haraḥ ।।

sarvadharmamayī buddhiḥ kṣamāsatyam ayaṃ tapaḥ ।
brahmacaryaṃ tapomūlaṃ pañcendriyavinigrahaḥ ।।

kṣamā satyaṃ japo adhītaṃ tapaḥ saṃyamalakṣaṇam ।
etat te kathitaṃ rājaṃ śivena kathitaṃ purā ।।

mayā ca tava rājendra bhrātṝṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
na sāmānyatarā devī kathitā yā mayā tava ।।

dvīpeśvaraḥ kapileśvaras tathā vai narakeśvaraḥ ।
etān devān samutthāya yathāvat parikīrtayet ।।

sarvatīrthaphalaṃ prāpya śivaloke mahīyate ।
aghaughe ca parikṣīṇe prāpyate saptakalpagā ।।

śivaḥ saṃnihito yasyāṃ śivakṣetraṃ tataḥ param ।
śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya śivaloke mahīyate ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe dvīpeśvaravarṇano nāmaikasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadāsaṅgamaṃ puṇyaṃ surasiddhaniṣevitam ।
tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti pūjayitvā maheśvaram ।।

āgacchantī purā loke narmadā bharatarṣabha ।
stutā pūrvaṃ namaskṛtya devair brahmarṣibhis tathā ।।

tvayā pavitritaṃ puṇyaṃ martyalokaṃ carācaram ।
apāṃ rūpagatā revā harasya paramā kalā ।।

umā kātyāyanī gaṅgā yamunā ca sarasvatī ।
cāmuṇḍā carcikā devī revā tvaṃ saptakalpagā ।।

śivajā pravahā puṇyā mekalādrisutā stutā ।
yajñayūpā ca mūrdhā ca svargamokṣapradā tathā ।।

tāriṇī sarvabhūtānāṃ pāpaghnī ca taraṅgiṇī ।
lakṣmīḥ svāhā svadhā caiva puruhūtā yaśasvinī ।।

tvayā vyāptaṃ jagatkṛtsnam apāṃ rūpeṇa suvrate ।
saṅgamaṃ siddhaliṅgaṃ ca surāsuranamaskṛtam ।।

atra dattaṃ hutaṃ sarvam etad bhavati cākṣayam ।
atyadbhutaṃ mahārāja narmadāsnānam arcanam ।।

anekāni sahasrāṇi vimānāni yudhiṣṭhira ।
nānāratnaprabhājālaiḥ sūryakoṭisamāni ca ।।

gatāni dharmarājasya purīṃ vīṇādiniḥ svanaiḥ ।
nādayanti divaṃ bhūmiṃ vedanirghoṣaṇādibhiḥ ।।

ekasmin samaye dṛṣṭvāścaryaṃ vaivasvato nṛpaḥ ।
atriś caiva vaśiṣṭhaś ca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ ।।

ityādyāḥ sapta munayo dharmādharmavicārakāḥ ।
śivena sthāpitāḥ pūrvaṃ hariṇā brahmaṇā tathā ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
akṣīṇakarmabandhus tu puruṣo munisattama ।
paraṃ padam avāpnoti tan me kathaya kalpaga ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
viṣṇunā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇe ca mahātmane ।
prapadye puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim ।।

lokanāthaṃ sahasrākṣam akṣaraṃ paramaṃ padam ।
bhagavantaṃ prapadye ahaṃ bhūtabhavyabhavatprabhum ।।

sraṣṭāraṃ sarvabhūtānām anantabalapauruṣam ।
padmanābhaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ prapadye satyam avyayam ।।

hiraṇyagarbhaṃ bhūgarbham amṛtaṃ viśvatomukham ।
anaśvaramanāthaṃ ca prapadye bhāskaradyutim ।।

sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ tārkṣyavāhanam ।
prapadye sūkṣmam acalaṃ vareṇyam abhayapradam ।।

nārāyaṇaṃ hariṃ caiva yogātmānaṃ sanātanam ।
śaraṇyaṃ sarvalokānāṃ prapadye dhruvamīśvaram ।।

yaḥ prabhuḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yena sarvam idaṃ tatam ।
yaḥ saṃhārakaro devaḥ sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu ।।

yasmāj jātaḥ purā brahmā padmayoniḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
prasīdatu sa me viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaparaḥ prabhuḥ ।।

purā laye tu saṃprāpte naṣṭe loke carācare ।
ekas tiṣṭhati yogātmā sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu ।।

jayed yaḥ pṛthivīṃ satyaṃ kālo dharmaḥ kriyāphalam ।
gaṇākāraḥ sa tāṃ vāco vāsudevaḥ prasīdatu ।।

yogāvāsa namastubhyaṃ sarvāvāsa varaprada ।
yajñabhogin pañcabhogin nārāyaṇa namo astu te ।।

caturmūrte jagaddhāma lakṣmīvāsa varaprada ।
viśvāvāsa namaste astu sākṣībhūta jagatpate ।।

ajeyaḥ ṣaḍvibhāgaikaviśvamūrtir vṛṣākapiḥ ।
mṛgādhipaś ca kālaś ca namas te jñānasāgara ।।

avyaktādaṇḍam utpannam avyaktād aparaḥ prabhuḥ ।
yasmāt parataraṃ nāsti tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।।

cintayanto hi yaṃ nityaṃ brahmeśānādayaḥ prabhum ।
ekāṃśena jagatsarvaṃ yo viṣṭabhya vibhuḥ sthitaḥ ।।

agrāhyo nirguṇaḥ śāstā tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
divākarasya somasya madhye jyotir iva sthitam ।।

kṣetrajña iti yaṃ prāhuḥ sa mahātmā prasīdatu ।
sāṃkhyayogena ye cānye siddhāś caiva maharṣayaḥ ।।

yaṃ viditvā vimucyante sa mahātmā prasīdatu ।
namaste sarvatobhadra sarvato akṣiśiromukha ।।

nirvikāra namaste astu ādikalpa hṛdi sthita ।
atīndriya namastubhyaṃ paramātman namo astu te ।।

ye ca tvām abhijānanti saṃsāre na vasanti te ।
rāgadveṣavinirmuktā lobhamohavivārjitāḥ ।।

aśarīraḥ suguptaḥ san sarvadeheṣu tan mayaḥ ।
avyaktabuddhy ahaṃkāramahābhūtendriyāṇi ca ।।

tvayi tāni na teṣu tvaṃ te ca tāni na tu svayam ।
avyakto nātikūṭastho guṇānāṃ prabhurīśvaraḥ ।।

āvarto hetur ahitaḥ prabhuḥ svātmavyavasthitaḥ ।
namaste puṇḍarīkākṣa vāsudeva namo astu te ।।

īśvaro asi jagannātha kim ataḥ paramucyate ।
bhaktānāṃ muktidas tvaṃ ca guruś ca tridaśeśvaraḥ ।।

same bhūtapatis tvaṃ hi prabhur janmani janmani ।
ahaṃkāreṇa baddho vā tathā sattvādibhir gaṇaiḥ ।।

pṛthivīṃ yātu me ghrāṇaṃ yātu me rasanājalam ।
cakṣurhutāśanaṃ yātu sparśo me yātu mārutam ।।

śabdaś cākāśam āyātu mano vai kāraṇaṃ tathā ।
ahaṃkāraś ca me buddhiṃ tvayi buddhir mamāstv iti ।।

viyogaḥ sarvakaraṇair guṇair bhūtais tathā astu me ।
sattvaṃ rajastamaś caiva prakṛtiṃ svāṃ viśantu me ।।

prabhoḥ prabhumanavadyaṃ prapadye ahaṃ naraḥ prabhum ।
sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ maharṣiṃ bhūtabhāvanam ।।

brahmayoniś ca viśvasya sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu ।
brahmapatnyāṃ pralīyante naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ।।

āhūtasaṃplave caiva līyate prakṛtau mahat ।
hūyate ca punas tābhyāṃ sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu ।।

agnisomārkadevānāṃ brahmarudrendrayoginām ।
yaste jayati tejāṃsi sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu ।।

ajastvaṃ jagataḥ panthā amūrtirvīśvamūrtijit ।
navaṃ pradhānaṃ ca mahān puruṣaś cetano alasaḥ ।।

agopyo yaḥ parataras tam eva śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
somasūryopamas tejo yo avatārayati svayam ।।

vijāyante diśo yasmāt sa mahātmā prasīdatu ।
guṇavān nirguṇaś caiva cetano acetano svagaḥ ।।

sūkṣmaḥ sarvagato dehaḥ sa mahātmā prasīdatu ।
sūryamadhye sthitaḥ somas tasya madhye tu saṃsmṛtaḥ ।।

bhūtatvād yo acalo dīptaḥ sa mahātmā prasīdatu ।
ekatvāt tava nānātvaṃ ye viduryānti te param ।।

samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu pradveṣyātmajanapriyaḥ ।
samaṃ bhajaty anākāṅkṣī bhajate nānyacetasaḥ ।।

yo ayaṃ sarvātmanā jñeyaḥ sa me viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu ।
carācaram idaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtagrāmaṃ caturvidham ।।

tvayi taṃ tantuvat protaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇā iva ।
na te dharmo hy adharmo asti na garbho janma vā punaḥ ।।

jarājanmavimokṣārthaṃ tam eva śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
indriyāṇi guṇaś caiva śvāsocchvāsaś ca yoniṣu ।।

kevalaṃ dāruvad dehaṃ naśyaṃ yat paramāpadam ।
svayam ekākibhāvo me janmato atra punarbhavaḥ ।।

tvad buddhis tvad gataprāṇā tvad bhaktas tvat parāyaṇaḥ ।
tvām evāhaṃ smariṣyāmi maraṇe paryupasthite ।।

pūrvadehe kṛtā ye tu vyādhayaḥ praviśantu mām ।
vātādayaś ca duḥkhāni ṛṇaṃ tan muñcatāt prabho ।।

śreyasāṃ ca paraṃ śreyas tv anyeṣāṃ ca yaśasvinām ।
sarvapāpaviśuddhyarthaṃ puṇyaṃ yatparamaṃ padam ।।

prātar utthāya satataṃ madhyāhne ca dinakṣaye ।
ajasraṃ ca tathā japyaṃ sarvapāpopaśāntidam ।।

hariṃ kṛṣṇaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ vāsudevaṃ janārdanam ।
praṇato asmi jagannāthaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।।

govardhanadharaṃ devaṃ gobrāhmaṇahite ratam ।
praṇato asmi gadāpāṇiṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।।

śaṅkhinaṃ cakriṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ śārṅgiṇaṃ madhusūdanam ।
praṇato asmi patiṃ lakṣmyāḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।।

dāmodaraṃ mudā yuktaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam avyayam ।
praṇato asmi sthitaṃ sthityai sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।।

nārāyaṇaṃ naraṃ saumyaṃ mādhavaṃ ca janārdanam ।
śrīvatsaṃ śrīvapuḥ śrīmac chrīdharaṃ śrīniketanam ।।

praṇato asmi śriyaḥ kāntaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।
yam īśaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dhyāyanti ca tamakṣaram ।।

vāsudevamanirdeśyaṃ tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
sarvabandhavinirmukto yaṃ praviśya punarbhavam ।।

puruṣo naiva prāpnoti tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
kṛtvā brahmavapuḥ sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।।

yaḥ karoti punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ tam asmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
brahmarūpadharaṃ devaṃ yonirūpaṃ janārdanam ।।

sṛṣṭitve saṃsthitaṃ nityaṃ praṇato asmi janārdanam ।
yasmān nānyat paraṃ kiṃcid yasmin sarvam idaṃ jagat ।।

yaḥ sarvamadhyago anantaḥ sarvagaṃ taṃ namāmy aham ।
yo asti bhūteṣu sarveṣu sthāvare jaṅgameṣu ca ।।

viṣṇur eva sa vai pāpaṃ mamāśeṣaṃ praṇaśyatu ।
na vṛttaṃ nirvṛtaṃ karma viṣṇor yatkarma vā kṛtam ।।

anekajanmakarmotthaṃ pāpaṃ naśyati me tathā ।
niśāyāṃ ca tathā prātar madhyāhṇe cāparāhṇayoḥ ।।

ajñānāc ca kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ karmaṇā manasā girā ।
yatkṛtaṃ cāśubhaṃ kiṃcit tatsarvaṃ naśyatu kṣaṇāt ।।

tatsarvaṃ vilayaṃ yātu toyeṣu lavaṇaṃ yathā ।
parapīḍāṃ ca nindāṃ ca kurvato janma nārjitam ।।

paradravyaparakṣetravāñchā krodhodbhavaṃ ca yat ।
tatsarvaṃ vilayaṃ yātu toyeṣu lavaṇaṃ yathā ।।

viṣṇave vāsudevāya haraye keśavāya ca ।
janārdanāya kṛṣṇāya namo bhūyo namo namaḥ ।।

nābhāgo nāma rājarṣir narmadātīrasaṅgame ।
cakāra stotram atulaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tu prajāpatiḥ ।।

brahmaṇo aṅgirasā prāptaṃ tasmād indreṇa bhārata ।
vaśiṣṭhaḥ śrāvayāmāsa nābhāgaṃ rājasattamam ।।

snātvā ca narmadātoye dattvā dānāny anekaśaḥ ।
kāmikaṃ yānamāruhya nābhāgaḥ svapurīṃ yayau ।।

stauti nāmasahasreṇa yaḥ stavena janārdanam ।
na tasya punarāvṛttirghore saṃsārasāgare ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe viṣṇustutirnāma dvisaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchec ca rājendra meghanādam iti smṛtam ।
jalamadhye mahādevo yatra tiṣṭhaty adarśitaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
jalamadhye mahādevas tiṣṭhate kena hetunā ।
uttaraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ kūlaṃ varjayitvā dvijottama ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
etad ākhyānam atulaṃ puṇyaṃ śrutisukhāvaham ।
purāṇe yacchrutaṃ tāta tat te vakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ ।।

purā tretāyuge tāta paulastyo devakaṇṭakaḥ ।
trilokavijayī raudraḥ surāsurabhayaṃkaraḥ ।।

devadānavayakṣāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām ।
avadhyo varadānena yatra paryaṭate mahīm ।।

tatra devagirau ramye dānavo baladarpitaḥ ।
mayo nāmeti vikhyāto mahānāsīn nṛpeśvara ।।

rāvaṇas taṃ tato gatvā vinayāvanataḥ sthitaḥ ।
pūjito dānasaṃmānair mayaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।

kasyeyaṃ padmapatrākṣī pūrṇacandranibhānanā ।
kiṃ nāmadheyā tapate tapa ugraṃ kathaṃ vibho ।।

maya uvāca
dānavānāṃ patiḥ śreṣṭho mayo ahaṃ nāmanāmataḥ ।
bhāryā tejavatī nāma mameyaṃ tanayā śubhā ।।

mandodarīti vikhyātā tapate patikāraṇāt ।
śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tasya rāvaṇo madadarpitaḥ ।।

praśritaḥ praṇato bhūtvā mayaṃ vacanam abravīt ।
paulastyo nāma rājāhaṃ devadānavadarpahā ।।

prārthayāmi mahābhāga sutāṃ tvaṃ dātum arhasi ।
jñātvā paitāmahaṃ vaṃśaṃ mayenāpi mahātmanā ।।

sutā dattā rāvaṇāya kṛtvā vidhividhānataḥ ।
gṛhītvā tāṃ tadā rakṣaḥ pūjyamāno niśācaraiḥ ।।

divyair yānair vimānaiś ca krīḍate tu tayā saha ।
putraṃ putravatāṃ śreṣṭho janayāmāsa bhārata ।।

tenaiva jātamātreṇa ravo mukto mahātmanā ।
saṃvartakasya meghasya yena loko jaḍīkṛtaḥ ।।

śrutvā tanninadaṃ ghoraṃ trasto lokapitāmahaḥ ।
nāma cakre tadā tasya meghanādo bhaviṣyati ।।

etan nāmakṛtaṃ so api paramaṃ vratam āsthitaḥ ।
bhāvayāmāsa deveśam umayā saha śaṅkaram ।।

vratair niyamadānaiś ca homair jāpyairvidhānataḥ ।
kṛcchracāndrāyaṇair divyaiḥ kliśyate ca kalevaram ।।

evam anyad dine tāta kailāsaṃ dharaṇīdharam ।
gatvā liṅgam ayaṃ prāpya prasthito dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ।।

narmadātaṭam āśritya snātukāmo mahābalaḥ ।
nikṣipyāpūjayad devaṃ kṛtvā jāpyaṃ janeśvaraḥ ।।

gantukāmaḥ paraṃ mārgaṃ laṅkāyāṃ nṛpasattama ।
ekaṃ samuddhṛtaṃ liṅgaṃ gṛhitaṃ savyapāṇinā ।।

prathamaṃ ca dvitīyaṃ ca bhaktyā paulastyanandanaḥ ।
tadā devamahāliṅgaṃ patitaṃ narmadāmbhasi ।।

pāhi pāhīti tenokto liṅgena parameṣṭhinā ।
dvitīyaṃ patitaṃ tāvad uttare narmadātaṭe ।।

meghanādeti vikhyātaṃ liṅgaṃ tatra suśobhanam ।
madhyameśvaranāmeti jalamadhye vyavasthitam ।।

yāvad uddhartukāmo asau saptapātālam āgamat ।
devayor niścayaṃ jñātvā nivṛtto asau niśācaraḥ ।।

jagāmākāśam āviśya pūjyamāno niśācaraiḥ ।
tadā prabhṛti tattīrthaṃ meghanādeti viśrutam ।।

meghāraveti vikhyātam uttare kheṭakaḥ śubhaḥ ।
pūrve tu garjanaṃ nāma sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram ।।

tasmiṃs tīrthe tu rājendra yas tu snānaṃ samācaret ।
ahorātroṣito bhūtvā sa labhecchāśvataṃ śubham ।।

piṇḍadānaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃs tīrthe narādhipa ।
tena dvādaśa varṣāṇi pitaras tarpitā divi ।।

yas tu bhojayate viprāṃs tasmiṃs tīrthe narādhipa ।
yatphalaṃ yogināṃ tatra labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

agniveśaṃ jale vāpi athavāpi hy anāśakam ।
anivartikā gatis tasya syād idaṃ śaṅkaro abravīt ।।

evaṃ te naraśārdūla garjiteśvaram uttamam ।
kathitaṃ smaraṇād eva sarvapāpakṣayaṃ karam ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe meghanādeśvaramahimānuvarṇano nāma trisaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchec ca rājendra dārutīrtham anuttamam ।
dāruko yatra saṃsiddhim indrasya dayitaḥ sakhā ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
dārukeṇa kathaṃ tāta tapaścīrṇaṃ purā anagha ।
vidhānaṃ śrotum icchāmi sarvapāpakṣayaṃ karam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ahaṃ te kathayiṣyāmi vicitraṃ yat purātanam ।
vṛttaṃ samabhavat tatra ṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।।

sūto vajradharasyāsīt mātalirnāmanāmataḥ ।
sa putraṃ śaptavān pūrvaṃ kathaṃcit kāraṇāntare ।।

śāpahetor vepamāna indrasya caraṇau śubhau ।
prapīḍya tatra devendraṃ vijñāpayati bhārata ।।

mama tātābhiśaptasya anāthasya sureśvara ।
karmaṇā kena śāpasya ghorasyānto bhaviṣyati ।।

śakra uvāca
narmadātaṭam āśritya toṣaya tvaṃ maheśvaram ।
tiṣṭha yāvad yugasyāntaṃ punarjananam āpsyasi ।।

punarbhūtvā yadukule dāruko nāma nāmataḥ ।
ārohayitvā deveśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।।

mānuṣaṃ tatra sampannaṃ tataḥ siddhim avāpsyasi ।
evam uktas tu devena sahasrākṣeṇa bhārata ।।

praṇamya śirasā bhūmim āgato asau hataprabhaḥ ।
narmadā taṭam āśritya karśitasvakalevaraḥ ।।

vratopavārsair vividhair japahomaparāyaṇaḥ ।
mahādevaṃ mahātmānaṃ varadaṃ śūlapāṇinam ।।

abhajat parayā bhaktyā yāvad āhūtasamplavam ।
aṃśāvataraṇe viṣṇos tato bhūtvā mahāmatiḥ ।।

toṣayitvā jagannāthaṃ tato yātaḥ sa sadgatim ।
eṣa te sambhavas tāta dārutīrthasya suvrata ।।

kathitas tu mayā pūrvaṃ yathā me śaṅkaro abravīt ।
tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā vismayāviṣṭacetanaḥ ।।

bhrānto avalokayāmāsa stabdharomā muhur muhuḥ ।
tasmiṃs tīrthe naraḥ snātvā vidhipūrvaṃ nareśvara ।।

upāsya sabhyāṃ tatraiva saṃtarpya pitṛdevatāḥ ।
dehatyāgaṃ ca tatraiva yaḥ karoti samāhitaḥ ।।

so aśvamedhaphalaṃ prāpya ramate śivasannidhau ।
tasmiṃs tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā bhojayed brāhmaṇaṃ śuciḥ ।।

sa tu viprasahasrasya labhate phalam uttamam ।
snānaṃ dānaṃ tapo homaḥ svādhyāyaḥ pitṛtarpaṇam ।।
yatkṛtaṃ tu śubhaṃ tatra tatsarvaṃ labhate akṣayam ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe dārutīrthatamahimānuvarṇano nāma catuḥsaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchec ca rājendra devatīrtham anuttamam ।
yatra devās trayastriṃśat taptvā siddhiṃ parāṃ gatāḥ ।।

purā devāsure yuddhe dānavair baladarpitaiḥ ।
indro devagaṇaiḥ sārddhaṃ svarājyāc cyāvito bhṛśam ।।

hastyaśvarathayānaughair mardayitvā ca vāhinīm ।
viśaktā bhejire mārgaṃ prahārair jarjarīkṛtāḥ ।।

jambhaśumbhaniśumbhādyais tu huṇḍagrahakaiḥ saha ।
balibhir bādhitāḥ sarve brahmāṇam upatasthire ।।

praṇamya śirasā devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ parameṣṭhinam ।
vyajñāpayanta deveśam indrāgnikapurogamāḥ ।।

paśya paśya mahābhāga dānavair ākulīkṛtāḥ ।
bādhitāḥ putradārābhyāṃ tvām eva śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।।

paritrāyasva deveśa sarvalokapitāmaha ।
nānyā gatiḥ sureśāna muktvā tvāṃ parameṣṭhinam ।।

brahmovāca
dānavānāṃ vighātārthaṃ narmadātaṭam āśritāḥ ।
tapaḥ kuruta bho devās tapo hi paramaṃ balam ।।

nānyopāyo na vai mantro na vidyā na ca vikramaḥ ।
vinā revājalaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃ karam ।।

dāridryavyādhimaraṇabandhanavyasanāni ca ।
etāni caiva pāpasya phalānīti matir mama ।।

evaṃ jñātvā vidhānena tapaḥ kuruta duṣkaram ।
pūjyate śāmbhavaṃ sarvaiḥ prāpnuyātābhayaṃ tataḥ ।।

tacchrutvā vacanaṃ devā brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।
narmadāmāgatāḥ sarve tadendrāgnipurogamāḥ ।।

vicerus tatra vipulaṃ tapaḥ paramaduḥsaham ।
sakalpaiḥ paramāṃ rājaṃs tat te siddhim avāpnuvan ।।

tadā prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ devatīrtham iti śrutam ।
gīyate sarvalokeṣu sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram ।।

tatra śraddhātmanā yo api vidhināpi samanvitaḥ ।
snānaṃ samācared bhaktyā sa labhen mauktikaṃ phalam ।।

yas tam arcayate devaṃ sarvadevais tu pūjitam ।
labhate cāśvamedhasya phalaṃ yāgasya cottamam ।।

yas tu bhojayate viprāṃs tasmiṃs tīrthe narādhipa ।
tatra devaśilā ramyā mahāpuṇyādrirvadhinī ।।

saṃnyāsena mṛtānāṃ tu narāṇāmakṣayā gatiḥ ।
agnipraveśaṃ yaḥ kuryād devatīrthe yudhiṣṭhira ।।

rudraloke vaset tāvad yāvad āhūtasamplavam ।
evaṃ snānaṃ japo homaḥ svādhyāyo devatārcanam ।।

sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ vāpi tatra tīrthe akṣayaṃ bhavet ।
etāvad vidhir uddiṣṭā utpattiś caiva bhārata ।।
devatīrthasya caritaṃ sarvatīrtheṣv anuttamam ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe devatīrthamahimānuvarṇano nāma pañcasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tatogacchec ca rājendra guhāvāsīti cottamam ।
yatra siddho mahādevo guhāvāsīti śaṅkaraḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kena kāryeṇa viprendra guhāvāsīti śaṅkaraḥ ।
etad vistarataḥ sarva kathayasva mamānagha ।।

śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ deva sarvaṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca mahāpraśnaḥ kṛto māṃ yo mahāprājña nareśvara ।।

purāṇe vistaro apy asya na śakyo hi mayādhunā ।
vṛddhabhāvāt kathayitum ahaṃ ca bahukālikaḥ ।।

pūrva dāruvane viprā vasanti sma suraiḥ samāḥ ।
brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca vānaprastho yatis tathā ।।

svadharmaniratānāṃ ca kathitaṃ paramaṃ padam ।
tāvadvasantasamaye kasmiṃścit kāraṇāntare ।।

vimānastho mahādevo gamyamānomayā saha ।
dadarśa ca janāvāsaṃ vedadhvaninināditam ।।

agatāgatasaṃvāsaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃ karam ।
taddṛṣṭvā muditāṃ devīṃ harṣagadgadayā girā ।।

uvāca vacanaṃ devo dṛṣṭvā tāpasayoṣitaḥ ।
nānyaṃ devaṃ na vai dharmaṃ dhyāyanti himanandini ।।

etac chrutvā paraṃ vākyaṃ devadevena bhāṣitam ।
kautūhalasamāviṣṭā śaṅkaraṃ punar abravīt ।।

yat tvayoktaṃ mahādeva patidharmaparāstriyaḥ ।
tāsām anaṅgo bhūtvā tvaṃ caritraṃ kṣobhaya prabho ।।

mahādeva uvāca
tvayoktaṃ vacanaṃ devi na caitad rocate priye ।
brāhmaṇā hi mahābhāgā na teṣāṃ vipriyaṃ caret ।।

manyupraharaṇā viprāś cakrapraharaṇo hariḥ ।
cakrāt tīkṣṇataro manyus tasmād vipraṃ na kopayet ।।

na te devā na te lokās te nāgā nāsurās tathā ।
dṛśyante ca tribhir lokair etair uṣṭair na vañcitāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ kṣobhakaraḥ prāyaḥ svargabhogaphalacyutaḥ ।
yeṣāṃ tuṣṭā mahābhāgā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣitidevatāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ dharmas tathārthaś ca kāmo mokṣo na saṃśayaḥ ।
evaṃ jñātvā mahābhāge āgrahastyajyatām ayam ।।

etal lokaviruddhaṃ hi yadīcchasi vaśe sukham ।

devy uvāca nāhaṃ te dayitā deva nāhaṃ te vaśavartinī ।।

anyāyadharṣaṇāṃ cātra sarvāsāṃ kuru suvrata ।
lokāloke mahādeva aśakyaṃ nāsti te vibho ।।

kriyatāṃ mama devaitatparaṃ kautūhalaṃ prabho ।
evam ukto mahādevo devyāḥ priyahite rataḥ ।।

kṛtvā kāpālikaṃ rūpaṃ yayau dāruvanaṃ prati ।
mahāhināṃ jaṭājūṭaṃ niyamya śaśibhūṣaṇaḥ ।।

kaṅkatrāṇaṃ paraṃ kṛtvā tathā sauvarṇakuṇḍale ।
vyāghracarmaparīdhāno hārakeyūrabhūṣitaḥ ।।

nūpurārāvanirghoṣaiḥ kampayaṃś ca vasundharām ।
mahāḍamarughoṣeṇa vīraghaṇṭāninādinā ।।

prabhātasamaye prāpte tatra dāruvanaṃ gata ।
tāvad viprajanaḥ sarvaḥ puṣpamūlaphalāśanaḥ ।।

nirgato bahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ paṭhyamāna itas tataḥ ।
taddṛṣṭvā mahadāścaryarūpaṃ devasya bhārata ।।

yuvatījanaḥ pramattaś ca kāmena kaluṣīkṛtaḥ ।
surūpaṃ paramaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvās tāś ca varānanāḥ ।।

kleśabhāvaṃ tadāgacchan yāś ca dāruvane striyaḥ ।
vikārā bahavas tāsāṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭvā manojavam ।।

saṃjātā viprapatnīnāṃ tāṃ śṛṇuṣva nṛpottama ।
paridhānaṃ na jānanti paribhraṣṭaṃ karodyatāḥ ।।

dātukāmā tathā bhaikṣyaṃ ceṣṭituṃ naiva śakyate ।
kācid dṛṣṭvā mahādevaṃ rūpayauvanagarvitā ।।

utsaṅge saṃsthitaṃ vālaṃ patitaṃ vyasmarat tataḥ ।
kāmabāṇahatā cānyā bāhubhyāṃ pīḍati stanau ।।

niḥśvasantī tathā cānyā na kiṃcit parijalpate ।
evam akṣobhayat sarvā maheśaḥ patidevatāḥ ।।

cālitāstā viditvā tu nirjagmur dvārisatvarāḥ ।
saṃcitāḥ paramaṃ kṛtvā sarvā devo maheśvaraḥ ।।

kṣobhayitvā gaṇaṃ strīṇāṃ gataś cādarśanaṃ ca tam ।
tato vipragaṇaḥ sarvaḥ samāyāto dadarśa ha ।।

kṣobhitaṃ strījanaṃ sarvaṃ hareṇa krodhamāviśat ।
krodhāviṣṭo dvijaḥ kaścid daṇḍam udyamya dhāvati ।।

kuṭhārahasto hy aparas tathānyo darbhamuṣṭimān ।
itaścetaśca te sarve bhramitvā tac ca kānanam ।।

ekībhūtā mahātmāno vyājahuś ca ruṣā giram ।
yadi dattaṃ hutaṃ kiṃcid guravastoṣitā yadi ।।

tena satyena devasya liṅgaṃ patatu bhūtale ।
evaṃ satyaprabhāveṇa vacanena dvijanmanām ।।

devasya paśyato liṅgaṃ patitaṃ dharaṇītale ।
hāhākāro mahānāsīl lokāloke tu bhārata ।।

devasya patitaṃ liṅgaṃ jagaty eva mahākṣayam ।
patamānasya liṅgasya śabdo abhūt tatra dāruṇaḥ ।।

patanti parvatāgrāṇi śoṣam āyānti sāgarāḥ ।
devasya patite liṅge vimānair devadānavāḥ ।।

sametya sahitāḥ sarve brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā ।
kṛtāñjalipuṭā devaṃ stuvanti vividhaiḥ stavaiḥ ।।

tatas tuṣṭo jagannātho devānāṃ varado abhavat ।
devo api patite liṅge śāpena dharaṇītale ।।

gatvā dāruvanaṃ viprāṃs toṣayāmāsa bhārata ।
viśvāmitro vaśiṣṭhādyā jābālir atha kāśyapaḥ ।।

sametya sahitāḥ sarve tam ūcus tripurāntakam ।
mahājano api balavān nāvajñeyaḥ sureśvaraḥ ।।

kṣāntiyukto api bhūtvā ca bhaviṣyasi gataklamaḥ ।
vidhvaṃsitā vipradārā yad etal liṅgam uttamam ।।

patitaṃ te mahādeva etat puṇyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।
tatpuṇyaṃ nāgnihotreṇa agniṣṭomair na labhyate ।।

yaccharma rudra prāpsyanti mānavā liṅgapūjayā ।
devānāṃ caiva yakṣāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām ।।

vacanena tu viprāṇām etat puṇyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।
brahmaviṣṇvindrarudrāṇāṃ darśanena ca yatphalam ।।

tatphalaṃ tasya liṅgasya darśane sakalaṃ labhet ।
evam ukto jagannāthaḥ praṇipatya dvijottamān ।।

mudā paramayā yuktas tāṃś caiva pratyabhāṣata ।
brāhmaṇā jaṅgamaṃ tīrthaṃ nirjalaṃ sarvakāmikam ।।

yeṣāṃ vākyodayenaiva śuddhyanti malanā janāḥ ।
kiṃcit tīrthaṃ na hi kṣetramūṣaraṃ gahvarāṇi ca ।।

brāhmaṇāc chreṣṭham uddiṣṭaṃ yatra gatvā viśuddhyati ।
pṛthivyāṃ yāni tīrthāni gaṅgādyāḥ saritas tathā ।।

ekasyā vipravākyasya kalā nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।
abhinandya dvijān sarvān anujñāto mahānṛṣiḥ ।।

tato agāc ca mahādevo narmadātaṭam uttamam ।
parama vratam āsthāya guhāvāsaṃ mahārbudam ।।

maunaṃ cacāra bhagavāñjapadhyānarataḥ sadā ।
samāpte niyame tāta sthāpayitvā maheśvaram ।।

vandyamānaḥ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ kailāsam agamat prabhuḥ ।
narmadāyās taṭe yena sthāpitaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।

tenaiva kāraṇenāsau narmadeśvaramuttamam ।
yad yad ācarati śreṣṭhas tattad evetaro janaḥ ।।

sa yatpramāṇaṃ kurute lokas tad anuvartate ।
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā vidhinā sujitendriyaḥ ।।

arcayitvā mahādevam aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।
pitṛbhyo dadate yas tu tilapuṣpakuśodakam ।।

trisaptapuruṣās tasya svarge pāṇḍava modante ।
yas tu bhojayate viprān yathāśaktyā narottamaḥ ।।

tasya tīrthaprabhāveṇa dattaṃ bhavati cākṣayam ।
suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ vāpi brāhmaṇebhyo yudhiṣṭhira ।।

dadate toyam āspṛśya so agniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet ।
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ pūjayec ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

narmadeśvaram āsādya avāptaṃ janmanaḥ phalam ।
agniveśe jale vāpi anāśakamṛtaś ca yaḥ ।।

anivartikā gatis tasya yathā me śaṅkaro abravīt ।
etat kīrtayate yas tu narmadeśvaram uttamam ।।
bhaktyā śṛṇoti yo rājann aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe dāruvanaprasaṅge narmadeśvarakīrtanaṃ nāma ṣaṭsaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

tato gacchec ca rājendra kapilātīrtham uttamam ।
snānamātraḥ prasaṅgena narmadeśvarakīrtanam ।।

tasmiṃs tīrthe tu rājendra kapilāṃ yaḥ prayacchati ।
yāvanti romakūpāni tatprasūtikuleṣu ca ।।

tāvanty abdasahasrāṇi viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।
jale vāgnipraveśe vā athavānaśake naraḥ ।।

tatra tīrthe mṛto yas tu na garbhe jāyate kvacit ।
eva hi vidhir uddiṣṭaḥ sakalo nṛpasattama ।।

tīrthasya ca phalaṃ puṇyaṃ kim anyat paripṛcchasi ।
dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ sarvaduḥkhaghnam uttamam ।।

etac chrutvā naro rājan sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।
tato gacchet tu rājendra karañjeśvaram uttamam ।।

tatra siddho mahābhāga daityo vai lokaviśrutaḥ ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca ko asau siddho mahābhāga tatra tīrthe mahātapāḥ ।।

kasya putro atha kiṃkāryaṃ kālaḥ kaḥ kathaya dvija ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca purā cādiyuge rājan mānaso brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।।

vedavedāṅgatattvajño marīcir nāma nāmataḥ ।
tasyā api kaśyapo rājan kālena mahatānagha ।।

putro atha mānaso jātaḥ sākṣād brahmeva cāparaḥ ।
kṣamā damā dayā dānaṃ satyaṃ śaucam athārjavam ।।

marīces tu guṇās tv ete santi bhānti ca bhārata ।
evaṃ guṇagaṇāḥ kīrtiḥ kaśyape dvijasattame ।।

jñātvā prajāpatir dakṣo bhāryārthe svasutāṃ dadau ।
aditir vai danuś caiva tathā hyekādaśā parāḥ ।।

yāsāṃ putrāś ca pautrāś ca jātā bhrātarasaṃkhyakāḥ ।
aditir janayāmāsa putrānindrapurogamān ।।

nāgān pretapiśācāṃś ca patatrīn yakṣarākṣasān ।
siṃhavyāghravarāhāṃś ca anyā ity evam ādayaḥ ।।

jātās tasya mahābāho kaśyapasya prajāpateḥ ।
yais tu lokatrayaṃ vyāptaṃ sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ mahat ।।

tathānyaś ca mahābhāgo danoḥ putro vyajāyata ।
sarvalakṣaṇasampannaḥ karañjo nāma nāmataḥ ।।

baler iva mahābhāga cacāra sumahat tapaḥ ।
vareṇa chandayāmāsa tripurāntakaraḥ prabhuḥ ।।

bhoḥ karañja mahāsattva parituṣṭo asmi te anagha ।
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te yat te manasi vartate ।।

karañja uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo asi me deva tripurāntakara prabho ।
tataḥ putraiś ca pautraiś ca sahitaṃ me dhanaṃ kuru ।।

tathety uktvā mahādeva umayā sahitas tadā ।
vṛṣārūḍho gaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।

gate cādarśanaṃ deve so api daityo mudānvitaḥ ।
svanāmnā ca mahādevaṃ sthāpayitvā gṛhaṃ yayau ।।

tadā prabhṛti tattīrthaṃ karañjeśvaram uttamam ।
snānamātro naro rājan mucyate brahmahatyayā ।।

tasmiṃs tīrthe mahārāja tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ ।
so agniṣṭomasya yatpuṇyaṃ phalaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam ।।
anāśakaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃs tīrthe narottama ।।
athāgnau ca jale prāṇān bhūtale vāpi yas tyajet ।
svarge sa tu vasen nūnaṃ varṣāṇām ayutadvayam ।।

dhanavān sukule cānte jāyate vipule kule ।
vedavedāṅgatattvajñaḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ ।।

rājā vā rājatulyo vā jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
putrapautrasamāyuktaḥ sarvavyādhivivarjitaḥ ।।

etat te sarvamākhyātaṃ yat tvaṃ māṃ paripṛcchasi ।
tīrthasya tu phalaṃ yuktyā sarvadāneṣu bhārata ।।

etat puṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥkhapraṇāśanam ।
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva tīrthamāhātmyam uttamam ।।

yas tu śrāvayate śrāddhe sa tatpitṛparāyaṇaḥ ।
akṣayaṃ tasya sarvaṃ syāc chaṅkaras tv idam abravīt ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe karañjeśvaramahimānuvarṇano nāma saptasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha aṣṭasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchec ca rājendra kuṇḍaleśvaram uttamam ।
yatra siddhiṃ gato devaḥ kuṇḍadhāro nṛpottama ।।

tapaḥ kṛtvā tu vipulaṃ surāsurabhayaṃ karam ।
kuṇḍadhāro mandarasthaḥ krīḍate sa nṛpottama ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kasyānvaye samutpannaḥ kasya putro mahāmatiḥ ।
tapas taptvā suvipulaṃ toṣito yena śaṅkaraḥ ।।

etad vistaratas tāta kathayasva mamānagha ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca purā tretāyuge rājan paulastyo nāma viśravāḥ ।।

upaye me mahābhāga bharadvājasutāṃ nṛpa ।
putraḥ putraguṇairyuktas tasyāṃ jāto dhanaṃ jayaḥ ।।

jātamātraṃ sutaṃ jñātvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।
cakāra nāma suprīta ṛṣidevasamanvitaḥ ।।

yasmād viśravaso jāto mama pautratvam āgataḥ ।
tasmād vaiśravaṇo nāma mayā dattaṃ tavānagha ।।

yaḥ svayaṃ sarvadevānāṃ dhanagoptā bhaviṣyati ।
caturtho lokapālānām akṣayo yakṣapo api vā ।।

yakṣo yakṣādhipaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kuṇḍadhāro abhavat sutaḥ ।
susvaṃrūpavayaḥ prāpya mātāpitroranujñayā ।।

tapaś cakāra vipulaṃ narmadātīram āśritaḥ ।
yatra vyāghreśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ vyāghrakheṭakam uttamam ।।

kuṇḍadhāreṇa tatraiva tapas taptaṃ sudāruṇam ।
grīṣme pañcāgnimadhyastho varṣāsvāsārathāraṇaḥ ।।

śiśire jalamadhyastho vāyubhakṣaḥ śataṃ samāḥ ।
evaṃ varṣaśate pūrṇe ekāṅguṣṭho abhavat tataḥ ।।

cakravad bhramate sūryamabhito bharatarṣabha ।
caturthe pañcame tāvat tutoṣa vṛṣavāhanaḥ ।।

varaṃ vṛṇīṣva he vatsa yat te manasi rocate ।
tad dadāmi na sandehas tapasā toṣito hy aham ।।

kuṇḍadhāra uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo asi me deva varaditsur ihāgataḥ ।
tato mannāmakaṃ liṅgaṃ tīrthaṃ caitad bhavatv iti ।।

tathetyuktvā mahādevaḥ somo antardhānamāgamat ।
jagāmā kāśam āviśya kailāsaṃ dharaṇidharam ।।

gate cādarśana deva so api yakṣo mudānvitaḥ ।
sthāpayāmāsa deveśaṃ kuṇḍaleśvaramuttamam ।।

alaṃkṛtvā gajaṃ dhenuṃ dhūpapuṣpavilepanaiḥ ।
vitānaiś cāmaraiś chatrais tathaiva liṅgapūjanaiḥ ।।

tarpayitvā dvijān samyag annapānādi bhūṣaṇaiḥ ।
prīṇayitvā mahādevaṃ tataḥ svabhavanaṃ yayau ।।

tadā prabhṛti tat tīrthaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam ।
yudhiṣṭhira paraṃ puṇyaṃ kuṇḍaleśvarasaṃjñakam ।।

tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kaścid upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ ।
arcayed devam īśānaṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ vāpi maṇiṃ mauktikam eva ca ।
brāhmaṇebhyo dadātyatra sa mukhyo modate divi ।।

tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā ṛgyajuḥ sāmasu dvijaḥ ।
ṛcam ekāṃ japitvā ca caturvedaphalaṃ labhet ।।

tasmiṃs tīrthe tu godānam annadānam athāpi vā ।
yaḥ prayacchati viprebhyas tatphalaṃ śṛṇu pāṇḍava ।।

yāvanti tasya romāṇi tatprasūtikuleṣu ca ।
tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate ।।

svargavāso bhavet tasya putrapautrasamanvitaḥ ।
tasmiṃs tīrthe mahābhāga vyāghraś caiva pipāsitaḥ ।।

niṣādānāṃ bhayenaiva aṭavyāmaṭati svayam ।
niṣādānāṃ bharyair naṣṭaḥ patito narmadājale ।।

jalapluto mahābhāga liṅgarūpadharo abhavat ।
uktaścākāśavāṇyā vai vyāghreśvaram anuttamam ।।

pūjyaṃ vai triṣu lokeṣu khyātiṃ yāsyaty asaṃśayam ।
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā tal liṅgam arcayet tu yaḥ ।।

brahmahatyādipāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
etat te kathitaṃ rājan kuṇḍaleśvaram uttamam ।।
śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe kuṇḍaleśvaramahimā anuvarṇanonāma aṣṭasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra pippaleśvaram uttamam ।
yatra siddho mahāyogī pippalādo mahātapāḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
pippalādasya caritaṃ śrotumicchāmy ahaṃ prabho ।
māhātmyaṃ tasya tīrthasya yatra siddho mahātapāḥ ।।

kasya putro mahābhāga kimarthaṃ taptavāṃs tapaḥ ।
etad vistarataḥ sarvaṃ kathayasva mamānagha ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
mithilāstho mahābhāga vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।
yājñavalkyaś ca purataś cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ।।

tāpasī tasya bhaginī yājñavalkyasya dhīmataḥ ।
cacāra sāpi tatrasthā śuśrūṣantī mahattapaḥ ।।

tatas tv ekasmin samaye snātāhani rajasvalā ।
antarvāsaṃ kṛtavatī dṛṣṭvā karkaṭakaṃ rahaḥ ।।

yājñavalkyo api tad rātrau paridhānena tena vai ।
svapnaṃ dṛṣṭvātyajac chukraṃ prabhāte anvaiṣayat punaḥ ।।

tata sā brāhmaṇī tāta kim anveṣyasi bhārata ।
kena kāryaṃ tava vibho vadasva mama tattvataḥ ।।

yājñavalkya uvāca
apavitro mayā bhadre svapno dṛṣṭo adya vai niśi ।
śuklaṃ me cātra vastraṃ svaṃ nikṣiptaṃ tan na dṛśyate ।।

tacchrutvā brāhmaṇī vākyaṃ bhītabhītābhavan nṛpa ।
tadvastraṃ tu mayā brahman snātvāntardhānakaṃ kṛtam ।।

tasyās tad vacanaṃ śrutvā hāhetyuktvā mahātapāḥ ।
papāta sahasā bhūmau chinnamūla iva drumaḥ ।।

kim etad iti jalpantam ākāśād vāgvinirgatā ।
toṣayantī ca taṃ vipraṃ provāca nṛpate tadā ।।

nāsya doṣo mayā dṛṣṭas tava caiva śubhavrate ।
tava garbhodayo yena tatra daivaṃ parāyaṇam ।।

na vināśo asya kartavyo yāvat kālasya paryayaḥ ।
tatheti vrīḍitā sā ca durmaneti vimānataḥ ।।

pālayāmāsa taṃ garbhaṃ yāvat putro vyajāyata ।
jātamātraṃ tu taṃ garbhaṃ kathayitvā na kaṃcana ।।

aśvasthavṛkṣamāsādya sotsasarja mahītale ।
yāni sattvāni lokeṣu sthāvarāṇi carāṇi vai ।।

tāni vai pālayantv enaṃ bālakaṃ tyajati sma sā ।
evamuktvā tataḥ sādhvī brāhmaṇī nṛpasattama ।।

yathāgataṃ jagāmātha sāvasthāya muhūrtakam ।
pādau pāṇī vinikṣipya vimṛjya nayane śūbhe ।।

āsyaṃ ca vikṛtaṃ kṛtvā rurodoccairanāthavat ।
tena śabdena vitrastāḥ sthāvarā jaṅgamāś ca ye ।।

akampayat mahīṃ tāta saśailavanakandarām ।
tato jñātvā mahadbhūtaṃ kṣudhāviṣṭaṃ dvijarṣabham ।।

na jahāti nagaś chāyāmārpayac ca tataḥ payaḥ ।
āpyāyitas tatas tena amṛtenaiva bhārata ।
tataḥ sa cintayāviṣṭo nirmame grahagocaram ।।

tena krūrasam ācāraḥ krūradṛṣṭyā nirīkṣitaḥ ।
papāta sahasā bhūmau śanaiścārī śanaiścaraḥ ।।

śanaiścaraṃ bālako api pādenaiva parāmṛśat ।
pīḍitaḥ so api bālena uvāca vacanaṃ tadā ।।

kiṃ mayā apakṛtaṃ vipra pippalāda mahāmune ।
niṣkrāman gagane caiva pātito dharaṇītale ।।

sauriṇāpy evam uktas tu pippalādo mahāmuniḥ ।
krodharūpo abravīd vākyaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva narādhipa ।।

pitṛmātṛvihīnasya bālabhāvasya durmate ।
pīḍāṃ karoṣi kasmāt tvaṃ saure tvam avaśeṣitaḥ ।।

śanaiścara uvāca
krūrasvabhāvasaṃjātā mama dṛṣṭi dvijottama ।
muñca tvaṃ māṃ ca kartāhaṃ yad bravīṣi na saṃśayaḥ ।।

pippalāda uvāca
adya prabhṛtibālānāṃ janmataḥ ṣoḍaśīḥ samāḥ ।
pīḍā tvayā na kartavyā eṣa te samayaḥ paraḥ ।।

evam astv iti taṃ coktvā prajagāma yathāgataḥ ।
devamārgaṃ śanaiścārī praṇamya ṛṣisattamam ।।

tataś cādarśanaṃ tatra gatavān sa mahāgrahaḥ ।
vicintayānaś caikākī krodhena kaluṣīkṛtaḥ ।।

āgneyīṃ hi diśaṃ dhyātvā janayāmāsa pāvakam ।
kṛttvā māṃsaṃ juhāvāgnau kriyāsambhavatattvataḥ ।।

tāvac ca janitā kṛtyā jvālāmālāvibhūṣitā ।
hutabhuksadṛśākārā kiṃkaromīti cābravīt ।।

śoṣayāmi samudraṃ kiṃ cūrṇayāmi ca parvatam ।
bhūmiṃ ca veṣṭayāmīha pātayitvā nabhastalam ।।

kasya mūrdhni patiṣyāmi ghātayāmi ca kaṃ dvija ।
śīghramādiśa me kāryaṃ na kālātikramo bhavet ।।

tasyās tad vacanaṃ śrutvā pippalādo mahātapāḥ ।
krodharaktāntanayana idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।

mahatā krodhavegena mayā tvaṃ cintitā śubhe ।
pitā me yājñavalkyas tu taṃ tvaṃ ghātaya māciram ।।

evamuktā tu sā śīghraṃ sphuṭantīva nabhas talam ।
mithilāstho mahāprājño yatra tepe mahātapāḥ ।।

yāvat paśyati diṅmārgaṃ jvalanārkasamaprabham ।
yājñavalkyo mahātejās tadbhūtaṃ samupasthitam ।।

tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasāyāntīṃ bhītabhīto mahāmuniḥ ।
bhūtenākramito vipro janakaṃ nṛpatiṃ yayau ।।

śaraṇārtham anuprāptaṃ viddhi māṃ nṛpasattama ।
mahābhūtāc ca māṃ rakṣa yadi śaknoṣi mānada ।।

rājovāca
brahmatejobhavam bhūtam anivāryaṃ durāsadam ।
prabhur naivādya śaknomi anyaṃ gaccha mahāmate ।।

tataś cānyaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭhaṃ śaraṇārthī mahātapāḥ ।
jagāma tena caivokta indrasya śaraṇaṃ yayau ।।

devarāja namaste astu mahābhūtāc ca rakṣa mām ।
tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvābravīd indras tadā vacaḥ ।।

na ca śaktaḥ paritrātuṃ brahmatejo hi duḥsaham ।
tataś ca brahmabhavanaṃ brāhmaṇo brahmavittamaḥ ।।

jagāma viṣṇubhavanaṃ śakto api tyaktavān bhayāt ।
tataḥ sa paramodvigno nirāśo jīvite nṛpa ।।

anugamyamāno bhūtena agacchac ca maheśvaram ।
tasya yogabalopeto mahādevasya pāṇḍava ।।

nakhamāṃsāntare lupto yathā devo na paśyati ।
adṛṣṭam agamad bhūtaṃ jvalanārkasamaprabham ।।

muñca muñceti puruṣa muñceśvaram uvāca ha ।
evam ukto mahādevas tena bhūtena bhārata ।।

yogīndraṃ darśayām āsa nakhamāṃsāntare sthitam ।
saṃsthāpya kṛtyāṃ bhūteśo jvalatkālānalaprabhām ।।

uvāca mā bhaistvaṃ vipra mā ca gaccha mahāmune ।
tatas taṃ sūkṣmadehasthaṃ mahādevo abravīd idam ।।

kimasya tvaṃ mahābhūta kartā kṛtya vadasva me ।

kṛtyovāca krodhadīptena deveśa pippalādena cintitā ।।

asya dehe patiṣyāmi ahiṃsyāṃ viddhi māṃ prabho ।
etac chrutvā mahādevo bhūtasya vadanāc cyutam ।।

variṣṭhaṃ bandhayāmāsa yājñavalkyasya ghātakam ।
yogīśvaraṃ taṃ viprendraṃ dattvābhītiṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।।

visarjayitvā devas taṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata ।
preṣayitvā tu taṃ bhūtaṃ pippalādo api durmanāḥ ।।

mātāpitṛvihīnas tu narmadātaṭam āśritaḥ ।
ekaniṣṭho nirāhāro varṣāṇi ṣoḍaśaiva tu ।।

toṣayāmāsa deveśam umayā saha śaṅkaram ।

hara uvāca parituṣṭo asmi te vipra tapasānena suvrata ।।

varaṃ vṛṇīṣva te dadyāṃ manasābhīpsitaṃ śubham ।

pippalāda uvāca yadi me bhagavāṃs tuṣṭo yadi deyo varo mama ।।

atra sannihito deva mama nāmnā ca śaṅkara ।
evam uktas tathety uktvā pippalādaṃ mahāmunim ।।

jagāmādarśanaṃ devo bhūtasaṅghair niṣevitaḥ ।
pippalādo gate deve snātvā tatra mahāmbhasi ।।

sthāpayitvā mahadevaṃ jagāmottaraparvatam ।
tatra tīrthe naro bhaktyā snātvā mantrayuto nṛpa ।।

tarpayitvā pitṝn devān pūjayitvā maheśvaram ।
aśvamedhasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoty anuttamam ।।

mṛto rudrapuraṃ yāti pippaleśvarasannidhau ।
athavā bhojayed viprān pitṝn uddiśya bhaktitaḥ ।।

dvādaśābdasahasrāṇi tṛptā gacchanti sadgatim ।
saṃnyāsena tu yaḥ kaścit tatra tīrthe tanuṃ tyajet ।।

anivartikā gatis tasya yathā me śaṅkaro abravīt ।
etat sarvaṃ samākhyātaṃ yat tvaṃ māṃ paripṛṣṭavān ।।

māhātmyaṃ pippalādasya pippaleśvaram uttamam ।
etat puṇyaṃ pāpaharaṃ dhanyaṃ duḥkhapraṇāśanam ।।
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva sarvapāpapramocanam ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe pippaleśvaramahimānuvarṇano nāmaikonāśītitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra vimaleśvaram uttamam ।
tatra devaśilā ramyā mahādevena bhāṣitā ।।

garjanaṃ kheṭakaṃ nāma tatra devaśilā śubhā ।
tatra snātvā tu yo bhaktyā tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ ।।

tasya te dvādaśābdāni sutṛptā divi moditāḥ ।
tasmiṃs tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā brāhmaṇān pūjayen nṛpa ।।

svalpenāpi hi dānena tasya cānto na vidyate ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca kāni dānāni viprendra śastāni dharaṇītale ।।

yāni dattvā naro bhaktyā mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ maṇiṃ mauktikam eva ca ।।

bhūmidānaṃ tathā gāvo mocayanty aṃśumān naram ।
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ kaścit kurute prāṇasaṃkṣayam ।।

rudraloke vaset tāvad yāvad āhūtasaṃplavam ।
tataḥ puṣkariṇīṃ gacchet kurukṣetrasamāṃ nṛpa ।।

pūrvaṃ puṣkariṇī nāma kurukṣetraṃ kalau smṛtam ।
tatra snātvā yajed devaṃ tejorāśiṃ divākaram ।।

ṛcam ekāṃ japet saumyaḥ sāmavedaphalaṃ labhet ।
yajurvedasya japanaṃ ṛgvedasya tathaiva ca ।।

tryakṣaraṃ vā japen mantraṃ dhyāyamāno divākaram ।
ādityahṛdayaṃ japtvā mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ ।।

tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā vidhinā pūjayed dvijān ।
tasya koṭiguṇaṃ dānaṃ jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

kārtikyāṃ ca tathā mādhyāṃ vaiśākhyāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ ।
amāvāsyāṃ vyatīpāte saṃkrame vaidhṛtau ravau ।।

kurukṣetre naraḥ snātvā rudrasyānucaro bhavet ।
anāśake jale hy agnau pañcāgnau vā tathāpi vā ।।

tasmiṃs tīrthe mṛto yas tu sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śūdro vā nṛpasattama ।।

vihitaṃ karmakurvāṇaḥ sa gacchati satāṃ gatim ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca kiṃ japan mucyate vyādher jñātvā varṇaṃ dvijottama ।।

kiṃ kurvan mucyate prāṇī yāti lokam anāmayam ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca śṛṇu rājann avahita itihāsaṃ purātanam ।।

guhyatīrthe samāsādya brāhmaṇo muktavān yathā ।
purā dvijavaraś cāsīd govindo nāma nāmataḥ ।।

tasya bhāryā susampannā brāhmaṇī ca pativratā ।
tasyāṃ saṃjanayāmāsa putram ekaṃ ca sundaram ।।

sa bāla eva bhavane krīḍate śiśulīlayā ।
kadācid brāhmaṇaśreṣṭhaḥ kāṣṭhamānayituṃ gataḥ ।।

vanān nītvā kāṣṭhabhāraṃ gṛhe paścāc ca kṣiptavān ।
krīḍann āste śiśus tatra kāṣṭhabhāreṇa pīḍitaḥ ।।

mamāra bālakas tatra dvijo na jñātavāṃs tadā ।
brāhmaṇy api tadā tasmai na śaśaṃsa bhayāt tathā ।।
purnadvijaḥ sa govindo vipinaṃ saṃjagāma ha ।।
brāhmaṇy uvāca
rāvaṇo brahmaṇaḥ pautras trailokyaṃ yasya śaṅkate ।
sa hato rāmacandreṇa saputrāmātyabāndhavaḥ ।।

evaṃ putraṃ vinā saukhyaṃ martye nāke na vidyate ।
yaśa ākhyāyitaṃ yasya svargārthaṃ yasya bhāratī ।।

miṣṭānnaṃ brāhmaṇasyārthe svargavāso api vidyate ।
putrotpattivināśābhyāṃ nāparaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ ।।

brahmahatyāśvamedhābhyāṃ nāparaṃ pāpapuṇyayoḥ ।
kiṃ bravīmīti he vatsa nānusaukhyaṃ sutaṃ vinā ।।

evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ duḥkhaṃ pralapitvā punaḥ punaḥ ।
bālaṃ gṛhagate vipre saṃgopya brāhmaṇī tathā ।।

evaṃ tasyāṃ vilapantyāṃ gatā rātrir yudhiṣṭhira ।
bhūmyāṃ prasuptaṃ govindaṃ putraśokena pīḍitā ।।

yāvan nirīkṣate bhāryā bhartāraṃ duḥkhapīḍitam ।
kṛmirāśim ayaṃ tāvad govindaṃ nṛpasattama ।।

duḥkhād duḥkhatare magnā dṛṣṭvā taṃ pātakānvitam ।
evaṃ duḥkhanimagnāyāḥ śarvarī vigatā tadā ।।

punaḥ prātas tu govindo darbhāya ca vanaṃ gataḥ ।
evaṃ na jñātavān vipraḥ kāṣṭhena ca hataṃ sutam ।।

gatāś ca divasāḥ pañcabrāhmaṇyā gopitaṃ ca yat ।
paśupālaḥ pañcame ahni mahiṣīruttamāś ca gāḥ ।।

araṇye mahiṣīr muktvā gāś ca bhoktuṃ gṛhaṃ gataḥ ।
vijñaptaḥ paśupālena govindo brāhmaṇottamaḥ ।।

yāvad bhakṣāmy ahaṃ svāmin mahiṣīr gāś ca rakṣaya ।
tataḥ sa tvarito gāś ca brāhmaṇo mahiṣīḥ prati ।।

jagāma mahiṣīr gāś ca viprasya tasya rakṣataḥ ।
dhāvamānasya gāvaś ca mahiṣyaḥ saṅgamaṃ gatāḥ ।।

tatra praviṣṭās tu jale nadyā revāsusaṅgame ।
taj jalaṃ pītamātraṃ tu tvarayā tena vāritāḥ ।।

akāmāt salilaṃ pītvā prakṣālya nayane śubhe ।
ājagāma tataḥ paścād bhavanaṃ dinasaṃkṣaye ।।

bhuktvā duḥkhānvito rātrau govindaḥ śayanaṃ yayau ।
nidrābhibhūto duḥkhena śrameṇaiva tu kheditaḥ ।।

punas taṃ cārdharātre tu tasya bhāryā nirīkṣate ।
kṛmibhir veṣṭitaṃ gātraṃ kvacit paśyaty aveṣṭitam ।।

punaḥ sā vismayāviṣṭā tasya bhāryā guṇānvitā ।
uvāca duṣkṛtaṃ tasya sādhvasāviṣṭacetanā ।।

bhāryovāca
atīte pañcame cāhṇi indhanaṃ kṣipatā tu te ।
gṛhe paścāt sthito bālas tv ajñāto ghātitas tvayā ।।

mayā tat pātakaṃ ghoraṃ tvat kṛtaṃ na prakāśitam ।
tena pracchannapāpena dahyamānā divāniśam ।।

na sukhaṃ tava gātrasya na ca paśyāmi cātmanaḥ ।
nidrā praṇaṣṭā me nātha ratiś caiva tvayā saha ।।

śrūyate mānave śāstre śloko gīto maharṣibhiḥ ।
smṛtvā smṛtvā ca taṃ rātrau paritāpo na śāmyati ।।

kīrtanān naśyate adharmo vardhate asau ca gūhanāt ।
iha loke pare caiva pāpasyānto na vidyate ।।

evaṃ saṃcintyamānāhaṃ sthitā rātrau bhayāturā ।
kṛmirāśimayaṃ tvāṃ tu paśyāmi kathayāmi kim ।।

punaś ca kānta tvad dehaṃ bhrūṇahatyākṛmiplutam ।
kvacit tudanti te caiva kvacinnaṣṭāḥ samantataḥ ।।

etatsaṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya vimṛśantī punaḥ punaḥ ।
na jāne kāraṇaṃ kiṃcit pṛcchāmi kathayasva me ।।

taḍāgaṃ vāpi saritaṃ tīrthaṃ vā devatālayam ।
yaṃ gato asi prabhāvo ayaṃ tasya nānyasya me matiḥ ।।

evam uktas tv asau vipraḥ kathayāmāsa bhārata ।
bhāryayā pūrvavṛttāntaṃ ramamāṇo nṛpottama ।।

golulāyī nivṛttyarthaṃ narmadā saṅgamaṃ gataḥ ।
nābhimātre jale magnas toyaṃ pītaṃ yatheṣṭataḥ ।।

nānyat tīrthaṃ vijānāmi narmadā ca saridvarā ।
evaṃ śrutvā ca tatsarvam upavāsaḥ kṛtaḥ kṣaṇāt ।।

bhartrā saha gatā tatra saṅgame varavarṇinī ।
snātvā vidhiprayuktena saṅgame surapūjite ।।

tarpayāmāsa deveśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ ca sahomayā ।
pañcāmṛtaiḥ snāpayitvā brāhmaṇyā sahito dvija ।।

gandhamālyādidhūpaiś ca naivedyaiś ca suśobhanaiḥ ।
apūjayat tatra liṅgaṃ devīṃ kātyāyanīṃ śubhām ।।

rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kṛtvā bhartrā tena sahaiva sā ।
tataḥ prabhāte vimale dvijaṃ sampūjya yatnataḥ ।।

godānena hiraṇyena vastreṇānnena bhārata ।
govindaḥ pūjayāmāsa svaśaktyā brāhmaṇaṃ śubham ।।

uktaś cākāśavāṇyā tu tīrthaṃ guhyāvatī tv idam ।
guhyeśvaraṃ tatra liṅgaṃ pātālādutthitaṃ tadā ।।

guhyāvatīnarmadayoḥ saṅgamo guṇavānabhūt ।
muktapāpo gṛhaṃ yātaḥ svabhāryāsahito dvijaḥ ।।

etat tīrthaṃ pāpaharaṃ bālahatyāpraṇāśanam ।
tatra snātvā ca japtvā ca dattvā brāhmaṇabhojanam ।।

upāsya śrāddhakaraṇāt tilodakapradānataḥ ।
nivasecchivaloke hi yāvad āhūta saṃplavam ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe guhyāvatītīrthamahimānuvarṇano nāmāśītitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra uttare narmadātaṭe ।
meghanādasamīpe tu viśvarūpā saridvarā ।।

nirgatā viśvarūpasya śarīrād upakurvataḥ ।
purā dāruvane devo liṅgahīnaḥ kṛto dvijaiḥ ।।

narmadātaṭam āśritya tapaḥ kurvaṃs tadā nṛpa ।
viśvarūpo abhavad devo nirgatā saritāṃ varā ।।

gatā sā narmadātoyaṃ saṅgamo guṇavān abhūt ।
tasmiṃs tīrthe naraḥ snātvā sa bhave na punar bhavet ।।

tatra yat kriyate karma sarvaṃ tadakṣayaṃ bhavet ।
sārikā siddhim āyātā patitā tīrthasaṅgame ।।

pūrvam apsarasāṃ śreṣṭhā śakraśāpād akāmataḥ ।
citrāṅgadena ramitā kācit kaṣṭamavāpa ha ।।

sārikā bhava kalyāṇi varṣāṇāṃ sā agraviṃśatim ।
mṛtvā tvaṃ narmadātoye viśvarūpā susaṅgame ।।

vicitrā bahucārvaṅgī sañjātā sārikā nṛpa ।
jātismarā surābhāvā narmadātaṭam āśritā ।।

tataḥ kāle ca saṃprāpte prajvālya pāvakaṃ śubham ।
praviṣṭā sā śubhācārā viśvarūpā susaṅgame ।।

divyadehadharī rājan prāptā śakrasya mandiram ।
etad antaram āsādya sārikātīrthamucyate ।।

tatra yat kriyate karma śrāddhaṃ yajñaḥ śivārcanam ।
sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ vidyān meghanādasya darśanāt ।।

avaśaḥ svavaśo vāpi yas tu prāṇān parityajet ।
na tasya punarāvṛttirghore saṃsārasāgare ।।

khyātāni pañcaliṅgāni yāni dṛṣṭvā śivaṃ vrajet ।
mānavo manujaśreṣṭha śṛṇu tāni yudhiṣṭhira ।।

meghanādaṃ ca goṣṭheśaṃ vāgīśaṃ kākaḍeśvaram ।
lakṣeśvaraṃ pañcaliṅgāny ekāhe yas tu pūjayet ।।

anenaiva śarīreṇa sa naro hi śivaṃ vrajet ।
koṭiyajñaphalaṃ prāpya paścān mokṣamavāpnuyāt ।।

ākhyānaṃ kathayiṣyāmi purāvṛttaṃ tavānagha ।
dharmasenaḥ purā rājā ayodhyādhipatirbalī ।।

dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kṛtavān yajñāṃś ca bahudakṣiṇān ।
śṛṇvan sa dharmaśāstrāṇi narmadācaritaṃ tathā ।।

śrutvā vinirgato rājā revāyā uttare taṭe ।
meghanādaṃ samabhyarcya snātvā vai narmadājale ।।

udgacchati dinakare aśvārūḍho nareśvaraḥ ।
uttarāṃ diśamāśritya gato goṣṭheśvaraṃ śivam ।।

yathāvidhānaṃ sampūjya vāgīśvaraṃ gatas tataḥ ।
tatra snātvā vidhānena pūjayitvā śivaṃ nṛpaḥ ।।

candanāgurukarpūrair dhūpair dīpair vidhānakaiḥ ।
aśvārūḍho nṛpaśreṣṭhaḥ kākaḍeśvaram āgataḥ ।।

taṃ prapūjya tato rājā gatvā vai nārmade jale ।
lakṣeśvaraṃ pūjayitvā sthitaṃ vai vidhipūrvakam ।।

meghanādaṃ tato gatvā sūryaścāstam upāgamat ।
dhyātvā svayaṃ kālarūpaṃ yāvat tiṣṭhati vai nṛpaḥ ।।

tāvad ghoro api turago hy antarikṣacaras tadā ।
divyadehadharaḥ saścāpy apsarobhiḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।।

vimāne devarājasya yayāvindrapurīṃ sthitaḥ ।
śunī pṛṣṭhe tu yā rājñastīrthayātrāṃ prakurvatī ।।

divyadehadharā sāpi vimānena gatā divi ।
dharmaseno api tāṃ dṛṣṭvā vismayāviṣṭacetanaḥ ।।

aśvarūpaṃ jagādātha kim etad iti bhārata ।
uvācākāśago vācaṃ kathaṃ tvaṃ khidyase nṛpa ।।

śarīrajena kaṣṭena tapaḥ sādhyā vibhūtayaḥ ।
pādacārī hi gaccha tvaṃ parapādair gato hyasi ।।

bhūyo yātrāṃ prakuruṣe tadā siddhim avāpsyasi ।
tato rājā ca tasyātha śrutvā tadvacanaṃ tadā ।।

punar dvitīyadivase prasthito liṅgapūjanam ।
pañcaliṅgān samabhyarcya samāyātas tu narmadām ।।

meghanādaṃ yadāpaśyad dvāre devaṃ ca dṛṣṭavān ।
pañcavaktraṃ daśabhujaṃ trinetraṃ śūlapāṇinam ।।

vṛṣārūḍhaṃ jagadgarbhaṃ śaśāṅkakṛtaśekharam ।
dṛṣṭvā taṃ devadeveśaṃ tuṣṭāva parameśvaram ।।

jaya deva mahādeva mahāpātakanāśana ।
saṃsārasāgare magnaṃ māṃ samuddhara sāmpratam ।।

hara uvāca
varaṃ vṛṇu mahābhāga yat te manasi vartate ।
tad dadāmi na sandehaś śvibhakto hi putraka ।।

yadi tuṣṭo asi me deva tanmāṃ sahacaraṃ kuru ।
ekāhe pañcaliṅgāni pūjayiṣyati yo naraḥ ।।

sa tavānucaro deva bhavatv eṣa varo mama ।
dharmasenavacaḥ śrutvā bhavatv evaṃ haro abravīt ।।

taṃ gṛhītvā tu rājānaṃ kailāsaṃ sa jagāma ha ।
svadehasthaṃ cakārāsau dharmasenaṃ nṛpaṃ nṛpa ।।

etat te kathitaṃ rājann itihāsaṃ purātanam ।
śravaṇāt kīrtanād asya aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe pañcaliṅgamahimānuvarṇano nāmaikāśītitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athānyat kathayiṣyāmi tīrthaṃ pāpapraṇāśanam ।
mayūrakukkuṭaṃ nāma brahmahatyā vyapohanam ।।

mṛkaṇḍasyāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ narmadādakṣiṇe taṭe ।
mṛkaṇḍo nāma bhūpāla ṛṣiḥ paramadhārmikaḥ ।।

tapas tepe mahābhāga divyair varṣasahasrakaiḥ ।
tasyāśramapade ramye munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ ।।

vasanti sma jalāhārāḥ śuṣkapatrakṛtāśanāḥ ।
kecit tanna nirāhārā mokṣopāyavicintakāḥ ।।

etasminn antare rājan gandharvau śakragāyanau ।
hetiprahetināmānau gatau śakrasabhāṃ nṛpa ।।

vadhūrapsarasāṃ śreṣṭhā dṛṣṭā tābhyāṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।
dṛṣṭamātrau tu gandharvau kāmabāṇaprapīḍitau ।।

hetiḥ kukkuṭaśabdena prahetir barhiṇas tathā ।
ghoṣyamāṇau sumadhuraṃ sādayāmāsa tu ca tām ।।
vṛtrahā tad abhiprāyaṃ jñātvā śāpaṃ dadau tavā ।।
pūrṇe divyaśate varṣe paścād atrāgamiṣyathaḥ ।
tiryagyonau tu saṃprāptau gandharvau hi yudhiṣṭhira ।।

jātismarau durācārau pakṣiṇau priyadarśīnau ।
sarvatīrthāny uttaran tau nāradaṃ ca dadarśatuḥ ।।

gandharvāv ūcatuḥ
bhaviṣyāvaḥ śubhācāra brahmaputra tapodhana ।
