agastya uvāca yadi tuṣṭo asi deveśa yadi deyo varo mama ।।

pratyakṣo bhava tīrthe asmin yadi satyaṃ varapradaḥ ।
antarjale sadākālaṃ dharmādhyakṣo maheśvara ।।

śilāyāṃ bhava nityaṃ ca narmadāyottare taṭe ।
devakāryasya kartāhaṃ tvatprasādāj jagatpate ।।

tatheti coktvā vṛṣavāhano api jagāma kailāsanagaṃ nageśaḥ ।
ayonijo yogabalena yuktaḥ pravidyayā liṅgabalāc chivasya ।।

jagāma dakṣiṇām āśāṃ surasaṅghair abhiṣṭutaḥ ।
tapovanaṃ yathāpuṇyaṃ devadānavasevitam ।।

praviṣṭo muniśārdūlaḥ pavitraṃ devakambalam ।
niścalā suṣamādevī saṃsthitā dharaṇī tathā ।।

puṣpāṇi vavṛṣurdevā jayaśabdaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca tasya tīrthasya yatpuṇyaṃ kathyatāṃ munisuvrata ।।

ādimadhyāvasāne ca brāhmaṇaiḥ saha bāndhavaiḥ ।
pitṝṇāṃ sarvatīrthānāṃ sarvasattvopakārakam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
pitṝn mokṣadaṃ proktaṃ sarvakāle janādhipa ।
śivākhyāṃ kārttike māsi kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśīm ।।

upoṣya yo naro bhaktyā kāmakrodhavivarjitaḥ ।
śamītaruṃ samāsthāya rātrau kurvīta jāgaram ।।

tatkathālāpasaṃyukto dharmākhyānair dvijaiḥ saha ।
gavāṃ ghṛtena deveśaṃ rātrau ca snāpayet punaḥ ।।

ghaṭenaiva ghaṭārdhena tadardhena svaśaktitaḥ ।
ghṛtena bodhayed dīpaṃ ghṛtaṃ viprāya dāpayet ।।

pañcāmṛtena gavyena snāpayet parameśvaram ।
prabhāte pūjayed viprān svadāraniratān sadā ।।

vedābhyasanaśīlāṃś ca paradāravivarjitān ।
śūdrasevāratā nityaṃ dhūrtakarmaratā janāḥ ।।

patitāḥ kūṭasākṣyeṇa pratigraharatāḥ sadā ।
vedadveṣaṇaśīlāś ca kubjāś ca vikalāḥ sadā ।।

hīnātiriktagātrā ye dvijāḥ śrāddhe vivarjitāḥ ।
vedoktena viśuddhāṅgāḥ pūjyā nityaṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।।

bhūmidānena vastreṇa kanyādānair viśeṣataḥ ।
śrāddhakāleṣu yogeṣu bhartavyā bhaktitatparaiḥ ।।

godānaṃ tatra kartavyaṃ śreyo artham ātmanas tathā ।
savatsāṃ kṣīriṇīṃ śubhrāṃ puṣṭāṃ vai śīlasaṃyutām ।।

kambalaṃ parayā bhaktyā pādukopānahau tathā ।
hiraṇyarukmiṇīṃ kanthāṃ tāmbūlaṃ bhojanaṃ tathā ।।

ghaṇṭābharaṇaśobhāḍhyāṃ vastrayugmāvaguṇṭhitām ।
svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakhurīṃ kāṃsyadohena saṃyutām ।।

uccārya parayā bhaktyā yāvad āhūtasaṃplavam ।
sarva koṭiguṇaṃ pārtha śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham ।।

tīrthākhyānaṃ ca yo bhaktyā paṭhate śṛṇute athavā ।
mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ śivaloke vasaty api ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe agastyatīrthavarṇano nāma pañcanavatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
athānandeśvaraṃ gacchet sarvadevanamaskṛtam ।
rudrasya paramānando yatra jāto yudhiṣṭhira ।।

tattīrthaṃ kathayiṣyāmi sūryapāpakṣayaṃ karam ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca ānandaś caiva saṃjāto rudrasya dvijasattama ।।

kathayasva mahābhāga saṃkṣepān munisattama ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca kathayāmi nṛpaśreṣṭha ānandeśvaram uttamam ।।

dānavānāṃ vadhaṃ kṛtvā devadevaś ca śaṅkaraḥ ।
pūjito daivataiḥ sarvaiḥ kinnarair yakṣapannagaiḥ ।।

ānandaṃ paramaṃ prāpya nanarta vṛṣavāhanaḥ ।
bhairavaṃ rūpam āsādya gaurī cārddhāṅgadhāritā ।।

bhūtavetālakaṅkālair bhairavair bhairavo vṛtaḥ ।
narmadāyottare tīre dakṣiṇe pāṇḍunandana ।।

tuṣṭair marudgaṇais tatra sthāpitaḥ kamalāsanaḥ ।
tadā prabhṛti vai deva ānandeśvara ucyate ।।

aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ narādhipa ।
vidhiṃ snātvārcayed devāṃ sugandhena vilepayet ।।

brāhmaṇān pūjayet tatra yathāśaktyā yudhiṣṭhira ।
godānaṃ tatra kartavyaṃ vastradānaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

vasantasya trayodaśyāṃ śrāddhaṃ tatraiva kārayet ।
iṅgudair badarair bilvair akṣatena jalena vā ।।

pretānāṃ kārayec chrāddham ānandeśvaratīrthake ।
pretā ānanditāḥ syus te yāvad āhūta samplavam ।।

santatirdhanasaukhyaṃ ca saptajanmani jāyate ।
ānandaś ca bhavet teṣāṃ janma janma yudhiṣṭhira ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra mātṛtīrtham anuttamam ।
saṅgamasya samīpasthaṃ narmadādakṣiṇe taṭe ।।

mātaras tatra rājendra saṃjātā narmadātaṭe ।
umayā yācitas tatra vyālayajñopavītakaḥ ।।

uvāca yoginīvṛndaṃ kaṣṭaṃ kaṣṭaṃ na śobhanam ।
uvāca varadaś cāsmi yogivṛndavarapradaḥ ।।

yoginya ūcuḥ
ajeyāḥ sarvadevānāṃ tvat prasādān maheśvara ।
tīrthānāmabhisaṃkhyāne prakhyātā vasudhātale ।।
evaṃ bhavatu yoginyas tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tasmiṃs tīrthe tu yo martyo navamyāṃ vijitendriyaḥ ।
upoṣya parayā bhaktyā pūjayen mātṛmaṇḍalam ।।

tasya tā mātaraḥ prītāḥ prīto ayaṃ vṛṣavāhanaḥ ।
bandhyāyā mṛtavatsāyā aputrāyā yudhiṣṭhira ।।

snapanaṃ cārabhet tatra mantrajñair brāhmaṇottamaiḥ ।
sahiraṇyena kumbhena pañcaratnaphalānvitam ।।

snāpayet putrakāmā ca kāṃsyapātreṇa mantrataḥ ।
putrān sā labhate nārī vīryayuktān guṇānvitān ।।

yaṃ yaṃ kāmam abhidhyāyet taṃ taṃ sā labhate nṛpa ।
mātṛtīrthāt paraṃ tīrthaṃ nāsty anyat pāṇḍunandana ।।

tasyaivānantaraṃ tāta jalamadhyeśvaraṃ param ।
liṅgeśvaramiti khyātaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
atyaktā sā tu revā yā kathaṃ tyaktā ca śambhunā ।
jalamadhye hi tiṣṭheta śūlapāṇiḥ pinākadhṛk ।।

tadahaṃ śrotum icchāmi tava vākyād dvijottama ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca āścaryabhūtā loke asmin pratiṣṭhā pāṇḍunandana ।।

paṇḍito vṛddhabhāvena kathayāmi nṛpottama ।
ādau kṛtayuge tāta dānavo baladarpitaḥ ।।

kālabāṣpa iti prokto durjayo devadānavaiḥ ।
tapaś cacāra vipulaṃ narmadāyā jale śubhe ।।

ārādhayan mahādevam ugreṇa tapasā bhṛśam ।
tatas tutoṣa bhagavān sapatnīko maheśvaraḥ ।।

īśvara uvāca
bho bho vatsa varaṃ brūhi tuṣṭo ahaṃ tava bhaktitaḥ ।
devasya vacanaṃ śrutvā kālabāṣpo abravīd vacaḥ ।।

devāś caiva mayā bhagnāḥ prasādāt tava śūlinaḥ ।
saṃgrāme ca viṣaṇṇo ahaṃ tasmād ārādhanaṃ kṛtam ।।

hastaṃ śirasi yasyaiva dāsyāmi ca maheśvara ।
na sa jīvet pumāṃl loke varam etaṃ dadasva me ।।

īśvara uvāca
yat te abhilaṣitaṃ daitya tat tathaiva bhaviṣyati ।
iti śrutvā vaco daityaḥ śambhum evābhidudruve ।।

hastaṃ te mūrdhni dāsyāmi na tatsatyaṃ vacas tava ।
rudraḥ palāyitas tena keśavaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।।

nivedya keśavaṃ sarvaṃ tasminn eva nyalīyata ।

keśava uvāca hanmy ahaṃ taṃ mahādeva duṣṭaṃ daityajaneśvaram ।।

hastaṃ śirasi tasyaiva dāpayāmi maheśvara ।
tatas tvaritamāpannaḥ praviṣṭo namadātaṭe ।।

kṛṣṇaḥ strīveṣadhārī ca daityasaṃmukham āgataḥ ।
dvātriṃśallakṣaṇopetā niyuktā kāmasāyakaiḥ ।।

madhumāthavake śambhuṃ dhyātvā sarvatra kaiśavī ।
vanaṃ babhrāma sarvatra suśīlā vaṭapādapam ।।

kṣobhayantīva cittāni sā reme dharmanandana ।
riṅgamāṇaś ca daityo asau kālabāṣpaḥ sudurjanaḥ ।।

praviṣṭaḥ sa vane ramye yatra sā śubhalocanā ।
ahaṃ bhavāmi te bhartā durjayo devadānavaiḥ ।।

trailokyasvāminī tvaṃ ca prasīda mama sundari ।

śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca yadi māṃ manyase bhāryāṃ pratyayaś ca bhaven mama ।।

dānava uvāca
svayaṃ bhavāmi tanvaṅgi śapathaṃ mama sādhanam ।
tad ahaṃ ca kariṣyāmi iti me satyabhāṣitam ।।

stryuvāca kuruṣva tvaṃ mahābhāga śiro haste pradīyatām ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca kāmāndhenaiva rājendra nikṣipto mastake karaḥ ।।

tatkṣaṇād abhavad bhasma dagdhas tṛṇacayo yathā ।
keśavasyopari tadā puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ha ।।

gatāḥ sarve divaṃ devāḥ svasthānaṃ vigatajvarāḥ ।
kṣaurābdhim agamad viṣṇuḥ kālabāṣpe nipātite ।।

ya idaṃ śṛṇuyād bhaktyā caritaṃ dānavasya ca ।
śrāddhaṃ tatraiva yaḥ kuryāt kāmakrodhavivarjitaḥ ।।

uddhṛtās tena sarve vai narakāc ca pitāmahāḥ ।
kṣetre tasmiṃs tu yo dadyād brāhmaṇe vedapārage ।।

tasya dānaphalaṃ sarvaṃ kurukṣetrād viśiṣyate ।
sparśate ya idaṃ liṅgaṃ śaṅkareṇa ca nirmitam ।।

sparśamātro manuṣyas tu rudravāso abhijāyate ।
etasmāt kāraṇād rājaṃl lokapālāśca devatāḥ ।।

durgādevī tathā caiva madhuhantā caturbhujaḥ ।
dānavādyāś ca sarve api rakṣaṇe ceśvarasya ca ।।

rakṣante ca sadākālaṃ gṛhavyāpārarūpataḥ ।
putrabhrātṛsamā bhūtvā svāmisambandharūpiṇaḥ ।।
liṅgeśvaraṃ tu rājendra devairadyā api rakṣyate ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe bhasmāsuravadho nāma ṣaṇṇavatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchec ca rājendra dhanadaṃ tīrtham uttamam ।
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram ।।

sarvatīrthaphalaṃ tatra prāpyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
caitramāse trayodaśyāṃ śuklapakṣe jitendriyaḥ ।।

upoṣya parayā bhaktyā rātrau kurvīta jāgaram ।
pañcāmṛtena rājendra snāpayed varadaṃ vibhum ।।

pūjayedbhaktiyuktena gītavādyaṃ pradāpayet ।
prabhāte pūjayed viprānātmanaḥ śreya icchatā ।।

pratigrahāvimuktāś ca vidyāsiddhāntavādinaḥ ।
bhartavyā hi priyair bhaktyā parivādavivarjitāḥ ।।

pūjayed gohiraṇyena vastrālaṃkaraṇena ca ।
hastyaśvarathadānena sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet ।।

trijanmajanitaṃ pāpaṃ dhanadasya prabhāvataḥ ।
svargadaṃ durvinītānāṃ vinītānāṃ ca muktidam ।।

dhanavān sa naravyāghra bhavej janmani janmani ।
kulīnatvaṃ svarūpatvaṃ duḥkhaṃ nāsti nirantaram ।।

vyādhes tu na bhayaṃ teṣāṃ nanded dhanadasevanāt ।
dhanasya ca yas tīrthe vidyāṃ vai pradadāti hi ।।

sa yāti bhāskaraṃ lokaṃ sarvaduḥkhavivarjitaḥ ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca ahaṃ te kathayiṣyāmi cetihāsaṃ purātanam ।।

dve bhāryye kaśyapasyāstāṃ sarvalokeṣv anuttame ।
garutmān vinatāputraḥ kadrūputroragāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

santoṣeṇa dvayaṃ tāta tiṣṭhataḥ kāśyape gṛhe ।
kadrvās tu bhaginī tatra iṣṭā ca vinatā tathā ।।

krīḍed vinatayā sārdhaṃ kaśyapo api prajāpatiḥ ।
tatas tv ekadine pārtha āśramasthā suśobhanā ।।

uccaiḥśravohayaṃ dṛṣṭvā ativegaṃ nabhaḥsthitam ।
paśya paśya ca tanvaṅgi aśvaṃ sarvatra pāṇḍuram ।।

dhāvamānam aviśrāntaṃ javena mānasopamam ।

kadrūr uvāca katham etat tu tanvaṅgi kṛṣṇaṃ jalpasi pāṇḍuram ।।

asatyaṃ bhāṣitaṃ bhadre yamalokaṃ gamiṣyasi ।

vinatovāca satyānṛte tu vacane paṇo ayaṃ me astu te adhunā ।।

sahasraṃ caiva varṣāṇām ajñātvā dāsyatāṃ vrajet ।
asatyā yadi me vāṇī kṛṣṇa uccaiḥśravāhayaḥ ।।

tadāhaṃ tvad gṛhe dāsī sarvadaiva bhavāmi hi ।
yadi tūccaiḥśravāḥ śveto dāsī tvaṃ madgṛhe punaḥ ।।

evaṃ parasparaṃ dvābhyāṃ dāsīyam abravīd iti ।
svāśramaṃ hi gatā kadrū rātrau cintāturā sthitā ।।

śvetavarṇaṃ tu kathitaṃ śyāmaṃ tamaśvakaṃ tadā ।
putrāṇāṃ kathitaṃ pārtha paṇaścaiva kṛto mayā ।।

śrutaṃ sarvais tathā vākyaṃ sarpair mātṛpaṇas tadā ।
jātā dāsī na sandehaḥ śveto bhāskaravāhanaḥ ।।

kadrūr uvāca
yathāhaṃ na bhave dāsī tatkāryaṃ ca vicintyatām ।
uccaiḥśravo romakūpe viśadhvaṃ yūyameva ca ।।

ekaṃ muhūrtaṃ tiṣṭhadhvaṃ yāvat kṛṣṇaḥ pradṛśyate ।
kṣaṇenaikena bhavatāṃ dāsī sā bhavate mama ।।

dāsītve yā tu tanvaṅgī vinatā satyagārvitā ।
tataḥ svasthānagāḥ sarve bhavantu sukhinaḥ sadā ।।

sarpā ūcuḥ
yathā tvaṃ jananī caiva sarveṣāṃ bhuvi pannagī ।
tathā sāpi viśeṣaṇa vañcitavyā na mātṛvat ।।

tataḥ sā tena vākyena kruddhā kālānalopamā ।
mama vākyam akurvāṇā ye kecid bhuvi pannagāḥ ।।

havyavāhamukhaṃ sarve yāsyantīty avicāriṇaḥ ।
tena vākyena bhītāste hayaromasuveṣṭitāḥ ।।

naṣṭāḥ kecid diśo divyāḥ kadrūśāpabhayānvitāḥ ।
kecid gaṅgājale naṣṭāḥ kecin naṣṭāḥ sarasvatīm ।।

kecin mahodadhiṃ nītāḥ praviṣṭā vindhyakandare ।
āśritya narmadātoyaṃ maṇināgottamo nṛpa ।।

cacāra vipulaṃ bhaktyā uttare narmadātaṭe ।
mātṛśāpadharo nāgaḥ praviṣṭo narmadājale ।।

tvatprasādena bho nātha mātṛśāpaṃ tarāmy aham ।
havyavāhamukhaṃ yasmāt prayāmi na jagatpate ।।

īśvara uvāca
havyavāhamukhaṃ vatsa na yāsyasi mamājñayā ।
mama lokanivāso api tava putra bhaviṣyati ।।

maṇināga uvāca
asmin sthāne mahādeva sthīyatām aṃśabhāgataḥ ।
sahasrāṃśena bhāgena sthīyatāṃ narmadājale ।।

upakārāya lokānāṃ mama nāmnā ca śaṅkara ।

īśvara uvāca sthāpaya svaparaṃ liṅgamājñayā mama pannaga ।।

ityuktvāntardadhe devastadaiva śivayā saha ।
tatra tīrthe tu ye bhaktyā śucayo yatamānasāḥ ।।

pañcamyāṃ ca caturdaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ śuklapakṣake ।
arcayanti sadā pārtha nopasarpanti te yamam ।।

dadhnā ca madhunā caiva ghṛtena kṣīrato janāḥ ।
snāpayanti virūpākṣam umādehārdhadhāriṇam ।।

kāmāṅgadahanaṃ devaṃ mahāsuraniṣūdanam ।
saṃsnāpayanti ye bhaktyā paśyanti paramaṃ padam ।।

ṣaṭkarmaniratās tāta śūdrapraṇayavarjitāḥ ।
te api yānti paraṃ lokaṃ sarvapāpavivarjitāḥ ।।

vrātyāṃś ca durdharān ṣaṇḍhān vārdhakyāṃś ca kṛṣīvalān ।
bhinnadṛṣṭikarān viprān kaścinnaiva ca pūjayet ।।

vṛṣalī mandire yasya mahiṣaṃ yas tu vāhayet ।
te viprā dūratas tyājyā vrate śrāddhe nṛpeśvara ।।

kāṇāḥ kuṇḍāś ca golāś ca vaidyāś caiva vivarjitāḥ ।
naite pūjyā dvijāḥ pārtha maṇināgeśvare śubhe ।।

yadīcched ūrdhvagamanāṃ pitṛṇām ātmanas tathā ।
sarvāṅgarucirāṅgāś ca sadā pūjyā dvijās tu vai ।।

sa yāti paramaṃ lokaṃ yāvad āhūtasamplavam ।
tataḥ svargāc cyutaḥ so api jāyate vipule kule ।।

maṇināgeśvaraṃ devaṃ yaḥ paśyati narādhipa ।
dhenuṃ śayyāṃ tathā chatraṃ kanyāṃ dāsīṃ subhaktitaḥ ।।

pātre dadyāt tu rājendra yadīcchec chreya ātmanaḥ ।
surabhīṇi ca puṣpāṇi gandhavastrāṇi dāpayet ।।

dīpaṃ dhānyaṃ gṛhaṃ śubhraṃ sarvopaskarasaṃyutam ।
dadate ye narā bhaktyā te vrajanti triviṣṭapam ।।
maṇināge nṛpa svarṇapannago yaḥ pradīyate ।।
pātakāni pralīyanta āmapātre jalaṃ yathā ।
narmadātoyasaṃsiddhaṃ bhojyaṃ viprāya dīyate ।।

te api pāpair vinirmuktāḥ krīḍante daivataiḥ saha ।
tyāgino bhogasaṃyuktā dharmākhyānaratāḥ sadā ।।

devadvijaguror bhaktās tīrthasevāparāyaṇāḥ ।
mātāpitṛsvāmibhaktāḥ krodhadrohavivarjitāḥ ।।

etaiḥ sarvair guṇair yuktā ye narāḥ pāṇḍunandana ।
jāyante svargakāmāś ca svarge vāso bhaviṣyati ।।

sarvatīrthavaraṃ tīrthaṃ maṇināgaṃ nṛpottama ।
tīrthākhyānam idaṃ puṇyaṃ yaḥ paṭhec chṛṇuyād api ।।

so api pāpavinirmuktaḥ śivaloke mahīyate ।
na viṣaṃ kramate teṣāṃ vicaranti yathecchayā ।।

bhādrapadyāṃ ca yaḥ ṣaṣṭhyāṃ bhādre snāyāc ca darśake ।
tasya puṇyaphalāvāptir ākhyānakathanena tu ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe maṇināgatīrthavarṇano nāma saptanavatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
dakṣiṇe narmadātīre tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam ।
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ gopāleśvaram uttamam ।।

godehān niḥsṛtaṃ liṅgaṃ puṇyaṃ bhūmitale nṛpa ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca godehāt niḥsṛtaṃ kasmāl liṅgaṃ pāpakṣayaṃ karam ।।

dakṣiṇe narmadā tīre maṇināgasamīpataḥ ।
saṃkṣepāt kathyatāṃ vipra gopāleśvaram uttamam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
kāmadhenus tapas tatra putrārthaṃ ca cakāra ha ।
dhyāyatī parayā bhaktyā devadevaṃ maheśvaram ।।

tuṣṭas tasyā jagannāthaḥ kapilāyā maheśvaraḥ ।
niḥsṛto dehamadhyāt tu akṣayaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।

maheśvara uvāca
tuṣṭo devi jaganmātaḥ kapile parameśvari ।
ārādhanaṃ kṛtaṃ kasmād vada devi varānane ।।

surabhir uvāca
lokānām upakārāya sṛṣṭāhaṃ parameṣṭhinā ।
loke kāryaṃ hi sarvaṃ vai matprasādāt prasidhyati ।।

lokāḥ sarve prapaśyanti tvatpasādāt triśūlinam ।
tīrthe tvaṃ bhava bhoḥ śambho lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tadā prabhṛtitattīrthaṃ vikhyātaṃ vasudhātale ।
snānenaikena rājendra sarvapāpaṃ vyapohati ।।

gopāleśe tu godānaṃ yas tu bhaktyā pradāpayet ।
yogye dvijottame deyā yogyā dhenuḥ sakāñcanī ।।

savastrā taruṇī śubhrā kṣīriṇī vṛṣasaṃyutā ।
kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ vā yudhiṣṭhira ।।

sarveṣu caiva māseṣu kārttike ca viśeṣataḥ ।
dāpayet parayā bhaktyā dvije svādhyāyatatpare ।।

vidhinā ca pradāsyanti vidhinā pratigṛhṇate ।
ubhayoḥ puṇyakarmāṇi prekṣakāḥ puṇyabhājanāḥ ।।

piṇḍadānaṃ prakartavyaṃ pretānāṃ bhāvasaṃyutaiḥ ।
piṇḍenaikena rājendra pretā yānti parāṃ gatim ।।

bhaktyā praṇāmaṃ rudrasya ye kurvanti dine dine ।
teṣāṃ pāpaṃ pralīyeta bhinnapātre jalaṃ yathā ।।

tasmiṃs tīrthe tu yo rājan vṛṣaṃ caiva samutsṛjet ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca vṛṣotsarge kṛte tāta yatphalaṃ bhavate nṛṇām ।।

tatsarvaṃ kathayasvādya prayatnena dvijottama ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca sarvalakṣaṇasampanne vṛṣe caiva tu yatphalam ।।

tad ahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi śṛṇu tvaṃ dharmanandana ।
kārttike caiva vaiśākhe paurṇamāsyāṃ narādhipa ।।

rudrasya sannidhau bhūtvā śuciḥ snātvā jitendriyaḥ ।
vṛṣotsargaṃ tathā rājan kārayed dharaprītaye ।।

sthāne sthitvā pavitre tu catasro vatsikāḥ śubhāḥ ।
vṛṣabhāya ca muñceta sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutāḥ ।।

prīyatāṃ ca mahādevo brahmāviṣṇus tathā pare ।
vṛṣabhe romasaṃkhyā tu sarvāṅgeṣu narādhipa ।।

tāvad varṣapramāṇaṃ tu śivaloke mahīyate ।
śivaloke uṣitvā tu paścān martye ca jāyate ।।

kule mahati sambhūto dhanadhānyasamākule ।
surūpe rūpavāṃś caiva vidyāḍhye satyavādinām ।।

gopāleśvarakaṃ puṇyaṃ mayākhyātaṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।
godehāt niḥsṛtaṃ liṅgaṃ narmadādakṣiṇe taṭe ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe gopāleśvaramahimānuvarṇano nāmāṣṭanavatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
narmadāyottare kūle tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam ।
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ nāmnā vai gautameśvaram ।।

sthāpitaṃ gautamenaiva lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।
svargasopānarūpeṇa tīrthaṃ puṃsāṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।।

gaccha tvaṃ parayā bhaktyā yatra devo jagadguruḥ ।
pātakānāṃ vināśāya svargavāsāptaye nṛpa ।।

saukhyasya vardhanaṃ liṅgaṃ jayadaṃ duḥkhanāśanam ।
piṇḍadānena caikena kulānāṃ uddharet trayam ।।

yat kiṃcid dīyate bhaktyā svalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu ।
tatsarvaṃ śatasāhasram ājñayā gautamasya ca ।।

tīrthānāṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ svayaṃ rudreṇa bhāṣitam ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca dakṣiṇe narmadākūle tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam ।।

śaṅkhacūḍeśvaraṃ tatra prasiddhaṃ bhūmimaṇḍale ।
śaṅkhacūḍeśvaras tatra saṃsthitaḥ pāṇḍunandana ।।

vainateyabhayāt pārtha saṃsthito narmadātaṭe ।
tatra tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ ।।

snāpayec chaṅkhacūḍaṃ tu kṣaudreṇa dadhisarpiṣā ।
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kṛtvā devasyāgre narādhipa ।।

dadhibhaktena sampūjya brāhmaṇān chaṃsitavratān ।
godānaṃ ca tathā deyaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃ karam ।।

tasmiṃs tīrthe tu yaḥ pārtha sarpadaṣṭo api naśyati ।
so api yāti paraṃ lokaṃ śaṅkhacūḍasya cājñayā ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe śaṅkhacūḍatīrthamahimānuvarṇano nāma navanavatitamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra parāśaravarottamam ।
parāśaro mahātmā ca narmadāyās taṭe śubhe ।।

tapaś cacāra vipulaṃ putrārthaṃ pāṇḍunandana ।
himācalasutā gaurī lakṣmīnārāyaṇānvitā ।।

toṣitā parayā bhaktyā narmadāyottare taṭe ।
parāśareṇa ṛṣiṇā tasya tuṣṭā varaṃ dadau ।।

devy uvāca
bho bho ṛṣivaraśreṣṭha tuṣṭāhaṃ tava bhaktitaḥ ।
varaṃ yācasva viprendra parāśaramahāmate ।।

parāśara uvāca
yadi tuṣṭāsi me devi yadi deyo varo mama ।
putro me dīyatāṃ śīghraṃ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ ।।

tīrthaṃ cātra bhaved devi sannidhānaṃ vareṇa tu ।
lokopakārahetv arthaṃ sthīyatāṃ girinandini ।।

parāśarābhidhānena narmadādakṣiṇe taṭe ।
parāśaravacaḥ śrutvā devī himavataḥ sutā ।।

evaṃ bhavatu te vipra ityuktvāntaradhīyata ।
parāśaro mahātmā ca sthāpayāmāsa pārvatīm ।।

śaṅkaraṃ sthāpayāmāsa surāsuranamaskṛtam ।
arcitaṃ sarvadevānāṃ dānavānāṃ durāsadam ।।

parāśaro mahātmā ca kṛtārtho vigatajvaraḥ ।
tasmiṃs tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā śuciḥ prayatamānasaḥ ।।

māse caitre ca vikhyāte śrāvaṇe nṛpanandana ।
māsi mārgaśire caiva śuklapakṣe tu sarvadā ।।

śaṅkaraṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha girijāṃ pūjayet tathā ।
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ sūryaparvaṇi sarvadā ।।

striyo vā puruṣā vāpi kāmakrodhavivarjitāḥ ।
tatra gatvā śūcau sthāne narmadādakṣiṇe taṭe ।।

upoṣya parayā bhaktyā vrataṃ kuryur mahāmune ।
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kṛtvā dīpadānaṃ svaśaktitaḥ ।।

sapatnīkānuttamāṃś ca śīlaśraddhāsamanvitān ।
pūjayed brāhmaṇān pārtha annadānahiraṇmayaiḥ ।।

vastreṇa cchatradānena śayyā tāmbūlabhojanaiḥ ।
śrāddhaṃ kāryaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha āmaśrāddhaṃ praśasyate ।।

āmaṃ caturguṇaṃ proktaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।
vedoktena vidhānena dvijāḥ pūjyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।।

hastamātrakuśaiś caiva tilaiś ca vāñcchitair nṛpa ।
vipraṃ codaṅmukhaṃ caiva ātmānaṃ dakṣiṇāmukham ।।

āmaṃ darbheṣu niḥkṣipya ityuccārya dvijāgrataḥ ।
pretā yāntu paraṃ lokaṃ tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।।

pāpaṃ me praśamaṃ yātu yātu vṛddhiḥ sadā śubham ।
vṛddhiṃ yātu sadā vaṃśo jñātivargo dvijottama ।।

evam uccārya viprendraṃ deyaṃ parāśarāśrame ।
gobhūnīlahiraṇyāni annaṃ vastraṃ ca śaktitaḥ ।।

dātavyaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha parāśaravarāśrame ।
yaḥ śṛṇoti naro bhaktyā so api pāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe parāśaratīrthamahimānuvarṇano nāma śatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
bhīmeśvaraṃ tato gacchet sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram ।
sevyate ṛṣisaṅghaiś ca bhīmavratadharair api ।।

tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā sopavāso jitendriyaḥ ।
japaṃś caikākṣaraṃ mantram ūrdhvabāhur divākaram ।।

tasya janmārjitaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati ।
saptajanmārjitaṃ pāpaṃ gāyatryā naśyate dhruvam ।।

daśabhir janmajanitaṃ śatena ca purākṛtam ।
trijanmanā sahasreṇa gāyatrī hanti kilbiṣam ।।

vaidikaṃ laukikaṃ cāpi jāpyaṃ japtaṃ janeśvara ।
tatkṣaṇād dahate pāpaṃ tṛṇaṃ ca jvalano yathā ।।

tadeva balamāśritya kadācit pāpam ācaret ।
ajñānāt tasya tatkṣipraṃ na phalaṃ hi kadācana ।।

tatra tīrthe tu godānaṃ śaktimātreṇa dāpayet ।
tad akṣayaṃ phalaṃ sarvaṃ jāyate pāṇḍunandana ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra nāradeśvaram uttamam ।
tīrthānāṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ nirmitaṃ nāradena tu ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
nāradena muniśreṣṭha kasya tīrthaṃ vinirmitam ।
etad ākhyāhi me sarva prasanno yadi sattama ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
parameṣṭhisutaścāpi nārado bhagavānṛṣiḥ ।
narmadāyotare kūle tapas tepe purākṛte ।।

navanāḍīnirodhena kāṣṭhāvasthāṃ gatena ca ।
toṣitaḥ śrīmahādevo nāradena yudhiṣṭhira ।।

īśvara uvāca
tuṣṭo ahaṃ tava viprendra yogīśvara ayonija ।
varaṃ prārthaya he deva yat te manasi vartate ।।

nārada uvāca tvatprasādena bho deva yogaś caiva prasidhyatu ।

īśvara uvāca yogo bhavatu bhaktis te sarvakālaṃ mamaiva tu ।।

svecchācāro bhave gaccha svargapātālagocare ।
martye ca bhramase yogin na kenāpi nivāryase ।।

saptasvarāstrayo grāmā mūrchanās tv ekaviṃśatiḥ ।
mama priyakaraṃ divyaṃ nṛtyaṃ gītaṃ ca yoginā ।।

kaliṃ ca paśyase nityaṃ devadānavakinnaraiḥ ।
tvat tīrthaṃ bhūtale puṇyaṃ matprasādād bhaviṣyati ।।

ityuktvāntardadhe devo nāradas tatra liṅginam ।
sthāpayāmāsa rājendra sarvasattvopakārakam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
pṛthivyām uttamaṃ tīrthaṃ nirmitaṃ nāradena tu ।
tasmiṃs tīrthe naraśreṣṭha nāgacched vijitendriyaḥ ।।

māsi bhādrapade ramye kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśīm ।
upoṣya parayā bhaktyā rātrau kurvīta jāgaram ।।

chatraṃ tatra pradātavyaṃ brāhmaṇe śubhalakṣaṇam ।
śastreṇa nihatā ye tu teṣāṃ śrāddhaṃ pradāpayet ।।

yānti te paramaṃ lokaṃ piṇḍadānaprabhāvataḥ ।
kapilā caiva dātavyā tatra deśe narādhipa ।।

asya śrāddhaprabhāveṇa brāhmaṇānāṃ narādhipa ।
narmadātoyapānasya nyāyārjitadhanasya ca ।।

eteṣāṃ ca prabhāveṇa pretā yāntu parāṃ gatim ।
ityuccārya dvije deyā dakṣiṇā ca svaśaktitaḥ ।।

haviṣyānnaṃ viśālākṣa dvijānāṃ caiva dāpayet ।
vidyādānena caikena akṣayā gatirāpyate ।।

tasmiṃs tīrthe tu rājendra yo dadyād agrajanmane ।
kāṃcanaṃ sa tilaṃ caiva sa gacchec ca triviṣṭapam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchettu rājendra tīrthadvayam anuttamam ।
dadhichandaṃ madhuchandaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃ karam ।।

dadhicchande naraḥ snātvā yo dadyāc ca dvije dadhi ।
upatiṣṭhati tasyaitat saptajanmasu bhārata ।।

na vyādhir na jarā tasya na śoko na ca matsaraḥ ।
daśacandraśataṃ yāvaj jāyate vipule kule ।।

madhucchande tu madhunā miśritaṃ ca tilodakam ।
na ca vaivasvataṃ devaṃ paśyate saptajanmasu ।।

madhunā saha miśraṃ ca tilaṃ yas tu prayacchati ।
tasya putrasya pautrasya dāridryaṃ naiva jāyate ।।

madhunā saha saṃmiśraṃ tilaṃ yas tu prayacchati ।
madhunā saha saṃmiśraṃ yas tu piṇḍaṃ pradāpayet ।।

tasmiṃs tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā vidhivad dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ।
pitā pitāmahaś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ ।।

ṣoḍaśābdāni tuṣyanti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca tato gacchet tu rājendra nanditīrtham anuttamam ।।

yatra siddhaś ca vai nandī tat sarvaṃ kathayāmy aham ।
narmadāṃ purataḥ kṛtvā purā nandī maheśvaram ।।

tapas taptaṃ japaṃś caiva tīrthāt tīrthaṃ jagāma ha ।
dadhicchandaṃ madhucchandaṃ yāvat tyaktvā ca gacchati ।।

tatas tuṣṭo mahādevo nandinaṃ tamuvāca ha ।

maheśvara uvāca bho bhoḥ prasanno nandīśa varaṃ vṛṇu yathepsitam ।।

tapasā tena tuṣṭo ahaṃ tīrthayātrākṛtena ca ।

nandy uvāca na cāhaṃ kāmaye vittaṃ na cāhaṃ kulasantatim ।।

muktiṃ na kāmaye cānyad deveśa caraṇāmbujam ।
kṛmikīṭapataṅgeṣu tiryagyonigateṣu ca ।।

janmajanmani yāsyāmi tvadbhaktiracalā ca me ।
tatheti cokto devena parameśena nandikaḥ ।।

gṛhītvā taṃ kare śīghraṃ jagāma nilayaṃ haraḥ ।
tasmiṃs tīrthe tu yaḥ snātvā bhaktyā tryakṣaṃ prapūjayet ।।

agniṣṭome ca yatpuṇyaṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।
tatra tīrthe mahāpuṇye prāṇatyāgaṃ karoti yaḥ ।।

śivasyānucaro bhūtvā modate kalpamakṣayam ।
tataḥ kālena mahatā jāyate vipule kule ।।

vedavedāṅgatattvajñe jīvec ca śaradāṃ śatam ।
etat te kathitaṃ pārtha sarvatuṣṭipradaṃ śubham ।।
durlabhaṃ satyasaṃjñasya sarvapāpakṣayaṃ karam ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe nanditīrthavarṇano nāmaikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra varuṇeśvaram uttamam ।
yatra siddhaḥ purā devo varuṇo nṛpasattama ।।

piṇyākaśākaparṇaiś ca kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādibhiḥ ।
ārādhya girijānāthaṃ tataḥ siddhiṃ gatā janāḥ ।।

tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā saṃtarpya pitṛdevatāḥ ।
pūjayec chaṅkaraṃ bhaktyā sa gacchet paramaṃ padam ।।

kuṇḍikāṃ vardhanīṃ vāpi mahadvā jalabhājanam ।
annena sahitaṃ pārtha tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ।।

yatphalaṃ labhate martyaḥ satre dvādaśavārṣike ।
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।

sarveṣām eva dānānām annadānam anuttamam ।
yadyat prītikaraṃ caiva toyaṃ ca nṛpasattama ।।

tatra tīrthe mṛtānāṃ ca narāṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।
vāruṇe ca pure vāso yāvad āhūta samplavam ।।

bhuktvā tatra bahuṃ kālaṃ martyaloke abhijāyate ।
annadānaprado nityaṃ jīvec ca śaradāṃ śatam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchec ca rājendra agnitīrtham anuttamam ।
yatra siddho mahātejās tapaḥ kṛtvā hutāśanaḥ ।।

sarvabhakṣīkṛto yaś ca daṇḍake muninā purā ।
narmadātaṭam āśritya pūto jāto hutāśanaḥ ।।

tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā samabhyarcya jagadgurum ।
umayā sahita bhaktyā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā datte vai kāṃcanaṃ nṛpa ।
brāhmaṇebhyo jalaṃ dattvā labhate vārbudaṃ phalam ।।

dadhicchande madhucchande nandīśe vāruṇe tathā ।
āgneye tatphalaṃ tāta snātvā mucyeta kilbiṣaiḥ ।।

te vandyā mānuṣe loke dhanyāś cāptamanorathāḥ ।
yair hi dṛṣṭaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ narmadātīrthapañcakam ।।

svargalokam avāpuste yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ।
tataḥ svargāc cyutāś cāpi rājānaḥ santi dhārmikāḥ ।।

sarvapāpavinirmuktā bhuñjate te acalāṃ mahīm ।
ākhaṇḍalapratāpo ayaṃ narmadātaṭasevane ।।

gaṅgākanakhale puṇyā kurukṣetre sarasvatī ।
grāme vā yadi vāraṇye puṇyā sarvatra narmadā ।।

revātīraṃ vasen nityaṃ toyaṃ yas tu sadā pibet ।
snāto asau sarvatīrtheṣu somapānaṃ dine dine ।।

gaṅgādyāḥ saritaḥ sarvāḥ samudrāś ca sarāṃsi ca ।
kalpānte saṃkṣayaṃ yānti na mṛtaikā ca narmadā ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe tīrthapañcakavarṇano nāma dvyadhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
hanūmadīśvaran nāma kathaṃ jātaṃ mahāmate ।
brahmahatyāharaṃ tīrthaṃ revāyādakṣiṇe taṭe ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ mahābāho somavaṃśavibhūṣaṇa ।
guhyād guhyataraṃ tīrthaṃ nākhyātaṃ kasyacin mayā ।।

tava snehāt pravakṣyāmi pīḍito vārdhakena tu ।
jātaṃ pūrvaṃ mahāyuddhaṃ rāmarāvaṇayor api ।।

pulastyo brahmaṇaḥ putras tasya vai viśravāḥ sutaḥ ।
rāvaṇas tasya saṃjāto daśagrīvo api rākṣasaḥ ।।

trailokyavijayī jātaḥ prasādāc chūlinas tathā ।
gīrvāṇā nirjitāḥ sarve rāmasya gṛhiṇī hṛtā ।।

yad bhrātā kumbhakarṇo vai sītā sā vanamāśritā ।
vibhīṣaṇena pāpo ayaṃ mandas tyakto vicārya ca ।।

sa jitaḥ kārtavīryeṇa sa jito jāmadagninā ।
sa hato rāmacandreṇa tasya rājyaṃ hṛtaṃ tathā ।।

tato rāmeṇa rakṣo api jitaḥ saṃkhye mahābalaḥ ।
vanaṃ bhagnaṃ hato rakṣo gatvā vāyusutena vai ।।

rāvaṇasya sutaḥ saṃkhye hataś cākṣakumārakaḥ ।
evaṃ rāmāyaṇe jāte sītā mokṣe kṛte tataḥ ।।

ayodhyāyāṃ gate rāme hanūmāś ca mahābalaḥ ।
kailāsaṃ hi gataḥ pārtha praṇāmārthaṃ maheśvare ।।

tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cokto vai nandinā vānarottamaḥ ।
brahmahatyāyutas tvaṃ hi rākṣasānāṃ vadhena hi ।।

bhairavasyāsanaṃ puṇyaṃ na gantā asi mahābala ।

hanumān uvāca nandiṃs tvaṃ hi varaṃ yaccha pātakasyopaśāntaye ।।

bhūtvā niṣpātako ahaṃ vai praṇamāmi maheśvaram ।

nandy uvāca rudradehodbhavā puṇyā narmadā saritāṃ varā ।।

śravaṇāj janmacaritaṃ kīrtanād dviguṇaṃ vrajet ।
saptajanmārjitaṃ pāpaṃ naśyed revāvagāhanāt ।।

tasmāt tīre vasa tvaṃ ca revāsaṅgamadakṣiṇe ।
dhyāyamāno virūpākṣaṃ triśūlakarasaṃsthitam ।।

jaṭāmukuṭasaṃkāśaṃ vyālayajñopavītakam ।
umārdhāṅgadharaṃ devaṃ gorājāsanasaṃsthitam ।।

vatsarān subahūn yāvad dhyāyatas tasya tatra vai ।
tatra tuṣṭo mahādeva āgataḥ saha bhāryayā ।।

uvāca madhurāṃ vāṇīṃ meghagambhīrayā girā ।
sādhu vatsa tvayā cātra kaṣṭaṃ tapasi saṃsthitam ।।

hanūmāṃś ca haraṃ dṛṣṭvā umārdhāṅgadharaṃ sthitam ।
sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇato bhūtvā jayadeva namo astu te ।।

jaya cāndhakaghātāya bāṇāsuravimardine ।
jaya bhūtapanāthāya jaya bhairavabhūṣaṇa ।।

jaya kāmavināśāya gaṅgāṃ śirasi dhāriṇe ।
evaṃ stuto mahādevo varado vānarasya ca ।।

īśvara uvāca varaṃ prārthaya tvaṃ vatsa prārthitaṃ rabhasaṃ vada ।

hanumān uvāca brahmarakṣovadhāj jātā brahmahatyā maheśvara ।।

niṣpāpo ahaṃ bhaveyaṃ vai yuṣmat sambhāṣaṇena ca ।

īśvara uvāca narmadātīrthaṃ māhātmyadhyānayogaprabhāvataḥ ।।

manmūrtidarśanāt sadyo niṣpāpo nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
ityuktvāntardadhe deva umāsārdhaṃ trilocanaḥ ।।

hanumadīśvaraṃ tatra sthāpayāmāsa bhaktitaḥ ।
ātmayogabalenaiva brahmacaryaprabhāvataḥ ।।

īśvarasya prabhāveṇa kāmadaṃ sthāpitaṃ śivam ।
acchedyam apratarkyaṃ ca vināśotpattivarjitam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
hanumadīśvare tatra pratyayaṃ yatpurābhavat ।
yadvṛttaṃ dvāparasyādau tretānte ca nareśvarā ।।

suparṇo nāma rājarṣir babhūva vasudhātale ।
tasya rājye sadā saukhyaṃ dīrghāyur mānavaḥ sadā ।।

śatabāhurbabhūvāsya putro bhīmaparākramaḥ ।
āsaktaḥ sa sadākālaṃ japadhyāne nareśvara ।।

krīḍate pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ parvatāṃś ca vanāni ca ।
vadhārthaṃ mṛgayūthānām āgato vindhyaparvate ।।

mṛgajātisamākīrṇe hastijātisamāśrite ।
hasticitrakaśobhāḍhye mṛgavārāhasaṃkule ।।

krīḍitvā ca tato rājā cāsane saṃsthitaḥ sa ca ।
vanamadhye tadā dṛṣṭvā bhramantaṃ piṅgalaṃ dvijam ।।

rājovāca
eko vane vane kasmād bhramase pustikākaraḥ ।
itaśceto nirīkṣaṃs tvaṃ kathayasva dvijottama ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca kānyakubjāt samāyātaḥ preṣito rājakanyayā ।

rājovāca kathayasva prasādena kasmāt kāryād vada prabho ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca
śikhaṇḍī caiva rājā vai kānyakubjaṃ bubhukṣate ।
aputraḥ sa mahīpālaḥ kanyā jātā manorathaiḥ ।।

he nṛpa
jātismarā śubhācārā narmadāyāḥ prabhāvataḥ ।
pitroktā sā ca kanyā vai vivāhāya prakalpitā ।।

asāre cādya saṃsāre kanyādānaṃ dadāmyaham ।

kanyovācā yasmin kāle hy ahaṃ lipse tasmin kāle pradīyatām ।।

putrīvākyena rājāsau vismayāviṣṭacetanaḥ ।

śikhaṇḍy uvāca kathyatāṃ me mahābhāge bhāṣitaṃ hi tvayā katham ।।

pitṛvākyena sā vālā śirasāvanatā bhuvi ।
kathayāmāsa yadvṛttaṃ hanumadīśvare nṛpa ।।

kalāpiny asmy ahaṃ tāta sthitā bhartṛsahānugā ।
uraṅgameśa sānnidhye revāyā uttare taṭe ।।

hanumato vane puṇye krīḍāmi sma yadṛcchayā ।
bhartṛyuktā tatra guhye vañjule sarale drume ।।

āgatā lubdhakās tatra kṣudhārtā vanam uttamam ।
bhartṛkopayutaiḥ pāpair hatāhaṃ patinā saha ।।

grīvāṃ nimoṭayāmāsur bhakṣaṇotpāṭanaṃ kṛtam ।
hutāśanamukhe te tu hasantaś cāśu lubdhakāḥ ।।

bharjayitvā tato māṃsaṃ bhakṣayitvā yathecchayā ।
suptāḥ svasthendriyā rātrau vigatā śarvarī kṣayam ।।

tanmāṃsaśeṣaṃ juṣṭaṃ vai jambukair gṛdhravāyasaiḥ ।
maccharīrodbhavaṃ cāsthi snāyumāṃsena saṃyutam ।।

gṛhītvā patriṇaikena ākāśāt patatā tadā ।
sāmiṣaṃ pakṣiṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā pakṣiṇo anye samāgatāḥ ।।

dṛṣṭvā pakṣisamūhaṃ tu asthikhaṇḍaṃ vyasarjayat ।
vihagānāṃ samastānāṃ dhāvatāṃ cāpi paśyatām ।।

patitaṃ narmadātoye hanumadīśvare nṛpa ।
madīyamasthikhaṇḍaṃ ca patitaṃ narmadājale ।।

tasya tīrthaprabhāveṇa jātāhaṃ kṣatriye kule ।
bhūpa kanyāpy ahaṃ jātā sampūrṇaśaśivanmukhī ।।

jātismarā narendrāsmi jātāhaṃ kṣatriye kule ।
etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ kāraṇaṃ nṛpasattama ।।

madarthaṃ viṣamasthāne śakuntamṛgajātiṣu ।
yadi preṣayase tāta kam api narmadājale ।।

tasyāhaṃ kathayiṣyāmi sthānacihnaṃ samagrakam ।
kanyāyā vacanaṃ śrutvā śikhaṇḍī hyāha māṃ nṛpa ।।

grāmaviṃśaṃ ca dāsyāmi gaccha tvaṃ narmadātaṭe ।
prekṣaṇaṃ me pratijñātam alakṣyā apīḍitena tu ।।

gaccha tvaṃ narmadāṃ puṇyāṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarīm ।
agrajāṃ somanāthasya hanumadīśvare śubhe ।।

ardhakrośe tu revāyā vistīrṇe vaṭapādapaiḥ ।
kadambakavanaiś caiva saṃpradhāne vanasya ca ।।

nyagrodhavaṭasānnidhye asthilakṣyaṃ pradṛśyate ।
mṛttikāmasthisaṃgṛhya gaccha revān dvijottama ।।

āśvinasya site pakṣe tripurāritithau sthite ।
snāpaya śūlinaṃ bhaktyā rātrau kuru ca jāgaram ।।

prabhāte kṣipyatāṃ śīghraṃ nābhimātre jale sthitaḥ ।
ity uccārya dvijaśreṣṭha sugatis tasya jāyate ।।

asthi kṣiptvā punaḥ snānaṃ kartavyamaghanāśanam ।
kathitaṃ kanyayā yac ca tatsarvaṃ pustake kṛtam ।।

āgato ahaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha tasmiṃs tīrthe mahālaye ।
sābhijñānaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā gṛhītvāsthi nṛpottama ।।

pūrvoktena vidhānena nikṣiptaṃ narmadājale ।
puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papātātha sādhu sādhviti brāhmaṇa ।।

vimānaṃ tu tato divyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hanumadīśvare ।
tato brāhmaṇarājānau gṛhītvānaśanaṃ sthitau ।।

ātmānaṃ śoṣayitvā ca īśvarārādhane ratau ।
evaṃ sandhyāyato devaṃ śatabāhur dvijottamaḥ ।।

māsārdhāt tu mṛto rājā śatabāhur mahāmatiḥ ।
kiṅkiṇījālaśobhāḍhyaṃ vimānaṃ tatra cāgatam ।।

sādhu sādhu nṛpaśreṣṭha vimānārohaṇaṃ kuru ।

rājovāca ūrdhvamārgaṃ na gacchāmi vipro yāvan na saṃsthitaḥ ।।

upadeśaprado mahyaṃ garurūpo dvijottamaḥ ।

devā ūcuḥ hanumadīśvare rājanye mṛtāḥ santi mānavāḥ ।।

te yānti śivalokaṃ vai sarvapāpakṣayaṃ karam ।
naiva pāpakṣayaś cāsya brāhmaṇasya nareśvara ।।

gṛhaṃ ca gṛhiṇī vittaṃ brāhmaṇasya pravartate ।
śatabāhus tato vipraṃ bhāṣayāmāsa bhaktitaḥ ।।

tyaja mūlam adharmasya lobham ekaṃ dvijottama ।
ity uktvā prayayau rājā svargaṃ svargijanaiḥ saha ।।

dinaiḥ kaiścid gato vipraḥ svargaṃ sukṛtibhiḥ saha ।
vāhinyāḥ kāśirājasya putryāḥ tīrthaprabhāvataḥ ।।

ātmanaḥ kanyayā datte pūrvajanmārjitaṃ tapaḥ ।
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ sarvakālaṃ munīśvara ।।

viśeṣād āśvine māse kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśī ।
snāpayed īśvaraṃ bhaktyā kṣaudrakṣīreṇa sarpiṣā ।।

dadhnā ca khaṇḍayuktena tilatoyena vā punaḥ ।
śrīkhaṇḍena sugandhena cārcayet taṃ maheśvaram ।।

tataḥ sugandhapuṣpaiś ca bilvapatraiś ca pūtanam ।
śrāddhaṃ yaḥ kārayet tatra brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ ।।

sarvalakṣaṇasampūrṇaiḥ kulīnair gṛhapālakaiḥ ।
tarpayed brāhmaṇaṃ bhaktyā annavastrahiraṇyakaiḥ ।।

narakasthā divaṃ yānti ity uccārya dvijātayaḥ ।
svargasthāḥ paramaṃ lokam ityuktvā praṇamed dvijān ।।

patitān varjayed viprān vṛṣalī yasya mandire ।
svavṛṣaṃ tu parityajya vṛṣair anyair vṛṣāyate ।।

vṛṣalīṃ tāṃ vidurdevā na śūdrā vṛṣalī bhavet ।
brahmahatyā surāpānaṃ gurudāraniṣevaṇam ।।

suvarṇaharaṇaṃ tasya mitradrohabhavaṃ tathā ।
naśyanti pātakāḥ sarve ity evaṃ śaṅkaro abravīt ।।

vākpralāpena kiṃ vatsa bahunoktena kiṃ tu vā ।
sarvapāpasamopeto dadyād dānaṃ dvijottame ।।

sarvadevamayī dhenuḥ sarvadevātmikā sthitā ।
śṛṅgāgreṣu mahīpāla śakro vasati nityaśaḥ ।।

hari skandhe śiro brahmā lalāṭe vṛṣavāhanaḥ ।
candrārkau locane jñeyau jihvāyāṃ tu sarasvatī ।।

marudgaṇāḥ sadā sādhyās tasyāṅgāni nareśvara ।
oṃkāraścaturo vedāḥ saṣaḍaṅgapadakramāḥ ।।

ṛṣayo romakūpeṣu asthikhyātā mahānagāḥ ।
daṇḍahasto mahākāyaḥ kṛṣṇo mahiṣavāhanaḥ ।।

pṛṣṭhabhāgasthito nityaṃ śubhāśubhanirīkṣakaḥ ।
catvāraḥ sāgarāḥ puṇyāḥ kṣīradhārāḥ staneṣu ca ।।

viṣṇudehodbhavā gaṅgā darśanāt pāpahāriṇī ।
evaṃ yā saṃsthitā yasmāt tasmād eṣā sadā budhaiḥ ।।

lakṣmīś ca gomaye yasyāḥ pavitrā sarvamaṅgalā ।
gomayāl lepanaṃ tasmāt kartavyaṃ pāṇḍunandana ।।

gandharvāpsaraso gaṅgā gokhureṣu ca saṃsthitāḥ ।
aśvinau karṇayor nityaṃ vartete raviputrakau ।।

pṛthivyāṃ sāgarāntāyāṃ yāni tīrthāni pāṇḍava ।
tāni sarvāṇi prāptāni gavāṃ pādeṣu nityaśaḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
sarvatīrthasamā gāvo gīrvāṇaiḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ ।
etatkathaya me tāta kasmād goṣu samāśritāḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sarvadevamayo viṣṇurgāvo viṣṇuśarīrajāḥ ।
deyās tasmāt sadā vandyāḥ kalpitā vibudhair janaiḥ ।।

śvetā vā kapilā vāpi kṣīriṇī pāṇḍunandana ।
sarvāsāṃ kṣīriṇīr gāvaḥ śvetavastrāvaguṇṭhitāḥ ।।

kāṃsyadohanikā deyāḥ svarṇaśṛṅgīrvibhūṣitāḥ ।
hanūmadīśvarasyāgre bhaktyā vipreṣu dāpayet ।।

nisargasthena sā deyā svargamātmana icchatā ।
asamartho yamas teṣāṃ viṣṇulokaṃ prayānti te ।।

viṣṇulokacyutaḥ so api prayāti dvijamandiram ।
tatraiva jāyate putro vidvān vanasamanvitaḥ ।।

sarvapāpaharaṃ tīrthaṃ hanumadīśvaraṃ śubham ।
śṛṇoti mucyate pāpād varṇasaṅkarasambhavāt ।।
darśe saṃcintayed yas tu mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe hanumadīśvaravarṇano nāma tryadhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
āścaryaṃ kathitaṃ tāta yadabhūn narmadātaṭe ।
somanāthasyatīrthaṃ hi vārāṇasyā samaṃ nṛpa ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
nimagno duḥkhasaṃsāre hṛtarājyo dvijottama ।
yuṣmad vāṇī jalaiḥ snāto nirduḥkho ahaṃ sabāndhavaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahābāho somavaṃśa vibhūṣaṇa ।
pṛṣṭaṃ te durlabhaṃ tīrthaṃ guhyād guhyataraṃ yathā ।।

ādau pitāmahas tāta samas tasya janasya ca ।
manasā tasya saṃjātā ṛṣayo daśa puṅgavāḥ ।।

marīciratryaṅgirasau pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ ।
pracetāś ca vaśiṣṭhaś ca bhṛgur nārada eva ca ।।

jajñe pracetaso dakṣo mahātejāḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
dakṣasyāpi sutā jātāḥ pañcāśat kanyakāḥ kila ।।

dadau sa daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayodaśa ।
tathaiva ca mahābhāga saptaviṃśatim indave ।।

tāsāṃ hi rohiṇī candrasyābhīṣṭā sābhavat tadā ।
tasyāś ca kāraṇaṃ kṛtvā śapto dakṣeṇa candramāḥ ।।

kṣayarogyabhavac candro vivakṣāyāḥ prajāpateḥ ।
dakṣaśāpaprabhāveṇa nistejāḥ śarvarīpatiḥ ।।

gataḥ pitāmahaṃ somo vepamānaḥ praṇamya ca ।
brahmayone namas tubhyaṃ vedagarbha namo astu te ।।

brahmovāca
sarvatra durlabhā revā triṣu sthāneṣu bhārata ।
oṃkāre ca bhṛgukṣetre narmadā hy urageśvare ।।

kāṣṭhavat saṃsthitaḥ somo dhyāyate parameśvaram ।
yāvad varṣaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ tāvat tuṣṭo maheśvaraḥ ।।

pretyakṣaḥ somanāthasya vṛṣāsana umārdhagaḥ ।
sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇato bhūtvā jaya deva namo astu te ।।

jaya śaṅkara pāpakṛtānta namo jaya īśvara nātha namo astu namaḥ ।
jaya vāsukibhūṣaṇa bhūtapate jaya śūlakapāladharāya namaḥ ।।

jaya andhakadehavināśa namo jaya dānavadehavadhāya namaḥ ।
jaya niṣkalasakalakalāya namo jaya kālakalādamanāya namaḥ ।।

jaya nīlakaṇṭha umāpate jaya sūkṣmanirañjanaśabda namaḥ ।
jaya ādya anādya ananta namo jaya pāṇipinākatriśūla namaḥ ।।

evaṃ stuto mahādevaḥ somanāthena pāṇḍava ।
tuṣṭas tasya nṛpaśreṣṭha umayā saha śaṅkaraḥ ।।

īśvara uvāca varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te yat te manasi vartate ।

soma uvāca dakṣaśāpena dagdho ahaṃ kṣīṇadeho maheśvara ।।

pāpapraśamanaṃ deva kuru sarvaṃ mamaiva tu ।

maheśvara uvāca bhavadbhaktigṛhīto ahaṃ tūṣṭaś caivomayā saha ।।

niṣpāpaḥ somanāthasya saṃjātas tīrthasevanāt ।
ity uktvāntardadhe devaḥ somo dhyātvā kṣaṇaṃ nṛpa ।।

sthāpayāmāsa liṅgaṃ tu siddhidaṃ prāṇināṃ bhuvi ।
sarvaduḥkhaharaṃ devaṃ brahmahatyāvināśanam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
somanāthaprabhāvaṃ ca saṃkṣepāt kathayāmi te ।
śambaro nāma rājābhūt tasya putras trilocanaḥ ।।

trilocanasutaḥ kaṇṭhaḥ pāpaniṣṭho mahādhamaḥ ।
vane vibhramatas tasya mṛgayūthaṃ tv adṛśyata ।।

mṛgayūthaṃ hataṃ sarvaṃ trilocanasutena ca ।
mṛgarūpī dvijo madhye vicaran nirjane vane ।।

tadā hatas tu śastreṇa kaṇṭhena ṛṣisattamaḥ ।
brahmahatyāyutaḥ kaṇṭho nistejā vyacaran mahīm ।।

vicarann api saṃprāpto narmadānāgasaṃgame ।
kadambapāṭalākīrṇe bilvanāraṅgaśobhite ।।

ciñcinī campakopete agastitaruśobhite ।
unmattabhṛṅgasaṃyukte tathā sarvatra śobhite ।।

citrakair mṛgamārjāraiḥ siṃhaiḥ sarvatra śūkaraiḥ ।
śaśakair gavayair yukte śikhaṇḍiravanādite ।।

praviṣṭas tadvane kaṇṭhas tṛṣārtaḥ śramakarṣitaḥ ।
snāto revājale puṇye saṅgame pāpanāśane ।।

patrāṇi ca vicitrāṇi bhakṣayan saha kiṅkaraiḥ ।
suptaḥ pādapachāyāyāṃ śrānto mṛgavadhena ca ।।

ānarca parayā bhaktyā somanāthaṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।
pītvā toyaṃ kaṇṭhamātraṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram ।।

tāvat tīrthavare vipraḥ snānārthaṃ saṃgamaṃ prati ।
mārgago brāhmaṇo bhūyas tatas tad gatamānasaḥ ।।

mārge vṛkṣe samārūḍhā strī caikā ca bhayaṅkarī ।
uvāca brāhmaṇaṃ sā hi tiṣṭha tiṣṭha dvijottama ।।

trasto nirīkṣate yāvad diśaḥ sarvā nareśvara ।
tāvad vṛkṣa samārūḍhāṃ striyaṃ raktāmbarāvṛtām ।।

raktapuṣpadharāṃ vālāṃ raktacandanacarcitām ।
raktābharaṇaśobhāḍhyāṃ pāśahastāṃ dadarśa ha ।।

stry uvāca
sandeśaṃ śṛṇu me vipra yadi gacchasi saṃgamam ।
madbhartā tiṣṭhate tatra śīghram eva visarjaya ।।

ekākinī ca te bhāryā tiṣṭhate vanamadhyagā ।
ityākarṇya gato vipraḥ saṅgamaṃ suradurlabham ।।

vṛkṣachāyāsthitaṃ kaṇṭhaṃ brāhmaṇo hi dadarśa ha ।

brāhmaṇa uvāca vanānte ca mayā dṛṣṭā bālā kamalalocanā ।।

raktāmbaradharā tanvī raktacandanarcarcitā ।
raktamālyā suśobhāḍhyā pāśahastā mṛgekṣaṇā ।।

vṛkṣārūḍhāvadad vākyaṃ bhartāraṃ preṣayasva mām ।

kaṇṭha uvāca kasmin sthāne tu viprendra tiṣṭhate mṛgalocanā ।।

kasya sā kena kāryeṇa etat sarvaṃ vada hi me ।

brāhmaṇa uvāca saṃgamād ardhakrośe ca udyānānte praśobhite ।।

tatra tiṣṭhati sā nārī sotkaṇṭhitamanā vibho ।
tato bhṛtyam uvācedaṃ kaṇṭho rājā yudhiṣṭhira ।।

pṛccha tvaṃ gaccha kā cāsi āgatā kva gamiṣyasi ।
tataḥ kṣipraṃ gatas tatra yatra nārī sthitābhavat ।।

vṛkṣasthāṃ dadṛśe bālām uvāca nṛpasattama ।
tvāṃ rājā pṛcchate bāle kāsi tvaṃ kva gamiṣyasi ।।

stry uvāca
gurur ātmavatāṃ śāstā rājā śāstā durātmanām ।
iha pracchannapāpānāṃ śāstā vaivasvato yamaḥ ।।

brahmahatyāsya saṃjātā mṛgarūpadvijodvadhāt ।
mayā yukto api rājāsau muktas tīrthaprabhāvataḥ ।।

atrārdhakrośamātraṃ vai brahmahatyā na saṃviśet ।
somanāthaprabhāvāc ca tīrthaṃ vārāṇasīsamam ।।

gaccha tvaṃ preṣayeḥ kaṇṭhaṃ śīghram eva na saṃśayaḥ ।
samastaṃ kathayāmāsa tad vṛttāntaṃ nṛpaṃ prati ।।

tasya vākyena rājāsau papāta dharaṇītale ।

bhṛtya uvāca kasmāt tvaṃ śocase nātha pūrvajātaṃ śūbhāśubham ।।

ityākarṇya vacas tasya sa rājā tvidam abravīt ।
prāṇatyāgaṃ karomy atra somanātha samīpataḥ ।।

śīghram ānīyatāṃ vahṇir indhanāni bahūny api ।
ānītaṃ tatkṣaṇāt sarvaṃ bhṛtyaiḥ svair vaśavartibhiḥ ।।

snānaṃ kṛtvā śubhe toye saṃgame pāpanāśane ।
arcitvā parayā bhaktyā somanāthaṃ nareśvara ।।

triḥpradakṣiṇakaṃ kṛtvā jvalite jātavedasi ।
praviṣṭaḥ kaṇṭharājas tu hṛdi kṛtvā janārdanam ।।

pītāmbaradharaṃ devaṃ mahāmukuṭadhāriṇam ।
viṣṇor dhyānena cātraiva sugatir me bhavatv iti ।।

papāta puṣpavṛṣṭiś ca sādhu sādhu nṛpātmaja ।
āścaryamatulaṃ dṛṣṭvā nirīkṣa ca parasparam ।।

hutaṃ taiḥ pāvake bhṛtyair hṛdi dhyātvā gadādharam ।
vimānasthā divaṃ sarve saṅgatāḥ pāṇḍunandana ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
somanāthaprabhāvo ayaṃ śṛṇuṣvaikamanā nṛpa ।
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ sarvakāle śubhe dine ।।

viśeṣāc chuklapakṣe ca sūryavāreṇa saptamī ।
upoṣya yo naro bhaktyā rātrau kurvīta jāgaram ।।

pañcāmṛtena gavyena snāpayet parameśvaram ।
śrīkhaṇḍalepanaṃ kuryāt puṣpadhūpādikaṃ tathā ।।

ghṛtena bodhayed dīpaṃ gītaṃ nṛtyaṃ ca kārayet ।
somavāreṇa cāṣṭamyāṃ prabhāte pūjayed dvijam ।।

ātmavantaṃ jitakrodhaṃ dvijanindāvivarjitam ।
sarvāṅgaruciraṃ śāntaṃ svadāraparipālakam ।।

gāyatrīṃ paṭhamānaṃ ca vikarmarahitaṃ sadā ।
punar bhūrvṛṣalī śūdrī vartate yasya mandire ।।

hīnāṅgās tv atiriktāṅgā yeṣāṃ pūrvāpare na hi ।
vrate śrāddhe tathā dāne dvijā varjyāḥ sadā budhaiḥ ।।

puṃścalī taruṇī bhāryā dvijaḥ svādhyāyavarjitaḥ ।
ātmanā saha dātāramadho nayati pāṇḍava ।।

śālmalī naukayā tulyāḥ svadharmaniratā dvijāḥ ।
dātāraṃ caivam ātmānaṃ tārayanti taranti ca ।।

śrāddhaṃ someśvare pārtha yaḥ kuryāduta mānavaḥ ।
pitaras tasya tṛpyanti yāvad ābhūtasamplavam ।।

annaṃ vastraṃ hiraṇyaṃ ca yo dadyād agrajanmane ।
sa yāti śāṅkaraṃ lokam iti me satyabhāṣitam ।।

hayaṃ yo vai dadāt yatra sampūrṇābharaṇānvitam ।
raktaṃ vā pītavarṇaṃ vā sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam ।।

kuṅkumena viliptāṅgam aprajaṃ ca daded iti ।
sragdāmabhūṣitaṃ kaṇṭhe sitavastrāvaguṇṭhitam ।।

aṅghrirādhīyatāṃ skandhe madīyaṃ hayam āruha ।
ārūḍhe brāhmaṇe bhūyo bhāskaraḥ prīyatām iti ।।

sa yāti śāṅkaraṃ lokaṃ sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ ।
tasmāl lokāc cyutaś cāpi rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ ।।

tasya vaṃśe sadā rājyaṃ na naśyati kadācana ।
dīrghāyur jāyate putro bhāryā ca vaśavartinī ।।

jīved varṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ sarvaduḥkhavivarjitaḥ ।
somasya coparāge tu yo gacched vijitendriyaḥ ।।

sopavāso jitakrodho gāṃ tu dadyād dvijanmane ।
savatsāṃ kṣīrasaṃyuktāṃ śvetavarṇāṃ balānvitām ।।

śabalīṃ pītavarṇāṃ vā dhūmrāṃ vā nīlakandharām ।
kapilāṃ vā savastrāṃ vā ghaṇṭābharaṇabhūṣitām ।।

raupyakhurāṃ kāṃsyadohāṃ svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ nareśvara ।
śvetayā vardhate vaṃśo raktā saubhāgyavardhinī ।।

śabalī tāmravarṇā ca duḥkhaghnā ca prakīrtitā ।
kapilā tu haret pāpaṃ trijanmabhir upārjitam ।।

tasya lokam avāpnoti māndhātuś ca janeśvara ।
pakṣānte ca vyatīpāte vaidhṛtau ravisaṃkrame ।।

dinakṣaye gajacchāyā grahaṇe bhāskarasya ca ।
ye vrajanti viśuddhāṅgā vairañcye suradurlabhe ।।

mātṛhā guruhā yo hi ātmahā tu viśeṣataḥ ।
drupadādyaṃ japen nityaṃ prāṇāyāmaṃ tathā nṛpa ।।

gāyatrīṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ caiva saurīṃ śaivīṃ yadṛcchayā ।
so api pāpaiḥ pramucyeta ity evaṃ śaṅkaro abravīt ।।

yaḥ kuryāt somanāthasya tatra kartā pradakṣiṇam ।
pradakṣiṇīkṛtaṃ tena jambūdvīpaṃ nareśvara ।।

brahmahatyā surāpānaṃ gurudāraniṣevaṇam ।
bhrūṇahā śudhyate tatra evam eva na saṃśayaḥ ।।

tīrthākhyānam idaṃ puṇyaṃ yaḥ śṛṇoti jitendriyaḥ ।
vyādhito rājarogena atulāṃ śriyam āpnuyāt ।।

putrārthī labhate putraṃ niṣkāmaḥ svargam āpnuyāt ।
mucyate sarvapāpebhyas tīrthaṃ śrutvā varaṃ nṛpa ।।
etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ somanāthasya yat phalam ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe somanāthatīrthamahimānuvarṇano nāma caturadhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra piṅgalāvartakaṃ nṛpa ।
saṅgamasya samīpasthaṃ revāyā uttare taṭe ।।

havyavāhena rājendra sthāpitaḥ piṅgaleśvaraḥ ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca havyavāhena viprendra sthāpitaś ceśvaraḥ katham ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
retasā yadi rudreṇa tarpito havyavāhanaḥ ।
prāpto rudreṇa saumyena dehaṃ prāpya jagāma saḥ ।।

havyavāhamukhe kṣipte rudreṇāmitatejasā ।
rudrasya tejasā dagdhaḥ tīrthayātrāṃ karoti saḥ ।।

cacāra parayā bhaktyā dhyānam ugraṃ hutāśanaḥ ।
vāyubhakṣaḥ śataṃ sāgraṃ yāvad āsīt hutāśanaḥ ।।

tāvat tuṣṭo mahādevo hutāśanam uvāca ha ।
havyavāha varaṃ brūhi yat te manasi vartate ।।

hutāśana uvāca
namaste sarvalokeśa ugrarūpa namo astu te ।
yuṣmad retena saṃpluṣṭaḥ kubjo jāto maheśvara ।।

śarīrārto hy ahaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ saṃsthito narmadātaṭe ।
ityuktvāntardadhe devo nīrujastvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।।

havyavāhena rājendra sthāpitaḥ piṅgaleśvaraḥ ।
jitakrodho api yas tatra upavāsaṃ samācaret ।।

atirātraphalaṃ tatra ante rudram avāpnuyāt ।
guṇānvitāya dīnāya kapilāṃ tatra bhārata ।।

alaṃkṛtvā savastrāṃ ca savatsāṃ rūpasaṃyutām ।
yaḥ prayacchati viprāya sa gacchet paramaṃ padam ।।

tato gacchet tu rājendra tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam ।
sthāpitaṃ hy ṛṣisaṅghaiś ca brahmavaṃśodbhavair dvijaiḥ ।।

ṛṇamocanavikhyātaṃ revātaṭasamāśritam ।
ṣaṇmāsaṃ manujo bhaktyā tatra yas tarpayet pitṝn ।।

divyaiḥ pitryair manuṣyaiś ca ṛṇair ātmakṛtaiḥ saha ।
mucyate tatkṣaṇāt so atha snātvā vai narmadājale ।।

pratyakṣaṃ pātakaṃ tatra dṛśyate caiva rūpi ca ।
tatra tīrthe tu yo rājann ekacitto jitendriyaḥ ।।

snānaṃ dānaṃ naro dhīmān kārayed bhaktitatparaḥ ।
ṛṇatrayavimuktas tu vīryavān modate divi ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tasyaivānantaraṃ pārtha kapilātīrtham uttamam ।
sthāpitaṃ kapilenaiva sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।।

aṣṭamyāṃ ca site pakṣe caturdaśyāṃ nareśvara ।
snāpayet parayā bhaktyā kapilākṣīrasarpiṣā ।।

madhunā khaṇḍayuktena dadhyakṣataphalena ca ।
kapileśaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha niśīthe taṃ jagatprabhum ।।

śrīkhaṇḍena sugandhena guṇṭhayec ca maheśvaram ।
tataḥ sugandhapuṣpaiś ca śvetaiś ca nṛpanandana ।।

arcayanti jitakrodhā na te yānti yamālayam ।
asipatravanaṃ ghoraṃ yamavallīṃ sudāruṇām ।।

te vrajanti sukhaṃ pārtha kapileśe supūjite ।
snātvā revājale puṇye pūjayed brāhmaṇaṃ śubham ।।

gopradānena vastreṇa annena kila bhāratā ।
chatraśayyāpradānena bhūmau rājā bhavet tu saḥ ।।

nīrogas tīvratejāś ca jīvatputraḥ priyaṃvadaḥ ।
śatravo mitratāṃ yānti jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe kapileśvaramahimānuvarṇano nāma pañcādhikaśatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra pūtakeśvaram uttamam ।
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram ।।

susthāpitaḥ śivas tatra lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।
yas tatra manujaḥ śambhuṃ pūjayet pāṇḍunandana ।।

sarvān kāmān avāpnoti na sa yāti yamālayam ।
kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ sarvakāmā narādhipa ।।
ye arcayanti mahākālaṃ na te yānti yamālayam ।।
jalaśāyīti nāmnā vai vikhyātaṃ vasudhātale ।
dānavānāṃ vadhaṃ kṛtvā suptas tatra janārdanaḥ ।।

cakraṃ ca kṣālitaṃ tatra devadevena śauriṇā ।
sudarśanaṃ ca niṣpāpaṃ revātoyaprabhāvataḥ ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
cakratīrthaṃ samācakṣva ṛṣisaṅghair niṣevitam ।
viṣṇoḥ prabhāvamatulaṃ revāyāś caiva yatphalam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahābhāga viṣṇunā ca yudhiṣṭhira ।
gṛhyād guhyataraṃ tīrthaṃ nirmitaṃ cakriṇā svayam ।।

tat te ahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi kathāṃ pāpapraṇāśinīm ।
āsīt purā mahādaityo nalamegha iti śrutaḥ ।।

tena devā jitāḥ sarve hṛtarājyā narādhipa ।
nalameghabhayāt pārtha viṣṇurudrāḥ savāsavāḥ ।।

yamaskandajaleśāgnivāyavo vai dhaneśvaraḥ ।
vasuvākpatisiddhāś ca pracetāś ca pitāmahaḥ ।।

gatā devāḥ paraṃ lokaṃ viṣṇurudranamaskṛtam ।
stuvanti vividhaiḥ stotrair vāgīśapramukhā surāḥ ।।

namaḥ śivamūrtaye tubhyaṃ prāk sṛṣṭeḥ kevalātmane ।
guṇatrayavibhāgāya paścād bhedam upeyuṣe ।।

indrādipramukhān devān vivarṇānavanīpate ।
prasādābhimukho devaḥ pratyuvāca divaukasaḥ ।।

svāgataṃ surasaṅghāś ca kāntir naṣṭā purātanī ।
himapluṣṭaprabhāṇīva jyotiṣāṃ ca mukhāni vai ।।

prasabhādarciṣām etad anudgīrṇaṃ surāyudham ।
vṛtrasya hantuḥ kuliśaṃ kuṇṭhitaśrīva lakṣate ।।

kiṃcāyamaridurvāraḥ pāṇau pāśaḥ pracetasaḥ ।
mantropahṛtavīryasya phaṇino dainyam āgataḥ ।।

kuberasya manaḥ śalyaṃ śaṃsatīva parābhavam ।
apaviddhāṅgado bāhurbhagnaśākha iva drumaḥ ।।

yamo api vyalikhad bhūmiṃ daṇḍenāpi hatatviṣā ।
kuru tasmai namo dehanirviṇṇo yāti lāghavam ।।

amī ca dvādaśādityāḥ pratāpakṣayaśītalāḥ ।
citranyastā iva gatāḥ prakāmālokanīyatām ।।

mayi sṛṣṭiś ca lokānāṃ rakṣā yuṣmāsv avasthitā ।
tato mandānilodbhūtakamalākaraśobhinā ।।

gurunetrasahasreṇa prerayāmāsa vṛtrahā ।
sadvinetro harastryakṣaḥ sahasranayanādhikau ।।

vācaspatir uvācedaṃ prāñjalirhaṃsavāhanam ।
yuṣmad vaṃśodbhavas tāta nalamegho mahābalaḥ ।।

tena devagaṇāḥ sarve nirastā dānavena ca ।
nalamegho na vadhyo ataś calitena mayā suraiḥ ।।

vinā mādhavadevena sādhyo bhavati naiva hi ।
śaṅkhapadmagadāpāṇe jaya cakradhara prabho ।।

iti devastutiṃ śrutvā prabuddho jalaśāyikaḥ ।
uvāca madhurāṃ vāṇīṃ meghagambhīrayā girā ।।

kimarthaṃ bodhito brahman samastaiś ca surāsuraiḥ ।

brahmovāca nalameghabhayeneha samprāptās tava mandiram ।।

na vadhyaḥ kasyacit pāpo nalamegho janārdana ।
tava hastena duṣṭātmā mṛtyuṃ prāpsyati nānyathā ।।

janārdana uvāca
svasthānaṃ yāntu gīrvāṇā vadhiṣyāmi mahābalam ।
sthānaṃ śaṃsantu me devā vasate yatra durmatiḥ ।।

devā ūcuḥ
himālayaguhāṃ kṛṣṇa vasate dānaveśvaraḥ ।
caturviṃśatsahasrais tu kanyābhis tu samāvṛtaḥ ।।

turaṅgaiḥ syandanaiś caiva saṃkhyā teṣāṃ na vidyate ।
bhavanāni vicitrāṇi asaṃkhyāni bahūny api ।।

dviradāḥ parvatākārā hayāś ca dviradopamāḥ ।
mahābalo avasat tatra gīrvāṇabhayadāyakaḥ ।।

śrutvā devo vacas teṣāṃ devānāmāturātmanām ।
garuḍaṃ cintayāmāsa śatrusaṅghavidāraṇam ।।

cakraṃ kareṇa saṃgṛhya gadāṃ śaṅkhaṃ tataḥ prabhuḥ ।
śārṅgaṃ ca muśalaṃ sīraṃ gṛhītvā hi janārdanaḥ ।।

ārūḍhaḥ pakṣirājaṃ tu vadhārthaṃ dānavasya ca ।
dānavasya gṛhe pārtha utpātā ghoradarśanāḥ ।।

gomāyurgṛhamadhye tu kapoto gṛham āviśat ।
vinā vātena tasyaiva dhvajadaṇḍaṃ papāta ha ।।

sarpamūṣakayor buddhaṃ tathā keśarināgayoḥ ।
unmārgāḥ saritas tatra vahante cakramāśritāḥ ।।

akāle tarupuṣpāṇi dṛśyante tatra parvate ।
tataḥ prāpto jagannātho himavantaṃ nageśvaram ।।

pāñcajanyaṃ ca kṛṣṇena pūritaṃ purasannidhau ।
pāñcajanyasya śabdena ārūḍho dānaveśvaraḥ ।।

nalamegha uvāca
ko ayaṃ mṛtyuvaśaṃ prāptas tv ajñānena samāvṛtaḥ ।
dhundhumāra vraja śīghraṃ svasainyaparivāritaḥ ।।

balādānaya taṃ baddhvā mamāgre balaśālinam ।

dhundhumāra uvāca ānayāmi na sandehaḥ surapakṣāṃś ca sāmpratam ।।

syandanaiśca samāyukto gajavājibhaṭaiḥ saha ।
dṛṣṭas tāto jagad yoniḥ suparṇastho mahābalaḥ ।।

gṛhyatāṃ gṛhyatām eṣa ity uktās te ca kiṅkarāḥ ।
caturdikṣu ca vartante kiṅkarāḥ keśavasya ca ।।

suparṇenāgnibāṇena hanyante śalabhā iva ।
dhundhumāro api kṛṣṇena śaraghātena tāḍitaḥ ।।

hato vakṣasthalopānte patitaḥ syandanopari ।
hāhākāraṃ tataḥ sarve dānavāś cakrurudyatāḥ ।।

nalameghas tataḥ kruddho rathārūḍho vinirgataḥ ।
dadarśa keśavaṃ pārtha śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।।

nalamegha uvāca
hanyatāṃ dānavāḥ kṛṣṇo nihato yena dānavaḥ ।
hatvā ca me camūmukhyamadhunā ca kva yāsyati ।।

ityuktvā dānavaḥ pārtha dharṣayāmāsa sāyakaiḥ ।
dānavasya śarāṃs tatra chedayāmāsa keśavaḥ ।।

garutmān bhakṣayāmāsa tatsainyam atibhīṣaṇam ।
kṛṣṇena dviguṇās tatra preṣitā hi śilīmukhāḥ ।।

dviguṇād dviguṇīkṛtya preṣayāmāsa dānavaḥ ।
te api cāṣṭaguṇāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ chādayāmāsurojasā ।।

tataḥ kruddhena devena āgneyaṃ preṣitaṃ tadā ।
vāruṇaṃ prativāyavyaṃ nalamegho vyasarjayat ।।

nārasiṃhaṃ nṛsiṃho ayaṃ preṣayāmāsa pāṇḍava ।
nārasiṃhaṃ tato dṛṣṭvā nalamegho mahābalaḥ ।।

uttīrṇaḥ syandanāc chīghraṃ khaḍgaṃ gṛhya kareṇa tu ।
preṣayāmāsa kṛṣṇāya taṃ hantuṃ balavattaraḥ ।।

kruddho atha dānavaḥ pārtha āgataḥ keśavaṃ prati ।
khaḍgena ghātayāmāsa gadāpāṇiṃ janārdanam ।।

maṇḍalāgraṃ tato gṛhya keśavo hṛṣṭamānasaḥ ।
hato vakṣasthale daityo nalamegho mahābalaḥ ।।

janārdanaṃ tadā daityo nārācena jaghāna ha ।
janārdanas tataḥ kruddho nalameghaṃ mṛdhe nṛpa ।।

amoghaṃ cakram ādāya śiras tasya nyapātayat ।
patatā śirasā tasya vasudhā ca prakampitā ।।

samudrāḥ kṣubhitāḥ pārtha bhayād unmārgagāminaḥ ।
puṣpavaṣṭiṃ tato devā vavṛṣuḥ keśavopari ।।

avadhyaḥ surasaṅghānāṃ sa hataḥ keśavena tu ।
svasthānaś ca gato devo nalameghe nipātite ।।

janārdano api kaunteya narmadātaṭam āśritaḥ ।
lakṣmīsamanvitaḥ kṛṣṇo vilīno narmadātaṭe ।।

cakraṃ vimocitaṃ pāpakṣālanāya malānvitam ।
patitaṃ narmadātoye jalaśāyi samanvitam ।।

nirdhūtakalmaṣaṃ jātaṃ narmadāyāḥ prabhāvataḥ ।
nalameghavadhotpannaṃ yatpāpaṃ manujādhipa ।।

tatsarvaṃ kṣālitaṃ śīghraṃ revāyāmbhasi bhārata ।
tadā prabhṛti loke asmin jalaśāyī mahītale ।।
cakratīrthaṃ vadanty anye anekāghaughanāśanam ।।
tat tīrthasya prabhāvaṃ vai śṛṇuṣvaikamanā nṛpa ।
nāgānāṃ ca yathānanto gīrvāṇānāṃ janārdana ।।

māsānāṃ mārgaśīrṣo api nadīpuṇyā hi narmadā ।
māsi mārge site pakṣe ekādaśyāṃ śubhe dine ।।

gatvā ye manujās tatra kāmakrodhavivarjitāḥ ।
snāpayanti śriyaḥ kāntaṃ nāgaparyaṅkaśāyinam ।।

rājendra parayā bhaktyā kṣaudrasāgarasarpiṣā ।
guḍena toyamiśreṇa jagad yoniṃ janārdanam ।।

snāpyamānāś ca paśyanti ye lokāgatapātakāḥ ।
te yānti paramaṃ lokaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam ।।

ghṛtena bodhayed dīpam athavā tailamiśritam ।
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kṛtvā devaḥ syān nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

kathāṃ ca vaiṣṇavīṃ bhaktyā ye śṛṇvanti narottamāḥ ।
brahmahatyādipāpebhyo mucyante nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

ye kurvanti pradakṣiṇaṃ jalaśāyi jagadgurum ।
pradakṣiṇīkṛtaṃ tena jambūdvīpaṃ nareśvara ।।

tataḥ prabhāte vimale pitṝn saṃtarpya yatnataḥ ।
śrāddhaṃ vai brāhmaṇais tatra pūjyaiḥ pāṇḍavasattama ।।

svadāranirataiḥ śāntaiḥ paradāravivarjitaiḥ ।
vedābhyasanaśīlaiś ca svakarmanirataiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।

nityaṃ sajjanaśīlaiś ca trisandhyāparipālakaiḥ ।
tādṛśaiḥ kārayec chrāddham iccheyuḥ śreya ātmanām ।।

te dhanyā mānuṣe loke puṇyāś caivātra mānuṣāḥ ।
ye vasanti sadā kālaṃ pade brahmāśraye hrade ।।

jalaśāyinaṃ ca paśyanti pratyakṣaṃ suranāyakam ।
pakṣopavāsaṃ ye kecid vrataṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ śubham ।।

māsopavāsam ugraṃ ca tathānyat paramaṃ vratam ।
tatra tīrthe tu yaḥ pārtha kuryāt svargam avāpnuyāt ।।

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi tiladhenos tu yatphalam ।
tathā yasmin yathā deyaṃ dānaṃ tasya śrutaṃ phalam ।।

etat kathāntare puṇye munīndraiḥ pāpanāśanam ।
śrutaṃ hi naimiṣāraṇye nāradādyair anekadhā ।।

idam ākhyānam āyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ kīrtivivardhanam ।
viprāṇāṃ śrāvayed yas tu sarvaṃ tat phalam āpnuyāt ।।

bahūnāṃ na pradeyāni gogṛhaṃ śayanaṃ kila ।
vibhaktadakṣiṇā hy eṣā dātāraṃ nopatiṣṭhati ।।

ekasmai sā pradātavyā bahūnāṃ na yudhiṣṭhira ।
sā ca vikrayamāpannā dahed āsaptamaṃ kulam ।।

tilāḥ śvetās tathā kṛṣṇās tilāḥ proktāś ca varṇataḥ ।
tilānāṃ ca pramāṇāni dhenor vatsasya kārayet ।।

dātavyā vatsakenātha bahūnāṃ kāmināṃ na tu ।
yasmin deśe ca yan mānaṃ tilānāṃ ca vicārataḥ ।।

tena mānena sā kāryā akṣayaṃ phalam icchatā ।
arcanīyā prayatnena gandhapuṣpākṣatair vibho ।।

nāsāyāṃ sarvagandhāś ca jihvāyāṃ ṣaḍ rasā dhṛtāḥ ।
muktāphalāni vā dantajaṅghāpuccheṣu yojayet ।।

kukṣau kārpāsakaṃ deyaṃ nābhyāṃ padmaṃ sakāñcanam ।
oṣṭhe madhughṛtaṃ dadyāt kuryāt sarpiś ca romake ।।

kambale kambalaṃ dadyāl lalāṭe tāmrabhājanam ।
skandhe tu śakalā deyā lohadaṇḍaṃ ca saṅkaṭe ।।

guḍaṃ caiva gude dadyāc chroṇyāṃ madhughṛte tathā ।
yavase pāyasaṃ dadyād ghṛtakṣaudrasamanvitam ।।

svarṇaśṛṅgī raupyakhurī muktālāṅgulabhūṣaṇā ।
vastraṃ sadannaṃ dātavyaṃ kāṃsyapātrasudohanā ।।

yat tu bālakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ yad vā kṛtam ajānatā ।
vācā kṛtaṃ karmakṛtaṃ manasā yac ca cintitam ।।

jalamātre ṣṭhīvane ca muśale vā vilaṅghite ।
vṛṣalīgamane caiva gurudāraniṣevaṇe ।।

kanyāyāṃ gamane caiva suvrarṇasteya eva ca ।
surāpānaṃ ca yac cāpi tiladhenuḥ punāti hi ।।

ahorātropavāsena vidhivat sā mayoditā ।
yāsau yamapure caiva nadī vaitaraṇī smṛtā ।।

bālukāyāḥ sthale caiva pacyate yatra duṣkṛtī ।
avīcinarakopetau yau vai yugalaparvatau ।।

yatra lohamukhāḥ kākā yatra sthānaṃ bhayānakam ।
asipatravanaṃ yatra taptaṃ ca bālukam ।।

tatsukhena vyatikramya dharmarājā aśramaṃ vrajet ।
dharmarājas tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā sūnṛtaṃ vākyam abravīt ।।

vitānaṃ vitataṃ yogyaṃ maṇiralavibhūṣitam ।
atrāgaccha nṛpaśreṣṭha gaccha tvaṃ paramāṃ gatim ।।

mā ca pāparate dānaṃ na tad dānaṃ paraṃ hitam ।
mā vikāle virūpe ca na vyaṅge tu tathaiva ca ।।

avedaviduṣe caiva brāhmaṇe madaviklave ।
mitraghne ca kṛtaghne ca vratahīne tathaiva ca ।।

vedāntagāya dātavyā tasya tat tvaṃ vijānate ।
vedāntage tu sā deyā śrotriye abhūtabālakā ।।

sarvāṅgarucire deyā pavitre ca priyaṃvade ।
paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāṃ kārtikyāṃ cāpi bhārata ।।

vaiśākhyāṃ mārgaśīrṣe ca grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ ।
ayane viṣuve caiva vyatīpāte ca sarvathā ।।

ṣaḍaśītimukhe caiva gajachāyāsu sarvadā ।
eṣa te kathitaḥ kalpastiladhenor mayānagha ।।

bhittvā ca bhāskaraṃ lokaṃ harilokaṃ vrajanti te ।
etat te sarvamākhyātaṃ cakratīrthaphalaṃ nṛpa ।।
śravaṇāt kīrtanād vā api gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe cakratīrthamāhātmyavarṇano nāma ṣaḍadhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam ।
candrādityaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha sthāpitaṃ caṇḍamuṇḍayoḥ ।।

āsītpurā mahābhāgau caṇḍamuṇḍau tu dānavau ।
tapaś ca ceratus tatra narmadāyāṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।।

dhyāyato bhāskaraṃ devaṃ tamo nāśaṃ jagadgurum ।
tābhyāṃ ca toṣitaḥ so api sahasrāṃśur uvāca ha ।।

sādhusādhv iti tau pārtha narmadāyās taṭe śūbhe ।
caṇḍamuṇḍau varaṃ brūtaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ manasepsitam ।।

caṇḍamuṇḍāv ūcatuḥ
ajeyau caiva deveśa sarveṣāṃ devatānṛṇām ।
rogaiś ceva parityaktau savikāśaṃ divākara ।।

tat tatheti śubhaṃ vākyaṃ bhāskaras tāv avīdat ।
tataś cāntardadhe bhānurdānavābhyāṃ ca bhāskaram ।।

sthāpitaṃ parayā bhaktyā pūjayed yo jitendriyaḥ ।
gīrvāṇatā manuṣyasya prāptā tatraiva vartate ।।

vasate bhāskare loke vairañce devasannidhau ।
ghṛtena bodhayed dīpaṃ ṣaṣṭhyāṃ ṣaṣṭhyāṃ nareśvara ।।

mucyate sarvapāpebhyo mṛto yāti puraṃ raveḥ ।
candrādityam iti khyātaṃ tatra tīrthaṃ narottama ।।
vijayante sadā kālaṃ candrādityaṃ vrajanti ye ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe candrādityeśvaramahimānuvarṇano nāma saptādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra yamahāsamanuttamam ।
sarvapāpaharaṃ pārtha revāyāstaṭam āśritam ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
yamahāsaṃ kathaṃ jātaṃ pṛthivyāṃ munipuṅgava ।
etat sarvaṃ samākhyāhi mama kautūhalaṃ param ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahābhāga pṛṣṭaṃ te dharmanandana ।
snānārthaṃ narmadāyāṃ tu āgatas te pitā purā ।।

rajakena yathā dhautaṃ nirmalaṃ vasanaṃ bhavet ।
tathaiva paśyatā rājan revājalam anuttamam ।।

hāsyaṃ kṛtaṃ yamenātha utthitaṃ liṅgam uttamam ।
tatas tadā hi rājendra vāguvācā aśarīriṇī ।।

yamahāsam idaṃ tīrthaṃ khyātiṃ yāsyati sarvadā ।
snāpayitvā śivaṃ tatra yamaḥ svargaṃ jagāma ha ।।

yamahāse tu rājendra jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ ।
viśeṣādāśvine māsi kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśīm ।।

upoṣya parayā bhaktyā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kṛtvā dīpaṃ devasya bodhayet ।।

ghṛtena caiva rājendra śṛṇu tasyaiva yatphalam ।
mucyate sarvapāpais tu agamyāgamanodbhavaiḥ ।।

abhakṣyabhakṣaṇaiḥ pāpaiḥ pāpair vā peyasambhavaiḥ ।
avāhyavāhaneyac ca adrohya drohaṇe tathā ।।

snānamātreṇa tac caiva naśyet pāpamanekadhā ।
yamalokaṃ na paśyec ca na tyajet pāṇḍunandana ।।

bahūnāṃ paramaṃ guptaṃ tīrthaṃ bhūmyāṃ nṛpātmaja ।
tad akṣayaphalaṃ teṣāṃ yamahāse pradāyinām ।।

amāvāsyāṃ jitakrodho yas tu pūjayate dvijān ।
bhūmidānena yo bhaktyā tiladānena bhārata ।।

kṛṣṇājinapradānena tiladhenupradānataḥ ।
vasubhe vṛddhiyoge ca ye pradāsyanti bhaktitaḥ ।।

odanaṃ vāri dhūrvāhaṃ hayaṃ cāpi mahābalam ।
kanyāṃ vastramajāṃ gāṃ vai mahiṣīm athavāśvinīm ।।

ye yacchanti nṛpaśreṣṭha nopasarpanti te yamam ।
yamo api bhavati prīto janmajanma yudhiṣṭhira ।।

yamasya vāhanaṃ strīṃ ca mahiṣīṃ tatra bhārata ।
tasya dānena satataṃ yamaḥ prīto bhaven nṛpa ।।

na sa yāti yame loke yadi pāpaiḥ samāśritaḥ ।
etasmāt kāraṇāt pārtha mahiṣīdānaṃ uttamam ।।

aurṇavastradvayaṃ kāryaṃ lohavarṇaṃ ca veṣṭitam ।
dāpayed dharmarājāya prīyatāṃ me dvijottama ।।

anenaiva tu dānena yamaḥ prīto astu me sadā ।
ityuccārya dvijasyāgre yamalokaṃ bhayāvaham ।।

asipatravane ghore yamavallī sudāruṇā ।
raudrā vaitaraṇī ceti kumbhīpākaḥ sudāruṇaḥ ।।

kālasūtraṃ mahābhīmaṃ tathā yamalaparvatau ।
krakacaṃ tailayantraṃ ca sthāne gṛdhrāḥ sudāruṇāḥ ।।

aniśvāso mahāraudro bhīṣaṇo rauravas tathā ।
ete ghorāś ca narakāḥ śrūyante dvijasattama ।।

tatprasādena te saumyās tīrthasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।
dānasyāsya prabhāveṇa yamahāsaprabhāvataḥ ।।
yamalokaṃ na vai yāti narakaṃ naiva paśyati ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe yamahāsamahimānuvarṇano nāmāṣṭādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra koṭīśvaram anuttamam ।
ṛṣikoṭiḥ samāyātā tatra vai kurunandana ।।

kṛṣṇadvaipāyanas tatra mokṣārthaṃ munipuṅgavaḥ ।
mantrayitvā dvijaiḥ sarvair vedamaṇḍalapāragaiḥ ।।

pañcāmṛtena gavyena tilamiśreṇa tatpara ।
pitṛṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā piṇḍadānaṃ yathāvidhi ।।

śrāvaṇasya tu māsasya pūrṇimāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
prāpyate cākṣayā tṛptir yāvad āhūtasamplavam ।।

pitṝṇāṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ revājalam upāśritam ।
mokṣadaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ nirmitaṃ munipuṅgavaiḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra vyāsatīrtham anuttamam ।
durlabhaṃ manujaiḥ pārtha antarikṣe vyavasthitam ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kasmād vai vyāsatīrthaṃ tu antarikṣe vyavasthitam ।
etad ācakṣva saṃkṣepān na ca granthasya vistaraḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahābāho dharmavān guruvatsalaḥ ।
svadharmanirataḥ pārtha tīrthayātrākṛtādaraḥ ।।

durlabhaṃ sarvajantūnāṃ vyāsatīrthaṃ nareśvara ।
dharṣito vṛddhabhāvena vaikalyena narādhipa ।।

gatacetās tu sañjātas tathā bhoḥ pāṇḍunandana ।
guhyād guhyataraṃ tīrthaṃ nākhyātaṃ kasyacin mayā ।।

kālas tatraiva rājendra na vased vāsavājñayā ।
antarikṣe ca saṃjātaṃ revāyāś ceṣṭitaṃ yataḥ ।।

virañcir naiva śaknoti revāyā guṇakīrtanam ।
vyāsatīrthaṃ viśeṣeṇa śrutamātraṃ vadāmy aham ।।

pratyakṣaḥ pratyayo yatra dṛśyate hi kalau yuge ।
vihaṅgo gacchate naiva bhittvā śūlaṃ sudāruṇam ।।

tasyotpattiṃ samāsena kathayāmi nṛpātmaja ।
āsīt pūrvaṃ mahārāja ṛṣiś caiva parāśaraḥ ।।

tena cograṃ tapas taptaṃ gaṅgāmbhasi tu bhārata ।
prāṇāyāmena cātiṣṭhat praviṣṭo jāhnavījale ।।

pūrṇe ca dvādaśe varṣe niṣkrānto jalamadhyataḥ ।
bhikṣārthe cāgato grāmaṃ nāvi tatraiva tiṣṭhatī ।।

tatra dṛṣṭā parotsṛṣṭā bālā tena manoramā ।
tāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā sa kāmārta uvāca madhurākṣaram ।।

māṃ ramasvādya tvaṃ kāsi kāmukaṃ mṛgalocane ।
nāvārūḍhe nadītīre mama cittapramāthinī ।।

evamuktā tu sā tena praṇamya ṛṣisattamam ।
nāvaṃ rakṣāmy ahaṃ vipra jānāmi svāminaṃ na tu ।।

mamedaṃ ca vayo brahmañc cheṣaṃ tvaṃ jñātum arhasi ।
evamuktas tayā so api kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvābravīd idam ।।

ahaṃ jñānabalād bhadre jānāmi tava sambhavam ।
kaivartaputrikā na tvaṃ rājaputrī hi sundarī ।।

kanyovāca
kaḥ pitā kathyatāṃ brahman kasyāhamudarodbhavā ।
kasmin vaṃśe prajātāhaṃ kaivartatanayā katham ।।

parāśara uvāca
kathayāmi ca te tātaṃ yaṃ tvaṃ māṃ paripṛcchasi ।
vasu nāmā ca rājābhūt somavaṃśe pratāpavān ।।

jambūdvīpādhipo bhadre śatrusaṃtrāsanas tathā ।
śatāni sapta bhāryāṇāṃ putrāṇāṃ tu daśaiva hi ।।

dharmeṇa pālitā lokāḥ śivapūjārataḥ sadā ।
mlecchās tasya virodhena śākadvīpanivāsinaḥ ।।

teṣāṃ ca sādhanārthāya gatollaṅghya mahodadhim ।
saṃyuktaḥ putrabhṛtyaiś ca pauruṣe mahati sthitaḥ ।।

sagrāmas taiḥ samārabdhaścārvaṅgi vasunā saha ।
jitā mlecchāḥ samastāś ca vasunā hyavanībhṛtā ।।

karadās te kṛtās tena sabhṛtyabalavāhanāḥ ।
pradhānā tasya mahiṣī tava mātā mṛgekṣaṇā ।।

pravāsasthe ca bhūpāle saṃjātā ca rajasvalā ।
nārīṇāṃ tu sadā kāle manmatho hy adhiko bhavet ।।

viśeṣeṇa ṛtau kāle bhidyate kāmasāyakaiḥ ।
manmathena tu saṃtaptācintayat sā śubhekṣaṇā ।।

dūtaṃ sampreṣayāmyadya vasurājasamīpataḥ ।
vyāhṛtaḥ satvaro dūto gaccha tvaṃ nṛpasannidhau ।।

dūta uvāca
pararājye vasurdevi gato rājā dviḍantakṛt ।
tatra gantuṃ na śakyeta jalayantrair vinā śubhe ।।

jalayānāni sarvāṇi neyāni ca pare taṭe ।
tasya vākyena sā nārī viṣaṇṇā madapīḍitā ।।

rājñīṃ dṛṣṭvā sakhī brūte kasmāt tvaṃ parikhidyase ।
lekho ayaṃ preṣyatāṃ devi śukahaste yathā tathā ।।

samudraṃ laṅghayitvā tu śakunto yāti sundari ।
vyāhṛto lekhakas tatra likha lekhaṃ amamājñayā ।।

tvāṃ vinā paṭṭarājñī sā vasurāja na jīvati ।
ṛtukālaś ca samprāptaḥ samastaṃ cāvadhāryatām ।।

likhito bhūrjapatre ca vṛttaḥ sa lekhakena tu ।
śūkaḥ pañjaramadhyastha ānītas tatra sannidhau ।।

rājñī uvāca taṃ tatra gṛhyalekhaṃ śuka vraja ।
gataḥ pakṣī tataḥ śīghraṃ vasurājasamīpataḥ ।।

kṣipto lekhaḥ śukenaiva satyabhāmā visarjitaḥ ।
lekhārthaṃ cintayāmāsa vīryaṃ gṛhya nareśvaraḥ ।।

amoghapuṭikāṃ kṛtvā pratilokena viśrutaḥ ।
śūkasya cārpayāmāsa gaccha rājñī samīpataḥ ।।

vasurājaṃ praṇamyātha bījaṃ gṛhya papāta ha ।
samudropari saṃprāptaḥ śuko yāti yathecchayā ।।

sāmiṣaṃ ca śukaṃ jñātvā śyenas tatrāpi dhāvitaḥ ।
hataścañcuprahāreṇa śukaḥ śyenena bhārata ।।

mūrchāpannasya tadvīrya patitaṃ jalamadhyataḥ ।
matsyena gilitaṃ tatra tadvīryaṃ pārthivasya ca ।।

dāśairmatsyo gahītaś ca ānītaḥ svagṛhaṃ prati ।
yāvat taṃ pāṭayāmāsūryamalaṃ dadṛśe tadā ।।

śaśimaṇḍalasaṅkāśaṃ sūryatejaḥ samaprabham ।
dṛṣṭvā te dharṣitāḥ sarve kaivartā jāhnavītaṭe ।।

harṣitās te gatāḥ sarve pradhānasya ca mandiram ।
putraṃ rājñe pradāyaiva putrīṃ ca pratyapālayat ।।

tat tvaṃ devi varārohe kaivartakanyakā nahi ।
tataḥ sā cintayāmāsa parāśaravacas tadā ।।

evamuktā tu sā tena dattvātmānaṃ nareśvara ।
uvāca sādhvī bho brahman matsyagandho nivartyatām ।।

tatas tena tu sā bālā divyagandhābhivāsitā ।
kṛtā yogabalenaiva jvālayitvā vibhāvasum ।।

kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ vahner uddhṛtā tena sā tadā ।
jvalamānasya madhye tu kāmasthānāni so aspṛśat ।।

jñātvā kāmotsukaṃ vipraṃ bhītā sā nṛpanandana ।
uvāca sahasā bālā divā ca lokasannidhau ।।

tatas tena kṣaṇaṃ dhyātā pūrayantī digambaram ।
āgatā tāmasī tāta yayā vyāptaṃ samantataḥ ।।

tataḥ savismayaṃ tena rahobālā mṛgekṣaṇā ।
kāmenaiva hi taptena strīsaukhyaṃ krīḍatā tadā ।।

tatas tena muhūrtenāpatyabhāreṇa pīḍitā ।
bālakaṃ tatra jaṭilaṃ subhagaṃ daṇḍadhārakam ।।

kamaṇḍaludharaṃ śāntaṃ mekhalākaṭibhūṣaṇam ।
dhṛtopavītakaṃ skandhe viṣṇumāyāvivārjitam ।।

mātā hi śaṅkitā tatra dṛṣṭvā putrasya cāpalam ।
vepamānā tato bālā gatā sā śaraṇaṃ muneḥ ।।

rakṣa rakṣa muniśreṣṭha parāśara mahāmune ।
jātamaty adbhutaṃ vipraṃ kaupīnāmbaramekhalam ।।

daṇḍahastaṃ jaṭāyuktamuttarīyavibhūṣitam ।

parāśara uvāca mā bhaiṣīstvaṃ suto jātaḥ kanyaiva tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।।

nāmnā satyavatī ceti dvitīyā gandhayojanā ।
śantanur nāma rājā vai sa te bhartā bhaviṣyati ।।

prathamā mahiṣī tasya somavaṃśavibhūṣaṇā ।
gaccha tvaṃ svāśramaṃ bhadre pūrvarūpeṇa saṃsthitā ।।

mā vaikalyaṃ kuruṣvedaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ jñānasya me balam ।
ity uktvā prayayau vipraḥ sā bālā sthalamāśritā ।।

natvā putraṃ parābhaktyā sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇayena ca ।
taṃ prayāntamathālokya satyavaty abravīt sutam ।।

kāmo deyas tvayābhīṣṭaḥ sneho vai yadi mātari ।
kimapy upādiśa tvaṃ māṃ yena siddhim avāpnuyām ।।

vyāsa uvāca
īśvarārādhane yatnaṃ kuruṣva tvaṃ sadāmbike ।
tataḥ sā putravākyena viṣaṇṇā pāṇḍunandana ।।

yojanagandhovāca
tvad viyogād ahaṃ putra pañcatvaṃ yāmi nānyathā ।
nāsti putrasamaḥ sneho nāsti bhrātṛsamaṃ balam ।।

putra uvāca
mā viṣādaṃ kuruṃ tvaṃ hi satyaṃ vai pitṛbhāṣitam ।
āpatkāle tvayāhaṃ vai smartavyaḥ kāryasiddhaye ।।

āpadastārayiṣyāmi kṣamyatāṃ mātarātmaje ।
ityuktvā tu yayau vyāsaḥ kanyā sā api piturgṛham ।।

parāśarasutas tatra niṣaṇṇo vanamadhyataḥ ।
tretāyugāvasāne tu dvāparādau nareśvara ।।

vyāso virañcaye jāta ākhyāto nāradena ca ।
ṛṣir mahānubhāvas tu putraḥ pārāśarasya ca ।।

kaivartakanyakājāto jānīhi jāhnavī taṭe ।
vākyoktyā nāradasyaiva āgatāḥ surasattamāḥ ।।

bhānuḥ pitāmahaḥ śakra ṛṣisaṅghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।
āśīrvādaṃ pṛthag dattvā sādhu sādhviti bhāṣitaḥ ।।

pitāmahena bālo asau jātamakarmādi saṃskṛtaḥ ।
dvaipāyano dvīpajanmā pārāśaryaḥ parāśarāt ।।

kṛṣṇagātrāt kṛṣṇanāmā havyādātur viśiṣyati ।
virañcinābhiṣikto asau ṛṣisaṅghaiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।

vyāsas tvaṃ sarvalokānām ity uktvā prayayuḥ punaḥ ।
tīrthayātrā samārabdhā kṛṣṇadvaipāyanena tu ।।

gaṅgāvagāhitā tena kedāraṃ puṣkaraṃ tathā ।
gayā ca naimiṣaṃ tīrthaṃ kurukṣetre sarasvatī ।।

ujjayinyāṃ mahākālaṃ somanāthaṃ yayau tataḥ ।
pṛthivyāṃ sāgarāntāyāṃ snāto vyāso mahāmuniḥ ।।

aṭan vai narmadāṃ prāpto rudradehodbhavāṃ nadīm ।
sāhlādaṃ narmadāṃ dṛṣṭvā cittaṃ viśrāmyapārthiva ।।

tapaś cacāra vipulaṃ narmadātaṭam āśritaḥ ।
grīṣme pañcāgnimadhyastho varṣāsu sthaṇḍileśayaḥ ।।

sārdravāsās tu hemante dhyāyamāno maheśvaram ।
sṛṣṭisaṃhārakartāram acchedyaṃ ca sadāśivam ।।

nityaṃ siddheśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ pūjayan pāṇḍunandana ।
arcanāt siddhaliṅgasya dhyānayogaprabhāvataḥ ।।

pratyakṣa īśvaro jātaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasya tu ।
toṣito ahaṃ tvayā vipra varaṃ prārthaya śobhanam ।।

vyāsa uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo asi me deva yadi deyo varo mama ।
pratyakṣo narmadātīre svayaṃ bhavādya me vibho ।।

atītānāgatajñānaṃ tvatprasādān maheśvara ।

īśvara uvāca evaṃ bhavatu te vipra matpasādāt na saṃśayaḥ ।।

tvayā bhaktigṛhīto ahaṃ pratyakṣo narmadātaṭe ।
ityuktvā prayayau devaḥ kailāsaṃ nagam uttamam ।।

patnīsaṃgrahaṇaṃ jātaṃ putro jāto yadāsya ca ।
devair adhyāsitaḥ sarvaiḥ sendrabrahmapurogamaiḥ ।।

putrajanmatatojñātvā āgatā ṛṣisattamāḥ ।
tīrthayātrāprasaṅgena parāśarapurogamāḥ ।।

manvatriviṣṇuhārītayājñavalkyośano aṅgirāḥ ।
yam āpastambasaṃvartā kātyāyanabṛhaspatī ।।

evam ādi sahasrāṇi lakṣakoṭir anekadhā ।
vyāsāśrame śubhe puṇye prāptāḥ sarve dvijottamāḥ ।।

dṛṣṭvā vyāsas tu viprendrānabhyutthāya kṛtodyamaḥ ।
pitṛpūrvaṃ praṇamyādau teṣāṃ vārtāṃ pradāpayan ।।

kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā idaṃ vākyam uvāca ha ।
uddhṛtaṃ tu mamānandaṃ yuṣmat sambhāṣadarśanāt ।।

āraṇyāni ca śākāni phalāny āraṇyakāni ca ।
tāni dāsyāmi sarveṣāṃ yuṣmākaṃ pitṛpūrvakam ।।

niyamaiḥ saṃyutān sarvān pratyekaṃ praṇanāma ca ।
tatas taṃ praṇataṃ dṛṣṭvā tatra dvaipāyanaṃ dvijam ।।

vardhayitvā jayāśīrbhis tato vīkṣa parasparam ।
parāśaraḥ samastaiś ca vīkṣito munipuṅgavaiḥ ।।

uttaraṃ dīyatāṃ tāta kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasya ca ।
evam uktas tu taiḥ sarvair bhagavāṃś ca parāśaraḥ ।।

uvāca svātmajaṃ vyāsam ṛṣibhir yac cikīrṣitam ।
necchanti dakṣiṇe kūle vratabhaṅgabhayāt suta ।।

paraṃ vai bhoktukāmāś ca tava śraddhāviśeṣataḥ ।

vyāsa uvāca karomi bhavatāṃ yuktam atraiva sthīyatāṃ kṣaṇam ।।

yāvad āsādya saritaṃ karomi vidhipūrvakam ।
evam uktvā śucir bhūtvā narmadātaṭam āśritaḥ ।।
stotraṃ jagāda sahasā taṃ nibodha janeśvara ।।
vyāsa uvāca
jaya devi namo varade śivade jaya pāpavimardini śūlakare ।
jaya bhairavadehavilīnakare jaya devi pitāmahasannamite ।।

jaya bhāskaraśakrasadānamite jaya ṣaṇmukhatātasute varade ।
jaya devaśarīrasamūhamaye jaya sāgaragāmini bhūmisute ।।

jaya jaya lokasamastakṛtābharaṇe jaya duḥkhadaridravināśakare ।
jaya putra kalatravivṛddhikare jaya devi sudarśanapāpahare ।।

etad vyāsakṛta stotraṃ yaḥ paṭhec chivasannidhau ।
gṛhe vā śuddhabhāvena kāmakrodhavivarjitaḥ ।
vyāsas tasya bhavet prītaḥ prīto ayaṃ vṛṣavāhanaḥ ।।

stutā ca narmadādevī tato vacanam abravīt ।

narmadovāca stutivādena tuṣṭāsmi bho bho vyāsamahāmune ।।

yam icchasi varaṃ samyak taṃ te sarvaṃ dadāmy aham ।

vyāsa uvāca yadi tuṣṭāsi me devi yadi deyo varo mama ।।

ātithyam uttare kūle mama dātuṃ tvam arhasi ।

narmadovāca ayuktaṃ cintitaṃ vyāsa amārge tvaṃ pravartase ।।

indracandrayamāḥ śaktā unmārgeṇa na vāhitum ।
anyaṃ yācasva he vatsa yatkiṃcid bhuvi durlabham ।।

eva śrutvā vaco devyā vyāso mūrcchāṃ gatas tadā ।
vṛthā kleśaś ca saṃjātaḥ patito dharaṇītale ।।

dharaṇī kampitā sarvā saśailavanakānanā ।
mūrchāpannaṃ tato vyāsaṃ jñātvā devāḥ parāśaram ।।

āyātā devatāḥ sarve hāhākāraṃ prakurvataḥ ।
utthāpayantas te vyāsam ūcuśca saritāṃ varām ।।

brāhmaṇārthaṃ tu saṃkliṣṭā nāmahetoḥ saridvare ।
gavārthe brāhmaṇārthe ca prāṇān parityajet ।।

evaṃ sā narmadā proktā brahmādyaiś ca surair drutam ।
vikūlatāṃ vai pradadau samantād revābhiṣiktaḥ sa jalena pūtaḥ ।।

sacetanaḥ satyavatī suto ayaṃ nanāma devaiḥ saha narmadāntaiḥ ।

vyāsa uvāca tīrthaṃ samastaṃ tvayi devatānāṃ phalaṃ pradiṣṭaṃ mama mandabhāgyam ।।

narmadovāca
yato yato vyāsamahānubhāva sumerunāmno dharaṇīdharasya ।
vindhyasya cānyasya ca te hi mārgaṃ yāsyāmi vai dharmadharasya dhanyā ।।

evamukto mahātejā vyāsaḥ satyavatīyutaḥ ।
dakṣiṇe cālayāmāsa svāśramān munipuṅgavān ।।

daṇḍahasto mahātejā huṅkārair nṛpanandana ।
vyāsahuṅkārabhītā ca calitā rudranandinī ।।

daṇḍena darśayan mārgaṃ devī tatra pravartitā ।
vyāsamārgagatāṃ devīṃ dṛṣṭvā cendrapurogamāḥ ।।

puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ dadur vyāse stutiṃ kurvanti kinnarāḥ ।
praphullanayanā jātāḥ parāśaramukhā dvijāḥ ।।

kiṃ kurmo atra mahimnā te karmaṇā te varaṃ jitāḥ ।

vyāsa uvāca tapaḥ kṛtvā suvipulaṃ dānaṃ dattvā mahatphalam ।।

etad eva naraiḥ kāryaṃ sādhūnāṃ paritoṣaṇam ।
suvibhaktā mahābhāgā anugrāhyasya samprati ।।

tasmān mamāśrame puṇye sthīyatāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
ātithyaṃ śākaparṇaiś ca udakena vimiśritaiḥ ।।

pratipannaṃ samastaiś ca parāśaramukhair dvijaiḥ ।
śrayadhvam āśramaṃ puṇyaṃ narmadāyottare taṭe ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
snānatarpaṇakṛtyāni kṛtāni ca dvijottamaiḥ ।
vyāsakuṇḍaṃ tato gatvā homaṃ samyagakārayan ।।

śrīphalair bilvapatraiś ca dhyānayuktāś ca juhvati ।
gautamo bhṛgumāṇḍavyau nārado lomaśas tathā ।।

parāśaras tathā śaṅkhaḥ kauśikaś cyavano muniḥ ।
pippalādo vaśiṣṭhaś ca nāśiketur mahātapāḥ ।।

viśvāmitro hy agastyaś ca uddālakayamau tathā ।
śāṇḍilyo jaiminiḥ kāvyo yājñavalkyośanāṅgirāḥ ।।

atriḥ śātātapaś caiva bharato mudgalas tathā ।
vātsyāyano mahātejāḥ saṃvartaḥ śaktir eva ca ।।

jātūkarṇo bharadvājo bālakhilyādayas tathā ।
ekacittā dvijā rājan mantratantraṃ prakurvataḥ ।।

tataḥ samutthitaṃ liṅgaṃ jvalatkālānalaprabham ।
sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇato vyāso devaṃ dṛṣṭvā trilocanam ।।

āśīrvādaṃ punar viprā dattvā vyāsaṃ tadā yayuḥ ।
tataḥ prabhṛti tattvajña tīrthaṃ khyātaṃ tu pāṇḍava ।।

snānadānavidhānaṃ ca yasmin kāle pratiṣṭhitam ।
kathayāmi samastaṃ te bhrātṝṇāṃ caiva pāṇḍava ।।

kārttikasyāsite pakṣe caturdaśyāṃ nṛpottama ।
upoṣya yo naro bhaktyā rātrau kurvīta jāgaram ।।
snāpayed īśvaraṃ bhaktyā kṣaudreṇa kṣīrasarpiṣā ।।
dadhnā ca khaṇḍayuktena kuśatoyena vā punaḥ ।
śrīkhaṇḍena sugandhena pūjayeta maheśvaram ।।

tataḥ sugandhapuṣpaiś ca bilvapatraiś ca pūjayet ।
kumudena ca kundena kuśapuṣpākṣatādibhiḥ ।।

unmattapuṣpaiś ca rasaiḥ saumyaiś caivāpy anuttamaiḥ ।
arcayet parayā bhaktyā dvīpeśvaram anuttamam ।।

mandārādikapuṣpaiś ca pūjayet parameśvaram ।
guḍamaṇḍapradānena pātakaṃ divasārjitam ।।

māsārjitaṃ ca naśyeta guḍamaṇḍaśatena ca ।
ṣaṇmāsaṃ ca sahasreṇa arkābdaṃ dviguṇena tu ।।

ājanmajanitaṃ pāpam ayutena praṇaśyati ।
paurṇamāsyāṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha snānaṃ kurvīta bhaktitaḥ ।।

mantroktena vidhānena kṛtvā pāpakṣayaṃkaram ।
vāruṇaṃ ca tathā jñeyaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃ karam ।।

devān pitṝn manuṣyāṃś ca vidhivat tarpayen nṛpa ।
ṛcam ekāṃ japet snātaḥ sāmavedaphalaṃ labhet ।।

yajurvedam atharvāṇaṃ gāyatryā sarvam āpnuyāt ।
japed aṣṭākṣaraṃ mantraṃ sauraṃ vā śaivam eva ca ।।

athavā vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ dvādaśākṣaram eva ca ।
pūjayed brāhmaṇān bhaktyā sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitān ।।

svadharmaniratān viprān dambhalobhavivarjitān ।
hīnāṅgānadhikāṅgāṃś ca patitāñ chūdrasevitān ।।

śūdrānnena ca saṃyuktā vṛṣalī yasya mandire ।
paunarbhavās tathā duṣṭā gurunindāparāyaṇāḥ ।।

vedādhyayanahīnāś ca hetukāḥ kākavṛttayaḥ ।
īdṛśān varjayec chrāddhe dāne caiva vrate tathā ।।

gāyatrī pāṭhamātreṇa varaṃ vipraḥ supaṇḍitaḥ ।
nāyaṃ bhṛtacaturvidyaḥ sarvāśīsarvavikrayī ।।

īdṛśān varjayec chrāddhe vrate dāne hiraṇmaye ।
upānahau ca vastraṃ ca śayyāṃ vā chatramāsanam ।।

yo dadyād brāhmaṇe bhaktyā so api svarge mahīyate ।
pratyakṣā surabhī tatra tiladhenus tathā matā ।।

tiladhenupradātāraḥ svasvadātāra eva ca ।
kṛṣṇājinapradātāro dātāraḥ kuñjarasya ca ।।

kanyāvidyāpradātāro akṣayaṃ lokam avāpnuyuḥ ।
dhūrvahau dakṣiṇāyuktau dhānyopaskarasaṃyutau ।।

dāpayet sarvakāmāya iti me satyabhāṣitam ।
sūtreṇa veṣṭayed īśam athavā jagatīruham ।।

mandiraṃ parayā bhaktyā athavā parameśvaram ।
atha pradakṣiṇā kāryā vinā śūdreṇa mānavaiḥ ।।

jambūplakṣāhvayau dvīpau śālmaliś ca bhaven nṛpa ।
kuśaḥ krauñcas tathā śākaḥ puṣkaraś ceti saptamaḥ ।।

saptasāgaraparyantā veṣṭitā tena bhārata ।
dvīpeśvare tu rājendra vṛṣotsargo jitendriyaiḥ ।।

vṛṣasya mokṣaṇe naiva aiśvaraṃ lokam āpnuyāt ।
yas tu vai pāṇḍuro vaktre lalāṭe caraṇe tathā ।।

lāṅgūle ca mukhe śubhraḥ sa vai nākasya darśanaḥ ।
nīlo ayamīdṛśaḥ prokto dadyād dvīpeśvare śūbhe ।।

pāmarāste apy asaṃkhyātā nāke gacchanti pārthiva ।
saure caṇḍeśvare loke pure vai cakrapāṇinaḥ ।।

sa bhuṅkte svecchayā lokaṃ vyāsatīrthaprabhāvataḥ ।
sapatnīkāṃs tato viprān pūjayet tatra bhaktitaḥ ।।

sitaratnāni vastrāṇi pradadyādagrajanmane ।
kṛtvā pradakṣiṇāyugmaṃ prīyatāṃ me jagadguruḥ ।।

nāsti viprasamo bandhur iha loke paratra ca ।
yamaloke mahāghore patitaṃ yo abhirakṣati ।।

puruṣāḥ parayā bhaktyā vedaśāstrārthacintakāḥ ।
dvīpeśvaraṃ mahādevaṃ saṃsmaranti gṛhe sthitāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ na jāyate śoko na hānir na ca duṣkṛtam ।
prathamaṃ pūjayet tatra liṅgaṃ siddheśvaraṃ nṛpa ।।

yatra siddho mahābhāgaḥ satyavatyāś ca nandanaḥ ।
asyaivārcanataḥ siddhaḥ pārāśaryo munis tataḥ ।।

tasmiṃs tīrthe tu ye rājan prāṇatyāgaṃ prakurvate ।
te yānti paramaṃ lokaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।

samā sahasrāṇi mṛto jale hi yo vai nimagnaḥ patane ca ṣoḍaśa ।
mahāhave ṣaṣṭiraśītigogṛhe tvanāśake bhārata cākṣayā gatiḥ ।।

atha yogena tenaiva prāpyate cākṣayā gatiḥ ।
sūryalokaṃ tato gatvā śivalokaṃ vrajanti te ।।

pitāpitāmahaś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ ।
anubhūtā nirīkṣante āgacchantaṃ svagotrajam ।।

tiṣṭhate caiva gotreṣu yo dadyāc ca tilodakam ।
kārtikyāṃ ca tathā māghyāṃ vaiśākhyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

svargaṃ ca te prayāntyante svasvaputraprabhāvataḥ ।
etat te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ dvīpeśvaraphalaṃ śubham ।।

yaḥ paṭhet prātar utthāya yaḥ śṛṇoti naro nṛpa ।
so api pāpair vinirmukto modate śivamandire ।।

īśvaraṃ sarvatīrthānāṃ nirmitaṃ ṛṣipuṅgavaiḥ ।
kāmadaṃ sarvajantūnāṃ revāyāṃ ca nṛpottama ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe dvīpeśvaravyāsatīrthavarṇano nāma navādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra prabhāseśvaram uttamam ।
vikhyātāṃ triṣu lokeṣu svargasopānam uttamam ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
prabhāsaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ tu yathājātaṃ mahāphalam ।
svargasopānamārgaṃ ca saṃkṣepāt kathayasva me ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
durbhagā ravipatnī ca prabhā nāmeti viśrutā ।
tayā cārādhitaḥ śambhur ugreṇa tapasā purā ।।

vāyubhakṣā sthitā varṣaṃ śivadhyānaparāyaṇā ।
tatas tuṣṭo mahādevaḥ prabhāṃ tāṃ pāṇḍunandana ।।

uvāca kliśyate kasmād bāle tvaṃ brūhi ceṣṭitam ।
ahaṃ ca bhāskaropetaś cāntaraṃ naiva vidyate ।।

prabhovāca
nānyo devas tathā śambho bhartā puṣyati na kvacit ।
saguṇo vāpi cākhyāto nirguṇo dravyavarjitaḥ ।।

priyo vā yadi vā dveṣyaḥ strīṇāṃ bhartā hi devatā ।
durbhagā tvena dagdhāhaṃ lokamadhye maheśvara ।।

alabdhasaukhyā bhartuś ca tena kliśye maheśvara ।

deva uvāca vallabhā bhāskarasya tvaṃ matprabhāvād bhaviṣyasi ।।

pārvaty uvāca
vallabhā tava vākyena bhāskare na bhaviṣyati ।
vṛthā kleśo bhaved eva prabhāyās tatra kā kathā ।।

devīvākyena rudreṇa dhyātas timiranāśanaḥ ।
āgato gaganād bhānur narmadāyottare taṭe ।।

bhānur uvāca kasmād āhvānito deva andhakāsuranāśana ।

deva uvāca prabhāṃ pālaya he bhāno santoṣeṇa pareṇa ca ।।

prabhāyā mandire nityaṃ sthīyatāṃ himanāśana ।
evaṃ labdhavarā devāt prabhā sthāpyāha śaṅkaram ।।

svāṃśena sthīyatām atra tīrthamunmīlayānagha ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca sarvadevam ayaṃ liṅgaṃ sthāpitaṃ pāṇḍunandana ।।

prabhāseśvaranāmedaṃ sarvaloke ca durlabham ।
anyāni yāni tīrthāni kāle te api phalanti vai ।।

prabhāsaṃcāpi rājendra sadyaḥ puṇyaphalapradam ।
māghamāse ca saptamyāṃ viśeṣaphaladaṃ bhavet ।।

aśvaṃ yo dāpayet tatra yathoktaṃ brāhmaṇe nṛpa ।
indrasya prāpyate lokam athavā bhāskaraṃ vrajet ।।

daurbhāgyaṃ naśyate tatra snānamātreṇa pāṇḍava ।
tatra tīrthe tu yo bhaktyā kanyādānaṃ prayacchati ।।

brāhmaṇāya vivāhārthe dāpeyat pāṇḍunandana ।
samānavayase vipre kulīne dhanine tathā ।।

yo dadāti mahārāja mahāpātakasaṃyutaḥ ।
tasya pāpaṃ ca naśyeta udake lavaṇaṃ yathā ।।

svāmidrohodbhavaṃ pāpaṃ yatpāpaṃ steyasambhavam ।
kūṭasākṣyapradaṃ pāpaṃ cāṇḍālavratacāriṇām ।।

dāmbhikaṃ vṛkṣakacchedam agamyāgamanodbhavam ।
grāmakūṭodbhavaṃ yac ca garadaṃ vā pravārakam ।।

vidyāvikrayaṇe yac ca saṃsargodbhavapātakam ।
patnīdrohodbhavaṃ ghoraṃ sarvadrohodbhavaṃ nṛpa ।।

brahmahatyā ca yatpāpaṃ yatpāpaṃ bhūmihāriṇaḥ ।
govadhe caiva yatpāpaṃ gurvagnibrāhmaṇeṣu ca ।।

jambūplakṣāhvayau dvīpau śālmaliś ca bhaven nṛpa ।
kuśakrauñcas tathā śākaḥ puṣkaraś caiva saptamaḥ ।।

tatpāpaṃ vilayaṃ yāti kanyādānena pāṇḍava ।
bhittvātha bhāskaraṃ lokaṃ śubhaṃ vrajet ।।

krīḍate rudralokastho yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ।
sarvapāpakṣaye jāte śivo bhavati bhāvataḥ ।।

tāvad bhramati tattīrthaṃ prabhāsaṃ pāṇḍunandana ।
so aśvamedhaphalaṃ prāpya satyam īśvarabhāṣitam ।।

godānaṃ ca mahatpuṇyaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram ।
pratyakṣaṃ surabhīṃ tatra jaladhenuṃ tathādṛtaḥ ।।

tiladhenupradātā ca aśvadātā tathaiva ca ।
kanyāvidyāpradātā ca akṣayaṃ lokam āpnuyāt ।।
