bhūrivastrāṃ kṣīrayuktāṃ dhānyopaskarasaṃyutām ।
dāpayet sarvakāmo atha surabhīṃ nṛpasattama ।।

saptasāgaraparyantā veṣṭitā tena bhārata ।
dvīpeśvare tu rājendra vṛṣotsargaṃ jitendriyaiḥ ।।
sarvakālaṃ tu kartavyaṃ caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe prabhāsatīrthamahimānuvarṇano nāma daśādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra narmadādakṣiṇe taṭe ।
sthāpitaṃ vāsuker nāmnā aśeṣāghaughanāśanam ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
āḥ kasmāt kāraṇāt tāta sthāpitaṃ dakṣiṇe taṭe ।
tattvaṃ sarvaṃ mamākhyāhi tv aśeṣaṃ dharmakāraṇam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu tvaṃ kuruśārdūla yaḥ praśnaḥ kriyate tvayā ।
bhairavaṃ rūpamāsthāya nṛtyaṃ śambhuś cakāra ha ।।

tac chramāj jāyate svedo gaṅgātoyavimiśritaḥ ।
tatraiva pannagaḥ snāto haratoyavimiśrite ।।

mandākinī tataḥ kruddhā vyālasyopari bhārata ।
ajagaratvamāpnoṣi uragaṃ cābravīt tadā ।।

vāsukir uvāca
anugrāhyo asmy ahaṃ pāpo bhavatyā harasambhṛte ।
trailokyapāvanī puṇyā sarit tvaṃ śubhalakṣaṇe ।।

saṃsāracchedanakarī ārtā nāmārtināśinī ।
svargadvārasthite devi dayāṃ kuru mamopari ।।

gaṅgovāca
cara tvaṃ vipulaṃ nāga tapo vai śaṅkaraṃ prati ।
tatas tapaś cacārāsāv īśvarārādhanaṃ param ।।

tataś ca dhyāyato devaṃ damayukto abhavat sa ca ।
tato varṣaśate pūrṇe uparuddho jagadguruḥ ।।

āgatya tatsamīpasthaḥ ślakṣṇāṃ vāṇīm udāharat ।
varaṃ varayatu śreṣṭhaṃ pannaga tvaṃ mahābala ।।

pannaga uvāca
yadi tuṣṭo asi me deva varaṃ dātuṃ triśūlabhṛt ।
tadā me dīyatāṃ sthānaṃ svakīyaṃ vṛṣavāhana ।।

īśvara uvāca
prasanno ahaṃ mahābāho revāṃ gaccha śubhāṃ tvaram ।
yāmye caiva taṭe puṇye snānaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ ।।

ityuktvā antardadhe devo vāsukis tvaritānvitaḥ ।
rūpeṇājagareṇātha viveśa narmadājale ।।

mārgeṇa tasya taj jātaṃ jāhnavyāḥ srota uttamam ।
nirdhūtakalmaṣaḥ sarpaḥ sa jāto narmadājale ।।

sthāpitaś ceśvaras tatra narmadāyā yudhiṣṭhira ।
tena nāgeśvaro bhūmyāṃ sarvapāpavināśanaḥ ।।

aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ madhunā snāpayec chivam ।
vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo jāyate hy analo yathā ।।

aputrā ye narāḥ pārtha snānaṃ kurvanti saṃgame ।
te labhante śubhān putrān kārtavīryopamān api ।।

śrāddhaṃ tatraiva ye bhaktyā upavāsaparāyaṇāḥ ।
kurvanti tārayanti svān narakān nṛpanandana ।।

evam ākhyātavān asmi tava snehād viśeṣataḥ ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca tato gacchec ca rājendra mārkaṇḍeśvaram uttamam ।।

narmadādakṣiṇe kūle gīrvāṇair vanditaṃ śubham ।
guhyād guhyataraṃ tīrthaṃ nākhyātaṃ kasyacin mayā ।।

sthāpitaṃ ca mayā puṇyaṃ svargabhogaṃ ca muktidam ।
jñānaṃ tatraiva me jātaṃ prasādāc chaṅkarasya ca ।।

anyasūktaṃ ca yo dhyāyed drupadaṃ ca jale japet ।
so api ghorād aghaughāc ca mucyate pāṇḍunandana ।।

vācikair mānasaiś cāpi karmajair api pāṇḍava ।
pañcendriyāṇyavaṣṭabhya yāmyāmāśāṃ ca saṃsthitaḥ ।।

yo japet salile bhaktyā ityevaṃ śaṅkaro abravīt ।
śrāddhaṃ tatraiva yo bhaktyā kurute nṛpanandana ।।

pitaras tasya vai tṛptā yāvadāhūtasamplavam ।
āmalair badarair bilvair akṣatair vā jalena vā ।।
tarpayet tatra yaḥ pretān pretā yānti śubhāṃ gatim ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe mārkaṇḍeśvaramahimānuvarṇano nāmaikādaśādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam ।
uttare narmadākūle yajñavāṭasya madhyataḥ ।।

saṃkarṣaṇaṃ ca vikhyātaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pāpanāśanam ।
tapaścīrṇaṃ purā rājan narmadāyās taṭe śubhe ।।

balabhadreṇa rājendra prāṇinām upakārakam ।
gīrvāṇaiś caiva tatraiva sannidhau nṛpanandana ।।

umayā sahitaḥ śambhuḥ sthitas tatraiva keśavaḥ ।
yas tatra snāpayed bhaktyā jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ ।।

ekādaśyāṃ site pakṣe mantreṇa snāpayec chivam ।
śrāddhaṃ tatra ca yo bhaktyā pretānāṃ vai pradāpayet ।।

sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ balabhadravaco yathā ।
tato gacchec ca rājendra manmatheśvaram uttamam ।।

snānamātro naro rājan yamalokaṃ na paśyati ।
anapatyā tu yā nārī snāpayet pāṇḍunandana ।।

putraṃ sā labhate pārtha satyavantaṃ dṛḍhavratam ।
tatra snātvā naro rājan muniḥ prayatamānasaḥ ।।

upoṣya parayā bhaktyā gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।
tatra nṛtyaṃ prakurvanti ye narā bhaktimānasāḥ ।।

gītavāditrasaṃyuktaṃ rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ śubham ।
sahāmbiko mahādevas tuṣṭo vai manmatheśvaraḥ ।।

kiṃ kariṣyati saṃruṣṭo yamas taṃ na ca paśyati ।
kāmena sthāpitaṃ tatra etasmāt kāraṇāt nṛpa ।।

annadānena bho rājan kīrtitaṃ phalam uttamam ।
sopānaṃ svargamārgasya pṛthivyāṃ manmatheśvaraḥ ।।

viśeṣāt tatra saṃkhyātaṃ śrāddhadānena bhārata ।
annadānena bho rājan kīrtitaṃ phalam uttamam ।।
etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ tava bhaktyā tu bhārata ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe manmatheśvaramahimānuvarṇanonāma dvādaśādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra eraṇḍīsaṅgameśvaram ।
prakhyātaṃ sarvalokeṣu brahmahatyāpraṇāśanam ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
kāraṇaṃ naiva jāne ahaṃ tatsarvaṃ kathayasva me ।
evam uktas tu dharmātmā dharmaputreṇa dhīmatā ।।

kathayāmāsa tatsarvam ṛṣisaṅghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca kathitaṃ comayā pūrvaṃ śambhunā parameṣṭhinā ।।

tat te ahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi śrūyatāṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha ।

maheśvara uvāca atrir nāmāhvayo deva mānaso brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।।

agnihotrarato nityaṃ devatā atithipūjakaḥ ।
somaḥ saṃsthāpito atraiva kṛto vipreṇa parvate ।।

anasūyeti nāmnā vai tasya bhāryā guṇānvitā ।
pativratā patiprāṇā patyuḥ kāryahite ratā ।।

evaṃ jātaḥ sadā kālo na putro na ca putrikā ।
aparāhṇe mahābāho sukhāsīnau tu tau kvacit ।।

vadataḥ sukhaduḥkhāni daivadattāni yāni ca ।

atrir uvāca saumye śubhe priye kānte surūpe priyabhāṣiṇi ।।

pūrṇacandranibhākāre priyakāme nirālase ।
na tvayā sadṛśī loke trailokye sacarācare ।।

patiputrapriyā nārī suhṛjjanahite ratā ।
putreṇa lokāj jayati putreṇa paramā gatiḥ ।।

nāsti putrasamo bandhuḥ pṛthivyāṃ caiva dṛśyate ।
asipatravane ghore patantaṃ yo abhirakṣati ।।

durbhikṣeṣv api dainyādau vṛddhakāle api putrakaḥ ।
putraṃ vinā ca kiṃ bhadre jīvitaiḥ sadhanair api ।।

vyādhibhiḥ paribhūto api nirviṇṇo api yadā sutaḥ ।
lokalajjānayatrastaḥ pavitraṃ kartum arhati ।।

etad guṇasamāyukto nirguṇaḥ saguṇaḥ sutaḥ ।
putrahīne kutaḥ saukhyam iha loke paratra ca ।।

ahaś ca madhyarātre ca cintyamānaś ca sarvadā ।
śuṣyanti mama gātrāṇi grīṣme kusarito yathā ।।

anasūyovāca
yat tvayā sūcitaṃ vipra tatsarvaṃ śocayāmy aham ।
tavodvegakaraṃ kāryaṃ tan me dahati cetasi ।।

ye ca putrā bhaviṣyanti dīrghāyur guṇasaṃyutāḥ ।
tatkāryaṃ ca samīkṣe ahaṃ yena tuṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।

atrir uvāca
tapas taptaṃ mayā bhadre janmaprabhṛtiduṣkaram ।
vratopavāsair niyamaiḥ śākāhāreṇa sundari ।।

kṣīṇaṃ dehaṃ tu paśyāmi aśakto ahaṃ śubhānane ।
sthātuṃ śocāmi cātmānaṃ rahasyaṃ kathitaṃ mayā ।।

anasūyovāca
bhartaḥ pativratā nārī patiputravivarddhinī ।
trivargasādhanā sā ca sevyā sā vipule jane ।।

japastapastīrthayātrā putrejyāmantrasādhanam ।
vadanti guravaḥ sarve yathoktaṃ gurubhāṣitam ।।

anujñātā ca duḥkhe ahaṃ tapas tapsyāmi duṣkaram ।
putrārthinī bahudināny ahaṃ yāmi surottamam ।।

atrir uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahāprājñe mama santoṣakāriṇi ।
anujñātā mayā bhadre putrārthaṃ tapa ācara ।।

devānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ pitṝṇām anṛṇaṃ kuru ।
na bhāryā sadṛśo bandhus triṣu lokeṣu vidyate ।।

nahi devāḥ praśaṃsanti bhāryayā rahitaṃ sukham ।
sammukhe sammukhā yāti vilome ca parāṅmukhī ।।

tena bhāryā praśaṃsanti sadevāsuramānuṣāḥ ।
mahāvrate mahāprajñe satyarūpe śubhe kṣaṇe ।।

tapaścarasva śīghraṃ tvaṃ putrārthaṃ ca mamājñayā ।
etad vākyāvasāne sā sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇatā abravīt ।।

tvatprasādena viprendra sarvam etad avāpnuyām ।
haṃsalīlāgatir yāntī lolākṣī varavarṇinī ।।

viṣamasthānasūyā tu prāptāsau narmadāṃ nadīm ।
somanāthena tat tulyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।

ye smaranti divā rātrau yojanānāṃ śatair api ।
mucyante sarvapāpebhyo rudraloke vasanti te ।।

narmadāyāḥ samīpe tu dve taṭe dve ca yojane ।
praviśantī tapas tatra revāyāṃ varavarṇinī ।।

yasyā darśanamātreṇa naśyate pāpasaṃcayam ।
tataḥ tasyottare tīre pare parṇāśanā śubhā ।।

niyamasthā viśālākṣī śākāhāreṇa sundarī ।
stuvantī tu tato devāñ chubhaiḥ stotraiś ca saṃyatā ।।

grīṣmeṣu ca mahādevī pañcāgniṃ sādhayet tataḥ ।
varṣākāle sārdravāsācarac cāndrāyaṇaṃ vratam ।।

hemante ca tataḥ prāpte toyavāsābhavat tataḥ ।
prātaḥ snānaṃ tataḥ sāndhyaṃ kuryād devāditarpaṇam ।।

devānām arcanaṃ kṛtvā homaṃ kṛtvā yathā vidhi ।
evaṃ varṣaśate prāpte viṣṇurudrapitāmahāḥ ।।

samprāptā dvijarūpeṇa eraṇḍyāḥ saṅgamaṃ prati ।
saṃsthitā agratas tasyā vedam abhyuccaranti te ।।

anasūyā japaṃ tyaktvā nirīkṣantī muhurmuhuḥ ।
utthitā sā viśālākṣī arghaṃ dattvā yathāvidhi ।।

adya me saphalaṃ janma adya me saphalaṃ tapaḥ ।
darśanena tu viprāṇāṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

pradakṣiṇāṃ tataḥ kṛtvā sāṣṭāṅgaṃ praṇatā abravīt ।
kandamūlaphalair divyair adyāhaṃ tarpayāmi vaḥ ।।

viprā ūcuḥ
tapasā tu vicitreṇa tava satyena suvrate ।
tṛptā vai sarvakāmais tu tapasvinyāś ca darśanāt ।।

asmākaṃ kautukaṃ jātaṃ kim arthaṃ tapyate tvayā ।
svargamokṣaṃ tu rakṣārthaṃ tapas tapyasi duṣkaram ।।

anasūyovāca
tapasā sidhyate svargas tapasā paramā gatiḥ ।
tapasā caiva bho viprāḥ sarvakāmam avāpnuyāt ।।

brāhmaṇā ūcuḥ
tanvī śyāmā viśālākṣī snigdhāṅgī rūpasaṃyutā ।
haṃsalīlāgatis tvaṃ hi kiṃ cātmānaṃ viśoṣasi ।।

anasūyovāca
yuvatve ca tapaḥ kāryaṃ yuvatve paramā gati ।
yuvatve ca sutotpattir vṛddhatve sarvam apriyam ।।

viprā ūcuḥ
sādhu sādhu mahāprājñe varaṃ prārthaya suvrate ।
yat tvayā cābhilaṣitaṃ tatsarvaṃ pradadāmy aham ।।

ahaṃ viṣṇur ahaṃ rudro hy ahaṃ sākṣāt pitāmahaḥ ।
gūḍharūpadharā loke svacihnair upalakṣitāḥ ।।

tasyā vākyāvasāne tu svarūpaṃ darśayanti te ।
svaiḥ svai rūpaiḥ sthitā devāḥ sūryakoṭisamaprabhāḥ ।।

caturbhujo vāsudevaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।
atasīpuṣpavarṇas tu pītavāsā janārdanaḥ ।।

garutmān vāhanaṃ yasya śriyā ca sahito hariḥ ।
prasannavadanaḥ śrīmāñ chivarūpo vyavasthitaḥ ।।

sitavāsā mahābhāgaś caturvadanasaṃyutaḥ ।
haṃsoparisamārūḍho hy akṣamālākaro anagha ।।

āgato narmadātīre brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।
vṛṣabhaṃ tu samārūḍho daśabāhusamanvitaḥ ।।

bhasmoddhūlitagātras tu pañcavaktrastrilocanaḥ ।
jaṭāmukuṭasaṃyuktaś candrārdhakṛtaśekharaḥ ।।

etadrūpadharo devaḥ sarvavyāpī maheśvaraḥ ।
anasūyā tu tatraiva devānāṃ darśanāt param ।।

vepamānā rahasye tu tān paśyantī muhur muhuḥ ।
ahaṃ brahmā hy ahaṃ viṣṇur ahaṃ rudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।

ānanditā tu sā devī dṛṣṭvaitān mahāvrata ।

anasūyovāca kiṃ vyāpārāś ca ke yūyaṃ viṣṇurudrapitāmahāḥ ।।

tad ahaṃ śrotum icchāmīmaṃ praśnaṃ kathayantu te ।

brahmovāca prāvṛṭkālo hy ahaṃ prokta āpaś caiva prakīrtitaḥ ।।

megharūpo hy ahaṃ prokto varṣāmi vasudhātale ।
ahaṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāni prāksandhyā hyudite ravau ।।

etasmāt kāraṇād bhāvarahasyaṃ kathitaṃ mayā ।

viṣṇur uvāca hemantatvāc ca vihitaṃ viṣṇurūpaṃ carācaram ।।

pālanīyaṃ jagat sarvaṃ viṣṇor māhātmyam uttamam ।

rudra uvāca grīṣmakālo hy ahaṃ proktaḥ sarvabhūtakṣayaṃkaraḥ ।।

śoṣayāmi jagatsarvaṃ rudrarūpas tapasvini ।
evaṃ brahmā ca viṣṇuś ca rudraś caiva mahīpate ।।

tisraḥ sandhyās trayo devās trayaḥ kālās trayo agnayaḥ ।
tathā brahmā ca viṣṇuś ca rudraś caikatvam āgatāḥ ।।

varaṃ dadāmi te bhadre yat te manasi vartate ।

anasūyovāca vandhyā lokair ahaṃ loke khyāpyamānā ca sarvadā ।।

brahmā viṣṇuś ca rudraś ca prasādāt sumukhā yataḥ ।
parituṣṭās trayo devā durdharṣā api mamopari ।।

asmiṃs tīrthe tu sānnidhyaṃ varaṃ dadatu me adhunā ।

devā ūcuḥ evaṃ bhavatu te vākyaṃ yat tvayā prārthitaṃ śubhe ।।

pratyakṣā vaiṣṇavī māyā eraṇḍī caiva nāmataḥ ।

anasūyovāca yadi tuṣṭās trayo devā mama bhaktiprabodhitāḥ ।।

mama putrā bhavantv atra harirudrapitāmahāḥ ।

viṣṇur uvāca arthadāḥ putratāṃ yānti na kadācic chrutaṃ mayā ।।

bhadre dadāmi tān putrān devatulyaparākramān ।
pitṛtulyaguṇopetān somayāji bahuśrutān ।।

anasūyovāca
īpsitaṃ tu pradātavyaṃ yan mayā prārthitaṃ hare ।
nānyathā tac ca kartavyaṃ nivasantu mamodare ।।

śrībhagavān uvāca
pūrvaṃ tu bhṛgusaṃvāde garbhavāsa upārjitaḥ ।
tasyāhaṃ caiva pāraṃ tu na ca paśyāmi śobhane ।।

smaramāṇaḥ purāvṛttaṃ cintayāmi punaḥ punaḥ ।
evaṃ saṃcintyamānau hi pitāmahamaheśvarau ।।

ayonijā bhaviṣyāmastava putrāḥ suśobhane ।
yonivāsaṃ ca vai devā naiva yānti varānane ।।

ity uktvā ca tayā sārdhaṃ pratyakṣāste abhavaṃs tadā ।
trayo devā gatāḥ pārtha narmadāyottare taṭe ।।

prāptā varaṃ tu sā devī priyaṃ māhendraparvate ।
kṣīṇadehā ca sā nārī śuṣkadehā sudāruṇā ।।

kṛtayajñopavītā sā taponiṣṭhā śubhekṣaṇā ।
śilātale niṣaṇṇā sā apaśyat kāntā mahāvratam ।।

hṛṣṭā tuṣṭā mahādevī tiṣṭha kānteti cābravīt ।
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa munir dhīmān punaḥ kāntām uvāca ha ।।

atrir uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahāprājñe anasūye mahāvrate ।
asādhyaṃ sarvanārīṇāṃ varaṃ prāptāsi durlabham ।।

anasūyovāca
tvatprasādān maharṣe ahaṃ varaṃ prāptā ca durlabham ।
tenāhaṃ te prayacchāmi putrān ṛṣitapodhanān ।।

evam uktvā tato devī harṣeṇa mahatā yutā ।
alokayat tadā kāntaṃ tenāpi śubhadarśanā ।।

darśanād eva saṃjātaṃ lalāṭe maṇḍalaṃ śubham ।
navayojanasāhasraraśmi jālasamāvṛtam ।।

kadambagolakākāraṃ trigaṇaṃ parimaṇḍalam ।
tasya madhye tu deveśaḥ puruṣo divyarūpadhṛk ।।

hemavarṇaḥ sa vai devaḥ sūryakoṭisamaprabhaḥ ।
pūrvaputro anasūyāyāḥ sākṣād devaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।।

candramā iti vikhyātaḥ somaḥ putro nṛpātmaja ।
iṣṭaḥ putro varīyāṃs tu kalāṣoḍaśasaṃyutaḥ ।।

pratipac ca dvitīyā ca tṛtīyā ca tathā nṛpa ।
caturthī pañcamī ṣaṣṭhī saptamī cāṣṭamī tathā ।।

navamī daśamī caiva tathā caikādaśī parā ।
dvādaśī ca trayodaśī caturdaśī tataḥ param ।।

tataḥ pañcadaśī devī pūrṇamāsī prakīrtitā ।
amāvāsyā tu vikhyātā atha sā ṣoḍaśī kalā ।।

caturvidhasya lokasya sūkṣmo bhūtvā varānane ।
āpyāyate jagat sarvaṃ somo ayaṃ sacarācaram ।।

surāsurāś ca gandharvā rākṣasāḥ pannagās tathā ।
piśācāś ca tathādityāḥ pitaraś ca pitāmahaḥ ।।

sarve tam upajīvanti hutaṃ dravyaṃ tu tatsthitam ।
vanaspatigate some yacchindyāc ca vanaspatim ।।

bhuṅkte duḥkhaṃ ca vai mūḍho dahaty abdakṛtaṃ śubham ।
vanaspatigate some yo bhakṣed dantadhāvanam ।।

candramā bhakṣitas tena pitṛvaṃśas tu ghātitaḥ ।
amāvāsyāṃ tu rājendra snānaṃ kuryād yathāvidhi ।।

abdam ekaṃ viśālākṣi pitṝṇāṃ paramā gatiḥ ।
hiraṇyaṃ rajataṃ vastraṃ yo dadati dvijātiṣu ।।

sarvaṃ lakṣaguṇaṃ rājaṃl labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
etad guṇaviśiṣṭo asau somarūpaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।

saṃjātaḥ prathamaḥ putro anasūyāyās tu nandanaḥ ।
dvitīyas tu mahābhāga durvāsā nāma nāmataḥ ।।

sṛṣṭisaṃhārakartā ca svayaṃ sākṣān maheśvaraḥ ।
indro api śāpitas tena dvitīyena varānane ।।

dvitīyasya tu putrasya sambhavaḥ kathito mayā ।
dattātreyas tu nāmnā vai tṛtīyo madhusūdanaḥ ।।

jagadvyāpī jagannāthaḥ svayaṃ devo janārdanaḥ ।
avatīrṇo mahābhāgabrahmaśambhusamanvitaḥ ।।

putraprāptipadaṃ tīrthaṃ narmadāyottare taṭe ।
anasūyākṛtaṃ pārtha sarvapāpakṣayaṃ karam ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe eraṇḍītīrthamahimānuvarṇano nāma trayodaśādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
etasyānantaraṃ pārtha sauvarṇaṃ tīrtham uttamam ।
vikhyātaṃ triṣu lokeṣu sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram ।।

revāyāṃ durlabhaṃ snānaṃ saṅgamasya samīpataḥ ।
vibhaktaṃ hastamātraṃ ca puṇyakṣetre narādhipa ।।

suvarṇaśilake snātvā śāntiṃ yāti parāṃ śubhām ।
nirmitvā bhāskaraṃ devaṃ hotavyaṃ tu hutāśane ।।

bilvena ghṛtamiśreṇa bilvapatreṇa bhūriṇā ।
prīyatāṃ hi jagannātho vyādhir naśyatu me sadā ।।

dvijebhyaś cet prayuktaṃ syād yāgasya phalam āpnuyāt ।
tatra dānena prītātmā mṛtaḥ svargam avāpnuyāt ।।

śuklapakṣe tathāṣṭamyāṃ sopavāso jitendriyaḥ ।
yas tatra kurute śrāddhaṃ nṛdevabhaktito naraḥ ।।

samuddharet kule tatra daśapūrvān daśāparān ।
kāṃcanaṃ vāpi yo dadyād dhenuṃ caiva suśobhanām ।।

sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yatra devo maheśvaraḥ ।
pūjayitvā śivaṃ tatra śatrūṇāṃ vijayo bhavet ।।

putravān guṇavāṃś caiva sarvavyādhi vivarjitaḥ ।
ity evaṃ kathitaṃ rājan sauvarṇaṃ tīrtham uttamam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
etasminn antare tīrthaṃ karaṇḍeśvaram uttamam ।
prakhyātaṃ sarvalokeṣu narmadāyottare taṭe ।।

sarvapāpaharaṃ proktaṃ sarvaduḥkhaghnam uttamam ।
tato gacchec ca rājendra tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam ।।

saubhāgyakaraṇaṃ divyaṃ narāṇāṃ pāpanāśanam ।
tatra yā durbhagā nārī naro vā nṛpanandana ।।

snātvā arcayed umāṃ rudraṃ saubhāgyaṃ tasya jāyate ।
tṛtīyāyām ahorātraṃ sopavāso jitendriyaḥ ।।

nimantrayed dvijaṃ tatra sapatnīkaṃ surūpiṇam ।
gandhamālyair alaṃkṛtya puṣpadhūpādhivāsitam ।।

bhojayet pāyasānnena kṛśareṇātha bhaktitaḥ ।
bhojayitvā yathā nyāyaṃ pradakṣiṇam athācaret ।।

tvaṃ tu devo mahādeva sapatnīko vṛṣadhvaja ।
yathā te deva deveśa na viyogaḥ kadācana ।।

somanāthākhyakārpaṇyāt taṃ dhyāyām īha cintayan ।
jyeṣṭhe śukle tṛtīyāyāṃ saubhāgye narmadājale ।।

snātvā dattvā ca subhagā na priyeṇa viyujyate ।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca na daurbhāgyaṃ na dāridryaṃ na śoko na ca durgatiḥ ।।

etat sarvaṃ bhaved yena tatsarvaṃ kathayasva me ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca daurbhāgyaṃ durgatiṃ caiva dāridryaṃ śokavardhanam ।।

vaidhavyaṃ saptajanmani jāyate na yudhiṣṭhira ।
karmaṇā yena pāpānāṃ kṣayas tac ca vadāmi te ।।

jyeṣṭhe māse site pakṣe tatīyāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
tatra snātvā tu yo bhaktyā pañcāgniṃ sādhayet tapaḥ ।।

so api pāpair aśeṣais tu mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
gugguluṃ dāhayed yas tu gaurī śivasamīpataḥ ।।

tasmin karmaṇi viprasya uktāni bhavate tataḥ ।
dehapāte kṛte svargam ity evaṃ śaṅkaro abravīt ।।

śvetairaktais tathā pītair vastraiś ca vividhaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।
brāhmaṇīrbrāhmaṇāṃś caiva pūjayitvā yathāvidhi ।।

puṣpair nānāvidhaiś caiva gandhadhūpaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ ।
kaṇṭhe sūtraṃ samādhāya kuṅkumena vilepayet ।।

kalpayitvā striyaṃ gaurīṃ brāhmaṇaṃ śivarūpiṇam ।
tābhyāṃ dadyāt samādṛtya dānam utsṛjya vāriṇā ।।

karṇaveṣṭaṃ tvaṅgadaṃ ca kāñcanīṃ mudrikāṃ tathā ।
saptadhānyaṃ tathā deyaṃ bhojanaṃ nṛpasattama ।।

anyāni caiva dānāni tasmiṃs tīrthe narottama ।
sarvadānaiś ca yatpuṇyaṃ tatpuṇyaṃ triguṇaṃ bhavet ।।

tatra sāhasraguṇitaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।
śaṅkareṇa samaṃ tatra bhuṅkte bhogān anuttamān ।।

saubhāgyaṃ tasya vipulaṃ jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
aputro labhate putraṃ nirdhano dhanam āpnuyāt ।।
kāmadaṃ tīrtharājaṃ tu narmadāyāṃ vyavasthitam ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe saubhāgyatīrthamahimānuvarṇano nāma caturdaśādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra bhāṇḍāraṃ tīrtham uttamam ।
dāridryabhedakaraṇaṃ puruṣāṃś caikaviṃśatim ।।

dhanadena tapastaptaṃ prasannaḥ padmasambhavaḥ ।
tatraiva svasvadānena prāptaṃ vittamanantakam ।।

tatra gatvā tu yo bhaktyā snātvā vittaṃ prayacchati ।
tasya vittaparicchedo na bhavec ca kadācana ।।

tasyaivānantaraṃ rājan rohiṇītīrtham uttamam ।
vikhyātaṃ triṣu lokeṣu sarvapāpaharaṃ param ।।

yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
rohiṇītīrthamāhātmyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।
śrotum icchāmi tat tvena tan me tvaṃ vaktum arhasi ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tasminn ekārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ।
tasyodare śayānasya devadevasya pāṇḍava ।।

nābhyām abhūn mahatpadmaṃ ravimaṇḍalasannibham ।
kīrṇakākesarayutaṃ patraiś ca samalaṃkṛtam ।।

tatra brahmā samutpannaś caturvadanapaṅkajaḥ ।
kiṃ karomīti deveśa cintyamānaḥ svadehataḥ ।।

bhagavān abhavat tatra marīcir bharatādhipa ।
marīceḥ kaśyapo jātaḥ sarvasṛṣṭikaras tataḥ ।।

dakṣasyāpi tadā jātāḥ pañcāśat kanyakās tu vai ।
dadau sa daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayodaśa ।।

tathaiva ca parāḥ kanyāḥ saptaviṃśatim indave ।
rohiṇī nāma yā tāsāṃ madhye tārādhipānanā ।।

abhīṣṭā sarvanārīṇāṃ bhartuścāpi viśeṣataḥ ।
punaḥ sā niścayībhūtā tapase bho narādhipa ।।

tataḥ sā narmadātīre cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ।
ekarātraṃ dvirātraṃ ca ṣaḍdvādaśa tathāparaiḥ ।।

pakṣamāsopavāsaiś ca karṣayantī kalevaram ।
ārādhayantī satataṃ mahiṣāsuramārdinīm ।।

snātvā snātvā jale nityaṃ narmadāyāḥ śuciḥ smitā ।
tatas tuṣṭā mahābhāgā devī nārāyaṇī nṛpa ।।

prasannā te mahābhāge vratena niyamena ca ।
dadāmi te na sandeho varaṃ vṛṇu yathepsitam ।।

evaṃ śrutvā tu vacanaṃ rohiṇī śaśinaḥ priyā ।
varaṃ vavre tato devīm idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।

sarvāsāṃ ca sapatnīnāmadhikā śaśinaḥ priyā ।
yathā bhavāni hy acirāt tvatprasādāt tathā kuru ।।

evam astv iti sā proktā bhavānyā bhaktitatparaiḥ ।
stūyamānā suragaṇais tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।

tadā prabhṛti sā devī rohiṇī śaśinaḥ priyā ।
saṃjātā sarvalokasya vallabhā nṛpasattama ।।

tatra tīrthe tu yā nārī naro vā snāti bhaktitaḥ ।
vallabhā bhavate sā tu bhartur vai rohiṇī yathā ।।

tatra tīrtheṣu yaḥ kaścit prāṇatyāgaṃ karoti ca ।
saptajanmani tasyaiva viyogo naiva jāyate ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato gacchet tu rājendra cakratīrtham anuttamam ।
senāpureti vikhyātaṃ sarvapāpakṣayakaram ।।

saināpatye abhiṣiktena devadevena cakriṇā ।
abhiṣikto mahāsenaḥ sa devendrapurogamaiḥ ।।

dānavasya vadhārthāya vijayāya divaukasām ।
bhūmidānena viprendrāṃs tarpayitvā yathā vidhi ।।

śaṅkhabherīninādena paṭahānāṃ ca niḥsvanaiḥ ।
vīṇābhiś ca mṛdaṇgaiś ca jhallarīkāṃsyatālakaiḥ ।।

tacchrutvā ninadaṃ ghoraṃ dānavo baladarpitaḥ ।
surāṇāmāvighātārtham abhiṣekasya cāgrataḥ ।।
hastyaśvarathapattyādyaiḥ paripūrṇo ravākulaiḥ ।।
tatas tu tām raudravasya vāhinīṃ śaraiḥ suśārṅgojjhitakaiḥ sutīkṣṇaiḥ ।
vidhvasya hastyaśvarathān mahātmā cakraṃ vimuktaṃ madhughātinā ca ।।

dṛṣṭvā tu bhīṣaṇaṃ cakramabhivyāptaṃ ṣaḍānanaḥ ।
tyaktvā tatrāpy avasthānaṃ cakāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ।।

cakraṃ muktaṃ vināśāya hariṇā lokadhāriṇā ।
vihvalāṃ dāhayāmāsa papāta vimale jale ।।

niṣpāpaṃ tac ca saṃjātaṃ narmadāyāḥ prabhāvataḥ ।
prāvṛṭkāle śubhe pakṣe dvādaśyāṃ caiva bhārata ।।

yaś ca yāti jitakrodhaś cakratīrthaṃ haripriyam ।
so api pāpaiḥ pramucyeta yamaṃ ghoraṃ na paśyati ।।

rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kṛtvā dīpaṃ devasya dāpayet ।
kathāṃ ca vaiṣṇavīṃ tatra devadevaṃ samāhitaḥ ।।

bhīmavrataṃ ca pārākaṃ kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ tathā ।
vrataṃ sāntapanaṃ deva trirātravratakaṃ bhṛśam ।।

tared vaitaraṇīm ante bhīmaṃ cakramaharniśam ।
kūṭaśālmalivṛkṣāṃś ca kadācin naiva paśyati ।।
etat te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ cakratīrthasya yatphalam ।।
iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe cakratīrthamahimānuvarṇano nāma pañcadaśādhika śatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
dhūmapātaṃ tato gacchen mahāpātakanāśanam ।
samīpe cakratīrthasyā viṣṇunā nirmitaṃ purā ।।

mekalāṃ paramāṃ devīm imāṃ trailokyapāvanīm ।
kadācit payasāṃ rājā sāntaḥpuraparicchadaḥ ।।

śiṣṭair iṣṭair bandhubhiś ca arghapātreṇa saṃyutaiḥ ।
hastābharaṇasaṃyuktaiḥ puṇyair amalakāntibhiḥ ।।

candramaṇḍalamānaiś ca yuktair muktāphalais tathā ।
pravālalatikābhiś ca indranīlasamanvitaiḥ ।।

arghaṃ dadau tadā tasyai varuṇaḥ saritāṃ patiḥ ।
gaṅgādyāḥ saritaḥ sarvās tāpī cāpi payoṣṇikā ।।

nandinī nalinī puṇyā sarvam arghaṃ dadus tadā ।

narmadovāca madīye saṅgame divye snātvā santarpayanti ye ।।

tasya saptakulotpannāṃs tārayāmi na saṃśayaḥ ।
jalāñjaliṃ tato dattvā samudro vākyam abravīt ।।

dhanyo ahaṃ kṛtakṛtyo ahaṃ tvayā devi varānane ।
samāyātāsi bhadraṃ te māṃ cātra pāvanaṃ kuru ।।

narmadovāca pavitro asi mahābhāga ekākī tvaṃ mahodadhe ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca evaṃ bhagavatī rājan narmadā mekalā śubhā ।।

pūjitā sāgareṇāpi śubhe siṃhāsane sthitā ।
pāṇigrahaṃ gṛhītā sā purukutsena bhārata ।।

purukutsasya bhāryā sā gṛhadharmeṇa saṃyutā ।
sadā vai vartate rājaṃs tatraiva saṅgame śubhe ।।

puṣpavṛṣṭis tadā hy āsīt tridaśānāṃ mahotsave ।
tatra svayaṃvaraścāsīt saritaḥ pṛthivīpate ।।

tatra yaḥ kurute śrāddhaṃ sthānaṃ ca pitṛtarpaṇam ।
lakṣayajñaphalaṃ prāpya sa mukto nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

evaṃ trailokyapūjyā te narmadā lokapāvanī ।
tasyā māhātmyam atulaṃ kīrtitaṃ hi mahābhuja ।।

bhaktyā śrutvā mahābhāga rudraloke mahīyate ।
ādimadhyāvasāneṣu revāmāhātmyam uttamam ।।

yaḥ kaścic chṛṇuyād bhaktyā tasya syād vāñchitaṃ phalam ।
śrutvā māhātmyam atulaṃ yo naro hi jitendriyaḥ ।।

dānaṃ kuryāt tadā tasya sarvakāmārthasiddhayaḥ ।
pustakaṃ pūjayitvā tu dhūpadīpakacandanaiḥ ।।

dānaṃ tatra prakartavyaṃ brāhmaṇāṃś cāpi pūjayet ।
śravaṇena tu dānena suprītā narmadā bhavet ।।

tīrthe tīrthe ca kathitaṃ tatpūrvaṃ pāṇḍunandana ।
puṇyaṃ śrutvā tu māhātmyaṃ tad dānenaiva pāṇḍava ।।

etasmāt kāraṇād dānaṃ śrutvā dānaṃ hi kāraṇam ।
tac chrutvā rājaśārdūlo mārkaṇḍeyasya bhāṣitam ।।

arghaṃ dattvā yathānyāyaṃ pūjayitvā ṛṣīn sadā ।
aśvairgajais tathā rathair bhrātṛbhiḥ saha dharmarāṭ ।।

tīrthayātrāṃ cakārāśu narmadāyāṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।
uttare dakṣiṇe tīre snānapānāvagāhanam ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇe revākhaṇḍe yudhiṣṭhiramārkaṇḍeyasaṃvāde narmadācaritravarṇano nāma ṣoḍaśādhikaśatatamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

iti śrīskandapurāṇasya revākhaṇḍaḥ ।।
